**Deployment Attestation**
- Measured pure module `scripts/vite-build-sha.ts` resolves exact lowercase 40-hex HEAD, rejects dirty/missing/invalid git output, fails when unavailable outside development, and returns literal `development` only for explicit development. `vite.config.ts` is executable configuration and is measured through focused import coverage; its invocation plus `define` wiring for `__SPOONJOY_BUILD_SHA__` is asserted behavior, not a coverage exclusion. Public DB/auth-free `GET /health` returns exact JSON `{ status:"ok", service:"spoonjoy", buildSha }`, header `X-Spoonjoy-Build-Sha: <same value>`, `Cache-Control: no-store`, and `Content-Type: application/json`; production/QA reject `development`.
- All probes are immediate at t=0, then fixed intervals while scheduled time `<= deadline`; no new request starts later. Health fetch uses cache-busting query, `cache:"no-store"`, and a fresh 4-second AbortController timeout, so the final scheduled sample ends by deadline+4s; network/abort/non-200/malformed/mismatched body/header records one failed Health sample and polling continues. Health samples are t=0,5,...,180s. GitHub workflow REST calls use 10-second request timeouts: source-CI and production-run discovery are t=0,10,...,300s, while the already-selected production run and its deploy job are watched at t=0,10,...,1800s. Production discovery stops as soon as at least one exact automatic candidate exists in `queued|in_progress|completed`; it does not wait for completion. Cloudflare deployment capture uses one 30-second request. Exhaustion or malformed oracle fails its stage; timers are fake-clock tested and always cleared.
- Production's staged MCP canary performs no product/stateful mutation until candidate-version routing is stable. Integrated main commits `b07d787e` and `dcf296bd` already repair the proven `e7b0e9ec` mismatch with two consecutive three-channel cycles: real-browser navigation and APIRequest both GET protected-resource metadata, while a second real browser loads then submits the no-store, side-effect-free `/.well-known/spoonjoy-release-readiness` React Router action to prove the browser mutation channel. That readiness POST is transport-only and explicitly allowed before stability; signup, auth grants, D1/R2 writes, and every other product mutation remain forbidden. Redirect-safe CDP interception adds the override to every same-origin hop and never leaks it cross-origin. Unit29.1 preserves those regressions and tightens stability to the final contract here. Each cycle requires all three responses HTTP 200 with exact candidate `X-Spoonjoy-Worker-Version`; three consecutive successful cycles run one second apart within one 120-second deadline. Any network/non-200/missing/old-version result resets the count to zero, each request is capped at `min(10 seconds, remaining deadline)`, and equality to the deadline fails. Every later same-origin canary request still sends the override and asserts the candidate header. The orchestrator's rollback remains authoritative on any later mismatch.
- QA base is exactly `https://spoonjoy-v2-qa.mendelow-studio.workers.dev`. Commands are exact: `pnpm cleanup:remote:qa:apply`; `pnpm cleanup:remote:qa -- --assert-clean`; `pnpm run qa:preflight`; `pnpm run deploy:qa`; health to branchHeadSha; `node scripts/smoke-api-live.mjs --target-env qa --base-url https://spoonjoy-v2-qa.mendelow-studio.workers.dev --out /Users/arimendelow/desk/spoonjoy-v2/clem-feedback-e2e/artifacts/release-<ReleaseRun.run>/unit-33/stage-<StageRun.run>/qa-api-smoke/attempt-<Command.attempt>/out`; `node scripts/smoke-live.mjs --target-env qa --base-url https://spoonjoy-v2-qa.mendelow-studio.workers.dev --release-identity-sha256 <identitySha256> --release-attempt-path <attemptPath> --out /Users/arimendelow/desk/spoonjoy-v2/clem-feedback-e2e/artifacts/release-<ReleaseRun.run>/unit-33/stage-<StageRun.run>/qa-lifecycle-smoke/attempt-<Command.attempt>/out`; crash-safe `qa-cleanup-reconcile` immediately after deployment capture and before broad cleanup; final `pnpm cleanup:remote:qa -- --assert-clean`. `--keep-smoke-data` is forbidden; smoke owns mutation cleanup in finally, and only assert-clean plus smoke's exact per-user proof are release oracles.
- Production base is exactly `https://spoonjoy.app`; workers.dev is not a release oracle. Commands after exact workflow/deploy/health are `pnpm run production:readiness`; crash-safe `production-cleanup-reconcile`; `pnpm cleanup:production -- --assert-clean`; API/lifecycle/visual smoke; final `pnpm cleanup:production -- --assert-clean`. The reconcile command is exact `node scripts/smoke-live.mjs --target-env production --reconcile-cleanup --failed-attempts-json <J> --release-identity-sha256 <identitySha256> --release-attempt-path <attemptPath> --out <O>`, where J is canonical compact JSON of BINARY-sourceIdentitySha256/attemptPath-sorted unique CleanupReconcileTarget values selected from the current identity and its hash-valid repair-predecessor chain, or `[]`; at most one target may still be incomplete because no next smoke may start until it is reconciled. Before signup each QA/production smoke creates a random 128-bit lowercase-hex recoveryNonce, derives memory-only email `codex-smoke-<first32 lowercase hex emailDigest>@example.com`, where emailDigest is HMAC-SHA-256 of UTF-8 token bytes and `spoonjoy-smoke-email-v1\0<recoveryNonce>`, and derives exact password `Sj1!<passwordDigest>`, where passwordDigest is unpadded base64url HMAC-SHA-256 over distinct message `spoonjoy-smoke-password-v1\0<recoveryNonce>`. Raw email, token, and password exist only in child memory and request bodies, never argv, stdout/stderr, artifacts, diagnostics, or persisted state. Exact `CleanupRecoveryIdentity={targetEnvironment:'qa'|'production',targetBaseUrl,userId:string|null,recoveryNonce,emailSha256,credentialDerivation:'hmac-sha256-v1',credentialKeySha256}` stores only its declared nonsecret target/user/nonce fields plus lowercase SHA-256 of the derived email and, as the sole explicit secret-digest exception, the raw D1 token; recovery reconstructs and hash-checks email/password in memory. A failed/incomplete cleanup alone writes compact canonical no-LF `cleanup-incomplete-diagnostic.json` with exact `CleanupIncompleteDiagnostic={version:1,phase,targetEnvironment,targetBaseUrl,sourceIdentitySha256,attemptLocator,recoveryIdentity,cleanupPhasePath,cleanupPhaseSha256,purgeTargets,completedTargets,remainingTargets,failureCode,createdAt}`; attemptLocator is a TaskArtifactLocator and remaining paths are source-task-relative, target arrays are exact BINARY-sorted subsets/partition, and the file is immutable after atomic write. Reconcile first compares the current token hash during side-effect-free preflight, derives the same password, reauthenticates only the recorded user, hash-validates diagnostic/phase/targets and its separate successor lineage and cleanup proof chains, and resumes the same purge/projection/user-delete state machine idempotently with the cleanup logs below. A missing or changed token returns typed preflight `credential_missing` with zero mutation; no alternate/global cleanup is attempted. Every selected attempt must produce a nonnull already_clean/reconciled proof and broad assert-clean must pass before a fresh Unit37 user is created. Recovery reruns the same J/output attempt read-first; no fresh smoke can strand prior residue. Normal smoke commands use resolver-owned identity.deskTaskRoot output paths. Unit30 updates `smoke:live` default/package script to canonical domain. Smoke owns finally cleanup; broad assert-clean plus exact per-attempt proof establish zero product residue while allowing only declared inaccessible DO metadata.
- The `cleanup-incomplete-diagnostic.json` chronology and schema replace “failed/incomplete alone writes” and the abbreviated schema above. Exact `CleanupRecoveryIdentity={targetEnvironment:'qa'|'production',targetBaseUrl,userId:string|null,recoveryNonce,emailSha256,credentialDerivation:'hmac-sha256-v1',credentialKeySha256}` and `CleanupIncompleteDiagnostic={version:1,phase,targetEnvironment,targetBaseUrl,sourceIdentitySha256,attemptLocator,recoveryIdentity,cleanupPhasePath,cleanupPhaseSha256,purgeTargets,completedTargets,remainingTargets,failureCode,createdAt}` use phase `prepared|user_created|targets_recorded|cleanup_incomplete`. Before signup the runner atomically creates prepared with null userId/cleanupPhase fields/failureCode and empty arrays. After signup and each target/cleanup checkpoint it crash-safely rewrites the complete file through a token-qualified fsynced candidate, preserving createdAt/nonce/key hash and advancing phase; userId becomes nonnull at user_created, target arrays form a BINARY-sorted exact partition at targets_recorded, cleanupPhase fields become nonnull when the phase log exists, and failureCode becomes nonnull only at cleanup_incomplete. If the child dies before a later phase, the executor accepts/hashes the latest complete schema-valid phase as the retained failed-attempt diagnostic; prepared recovery reauthenticates by derived email and rediscovers the exact disposable user/targets, or proves signup never occurred. Successful cleanup atomically removes the journal before the passed closed output is finalized, so it never enters the 14/38-file passed sets. A same-token partial candidate beside an intact main is removed and rebuilt because no dispatch precedes main readback; a same-token initial candidate without main is removed because signup cannot precede prepared-main readback; foreign, multiple, wrong-token, or corrupt-main state fails closed; tests fault before/after signup, response loss, every rewrite, process signal, TERM/KILL, and successful removal.
- Cleanup recovery identity and diagnostic target binding are replaced by exact `CleanupRecoveryIdentity={targetEnvironment:'qa'|'production',targetBaseUrl,userId:string|null,recoveryNonce,emailSha256,credentialDerivation:'hmac-sha256-v1',credentialKeySha256}` and `CleanupIncompleteDiagnostic={version:1,phase,targetEnvironment,targetBaseUrl,sourceIdentitySha256,attemptLocator,recoveryIdentity,cleanupPhasePath,cleanupPhaseSha256,purgeTargets,completedTargets,remainingTargets,failureCode,createdAt}`. Environment/base must be QA/QaBaseUrl or production/ProductionBaseUrl and byte-equal between diagnostic, recovery identity, reconcile target, and executing ProcessSpec; attemptLocator is the exact task-artifact locator for the failed command. Target/environment/base participate in every diagnostic hash and target key. Cross-environment, cross-base, raw physical path, or omitted locator recovery rejects before credential or provider access.
- Deployment capture calls exact single-page Cloudflare endpoint `GET https://api.cloudflare.com/client/v4/accounts/$CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_ID/workers/scripts/<script>/deployments` with bearer token, using script `spoonjoy-v2-qa` for QA and `spoonjoy-v2` for production. The API schema has no pagination cursor; success requires exact successful envelope/result.deployments array and rejects duplicate/invalid ids, noncanonical created_on, HTTP/API error, or an unexpected pagination field. Normalize source only to `github_actions|wrangler|dashboard|unknown|null`, never provider text; normalize each result to `{id,createdAt:created_on,source}`, sort createdAt descending then id BINARY, and compute after-minus-before ids sorted BINARY. Empty difference is legal and makes no activity claim; a nonempty QA delta selects the unique maximum `(createdAt,id)` and likewise makes no causality claim. Exact health SHA is QA authority and the automatic workflow is production authority.
- Immediately before merge Unit36 captures normalized production deployments. Unit37 carries that immutable set, first discovers completed-success canonical `.github/workflows/ci.yml` push at mergeSha, then discovers automatic `.github/workflows/production-deploy.yml` workflow_run with the same head and exact triggering CI databaseId and runAttempt. Unit29.1 modifies the production workflow run-name to use exact `ci-run-${{ github.event.workflow_run.id }}-attempt-${{ github.event.workflow_run.run_attempt }}`; discovery parses that immutable id and rejects a source-only match. At first candidate poll retain exact path/event/head/trigger candidates in queued|in_progress|completed, sort createdAt then databaseId, and freeze newest; workflow_dispatch/wrong edge never qualify. watch-workflow polls selected id through 1800 seconds and requires completed/success; later runs never replace it. verify-deploy-job requires completed-success deploy. Terminal workflow preserves selected databaseId/path/event/head/trigger/url/createdAt while status/conclusion evolve. Download exact canary artifact, hash/parse production-release.json, and require no-extra-fields `status:"promoted"`, sourceSha mergeSha, treeHash branchHeadTreeSha, triggeringCiDatabaseId/runAttempt equal CiWorkflow.databaseId/runAttempt, valid candidate Worker version, and databaseRollbackSupported false. CI edge, workflow, job, artifact, canonical health, and source-tagged Worker jointly attest production; unrelated deployments remain evidence and are never guessed as causal.

**Release Evidence Manifest**
- In TrackDisposition/TrackArchive, `taskArchiveKind` is exactly `desk_archive|predecessor_supersede`; `taskArchiveSha256` is Sha256 of final `desk-archive.v1.json` bytes for desk_archive or final `predecessor-supersede.v1.json` bytes for predecessor_supersede, never a directory/tree hash. `scanDeskSha` is the fetched Desk main commit whose tree was scanned. The later ArchiveValidationReceipt records `trackDispositionCommitSha`, the already-existing commit containing the disposition; TrackDisposition never self-references its own commit SHA.
- Unit37 `workflow-discovery` argv is the registered form already listed plus exact ordered pairs `--triggering-ci-database-id <CiWorkflow.databaseId> --triggering-ci-run-attempt <CiWorkflow.runAttempt>` immediately before `--out`; every later workflow/artifact command verifies the same field transitively.
- Previously named release schemas are exact: `BranchProtection={repo,branch,strict,requiredLinearHistory,requiredContextNames,capturedAt}`; `CheckSet={repo,prNumber,sourceSha,checks}`; `ReviewThreadSet={repo,prNumber,sourceSha,unresolvedCount,threadIds}`; `MergeReadiness={repo,prNumber,testedBaseSha,sourceSha,treeSha,remoteBaseSha,headSha,headTreeSha,strict,requiredLinearHistory,requiredContextNames,checks,unresolvedThreadIds,ready}`; and `Continuation={repo,prNumber,sourceSha,treeSha,mergeSha,excludedHeadRef,openPrNumbers,openBranchRefs,openPrCount,openBranchCount,unresolvedThreadIds,followUpIssueIds,ready}`. All are no-extra-fields; openPrNumbers is numeric-ascending unique, every string array is UTF-8/BINARY-sorted unique, counts are nonnegative safe integers equal to their paired array lengths, times canonical, identifiers exact, and ready is the conjunction of the stated identity/merged/exclusion and all-zero invariants. Provider-only observations are exact no-extra-fields `QaDeployObservation={targetSha,inventoryDisposition:'delta'|'no_delta',deployment,health}`, `PullRequestObservation={number,url,state:'OPEN',headRef,headSha,baseRef,baseSha,title,bodySha256}`, and `MergeObservation={prNumber,state:'MERGED',sourceSha,testedBaseSha,squash}`; they deliberately contain no disposition or intent/root hashes. `EnsureProbe={version:1,operation,operationKeySha256,targetSha,observedAt,result,observation}` has result `exact_effect|absent_complete|indeterminate|conflict`; observation is the matching provider-only observation only for exact_effect and null otherwise. Unit29.2 alone materializes the full QaDeployOutcome/PullRequest/MergeOutcome by adding the authority-selected disposition, intentSha256, and rootIntentSha256 after validating the probe against the current attempt. Production `Workflow` and `ProductionRelease` additionally require `triggeringCiDatabaseId` and `triggeringCiRunAttempt`, equal the selected CiWorkflow databaseId/runAttempt; `.github/workflows/production-deploy.yml` has an exact run-name `ci-run-${{ github.event.workflow_run.id }}-attempt-${{ github.event.workflow_run.run_attempt }}`, which discovery parses to prove the CI-to-production workflow_run edge. QaDeployObservation delta requires nonnull normalized after-minus-before Deployment; no_delta requires deployment null plus exact target health. Check object arrays use the execution-contract-defined comparator and reject duplicate names.
- Reservation mode has exact domain `process|agent`. ReleaseContinuity.nextUnit is deterministic: it is null for `superseded|failed|passed`; for active it is the earliest unit `32..37` whose latest StageRun is missing, running, or failed; after Unit37's latest stage is passed but before finish-run it is null. Initial transfer is exactly 32. The lastTerminal triplet names the numerically latest existing terminal StageRun, with greatest run number inside that unit, and is all null only when none exists.
- Release ownership is immutable and task-specific. Exact no-extra-fields `ReleaseTaskIdentity={kind,task,repairRootTask,repairPredecessorTask,repairDepth,branch,repoCwd,deskTaskRoot,taskSourcePath,taskArchivePath,trackPath,productPlanningPath,productDoingPath,productContinuityPath,deskDoingPath,prTitle,prBody}` uses `kind:'primary'|'repair_successor'`, normalized repo-relative document/Desk paths, absolute real non-symlink cwd/root paths, and nonempty title/body. Primary has repairRootTask equal task, repairPredecessorTask null, and repairDepth zero. A repair successor inherits repairRootTask, sets repairPredecessorTask to the immediate predecessor task, and sets repairDepth to predecessor depth plus one; depth is a safe integer and the chain rejects cycles, skipped depths, repeated task names, or a predecessor whose identity/hash cannot be resolved uniquely through active/task/archive/TrackArchive receipts. A repair successor derives task=`successorSlug`, branch=`worker/<successorSlug>`, repoCwd=`/Users/arimendelow/Projects/spoonjoy-v2-<successorSlug>`, deskTaskRoot=`/Users/arimendelow/desk/spoonjoy-v2/<successorSlug>`, source/archive/track/Desk-doing and reviewed planning/doing/continuity paths from the hash-valid successor task, prTitle=`Repair Spoonjoy post-merge <first12 successorKey>`, and prBody=`Repairs Spoonjoy post-merge failure <successorKey>; the reviewed execution contract is <productDoingPath>.` with no trailing LF. PostMergeSuccessorAttempt freezes only successorKey/slug/lineage while prepared, freezes task path plus immutable task-seed path/hash after task creation; mutable task.md may advance only through declared Desk lifecycle transforms, and freezes the complete identity/hash only at contract_approved; existing task/worktree/branch/doc/lineage drift rejects at every phase. Every manifest, ProcessSpec, AgentCommand prompt, PR head/title/body, continuation exclusion, validating transition, TerminalCleanup, DeskArchive, TrackDisposition, validator, and receipt reads only its manifest's identity. Fixed Clem literals elsewhere describe the primary identity only and are never inherited by a repair successor.
- Primary ReleaseTaskIdentity bytes are exactly kind `primary`, task `clem-feedback-e2e`, repairRootTask `clem-feedback-e2e`, repairPredecessorTask null, repairDepth `0`, branch `worker/clem-feedback-e2e`, repoCwd `/Users/arimendelow/Projects/spoonjoy-v2-clem-feedback`, deskTaskRoot `/Users/arimendelow/desk/spoonjoy-v2/clem-feedback-e2e`, taskSourcePath `spoonjoy-v2/clem-feedback-e2e`, taskArchivePath `spoonjoy-v2/_archive/clem-feedback-e2e`, trackPath `spoonjoy-v2/track.md`, productPlanningPath `worker/tasks/2026-07-14-1313-planning-clem-feedback-e2e.md`, productDoingPath `worker/tasks/2026-07-14-1313-doing-clem-feedback-e2e.md`, productContinuityPath `worker/tasks/2026-07-14-1313-doing-clem-feedback-e2e/AUTOPILOT-STATE.md`, deskDoingPath `spoonjoy-v2/clem-feedback-e2e/spoonjoy-v2/2026-07-15-adopted/doing.md`, prTitle `Ship Clem feedback end to end`, and prBody `Ships Clem's accepted feedback end to end; the reviewed doing contract is worker/tasks/2026-07-14-1313-doing-clem-feedback-e2e.md.`. Successor identity requires the same field order and the exact formulas above at contract_approved; no field may remain null at manifest init. Every `identitySha256` is lowercase SHA-256 of the UTF-8 bytes of compact `JSON.stringify` serialization of those exact fields in schema order, with no insignificant whitespace or final LF; no caller-supplied hash or alternate property order is accepted.
- The active manifest path is `<ReleaseTaskIdentity.deskTaskRoot>/artifacts/release-evidence.v1.json`; task archival moves it unchanged beneath that identity's taskArchivePath, and any whole-track archival re-roots it beneath the generation-qualified TrackArchive target. It has no extra fields and exact top-level `{version:1,identity:ReleaseTaskIdentity,writerId,revision,updatedAt,preReleaseArtifacts:PreReleaseArtifact[],terminalArtifacts:TerminalArtifact[],runs:ReleaseRun[]}`. `writerId` is one canonical lowercase UUID v4 created at initialization and immutable through archive: primary initializes at Unit32, while a repair successor initializes at manifest_ready before Work Doer. Primary preReleaseArtifacts and terminalArtifacts are empty; repair-successor membership follows the Round 59 closed registries. revision is a nonnegative safe integer and updatedAt is canonical ISO. Initialization stores revision zero and one clock reading; every successful state-changing manifest operation stores `revision+1` and `updatedAt=max(clockNow,previousUpdatedAt+1ms)` in the same atomic rewrite. An exactly idempotent/no-op call preserves both; recover increments once only when it repairs/interrupts state, while provisional winner-tree abandonment restores the pushed predecessor's unchanged pair. Revision/date overflow rejects before mutation. Canonical ISO means `new Date(x).toISOString()===x`; Sha is lowercase 40-hex; sha256 is lowercase 64-hex; required strings are nonempty. Every stored artifact/log/report/process/intent/arm/dispatch/handoff/outcome path is a normalized `/`-separated task-relative path beginning `artifacts/`, with no empty, `.`, or `..` segment, and resolves against identity.deskTaskRoot; the one root continuity path is exactly `release-continuity.v1.json`. No absolute stored artifact path is legal, so archive re-rooting preserves validity.
- Ordinary rewrites of an existing valid manifest use exact sibling `release-evidence.v1.json.tmp`, validate complete candidate bytes, fsync/close, rename over main, fsync the parent, and then remove any valid orphan ordinary temp; invalid main or temp fails closed. Initialization never uses that ordinary temp. It creates exact token-qualified `release-evidence.v1.json.init.<writerId>.tmp` plus no-extra-fields `manifest-init-candidate.v1.json={version:1,writerId,identitySha256,tempPath,tempSha256,initialManifestSha256,startedAt}` under the same same-host lock. Candidate is fsynced before the token temp; tempSha256 and initialManifestSha256 both bind the exact valid revision-zero bytes. Dead-owner recovery with missing main validates lock/candidate/identity: an absent or zero-byte owned temp is removed with candidate and retried using the same writerId; exact complete hash-valid bytes are promoted by rename and parent fsync; nonzero partial/mismatch, unbound temp, foreign token, multiple candidate, fixed ordinary temp, or malformed sidecar fails closed. If main is already exact, recovery removes only its matching init temp/candidate/lock. Thus every initialization crash has one deterministic promote/remove/fail-closed branch. The tested helper validates before and after every write.
- Release command execution uses `REPO_CWD=ReleaseTaskIdentity.repoCwd` and `DESK_TASK_ROOT=ReleaseTaskIdentity.deskTaskRoot`. A tested `resolveCommandAttemptPaths` accepts only a manifest-owned relative `artifacts/release-<positive>/unit-<32..37>/stage-<positive>/<logicalName>/attempt-<positive>` matching the active run/stage/command, resolves it below DESK_TASK_ROOT, and proves every existing parent real/non-symlink with no escape. Under manifest lock, start creates sibling `.attempt-<A>.<reservationToken>.tmp`, writes/fsyncs exact `attempt-reservation.v1.json={version:1,writerId,releaseRun,unit,stageRun,logicalName,attempt,mode,reservationToken}`, creates declared zero-byte scaffolding, and for ensure writes/fsyncs/hashes operation-intent plus ensure-arm. It fsyncs bottom-up, renames to `attempt-<A>`, fsyncs parent, then atomically records the matching command/token/artifacts in the manifest. Intent/arm authority remains provisional until exact remote Desk readback; no process may spawn earlier. Unreferenced recovery follows the exact Round 49 two-tree rule: zero-scaffold or byte-valid intent/arm reservation, with the latter removable only under unchanged remote predecessor, no remote arm/dispatch/handoff/gate/release/process/outcome, zero logs, and zero provider/child calls. Manifest-referenced provisional abandonment separately requires the execution-contract-defined winner-tree proof. Any extra/nonzero/malformed/unmatched/remote-armed tree fails closed. Referenced ordinary/armed attempts are terminalized only after exact liveness proof and never reused. Reviewer attempts use the same reservation protocol without process logs. Stored paths normalize to identity-task-relative artifacts and re-root only through identity DeskArchive/TrackArchive receipts.
- The unreferenced-reservation removal sentence above is replaced by this exact closed recovery rule. An exact next-attempt staging or final reservation may be removed when its tree is either reservation plus zero-byte declared scaffolding, or reservation plus zero-byte scaffolding plus the byte-valid operation-intent and ensure-arm named by that reservation. The second form additionally requires fetched origin/main still equals the frozen pre-attempt Desk predecessor, no manifest references the attempt, neither intent nor arm exists remotely, no dispatch/handoff/gate/release/process/outcome/artifact beyond those two files exists locally or remotely, both logs are zero, and the injected provider/child call count is zero. Any extra/nonzero log, remote trace, malformed cross-link, wrong predecessor, process evidence, or ambiguous state fails closed. This covers the crash after final-directory rename and before manifest rewrite without making a mutation-capable reservation adoptable.
- Provisional abandonment is a distinct nonterminal recovery operation, never an interrupted command. Local provisional commit L must be clean and contain only the exact next running ensure attempt atop pushed remote predecessor O; current origin/main must still have O's exact pre-attempt task tree. Recovery constructs/pushes the execution-contract-defined winner-tree merge K with tree O and parents O,L, ff-only advances local to K, and returns `abandoned:1` without adding a manifest command or continuity event. The next `start-command` therefore reuses the same attempt number with a fresh token/host/intent/arm. Any remote trace of the arm, nonzero log, process call, or tree mismatch makes abandonment illegal.
- `scripts/release-executor.ts` is the sole production ProcessCommand owner and package command `pnpm release:execute -- --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --command-json J`. Import-safe `createReleaseExecutor(deps)` performs the identical lifecycle in tests and production: side-effect-free environment/capability preflight, start-command, exact Desk commit/push/readback, optional ensure dispatch-CAS, prepare-spawn, spawn the nonmutating gate, record-process, release-spawn checkpoint, immutable release-file creation, gate-mediated child exec with streaming sanitizer and timeout enforcement, finish-command, terminal Desk commit/push/readback, and recovery/winner convergence. The gate and every generation are part of the same total timeout; actual registered argv cannot execute before its released checkpoint is remote-readable. Exported `runReleaseExecutorCli(argv,deps)` builds the complete result in memory and returns exact `{exitCode,stdout,stderr}` bytes without writing. The executable wrapper performs exactly one injected synchronous write of the selected nonempty stream and no write for the empty stream. On a passed terminal ProcessCommand it returns exit 0, exact compact finish-command success JSON plus newline on stdout, and empty stderr. On a terminal ProcessCommand failure it returns exit 1, empty stdout, and exact compact `{\"ok\":false,\"code\":\"process_failed\",\"failureReason\":<finite>}` plus newline on stderr. Argument, preflight, lifecycle, checkpoint, artifact, filesystem, or other executor failure returns exit 2, empty stdout, and exact compact `{\"ok\":false,\"code\":<argument|preflight|state|lock|schema|artifact|io|checkpoint>}` plus newline on stderr. A complete write preserves that exact contract; an injected short write or throw exits 2 and makes no byte-exact JSON claim because already-written process bytes cannot be retracted. No code path emits raw argv/path/prompt/secret/exception/stack/free text, and a persisted failed command can never produce exit zero. Units32-37 invoke this command for every ProcessCommand and never reproduce those steps manually. AgentCommand and terminal product/Desk cleanup remain outside this executor.
- Environment preflight is mandatory before state mutation, and its original in-memory deadlineStartedAt is persisted by start-command after success. Shared `preflightProcessEnvironment` returns exact public/secret proofs with the same PATH/HOME/TMPDIR/account/host/capability validation and nonserialization rules. Common gate/registered-child keys are PATH, HOME, CI=1, NO_COLOR=1, FORCE_COLOR=0, plus TMPDIR iff resolved. base is common; local-db adds exact `DATABASE_URL:'file:./test.db?connection_limit=1&socket_timeout=60'`; github uses HOME-backed gh; cloudflare adds account and HOME-backed Wrangler OAuth; cloudflare-rest additionally resolves exact Wrangler OAuth JSON to one memory-only bearer and maps it only into its registered Cloudflare REST child; cloudflare-d1 transports the raw D1 token through a fresh one-shot anonymous descriptor for the preflight probe and independently through a fresh descriptor for every later registered D1 command; only the child receives CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN; cloudflare-github uses both stores. Only the exact role, token, and authority-B64 internal keys defined below may supplement this table. Missing/invalid input rejects with zero mutation and a crash before start-command simply restarts preflight with no persisted attempt.
- Ensure dispatch is a second pushed compare-and-swap checkpoint, distinct from arm. After the armed `mutate_once` executor's production probe returns complete absence, it invokes exact `prepare-dispatch`, which creates/hashes `ensure-dispatch.v1.json`, records its task-relative path on the running ProcessCommand, commits, normal-pushes from the current arm checkpoint, fetches, and byte-verifies current origin/main before the registered provenance process may receive the sole mutation dependency. A cross-host handoff may transfer the same global root and retain `mutate_once` only when its normal push wins before any dispatch; rejected handoff/dispatch fetches the winner and forbids mutation. Once any authoritative dispatch exists, later attempts are `reconcile_only`; another host may observe an exact-effect probe in memory only but may not persist or materialize, certify absence/death, spawn, interrupt, replay, fail the run, or change dispatch. The dispatch host may replay or materialize only after exact role-tagged token-member liveness is false. Thus each operationKey has one immutable dispatch, at most one concurrent child, and at most one effective target state. Loss of the dispatch host blocks terminal progress rather than risking invented liveness.
- Unit29.2 is the sole file/manifest authority interpreter. It reads and schema/hash/cross-link validates the intent, arm, and dispatch files, then constructs canonical no-extra-fields `EnsureInvocationAuthority={version:1,operation,operationKeySha256,targetSha,releaseRun,reservationToken,executionHost,mode,rootIntentSha256,intentSha256,armSha256,dispatchSha256,dispatchProbeSha256}`. `mode` is `mutate_once|reconcile_only`; mutate_once requires current executionHost equal dispatch.executionHost and all hashes/identities byte-equal, while reconcile_only never exposes a mutation dependency. Unit29.1 provider code receives only this already-validated object (or null for the first read-only probe), parses its schema and checks operation argv identity, and is forbidden from reading manifest/intent/arm/dispatch/handoff/process paths or deciding liveness/replay. For a gate-mediated ensure child, Unit29.2 serializes unpadded base64url of the canonical UTF-8 object only as `SPOONJOY_RELEASE_ENSURE_AUTHORITY_B64`; the provider CLI parses it and exposes the named mutation dependency iff mode is mutate_once. This object, never path interpretation inside Unit29.1, is the complete serialized authority channel.
- Every ProcessCommand runs with cwd REPO_CWD through `createReleaseExecutor`, sanitized streams, and the seven exact policies: `base`, `local-db`, `github`, `cloudflare`, `cloudflare-rest`, `cloudflare-d1`, and `cloudflare-github`. Internal `SPOONJOY_RELEASE_ENSURE_AUTHORITY_B64` exists as opaque gate-to-child transport for ensures; `SPOONJOY_RELEASE_SPAWN_TOKEN` and `SPOONJOY_RELEASE_PROCESS_ROLE` exist on gate and child for liveness; `SPOONJOY_RELEASE_SECRET_FD` exists only in a `cloudflare-rest` or `cloudflare-d1` gate bootstrap until consumed as specified below. Every other SPOONJOY key is unset. Before each spawn, prepare-spawn appends exact `SpawnGeneration={generation,spawnToken,status,gatePath,releasePath,processIdentity,preparedAt,recordedAt,releasedAt,endedAt}`. Status/nullability remain prepared/recorded/released/aborted/ended as defined; role-tagged runtime members do not alter immutable generation history.
- Exact gate path is `<attempt>/spawn-<generation>-gate.v1.json` and exact release path is `<attempt>/spawn-<generation>-release.v1.json`. Gate bytes are immutable no-extra-fields `{version:1,releaseRun,unit,stageRun,logicalName,attempt,generation,spawnToken,executionHost,commandSha256,releasePath}`; releasePath is task-relative and commandSha256 hashes compact canonical JSON of the exact resolved execution argv passed after the gate's standalone `--`; the gate recomputes it before waiting. Release bytes are immutable no-extra-fields `{version:1,releaseRun,unit,stageRun,logicalName,attempt,generation,spawnToken,releasedAt}` and byte-equal the released manifest fields. Both are reservation infrastructure, not Artifacts, and the closed-set validator allows exactly the generation-declared files: gate always exists after prepare-spawn, release exists iff release authority was physically emitted. prepare-spawn atomically writes/fsyncs gate bytes plus the manifest generation and pushes/readbacks both before spawning.
- The executor spawns the same exact gate argv as detached group leader with token and role=gate. The gate validates file/token/command hash, waits for release, then spawns registeredArgv in the same PGID with the same token and role=child; ensure authority is inherited opaquely. It stays until child exit. Recovery accepts only the exact role/member matrices in Round 36 and treats any verified member as live. record-process persists gate identity; release-spawn pushes before release-file creation. TERM/KILL targets the verified group and completion requires every verified token member reaped.
- Gate/manifest crash classification retains exact orphan/spawn/release-file rules, but liveness is the complete role-tagged token member set. Synchronous spawn failure aborts prepared generation through finish-command spawn_error. A durable released generation with missing release file is recoverable only on its executionHost and only for the verified live gate; a dead set is reconciled before replay/materialization. Other hosts probe in memory only and never persist or terminalize. Replay marks every dead released generation ended then appends; postdispatch materialization does the same. Predispatch materialization instead requires zero generations/global dispatch. Only declared output specs receive out paths.
- Every ProcessSpec carries one exact total timeout started before preflight and covering every sequential preflight, filesystem, checkpoint, provider, gate, child, finish, and readback phase. One durable checkpoint has a 120000ms aggregate cap; normal lifecycle has five=600000ms and ensure lifecycle six=720000ms. Capability preflight is 30000ms and local file work 20000ms, so fixed overhead is 650000ms ordinary and 770000ms ensure. `operationPhaseCapMs`, rather than a contradictory child cap, includes every provider horizon, mutation child, final observation request, and gate wait: workflow-watch/deploy-job 1810000ms; QA ensure 1810000ms (=300000 pre-dispatch observation + 600000 mutation + 910000 post-dispatch reconciliation); PR/merge ensure 730000ms (=300000 + 120000 + 310000); CI/workflow discovery 310000ms; production visual 900000ms; lifecycle smokes and qa/production-cleanup-reconcile 360000ms; app/Workers coverage, E2E, and build 1200000ms; every other argv 300000ms. Exact totals are workflow-watch/deploy-job 2580000; qa-deploy-ensure 2700000; pr-ensure/merge-ensure 1620000; ci-workflow-discovery/workflow-discovery 1080000; production-visual-dogfood 1680000; lifecycle smokes and qa/production-cleanup-reconcile 1140000; app-coverage/workers-coverage/e2e/build 1980000; every other ProcessSpec 1080000. Thus the no-race maxima are respectively 2460000, 2580000, 1500000, 960000, 1550000, 1010000, 1850000, and 950000, each strictly below its total. The reconcile cap covers one incomplete cleanup's maximum 305 seconds plus termination; additional authorized ancestry entries must already be clean or are processed in separate fresh commands before any new smoke. Winner-convergence retries share the same total deadline and may exhaust it safely rather than extending time. Every async dependency accepts one AbortSignal and a remaining-time cap; no provider horizon is subordinate to a smaller phase cap. Each gate/child is one process group; deadline sends SIGTERM, waits exactly 5000ms, sends SIGKILL if needed, and reaps. TERM/KILL timeout results fail with null exit/warning. Unproven death leaves command running and same-host recovery resumes exact-generation kill/reap; another host cannot terminalize. Fake-clock tests exhaust every full phase sum, equality, checkpoint, TERM/KILL, descendant, recovery, and timer-cleanup branch.
- The sole executable manifest interface is `pnpm release:evidence -- <subcommand>` in import-safe `scripts/release-evidence-cli.ts`; all subprocesses receive argv arrays, never shell text. Every command requires flags in listed order; equals-style, duplicate/unknown/misordered flags, extras, empty values, and post-subcommand `--` reject before lock/mutation. Complete mutating grammar is: `init --manifest M --identity-json J`; `recover --manifest M --writer-id W`; `start-run --manifest M --writer-id W --tested-base-sha T --branch-head-sha H --branch-head-tree-sha B`; `start-stage --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --start-sha S`; `start-command --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --command-json J`; `prepare-spawn --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt A`; `record-process --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt A --generation N --pid I --pgid J --process-start-identity X`; `release-spawn --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt A --generation N`; `prepare-handoff --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt A --to-execution-host X`; `prepare-dispatch --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt A --probe-json E`; `materialize-ensure-outcome --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt A --probe-json E --authority predispatch_existing|postdispatch_reconciled`; `finish-command-without-process --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt A --reason predispatch_indeterminate|predispatch_conflict|dispatch_ambiguity`; `finish-command --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt A --generation N --process-result exit:<0..255>|spawn_error|signal|timeout:term|timeout:kill --stream-status clean|invalid_utf8|nul`; `start-agent-command --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --role Q`; `finish-agent-command --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt A --agent-id D --verdict CONVERGED`; `finish-agent-command --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt A --agent-id D --verdict FINDINGS --findings-json J`; `interrupt-agent-command --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt A --agent-id none|D --reason stalled|errored|tool_unavailable`; `append-artifact --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --kind K --path P`; `set-merge-sha --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --merge-sha S`; `record-pre-merge-disposition --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit 32|33|34|35|36 --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt none|A`; `record-post-merge-disposition --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt none|A`; `resume-external-wait --manifest M --writer-id W --wait-path P`; `resolve-pre-merge-blocker --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit 32|33|34|35|36 --stage-run G --logical-name L --disposition P`; `start-agent-runtime-probe --manifest M --writer-id W --wait-path P`; `finish-agent-runtime-probe --manifest M --writer-id W --wait-path P --probe-ordinal N --agent-id D --report-json J`; `resolve-post-merge-blocker --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --stage-run G --logical-name L --disposition P`; `finish-stage --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --status passed --end-sha S --evidence-json J`; `finish-stage --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --status failed --end-sha S`; `supersede-run --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --end-sha S`; `fail-run --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --end-sha S --reason dispatch_ambiguity|operator_abandonment|post_merge_finding|post_merge_repair`; and `finish-run --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --end-sha S`. The list also includes exact `transfer-continuity --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit 32 --stage-run G --tested-base-sha T --branch-head-sha H --branch-head-tree-sha B --out O`. Identity JSON is compact canonical ReleaseTaskIdentity and legacy init flags reject. Prepare/release-spawn obey gate-generation rules; prepare-dispatch requires absent_complete; materialize requires exact_effect provider observation and current authority; predispatch requires zero generations while postdispatch requires every released generation member dead; finish-command names latest generation. both disposition commands derive every decision/evidence byte from persisted evidence and have no decision override. Remaining lifecycle invariants are unchanged and byte-tested.
- Agent review is an exact non-process attempt lifecycle. `AgentCommand={mode:'agent',logicalName,attempt,reservationToken,status,role,promptSha256,requiredArtifactsSha256,outPath,agentId,verdict,interruptionReason,runtimeEpoch,retryOrdinal,deadlineStartedAt,deadlineAt,startedAt,endedAt,reportPath,reportSha256}` is no-extra-fields. `status` is `running|interrupted|failed|passed`; role is the frozen logical-name role; reservationToken and agentId are canonical lowercase UUIDs when nonnull; prompt/artifact/report hashes are Sha256; outPath/reportPath are task-relative and reportPath is inside outPath. Running has null agentId/verdict/interruptionReason/endedAt/report fields. Interrupted has canonical endedAt, reason `stalled|errored|tool_unavailable|recovery`, nullable agentId, and null verdict/report fields. Failed has nonnull agentId, verdict `FINDINGS`, canonical endedAt, null interruptionReason, and nonnull task-relative `review-findings.v1.json` path/hash. Passed has nonnull agentId, verdict `CONVERGED`, canonical endedAt, null interruptionReason, and the role-specific nonnull clean report path/hash. `start-agent-command` creates one fresh attempt/out directory, derives exact prompt/review-input hashes, appends the running command, and returns `{attempt,runtimeEpoch,retryOrdinal,deadlineStartedAt,deadlineAt,prompt,promptSha256,requiredArtifactsSha256,outPath}`. CONVERGED accepts only the token and writes/hashes/appends the canonical clean report; FINDINGS accepts only the Round 36 canonical JSON, writes/hashes/appends its sanitized finding report, and fails. Malformed/unstructured output fails schema without a repair artifact. Agent attempts have no process argv, executionHost, generations, exit/warning/failure/terminalSource, stdout, stderr, or log artifacts. runtimeEpoch and retryOrdinal are positive; retryOrdinal is sequential for the exact release/unit/logical-name/runtimeEpoch key and capped at two before the durable agent-runtime wait. deadlineStartedAt equals startedAt and deadlineAt is exactly +1800000ms.
- Every ProcessSpec stores exact `operands:{index,kind}[]`, BINARY/numeric unique and exhaustive for nonliteral positions; omitted indices are literal. Values after `--manifest|--out|--intent|--arm|--dispatch` are task_relative, values after `--workflow-path` are repo_relative, and git pathspecs after standalone `--` are repo_relative; these are the only nonliteral rules in the frozen registry and each concrete entry's array is source/byte-tested. Literal and repo_relative bytes remain unchanged, repo_relative resolves only under REPO_CWD, and task_relative alone stores normalized task paths and re-roots absolute. Sentinels are legal only at matching task_relative indices. `prepare-handoff` writes exact handoff/interrupt on source and target consumes it. prepare/record/release-spawn are per-generation/idempotent only for exact bytes. materialize requires exact_effect plus predispatch_existing with zero generations or postdispatch_reconciled with every released role-tagged member dead; it performs no provider mutation and terminalizes the command itself. fail-run reasons retain the finite domain above.
- Agent prompts are byte-frozen. Generic prompt is exact newline-terminated UTF-8: `Spoonjoy release review v1\nrole: <role>\nsource_sha: <sha>\nplanning_path: <ReleaseTaskIdentity.productPlanningPath>\ndoing_path: <ReleaseTaskIdentity.productDoingPath>\nrequired_artifacts_sha256: <sha>\nscope: <role-scope>\nrules: read-only; cite file and line for every finding; return exactly CONVERGED only when no findings; otherwise return canonical compact JSON with top-level verdict and findings conforming to the declared ReviewFinding schema\n`. Exact role-scope strings are `implementation=behavior, architecture, recovery, and integration correctness`; `test=coverage, oracle quality, boundary, race, and failure completeness`; `security_privacy=authentication, authorization, secrets, privacy, and destructive-operation safety`; `migration_config=schema, migration, Cloudflare, workflow, and deployment configuration`; `design_visual=responsive visual quality, interaction states, and design-system consistency`; `api_compatibility=REST v1, OpenAPI, MCP, generator, and backward compatibility`; and `visual_qa=live rendered routes, viewport evidence, interaction behavior, and artifact integrity`. Generic CONVERGED report bytes are exactly eight LF-terminated lines: `spoonjoy-release-review-v1`, `role: <role>`, `agent_id: <uuid>`, `verdict: clean`, `source_sha: <sha>`, `prompt_sha256: <sha256>`, `required_artifacts_sha256: <sha256>`, `finding_count: 0`. Visual CONVERGED reports use only the separately defined `# Spoonjoy Production Visual Review` eight-line format; generic and visual parsers reject the other format. For Unit37 visual roles the prompt inserts `live_target: https://spoonjoy.app\nvisual_artifact_set_sha256: <sha256>\nvisual_rule: invoke visual-qa-dogfood read-only against the declared live target and immutable artifact set.\n` immediately before rules; Unit34 design_visual does not. `ReviewInput={sourceSha,requiredArtifacts,requiredArtifactsSha256,liveTarget,visualArtifactSetSha256}` is exact: `requiredArtifacts` is a BINARY-path-sorted unique `{path,sha256}[]`, its hash is SHA-256 of compact canonical JSON with field order path/sha256, and live/visual fields are both null outside Unit37 visual roles. Selection is registry-owned, never caller-supplied: Unit32 uses every Artifact from latest passed attempts of its first eighteen ProcessCommands; Unit34 uses every Artifact from latest passed `fetch-drift` and `pr-ensure`; each Unit37 visual review uses all 38 immutable BINARY-sorted direct-child visual-runner output Artifacts plus that command's stdout/stderr log Artifacts. `ProcessCommand={mode:'process',logicalName,attempt,reservationToken,executionHost,status,command,storedCommandSha256,envNames,timeoutMs,deadlineStartedAt,deadlineAt,spawnGenerations,terminalSource,outPath,intentPath,armPath,dispatchPath,startedAt,endedAt,exitCode,warningCount,failureReason,interruptionReason,stdoutPath,stderrPath}` is no-extra-fields. `failureReason` is null except failed, where it is exactly `spawn|timeout_term|timeout_kill|signal|sanitizer_invalid_utf8|sanitizer_nul|exit|warning|output|provider_indeterminate|provider_conflict|dispatch_ambiguity`; `interruptionReason` is null except interrupted, where it is `recovery|cross_host_handoff|operator_abandonment`. Running and interrupted have terminalSource null; finish-command terminalizes with `process`; materialize terminalizes with `materialized`; finish-command-without-process terminalizes with `without_process`. Passed/failed have canonical endedAt; predispatch materialized pass requires zero generations and intent host, while postdispatch materialized pass requires every released role-tagged member dead on the dispatch host. `StageRun.commands` remains ordered ProcessCommand|AgentCommand.
- The continuity adapter makes Unit32's first logical command executable without mutating frozen tracked files. It verifies identity task root/state and the active ReleaseRun/Unit32 StageRun, validates supplied identities against the manifest, emits only `{status:'ready'}`, and creates no final file. `ReleaseContinuity={version:1,identitySha256,task,branch,planningPath,doingPath,continuitySourcePath,writerId,manifestRevision,releaseRun,testedBaseSha,branchHeadSha,branchHeadTreeSha,mergeSha,releaseStatus,lastTerminalUnit,lastTerminalStageRun,lastTerminalStatus,nextUnit,manifestPath:'artifacts/release-evidence.v1.json',updatedAt}` and `ContinuityTransfer={version:1,identitySha256,task,branch,planningPath,doingPath,continuitySourcePath,writerId,manifestRevision,releaseRun,testedBaseSha,branchHeadSha,branchHeadTreeSha,mergeSha:null,releaseStatus:'active',lastTerminalUnit:null,lastTerminalStageRun:null,lastTerminalStatus:null,nextUnit:32,manifestPath:'artifacts/release-evidence.v1.json',continuityPath:'release-continuity.v1.json',continuitySha256,updatedAt}` are exact/no-extra-fields; task/branch/paths/hash byte-equal ReleaseTaskIdentity and manifestRevision/time byte-equal the persisted manifest. Initial transfer has null merge/terminal fields, active status, and nextUnit 32. Later mergeSha is Sha/null; releaseStatus is `active|superseded|failed|passed`; terminal fields are all null or exact unit/stage/status; nextUnit is null or 32..37 from latest stages/run status. Finish-command crash-safely writes continuity around the authoritative manifest rename; every later mutation refreshes it to the same persisted revision/time, no-op preserves both, and recover repairs only from validated manifest without advancing time. Desk task remains lifecycle locator; release-evidence plus release-continuity are post-transfer authority and archive unchanged. Pre-resolution argv remains exact transfer-continuity vector with only the final task-relative out sentinel replaced.
- Read-only grammar is exactly `validate --manifest M --mode active|archive`; it has no writer/lock/mutation, re-roots by mode, and validates manifest/continuity/evidence/hashes/closed set/sidecar zero. Every success is one compact no-extra-fields JSON plus newline on stdout and empty stderr. Exact success objects are: init `{writerId}`; recover `{writerId,interrupted,repaired,abandoned,handoffPath}`; start-run `{releaseRun,status:'active'}`; start-stage `{stageRun,status:'running'}`; start-command `{attempt,reservationToken,executionHost,argv,envNames,stdoutPath,stderrPath,outPath,intentPath,armPath,dispatchPath}`; prepare-spawn `{generation,spawnToken,gatePath,releasePath,status:'prepared'}`; record-process `{generation,status:'recorded',pid,pgid,processStartIdentity}`; release-spawn `{generation,status:'released'}`; prepare-handoff `{status:'interrupted',handoffPath}`; prepare-dispatch `{status:'prepared',dispatchPath}`; materialize-ensure-outcome `{status:'materialized',outPath,sha256}`; finish-command-without-process `{status:'failed',warningCount:0,failureReason:'provider_indeterminate'|'provider_conflict'|'dispatch_ambiguity'}`; finish-command `{status:'passed'|'failed',warningCount,failureReason}`; start-agent-command `{attempt,runtimeEpoch,retryOrdinal,deadlineStartedAt,deadlineAt,prompt,promptSha256,requiredArtifactsSha256,outPath}`; finish-agent-command `{status:'passed'|'failed',reportPath}`; interrupt-agent-command `{status:'interrupted'}`; append-artifact, append-pre-release-artifact, and append-terminal-artifact `{path,sha256}`; transfer-continuity `{status:'ready'}`; set-merge-sha `{mergeSha}`; record-post-merge-disposition `{classification,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,retryOrdinal}` or zero-mutation `{classification:'preflight_recovered',dispositionPath:null,dispositionSha256:null,retryOrdinal}`; resume-external-wait provider returns `{status:'waiting',waitPath,waitSha256,waitOrdinal,notBefore}` or `{status:'resolved',resolutionPath,resolutionSha256,owningUnit,runtimeEpoch:null,nextRuntimeEpoch:null}`; resolve-pre/post-merge-blocker and authorize-pre/post-merge-blocker return blocked `{status:'blocked',dispositionPath,dispositionSha256}` where legal or resolved `{status:'resolved',resolutionPath,resolutionSha256,owningUnit}`; start-agent-runtime-probe `{probeOrdinal,runtimeEpoch,prompt,promptSha256,deadlineStartedAt,deadlineAt}`; finish-agent-runtime-probe returns waiting `{status:'waiting',waitPath,waitSha256,waitOrdinal,notBefore}` or resolved `{status:'resolved',resolutionPath,resolutionSha256,owningUnit,runtimeEpoch,nextRuntimeEpoch}`; record-pre-merge-disposition `{status:'retry_same_unit'|'external_wait'|'human_blocker'|'fix_current_branch',dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,evidencePath,evidenceSha256,retryOrdinal}`; finish-stage passed `{status:'passed',evidencePath}` or failed `{status:'failed',evidencePath:null}`; supersede-run `{status:'superseded'}`; fail-run `{status:'failed'}`; finish-run `{status:'passed'}`; validate `{valid:true,releaseRun,status}`. Successor initialize-manifest and terminal recovery/authorization use their Round 59 exact result objects. Every listed object rejects extra fields; paths/nulls/numbers follow their named schemas. CLI failure is nonzero, empty stdout, and one sanitized `{ok:false,code}` stderr line with finite `argument|preflight|state|lock|schema|artifact|io|checkpoint`; executor wrapper obeys its separate 0/1/2 contract. All dependencies are injectable and Unit29.2 byte-tests every result.
- One-time initialization is the sole mutation without an already-existing manifest writerId. Exact `init --manifest M --identity-json J` validates canonical ReleaseTaskIdentity bytes, generates the proposed writerId, acquires the ordinary hard-link lock with that writerId, and executes only the token-qualified candidate/temp protocol above. Dead same-host recovery reuses that writerId and deterministically promotes exact complete initial bytes or removes only absent/zero-byte owned temp state; live/cross-host/malformed/multiple/nonzero-mismatch state fails closed. Initialization never creates the ordinary rewrite temp and may never replace an existing nonidentical valid or invalid manifest.
- After initialization, every mutating helper call must present the manifest's exact writerId and acquire exact sibling `release-evidence.v1.lock` before reading the manifest. Acquisition writes, fsyncs, and closes exact owner `{version:1,writerId,token,executionHost,hostname,pid,processStartIdentity,acquiredAt}` at unique `release-evidence.v1.lock.<token>.candidate`; it hard-links candidate to absent lock, fsyncs parent, unlinks candidate, and fsyncs again. Token is lowercase UUID-v4; executionHost is the frozen host hash; hostname is nonempty informational text; pid positive; processStartIdentity exact; time canonical. Existing lock fails closed. Release rereads same writerId/token/executionHost then unlinks/fsyncs. Crash recovery permits lock+candidate only when byte-identical, token/filename match, and lstat proves equal device/inode. Live or EPERM exact pid/start identity fails closed; dead-owner recovery is legal only when current executionHost equals owner executionHost and exact start-identity probe proves ESRCH/reuse, never from hostname equality. It then uses token-qualified stale rename/fsync/reacquire. Different inode/content, extra sidecar, different executionHost, malformed owner, changed identity/token, link/rename race, or unknown probe fails hard. Lone dead candidate/lock uses same exact-host route. Read-only validation never touches sidecars. Every terminal StageRun checkpoint requires sidecar zero. Thus same-writer concurrency is locked and resume can recover only a proven dead exact-host predecessor.
- The sole exception to ordinary cross-host lock/liveness rejection is pre-dispatch ensure handoff. It never steals a lock: it begins from the clean pushed arm checkpoint after sidecar zero and uses normal Git push as CAS against prepare-dispatch. A winning handoff transfers the same root's mutate_once eligibility; a winning dispatch forbids handoff and leaves every other host read-only for exact-effect observation only.
- `ReleaseRun` is exact `{run,status,failureReason,createdAt,endedAt,testedBaseSha,branchHeadSha,branchHeadTreeSha,mergeSha,stages}`: run positive/sequential; status `active|superseded|failed|passed`; failureReason is exact `dispatch_ambiguity|operator_abandonment|post_merge_finding|post_merge_repair` iff failed and null otherwise; endedAt null iff active; captured SHAs immutable; mergeSha null through Unit35 then immutable. `stages` is exact unit32..unit37 arrays. At most one StageRun and one command attempt are running. A stage starts only after latest preceding units pass. Superseding first terminalizes work. Retryable failed stage leaves parent active and may append after pushed checkpoint. SHA/code change supersedes only before mergeSha. Failed is nonretryable after all running work terminalizes; either post-merge reason requires the pushed successor journal, with post_merge_finding restricted to reviewer finding. Passed requires every latest unit stage passed and nonnull mergeSha; terminal runs never receive later stages or change status.
- Every `StageRun` is exact `{ run,status,startedAt,endedAt,startSha,endSha,commands,artifacts,evidence }`: run is positive/sequential within its unit; status is `running|failed|passed`; endedAt/endSha are null iff running; evidence is null for running/failed and required for passed. Units32-35 use branchHeadSha for both SHAs. Unit36 starts at branchHeadSha and may fail only before `set-merge-sha`; after mergeSha is persisted it remains the same running stage until the exact merge effect, outcome, and evidence are reconstructed and it passes at mergeSha. Unit37 starts/ends at mergeSha and may append a retry StageRun only when no code/SHA change is required. Timestamps are monotonic within their parent run. A failed stage is immutable; only a later sequential same-unit StageRun may retry it while the parent remains active and all preceding units' latest stages still pass.
- ProcessCommand terminal semantics are exact: status `running|interrupted|failed|passed`, endedAt null iff running, and running/interrupted have null exitCode/warningCount/failureReason. Ordinary passed requires exit:0, clean stream, exitCode 0, warningCount 0, terminalSource `process`, null reason, and complete output. Predispatch or post-generation materialized passed requires terminalSource `materialized`, exitCode null, warningCount 0, null reason, empty sanitized logs, exact typed output, and its exact authority/liveness proof. finish-command-without-process failed requires terminalSource `without_process`, null exitCode, warningCount 0, empty sanitized logs, and the matching provider_indeterminate/provider_conflict/dispatch_ambiguity reason. Failed precedence is `spawn > timeout > signal > sanitizer > exit > warning > output`; spawn/timeout/signal/sanitizer have null exit/warning, while exit/warning/output store observed exit and count. Thus clean exit-zero empty policy with output fails output; nonzero JSON command fails exit without passed-only fiction. Paths are task-relative/immutable/distinct. Warning classification strips ANSI, splits streams, and counts each line once for repository WARN/warning/[WARNING]/Node/React/console.warn patterns. Fixtures cover every named warning, dirty git output, partial/missing output, gate/record/release, spawn, timeout/TERM/KILL, signal, UTF-8, and NUL; unrecognized text is not guessed. Crash recovery interrupts only pre-dispatch process/agent after liveness proof. Post-dispatch process remains running while any released role-tagged member lives, materializes exact effect after every released role-tagged member dies, or on exact dispatch host appends a generation and sequentially re-enters identical idempotent argv after exact reconciliation; only deadline ambiguity may fail it. AgentCommand retry always uses fresh agent. No command/evidence/artifact is overwritten.
- Cross-file recovery is deterministic at every write boundary. All command-owned JSON/text/report files use sibling `<basename>.tmp`, file fsync, rename, and directory fsync; command-owned out trees are closed before `append-artifact`, whose exact path+hash operation is idempotent and legal only while that attempt remains running. `finish-command` requires the complete spec-declared tree only to pass, except the `continuity` policy requires the child output tree absent and creates its declared ReleaseContinuity/ContinuityTransfer files itself from the new terminal revision/time before appending them. On failure it still rejects every undeclared path, symlink, credential-bearing byte, or malformed file that claims to be a closed Artifact, but missing/partial declared outputs remain immutable diagnostics and do not prevent terminalization; only semantically closed files are appended. It atomically appends accepted semantic output plus both sanitized log hashes with terminal status and is idempotent for the same process-result/stream-status/hash set. A crash before manifest rename leaves the command running and recovery marks it interrupted while retaining its immutable files, and a crash after rename is already terminal. `finish-agent-command` writes the canonical clean or FINDINGS report first. If recovery finds the sole schema-valid report under a matching running AgentCommand, it reconstructs agentId/verdict from that report and completes the exact passed-CONVERGED or failed-FINDINGS manifest transition; no report means interrupted and any extra/malformed report fails closed. `finish-stage passed` writes exact evidence before its manifest transition; recovery seeing one sole schema-valid/hash-complete `unit-<U>-evidence.json` for a still-running stage completes that pass, while no evidence leaves the idempotent finish call retryable and malformed/extra evidence fails closed. Failed-stage/run transitions create no evidence file and are idempotent by exact terminal identity. Manifest-first transitions (`set-merge-sha`, supersede/fail/finish-run) repair release-continuity from the authoritative manifest on recovery. A valid manifest always wins over its orphan manifest temp; a missing/invalid manifest never infers state from artifacts. Recovery scans every exact stage/attempt root and rejects unknown directories/files, noncanonical temps, or a file that cannot be classified by these rules. Unit29.2 injects a crash before and after every create/write/fsync/rename/unlink/manifest/continuity operation and proves byte-stable repair, no overwrite, no duplicate remote mutation, and sidecar-zero terminal validation.
- Each StageRun owns exact directory `artifacts/release-<ReleaseRun.run>/unit-<32..37>/stage-<StageRun.run>/` and its passed aggregate evidence is exact `unit-<U>-evidence.json` there, written only by `finish-stage`; failed/running stages have no such file; each command attempt owns exact immutable child `<logicalName>/attempt-<Command.attempt>/`. Stdout/stderr are exact `stdout.log`/`stderr.log` in that child, and no report/evidence/output path reuses another release, stage, or attempt directory. Artifacts are exact `{ kind:"log"|"report"|"screenshot"|"json",path,sha256 }`; each path follows the task-relative rule, is unique in its StageRun, exists, is a regular file, and hash-matches when appended. The helper owns an immutable required-logical-name plan per unit. - Ensure ProcessSpecs contain F, Q, and Z exactly once as values of `--intent`, `--arm`, and `--dispatch`. Global operation identity is `operationKeySha256`, derived from the immutable operation-specific parameters below rather than ReleaseRun. Under the manifest lock, `start-command` scans every ReleaseRun for the same key; rejects missing files/hashes, malformed links, multiple roots or dispatches, a wrong operation/target, concurrent running authority, and any mode inconsistent with global history. With no authoritative dispatch it creates `mutate_once` for the first root, for a same-host successor after every prior same-key attempt is terminal before dispatch, or for the winning pre-dispatch handoff; all retain the first root hash and only one may be running. A terminal pre-dispatch attempt does not consume mutation authority. With any authoritative dispatch it creates only `reconcile_only` and links that dispatch. Start writes/hashes the current OperationIntent and EnsureArm, reserves but does not create the canonical dispatch path, appends both Artifacts with the running ProcessCommand, and replaces F/Q/Z with canonical absolute paths. For the first root, OperationIntent.rootIntentSha256 is null while EnsureArm.rootIntentSha256 and every outcome rootIntentSha256 equal the current intent hash; every successor stores/uses that nonnull first-root hash. Intent and arm become authoritative only when current origin/main contains the exact arm/running checkpoint; dispatch becomes authoritative only after its separate winning push. No non-ensure command may contain F/Q/Z. An ensure subprocess may read only its supplied intent/arm, current or root dispatch when present, own out directory, internal token/host environment, and typed remote read dependencies; a mutator dependency exists only for the exact current authoritative dispatch.
