- Registry JSON schemas are exact/no-extra-fields. `ContinuityTransfer` is defined above. `DeploymentSnapshot={environment,script,capturedAt,deployments}` uses `qa|production`, exact script, canonical time, sorted Deployment[]. `GitDrift={repo,branch,remoteBaseSha,testedBaseSha,sourceSha,treeSha,ancestor,clean,pushed}` requires exact identities and all true. Each ensure derives operationKeySha256 from canonical UTF-8 JSON of exact operation parameters: QA `{operation:'qa_deploy',targetSha,script:'spoonjoy-v2-qa',baseUrl:QA_BASE}`; PR `{operation:'pr_create',targetSha,repo,headRef:identity.branch,baseRef:'main',title:identity.prTitle,bodySha256}`; merge `{operation:'squash_merge',targetSha,repo,prNumber,testedBaseSha,treeSha,method:'squash'}`.
- `OperationIntent={version:1,releaseRun,operation,operationKeySha256,targetSha,reservationToken,executionHost,mode,rootIntentSha256,rootDispatchPath,createdAt}` uses exact identities; mode is `mutate_once|reconcile_only`; root is null only for the first-ever root, otherwise immutable global root; rootDispatchPath is task-relative/nonnull exactly when a prior authoritative dispatch exists. `EnsureArm={version:1,releaseRun,operation,operationKeySha256,targetSha,reservationToken,executionHost,intentSha256,rootIntentSha256,createdAt}` carries current/nonnullable-effective-root hashes. `EnsureProbe={version:1,operation,operationKeySha256,targetSha,observedAt,result,observation}` uses the provider-only observation union defined above and never carries disposition/intent/root hashes. `EnsureDispatch={version:1,releaseRun,operation,operationKeySha256,targetSha,reservationToken,executionHost,intentSha256,armSha256,rootIntentSha256,probe,dispatchedAt,reconcileDeadlineAt}` embeds exact absent_complete/null-observation probe; deadline is dispatchedAt+900000ms for QA and +300000ms otherwise. `EnsureHandoff={version:1,releaseRun,operation,operationKeySha256,targetSha,fromHost,toHost,currentIntentSha256,rootIntentSha256,fromAttempt,baseDeskSha,claimedAt}` is legal only from a pushed arm with no dispatch. At most one authoritative dispatch exists per key across all runs.
- `PullRequest={number,url,state:'OPEN',headRef,headSha,baseRef,baseSha,title,bodySha256,disposition,intentSha256,rootIntentSha256}` and `QaDeployOutcome={targetSha,disposition,intentSha256,rootIntentSha256,inventoryDisposition,deployment,health}` are materialized only by Unit29.2 from a hash-valid exact_effect observation plus current authority; `MergeOutcome={prNumber,state:'MERGED',sourceSha,testedBaseSha,squash,disposition,intentSha256,rootIntentSha256}` follows the same rule. Created requires current authoritative dispatch and the child that first created the effect; existing is first-read exact effect before dispatch; reconciled is exact effect after dispatch/replay. BranchProtection, CheckSet, ReviewThreadSet, MergeReadiness, and Continuation retain the exact schemas above. `HealthSeries={baseUrl,sourceSha,workerVersionId,samples}` uses exact base/source, nullable Worker version only for QA, and complete scheduled Health[]; pass evidence requires every sample HealthSuccess while failed attempts retain HealthFailure. Existing CI/workflow/deploy/release/smoke/visual schemas remain with the exact workflow conclusion and triggering-CI domains above. Every output is atomic, semantically parsed, status-closed, and contains no credential/free text.
- Remote mutation authority is global by operationKey, not ReleaseRun. `start-command` creates current intent/arm and a reserved dispatch path, scans all prior runs, and retains mutate_once eligibility across terminal pre-dispatch retries without changing the first root. With any global dispatch, current mode is reconcile_only and intent names rootDispatchPath. Before dispatch, `createReleaseExecutor` calls production `probeEnsureOperation` with operation argv plus null authority and receives exact EnsureProbe. exact_effect materializes only through predispatch_existing on the intent host; after dispatch it materializes only through postdispatch_reconciled on the dispatch host after liveness proof; absent_complete alone enters prepare-dispatch; indeterminate/conflict follow fixed read-only horizons. A crash before spawn is legal: pre-dispatch may retry/handoff; post-dispatch the dispatch host may replay after proving no live process, while another host may probe in memory only and wait/block. Every re-entry probes first. Unit29.2 validates files and passes canonical EnsureInvocationAuthority; the subprocess parses that object and rejects authority path flags, never revalidating files. The guarantees are one dispatch, at most one concurrent child, and at most one effective target state, not one historical spawn.
- Ensure observation has persisted operation-specific horizons. Before dispatch every operation uses EnsureArm.createdAt offsets `[0,5000,10000,20000,40000,80000,160000,290000]` and deadline +300000ms. After dispatch PR create and squash merge use the same offsets from EnsureDispatch.dispatchedAt and +300000ms; QA deploy uses `[0,5000,10000,20000,40000,80000,160000,320000,640000,890000]` and +900000ms to contain provider rollout plus exact-health verification. Each request timeout is `min(10000,deadline-now)`; no request starts when `now>=deadline`, and a response at/after deadline cannot pass. GitHub reads follow every provider cursor until none, with at most 100 pages and 10000 records; cap, truncation, rate limit, network/timeout, malformed response, stale health, or unavailable oracle is indeterminate. exact_effect requires every operation identity/target invariant and includes canonical typed outcome; absent_complete requires a complete authoritative no-effect read; any wrong-identity target is conflict. Pre-dispatch indeterminate/deadline fails without spawn or consuming authority, so a later same-host attempt or winning handoff retains the first root. Post-dispatch exact_effect materializes the outcome; absent_complete/indeterminate continues to the immutable operation deadline and the dispatch host may then persist dispatch_ambiguity only after exact process-identity liveness is false. Cross-host returns finite state without mutation and must wait for dispatch host or exact effect. Fake-clock/crash tests cover every sample, equality, page cap, classification, and remaining-horizon resume.
- Arm, handoff, dispatch, completion, and takeover are Git compare-and-swap checkpoints. The production executor commits/pushes/fetches/byte-verifies the arm before probing. A recoverer requests handoff by running the exact source-attempt `prepare-handoff --to-execution-host <target>` grammar; its winning push atomically persists EnsureHandoff and cross_host_handoff, thereby fencing the old host before the target can consume it. The target's next attempt verifies handoff bytes/hash, source arm, target executionHost, root, and no dispatch, then retains mutate_once. If dispatch wins first, handoff push rejects and every other host is permanently read-only for absence. Every rejected push fetches/schema-validates the winning descendant; a losing clean commit L converges through merge K whose tree equals winner O and parents are O,L, normal-pushes K, then ff-only advances local. No reset/force/loser tree survives. Tests race handoff immediately before dispatch, dispatch before spawn, crash before process record, child running, safe same-dispatch replay, delayed provider visibility, accepted-response/outcome loss, later ReleaseRun with same operationKey, and winner convergence; dispatch count and effective target-state count are each at most one globally, with at most one concurrent child.
- Every Desk checkpoint uses one Git recovery matrix. Every `git add`, `git write-tree`, `git commit-tree`, `git push`, `git fetch`, `git merge-base`, `git rev-parse`, and index/worktree probe in this matrix has exact cwd `/Users/arimendelow/desk`; no command inherits identity.repoCwd or the caller cwd. Journal O/C per declared path are exact BlobState (present bytes/hash or absent). Legal worktree/index pairs are `(O,O)|(C,O)|(C,C)` including absence; create/delete/move use those declared transitions. Recovery materializes C, invokes exact `["git","add","--",...binarySortedDeclaredPaths]`, verifies the index, obtains `newTree` through exact `["git","write-tree"]`, and creates commits only through `git commit-tree`; no porcelain commit or shell is legal. `CheckpointOperation` is exact `manifest|command|continuity|terminal_cleanup|desk_archive|track_archive|archive_validation|repair_index|successor|slugger|cancellation|convergence`. Normal checkpoint message stdin is exact UTF-8 with final LF: `spoonjoy release checkpoint <operation>\n\nSpoonjoy-Release-Version: 1\nSpoonjoy-Release-Identity-SHA256: <identitySha256>\nSpoonjoy-Release-Operation: <operation>\nSpoonjoy-Release-Old-Tree: <oldTree>\nSpoonjoy-Release-New-Tree: <newTree>\nSpoonjoy-Release-Journal-SHA256: <journalSha256>\n`; argv is `["git","commit-tree",newTree,"-p",oldCommit]`. Convergence message is the same form with operation `convergence` followed before the final LF by `Spoonjoy-Release-Winner-Commit: <winnerCommit>\nSpoonjoy-Release-Loser-Commit: <loserCommit>\n`; argv is `["git","commit-tree",winnerTree,"-p",winnerCommit,"-p",loserCommit]` in that parent order. The six base trailer values derive only from the hash-valid identity, operation owner, parent tree, verified candidate tree, and compact canonical journal bytes; convergence winner/loser derive from the fetched winner and clean rejected candidate. Commit-tree environment is exactly `PATH=/opt/homebrew/bin:/usr/bin:/bin`, `HOME=/Users/arimendelow`, `USER=arimendelow`, `LOGNAME=arimendelow`, `LANG=C`, `LC_ALL=C`, `GIT_AUTHOR_NAME=Spoonjoy Release`, `GIT_AUTHOR_EMAIL=release@spoonjoy.app`, `GIT_AUTHOR_DATE=<journal.updatedAt>`, `GIT_COMMITTER_NAME=Spoonjoy Release`, `GIT_COMMITTER_EMAIL=release@spoonjoy.app`, `GIT_COMMITTER_DATE=<journal.updatedAt>` with every other key unset. Legal postcommit is the unique direct child with exact tree, parent list, message bytes, trailers, identity, and timestamp; remote is O, that child, or a schema-valid descendant. Convergence additionally requires winnerTree, creates no content change, and is legal only after a rejected normal push. Undeclared dirt, partial bytes, any other worktree/index pair, wrong ancestry/tree/message/trailer/time, swapped parents, same-tree unrelated commit, incompatible winner, or ambiguous valid commit fails closed. Exact ref publication is closed: after an initial `['git','fetch','--prune','origin','refs/heads/main:refs/remotes/origin/main']`, let L be `refs/heads/main` and R be `refs/remotes/origin/main`. If L equals R, oldCommit=L. If exact `['git','merge-base','--is-ancestor',L,R]` exits zero and the Desk worktree/index are clean, fast-forward locally with `['git','update-ref','refs/heads/main',R,L]` then `['git','read-tree','--reset','-u',R]`, verify HEAD/index/worktree exactly R, and set oldCommit=R. A crash between those two commands resumes from ref R plus the provably clean L worktree/index and runs only read-tree. If L is ahead/diverged, the worktree/index is dirty, either ref is missing, or ancestry is indeterminate, checkpoint creation fails closed before candidate bytes. After commit-tree emits one lowercase commit SHA candidateCommit, run `['git','update-ref','refs/heads/main',candidateCommit,oldCommit]`, then normal non-force `['git','push','--porcelain','origin','refs/heads/main:refs/heads/main']`, then `['git','fetch','--prune','origin','refs/heads/main:refs/remotes/origin/main']`; accepted push is exit zero with exactly one parsed porcelain `ok` ref record and empty warning/error stream, while rejection/response loss always proceeds to the exact fetch. If fetched origin/main equals candidateCommit, publication succeeded. If it is a schema-valid descendant preserving the exact candidate declared-path bytes, it is the winner and convergence rules apply. If it still equals oldCommit after a proven rejected/no-effect push, the exact same candidate may retry. Any other remote is rescanned under the race rules. Local advancement/recovery is explicit: a crash after update-ref adopts only the unique hash-valid candidate child; when fetched winner is R rather than candidateCommit, run `['git','update-ref','refs/heads/main',R,candidateCommit]` followed by `['git','read-tree','--reset','-u',R]` only after the clean O/C matrix proves no undeclared dirt, then verify HEAD/index/worktree equal R before rebuilding. Convergence candidate K uses the declared two-parent commit-tree argv, the same update-ref/push/fetch sequence with expected old local winner, and no force/lease. Every command uses the closed Desk environment; stdout/stderr/exit and ref/tree/index/worktree results are persisted before phase advance. Push response loss, local-ref-update crash, fetch failure, rejected winner, and read-tree recovery are fault-tested.
- Release-provenance exposes shared `normalizeReleaseProvenanceArgv(fullArgv)` requiring exact prefix `["pnpm","release:provenance","--"]`, and both executable wrapper and in-process tests pass only the returned suffix to `createReleaseProvenanceCli(deps)`. Every Unit33-37 release-provenance ProcessSpec, not only ensures, goes through this production normalizer/API and its actual stdout/stderr/output tree before finish-command ingestion. `verify-drift` runs exact fetch/read. `ensure-qa-deploy` classifies complete Cloudflare inventory plus exact QA health; its sole mutation child is `["pnpm","run","deploy:qa"]`, and exact health SHA remains authority even when inventory returns no delta. `ensure-pr` requires exact identity head/base/title/body hash discovery and its sole mutation child is `["gh","pr","create","--repo","spoonjoy/spoonjoy-v2","--head",I.branch,"--base","main","--title",I.prTitle,"--body",I.prBody]`. `merge-pr` accepts exact merged outcome or complete readiness and its sole mutation child is `["gh","pr","merge",P,"--repo","spoonjoy/spoonjoy-v2","--squash","--match-head-commit",H]`. There is no alternate/admin/merge/rebase/force/auto/delete-branch/reconciliation mutator. `capture-deployments` uses the exact endpoint/schema; every GitHub adapter pins identities and classifies incomplete pagination as indeterminate.
- The two Unit37 review commands are ordered immediately after `production-visual-dogfood` and before final production cleanup. Each owns its own command-attempt out directory outside the visual runner tree and writes exactly one canonical hashed report, respectively `visual-qa-review.md` and `visual-design-review.md`; neither may edit or add a file under the immutable 38-file runner output. `VisualReviewer={role,agentId,verdict:'clean',artifactPath,reportSha256,visualArtifactSetSha256}` is no-extra-fields with role `visual_qa|design_visual`, distinct canonical lowercase UUID agentIds, the matching task-relative report path/hash, and the exact immutable runner-set hash. Unit37 cannot pass without exactly one reviewer of each role, both latest command attempts passed, both canonical reports parse/hash/cross-link, and zero open finding.
- Every Unit37 StageRun failure decision after merge is first persisted by exact derived-only `record-post-merge-disposition --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt none|A`. It writes/hashes/pushes immutable stage-owned `post-merge-failure-disposition.v1.json`, creates its own sanitized capability evidence when required, appends both hashes, refreshes continuity atomically, and is byte-idempotent; failed StageRun, disposition, and capability bytes never gain resolution fields after terminalization. `PostMergeTerminalCode` is exact `credential_missing|billing_required|platform_capability_missing|agent_runtime_unavailable|review_findings|github_rate_limited|github_5xx|cloudflare_5xx|dns_failure|network_timeout|eventual_consistency|cleanup_incomplete|spawn|timeout_term|timeout_kill|signal|sanitizer_invalid_utf8|sanitizer_nul|exit_nonzero|warning|output_invalid|provider_indeterminate|provider_conflict|dispatch_ambiguity|validation_failed|configuration_failed|provenance_failed`. Exact no-extra-fields `PostMergeFailureDisposition={version:1,releaseRun,unit:37,stageRun,logicalName,attempt,commandMode,terminalCode,evidencePath,evidenceSha256,retryOrdinal,classification,maxRetries,runFailureReason,repairCode,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,createdAt}` and has no resolution member. `human_blocker` is discriminated as preflight with `attempt:null,commandMode:'preflight'` or process with positive attempt and `commandMode:'process'`; credential/billing/platform codes alone qualify, while agent runtime is external_wait. Reviewer FINDINGS is repair_successor/post_merge_finding/review_finding; provider/network ordinals 1 and 2 are transient_retry/maxRetries 2; ordinal 3+ is external_wait; cleanup_incomplete ordinals 1 and 2 retry and ordinal 3 becomes repair_successor/post_merge_repair/cleanup; ordinary code defects use the exact repair mapping. If an attempt-none preflight is available when rerun, no disposition or evidence is written and the CLI returns exact `preflight_recovered`, allowing a fresh same-unit StageRun. Retry ordinals use persisted disposition history only; wait ordinals use separate wait-checkpoint history below. Unknown/forged combinations reject without mutation.
- Post-merge disposition derivation is total over `(terminalCode,retryOrdinal,logicalName,commandMode,environmentPolicy)` and uses no default branch. Exact tuple families are: `credential_missing|billing_required|platform_capability_missing -> {classification:'human_blocker',maxRetries:0,runFailureReason:null,repairCode:null}`; `agent_runtime_unavailable -> {classification:'external_wait',maxRetries:2,runFailureReason:null,repairCode:null}` after its two journal-owned attempts; `review_findings -> {classification:'repair_successor',maxRetries:0,runFailureReason:'post_merge_finding',repairCode:'review_finding'}`; `github_rate_limited|github_5xx|cloudflare_5xx|dns_failure|network_timeout|eventual_consistency|provider_indeterminate|provider_conflict|dispatch_ambiguity|spawn|timeout_term|timeout_kill|signal -> {classification:'transient_retry',maxRetries:2,runFailureReason:null,repairCode:null}` for ordinals 1..2 and `{classification:'external_wait',maxRetries:2,runFailureReason:null,repairCode:null}` for ordinal 3+; `cleanup_incomplete -> transient_retry/maxRetries:2/nulls` for ordinals 1..2 and `repair_successor/0/post_merge_repair/cleanup` for ordinal 3+; `sanitizer_invalid_utf8|sanitizer_nul|exit_nonzero|warning|output_invalid|validation_failed -> repair_successor/0/post_merge_repair/production_validation`; `configuration_failed -> repair_successor/0/post_merge_repair/configuration`; and `provenance_failed -> repair_successor/0/post_merge_repair/provenance`. Typed provider/credential/configuration signals take precedence over generic exit/output/process codes, so an adapter-positive capability failure never falls through to exit_nonzero. Capability binding is also total: preflight credential/platform evidence names the exact blocked CapabilityEntry and its declared probe; process `pr-ensure` maps to `github_pr_write/process:pr-ensure`, `merge-ensure` to `github_merge_write/process:merge-ensure`, QA deploy to `cloudflare_workers_edit/process:qa-deploy-ensure`, D1 cleanup/reconcile/lifecycle operations to `cloudflare_d1_edit/process:<logicalName>`, and a provider-positive Cloudflare billing response to `cloudflare_billing/process:<logicalName>`. Exact process-only capability domain is `github_pr_write|github_merge_write|cloudflare_workers_edit|cloudflare_d1_edit|cloudflare_billing`; it never appears in preflight available proofs. A terminal code/context without exactly one table row or one capability mapping is schema-invalid and writes nothing. Tests enumerate the Cartesian legal rows, every retry boundary, every illegal context, and precedence over generic process failures.
- Units32-36 use a separate pre-merge lifecycle and can never create a repair successor. Every failed stage first invokes exact derived-only `record-pre-merge-disposition --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit 32|33|34|35|36 --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt none|A`, which writes/hashes/pushes one immutable stage-owned `pre-merge-failure-disposition.v1.json` before any retry or fix. Exact no-extra-fields `PreMergeFailureDisposition={version:1,releaseRun,unit:32|33|34|35|36,stageRun,logicalName,attempt,commandMode,terminalCode,evidencePath,evidenceSha256,classification,retryOrdinal,maxRetries,createdAt}` uses the same closed terminal-code domain, `attempt:null,commandMode:'preflight'` versus positive-attempt `commandMode:'process'|'agent'` discrimination, capability-evidence binding, and terminal-code precedence as PostMergeFailureDisposition, with classification `retry_same_unit|external_wait|human_blocker|fix_current_branch`. Credential, billing, and platform-capability codes are human_blocker/maxRetries 0; agent-runtime unavailability is external_wait and agent mode only after its two epoch-scoped attempts; provider/network/process transients are retry_same_unit/maxRetries 2 at ordinals 1..2 and external_wait at ordinal 3+; cleanup_incomplete is retry_same_unit at ordinals 1..2 and fix_current_branch at ordinal 3+; review findings (agent mode only), sanitizer/output/warning/exit, validation, configuration, and provenance failures are fix_current_branch/maxRetries 0. Unknown tuples reject. Before set-merge-sha, Unit36 obeys this matrix, but fix_current_branch is legal only after authoritative complete unmerged/no-effect observation; after set-merge-sha it can only reconcile/pass. retry_same_unit appends a fresh same-unit StageRun at unchanged HEAD; external_wait uses trigger-specific provider or agent-runtime recovery. A preflight human blocker uses resolve-pre-merge-blocker and the exact immutable PreMergeBlockerResolution only after a fresh successful read-only probe. A process-positive edit/billing blocker rejects read-only resolution and requires authorize-pre-merge-blocker; its operator authorization permits one fresh attempt without claiming capability success. fix_current_branch authorizes a tracked fix, supersedes the old ReleaseRun, and restarts Unit32. No Unit32-36 path writes post-merge repair files, initializes a successor, or enters repaired release-terminal.
- A repair_successor never reruns the defective tree without a reviewed repair. After the failed Unit37 stage disposition or passed-Unit37 terminal disposition push, Work Merger invokes strict measured `pnpm release:terminal -- --mode successor` actions. Exact `RepairBrief={code,artifactPath,artifactSha256,reviewerRole,promptSha256,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,affectedSurfaces}` retains finite code `review_finding|provenance|cleanup|configuration|production_validation`; `affectedSurfaces={ui:boolean,api:boolean,migrationConfig:boolean}` is derived from the failed command/artifact registry and cannot be caller-supplied. The sole exact `PostMergeSuccessorAttempt`, suite-attempt, phase/null, runtime-wait, and implementation-evidence schemas are the Round 52 declarations below. The successor doing doc contains implementation-only units and excludes Units32-37. Crash recovery validates/completes or interrupts one bounded suite attempt before a fresh ordinal, never skips or duplicates a phase. Only implementation_complete may initialize the successor manifest and run universal Units32-37 once, followed by its PR/merge/production/terminal/archive/index flow.
- Successor completion evidence is a closed registry, never an arbitrary path/hash collection. Exact `SuccessorImplementationRegistry={version:1,successorKey,doingPath,doingSha256,groups,reviewRoles,createdAt}` has BINARY-sorted unique `groups:{groupId,testUnitId,implementationUnitId,verificationUnitId}[]` parsed from the approved successor doing doc: every implementation group appears exactly once as contiguous status-bearing `a` test, `b` implementation, and `c` verification headers with What/Output/Acceptance; no other implementation unit shape is legal. `reviewRoles` is the BINARY-sorted set containing `implementation`, `migration_config`, `security_privacy`, and `test`, plus `design_visual` iff RepairBrief.affectedSurfaces.ui and `api_compatibility` iff RepairBrief.affectedSurfaces.api; therefore the only legal global order is the applicable subsequence of `api_compatibility|design_visual|implementation|migration_config|security_privacy|test`. migration_config remains required and records clean no-impact when unaffected. `SuccessorImplementationUnitReceipt={version:1,successorKey,unitId,phase:'test'|'implementation'|'verification',status:'completed',sourceBaseSha,sourceHeadSha,treeSha,redEvidencePath,redEvidenceSha256,commands,artifactPaths,artifactSetSha256,completedAt}` exists exactly once for every registry unit. All sourceHeadSha/treeSha equal the final clean pushed implementation head/tree and sourceBaseSha equals implementationBaseSha; test phase alone has nonnull immutable red evidence proving its expected nonzero assertion before implementation, while implementation/verification have both red fields null. `commands:{argv,expected:'red'|'green',exitCode,stdoutSha256,stderrSha256,warningCount}[]` is nonempty: test has at least one red command with exitCode 1..255 and then its final green replay; all other expected green commands have exitCode zero; every warningCount is zero. `SuccessorReviewReport={version:1,successorKey,role,agentId,verdict:'clean',sourceHeadSha,treeSha,completedAt}` exists exactly once for every registry reviewRole with distinct canonical agent ids. `SuccessorVerificationArtifact={version:1,successorKey,unitId,command,exitCode:0,stdoutSha256,stderrSha256,warningCount:0,sourceHeadSha,treeSha,createdAt}` exists at least once for every verification unit and exactly matches its receipt commands/artifacts. Implementation evidence arrays must be the BINARY-sorted normalized task-relative paths of these exact closed sets; all bytes schema/hash-validate, all unit IDs/roles equal the registry with no omission/extra/duplicate, every source/tree equals the final implementation head/tree, every group is complete, and every set hash covers compact canonical `{path,sha256}[]` with no final LF. `reviewReportPaths` points to the complete projected SuccessorReviewReport bytes; the enclosing `{path,sha256}` review set supplies the only report hashes, so no report self-hashes. The registry path is exact task-relative `artifacts/post-merge-successor/implementation-registry.v1.json`; unit receipts/red evidence live only under `artifacts/post-merge-successor/units/`, review reports only under `artifacts/post-merge-successor/reviews/`, verification artifacts only under `artifacts/post-merge-successor/verification/`, and coverage only under its declared sibling directory. Every one is appended to the successor manifest as a PreReleaseArtifact before implementation evidence, so terminal ordinary-file validation sees no task-root extras.
- Changed coverage scope is derived independently from coverage instrumentation and retained as an exact closed artifact set. Exact no-extra-fields `CoveragePathSet={version:1,kind:'diff'|'production_executable'|'instrumented',paths,pathsSha256,createdAt}` uses BINARY-sorted unique repo-relative paths and hashes compact canonical `paths` bytes with no final LF. The sole basenames under task-relative `artifacts/post-merge-successor/coverage/` are `coverage-diff-paths.json`, `coverage-production-executables.json`, `coverage-instrumented-paths.json`, `coverage-scope.json`, `coverage-total.json`, `coverage-changed.json`, `coverage-command-results.json`, and `coverage-summary.json`. Exact no-extra-fields `CoverageScope={version:1,diffPathSetPath,diffPathSetSha256,productionExecutablePathSetPath,productionExecutablePathSetSha256,instrumentedPathSetPath,instrumentedPathSetSha256,changedExecutablePaths,changedExecutableSetSha256,allChangedExecutablePathsInstrumented:true,createdAt}` cross-hashes the first three files. `CoverageTotal={version:1,metrics,createdAt}` carries exact CoverageMetricSet. `CoverageChanged={version:1,changed,coverageScopePath,coverageScopeSha256,createdAt}` carries exact ChangedCoverage and hashes CoverageScope. `CoverageCommandSet={version:1,commands,createdAt}` carries the exact nonempty zero-warning CoverageSummary command array. `diff` is exact `git diff --name-only implementationBaseSha...implementationHeadSha`. The independent production registry is every tracked regular file matching `app/**/*.{ts,tsx}`, `workers/**/*.{ts,tsx}`, or `scripts/**/*.{ts,mts,mjs}`, plus present root files `vite.config.ts`, `vitest.config.ts`, `playwright.config.ts`, and `react-router.config.ts`, minus `**/*.d.ts` and exact path segments `test`, `tests`, `__tests__`, `fixtures`, `generated`, `node_modules`, `coverage`, and build-output directories; classification never reads instrumentation. changedExecutablePaths is the intersection of diff and production paths; every member must occur in the independent instrumented set. For both measured and not_applicable, changedExecutableSetSha256 hashes compact canonical changedExecutablePaths bytes. Measured is required for a nonempty set and reports positive 100% metrics over exactly it; not_applicable requires an empty set and the hash of exact bytes `[]`. `coverage-summary.json` contains exact CoverageSummary and is the sole value legal for PostMergeImplementationEvidence.coverageSummaryPath at `artifacts/post-merge-successor/coverage/coverage-summary.json`; CoverageSummary.artifacts is exactly the BINARY-sorted seven-entry subordinate `{path,sha256}` set for every other basename in that directory, excludes the summary itself to avoid a self-hash, and permits no substitution or extras; its commands, total, and changed members byte-equal the command, total, and changed artifact payloads. Every path/hash cross-link, set membership, classifier exclusion, metric, and no-extra-fields boundary is independently validated.
- The predecessor remains terminal-pending until the successor final receipt/index are pushed/read back; its frozen archive state may be validating_active, archive_in_progress, or done_archived_pending. The successor Work Merger invokes repair-intermediate at positive predecessor depth or repair-root at depth zero. Release-terminal alone owns exact no-extra-fields `PredecessorSupersedeAttempt={version:1,predecessorIdentitySha256,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,successorReceiptLocator,successorReceiptSha256,successorArchiveValidationLocator,successorArchiveValidationSha256,predecessorTaskPath,predecessorDoingLocator,predecessorTaskArchivePath,successorJournalSha256,repairLinkSha256,terminalCleanupSha256,phase,taskBeforeSha256,taskDoneSha256,doingBeforeSha256,doingDoneSha256,trackTargetRowBeforeSha256,trackLandedRowSha256,startedAt,updatedAt}` with phase `prepared|lifecycle_done|root_moved|validated`. validating_active performs the existing task validating->done, doing VALIDATING->COMPLETE, Landed-row, and move transitions. archive_in_progress first reconciles its unique existing archive journal and continues as done_archived_pending. done_archived_pending starts at the uniquely resolved archive root: prepared derived hashes are null; lifecycle_done records taskDone=taskBefore and doingDone=doingBefore without a write; root_moved records trackLanded=trackTargetRowBefore without a move; validated appends only repair protocol and proves the same source-absent/target-present root. Each transition advances once with canonical updatedAt and no drift. Only validated atomically replaces the attempt with exact `PredecessorSupersedeReceipt={version:1,predecessorIdentitySha256,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,successorReceiptLocator,successorReceiptSha256,successorArchiveValidationLocator,successorArchiveValidationSha256,repairLinkSha256,terminalCleanupSha256,taskSourcePath,taskArchivePath,doingLocator,prNumber,prUrl,validatorMergeSha,taskBeforeSha256,taskDoneSha256,doingBeforeSha256,doingDoneSha256,trackTargetRowBeforeSha256,trackLandedRowSha256,sourceAbsent:true,targetPresent:true,archiveValid:true,completedAt}` at predecessor-supersede.v1.json. Receipt locators resolve uniquely, identities equal the repair lineage, and partial/retained/skipped/drifted state rejects. The predecessor is terminal only after this receipt, any required index, and its fresh final ArchiveValidationReceipt are pushed/read back. A legal pre-final transient never reopens a failed StageRun, and the all-the-way-through mandate continues through every successor in the same invocation.
- Before predecessor supersede preparation, release-terminal runs the host-bound TerminalCleanup protocol with the successor receipt as the special authorization replacing normal passed-Unit37 authorization. It builds the validator/runtime at the immutable repair leaf PostMergeRepairReceipt's `validatorMergeSha`, while original `mergeSha`/`branchHeadSha` are used only for ancestry, ref, and worktree cleanup and proof of original worktree/ref absence. Prepared supersede also freezes exact `PostMergeRepairLink={version:1,dispositionKind,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,successorKey,successorTaskPath,successorReceiptPath,successorReceiptSha256,successorPrNumber,successorPrUrl,successorMergeSha,predecessorTaskPath,predecessorReleaseRun,predecessorReleaseStatus,predecessorMergeSha,sourceDispositionPath,sourceDispositionSha256,repairBriefSha256s,completedAt}`. dispositionKind is `stage|terminal`; stage requires predecessorReleaseStatus failed and source PostMergeFailureDisposition, while terminal requires predecessorReleaseStatus passed and source TerminalFailureDisposition. At lifecycle_done it atomically writes `post-merge-repair-link.v1.json`, hash-verifies then removes `post-merge-successor.attempt.v1.json`, and records both hashes in the supersede attempt. Prepared hashes the existing successor journal and TerminalCleanup plus the frozen repair-link candidate, so successorJournalSha256, repairLinkSha256, and terminalCleanupSha256 are nonempty and immutable in every phase.
- Repaired closure archive validation is the second semantic `--mode archive` branch and uses only the Round 60 stage/state/checkpoint closed sets. It requires the exact PostMergeRepairLink, original TerminalCleanup, superseded task/history outcome, PredecessorSupersedeReceipt, consumed child index, and any current intermediate created index. The distinct relay/leaf/DeskArchive/TrackDisposition members are present exactly when that table requires; no handoff/supersede attempt remains. Logical cross-task locators resolve uniquely through active task, task archive, or TrackArchive target. A predecessor is terminal only after fresh final archive validation is pushed/readback and validator resources are absent; the same Work Merger invocation continues through every ancestor.
- Evidence is a unit-discriminated no-extra-fields union. `Reviewer={role,agentId,verdict:'clean',artifactPath,reportSha256,promptSha256}` is exact with finite role, lowercase UUID agentId, and matching passed AgentCommand hashes. `Deployment={id,createdAt,source:'github_actions'|'wrangler'|'dashboard'|'unknown'|null}` has nonempty id/canonical time; provider text maps only to that finite classification and is never retained. `Health=HealthSuccess|HealthFailure` records every scheduled sample through the exact closed schemas below. `Cleanup={outcomePath,phaseEvidencePaths,preDeleteRowsPath,userDeletePath,postDeleteRowsPath,retainedDoAllowlistPath,userAbsent,relationalProductRowsZero,contentBearingDoStateZero,identifierBearingDoMetadataRetained,residueClean,cleanupRecovered,cleanupIncomplete}` uses task-relative proof paths and derived flags. `Visual={baseUrl,reportPath,metricsPath,ledgerPath,screenshotPaths,visualArtifactSetSha256,cleanup,readyCount,reviewerGatedCount}` requires canonical production base, exact closed/hash-matched visual set, parsed report/metrics/ledger/Cleanup, and zero counts. `Check={name,url:CheckUrl,conclusion:'success',headSha}` requires exact PR head and the provider-discriminated URL/id binding below. `SquashCommit={sha,parents:[Sha],treeSha}` has one parent. `CiWorkflow={databaseId,runAttempt,workflowPath:'.github/workflows/ci.yml',headSha,status:'completed',conclusion:'success',url,createdAt,event:'push'}` requires positive id, expected SHA/time/url. Exact `GitHubWorkflowStatus` is `requested|queued|pending|waiting|in_progress|completed`; exact `GitHubWorkflowConclusion` is `action_required|cancelled|failure|neutral|skipped|stale|success|timed_out`, matching the GitHub workflow-run REST domain. `Workflow={databaseId,runAttempt,workflowPath:'.github/workflows/production-deploy.yml',headSha,triggeringCiDatabaseId,triggeringCiRunAttempt,status,conclusion,url,createdAt,event:'workflow_run'}` requires triggering id/run-attempt equal CiWorkflow.databaseId/runAttempt; status is one `GitHubWorkflowStatus`, conclusion is null exactly for every noncompleted status, and completed requires one `GitHubWorkflowConclusion`. `DeployJob={id,runId,runAttempt,headSha,name:'deploy',status,conclusion,url,startedAt,completedAt}` uses positive ids, merge SHA, GitHubJobUrl whose runId/jobId equal its runId/id, canonical/null times, exact GitHubJobStatus/GitHubJobConclusion, null conclusion/completedAt for every noncompleted status, null startedAt for requested/queued/pending/waiting, canonical startedAt for in_progress, and one job conclusion plus canonical completedAt and canonical/null startedAt for completed. Unknown status/conclusion strings reject, and discovery freezes first matching identity, rejects duplicates/drift, and passes only completed/success. `ProductionRelease={status:'promoted',sourceSha,runAttempt,phase:'complete',treeHash,triggeringCiDatabaseId,triggeringCiRunAttempt,reviewedMigrations:string[],migrationApply:'not_needed'|'succeeded',databaseRollbackSupported:false,previousVersionId,candidateVersionId}` is exact; triggering id/attempt equal CiWorkflow, runAttempt equals the selected Workflow runAttempt, migrations sorted/unique with matching apply state, and distinct valid Worker version IDs match health.
- Every top-level lifecycle-smoke Cleanup and nested Visual Cleanup derives from one final outcome envelope, one terminally immutable record log per executed phase, and four immutable fact proofs. Primary-only basenames are `cleanup-outcome.json`, `cleanup-phase-primary.json`, `cleanup-pre-delete-rows.json`, `cleanup-user-delete.json`, `cleanup-post-delete-rows.json`, and `cleanup-retained-do-allowlist.json`; a recovery adds `cleanup-phase-recovery.json`. Resolved paths stay inside the owning attempt `out/`; `lstat` proves regular non-symlinks and no pair shares a path or device/inode. `CleanupIdentity={userId,emailSha256,reportAttempts,purgeTargets}` uses a nonempty userId, Sha256 of the disposable email rather than raw email, and sorted unique exact `{recipeId,attemptId}` arrays with purgeTargets a subset. Lifecycle reportAttempts byte-equals A+B from `smoke-results.json` while purgeTargets is exactly B; Visual has its sole attempt in both arrays. `CleanupFailureCode` is finite `deadline|attempt_budget|cook_attempt_budget|network|rate_limited|server|protocol|identity|residue|purge|d1|user_delete|proof|sanitizer|unknown`; raw error names/codes map to `unknown`. `CleanupPass={phase,startedAt,endedAt,status,failureCode}` uses phase `primary|recovery`, status `passed|failed`, canonical times, and null failureCode iff passed. `CleanupCall={sequence,phase,at,method,status,recipeId,attemptId}` uses strictly increasing positive sequence, method `GET|DELETE`, safe-integer HTTP status `100..599`, and nullable attempt only for GET. `PurgeCompletion={recipeId,attemptId,phase,deleteCallSequence,purgeCompletedAt}` cross-links one exact target DELETE call whose status is 204 and whose at equals purgeCompletedAt; every purgeTarget has exactly one completion across all phases, every DELETE 202/204 names a purgeTarget, and any DELETE for a non-target rejects evidence. Recovery byte-verifies primary completions and never re-DELETEs an already completed target. `RetiredAttempt={recipeId,attemptId,terminalRevision,terminalStatus,terminalSnapshotSha256,replacementAttemptId,replacementStartSha256,finalResidueSha256}` is no-extra-fields and sorted by recipeId/attemptId; terminalRevision is a nonnegative safe integer, terminalStatus is `COMPLETED|ABANDONED`, hashes match unique canonical sanitized entries in the owning smoke report and phase residue, replacement start is later than terminal, and replacementAttemptId is a reportAttempt. Lifecycle has exactly one retirement for A with revision 4/status COMPLETED/replacement B; Visual has none. `CleanupPhaseEvidence={version:1,identity,phase,startedAt,endedAt,status,failureCode,priorPhaseSha256,calls,purgeCompletions,retiredAttempts,finalResidues,proofHashes}` exists only as the terminal record of its phase log; primary priorPhaseSha256 is null, recovery byte-verifies and names the complete terminal primary-log Sha256. `proofHashes={preDeleteRows,userDelete,postDeleteRows,retainedDoAllowlist}` contains Sha256/null only for fact files first created by that phase, and each final fact file appears nonnull in exactly one phase. Calls are the complete owner trace made by that phase. RetiredAttempts/finalResidues are nonempty only in the one phase that first creates retainedDoAllowlist and they byte-match that proof; earlier candidate residues are not persisted as final. A recovery after user deletion has zero calls/purgeCompletions/retirements/residues, preserves the terminal primary log byte-for-byte, and first creates only the recovery post-delete proof.
- For RetiredAttempt, “canonical sanitized entries” means only the exact LifecycleTerminalEvent, later LifecycleStartEvent, and FinalResidue schemas above serialized by their declared hash rule; no exchange, frame, diagnostic, client observation, or structurally similar arbitrary object qualifies.
- Each irreversible D1 cleanup mutation has a create-once pre-dispatch journal written and fsynced before the call: `CleanupMutationJournal={version:1,operation:'delete_retired_cook_session_indexes'|'delete_disposable_user',operationKeySha256,identity,targets,preStateSha256,preparedAt}`. `targets` is the exact BINARY-sorted retired tuple set or singleton user id; `preStateSha256` hashes the canonical proven-present rows, and the unique disposable identity plus owner trace proves no competing authorized deleter. `ProjectionRetirementReceipt={operation:'delete_retired_cook_session_indexes',at,journalPath,journalSha256,disposition:'deleted'|'reconciled',deletedAttempts,deletedRows,remainingRows}` is no-extra-fields; deletedAttempts is the sorted exact reportAttempts-minus-purgeTargets set selected by RetiredAttempt, remainingRows is zero, deleted requires deletedRows equal its length from the first returned transaction, and reconciled requires deletedRows zero only after a lost response, byte-valid journal/pre-state proof, and an exact read proving every target absent. The scoped runner validates userId and every retired recipeId/attemptId against their canonical identifier grammars before SQL construction, quotes each accepted value through the existing `sqlString` helper, and runs one transaction whose DELETE predicates exact userId, exact retired tuples, and terminal status before returning `changes()` plus the same-user remaining count; no raw caller value is interpolated. Lifecycle receipt is exactly A with deleted/1/0 or reconciled/0/0; Visual is empty with deleted/0/0 and never fabricates reconciliation. `CleanupPreDeleteRows={version:1,phase,identity,at,projectionRetirement,userRows:1,cookSessionIndexRows:0}`; `CleanupUserDelete={version:1,phase,identity,at,journalPath,journalSha256,disposition:'deleted'|'reconciled',deletedUserRows}` where deleted is exactly one returned row and reconciled is exactly zero only after response loss plus byte-valid journal/pre-state and exact user absence; `CleanupPostDeleteRows={version:1,phase,identity,at,userRows:0,productRowCounts}`; `CleanupRetainedDoAllowlist={version:1,phase,identity,at,residues}`. Journals precede their calls; result proofs are create-once after returned-or-reconciled observation and before the next irreversible step. Recovery byte-verifies and reuses every existing journal/proof, may derive only the exact reconciled outcome from its prepared pre-state plus target absence, and never overwrites or relabels it. Product counts equal `CLEANUP_USER_ROW_ITEMS` and are all safe-integer zero. `CleanupOutcomeProof={version:1,identity,passes,phaseEvidence,proofs}` is written atomically last only for a complete clean set; phaseEvidence is exact ordered `{phase,path,sha256}[]`, proofs is exact `{preDeleteRows:{path,sha256},userDelete:{path,sha256},postDeleteRows:{path,sha256},retainedDoAllowlist:{path,sha256}}`, every hash byte-matches, and passes byte-equals summaries derived from immutable phase files. The union of phase calls/completions/retirements/residues is canonical and complete. Final residues byte-equal retained residues; each PurgeCompletion precedes retained.at, then `retained.at <= projectionRetirement.at <= preDelete.at < userDelete.at < postDelete.at <=` the terminal passed phase endedAt. Every final residue satisfies allowed metadata/live-zero; A retirement cross-links terminal/replacement/live-zero evidence plus the exact projection-retirement journal/receipt, pre-delete CookSessionIndex zero, and post-delete ownership zero without any cook-session DELETE A; B has exact terminal DELETE 204. Any owner call at/after userDelete.at rejects evidence. No asserted no-post-delete field exists. For a valid outcome the parser derives the five clean flags, cleanupRecovered exactly from primary-failed/recovery-passed with recovery post-delete proof, and cleanupIncomplete false. A terminal failed phase or missing/incomplete facts produces only sanitized diagnostic smoke output with cleanupIncomplete true and no outcome envelope/Release Cleanup. Unit33/37 additionally require the exact primary-only six-file set, primary passed, and both recovery flags false. Fault tests lose each D1 response after commit and require truthful reconciled proof. Any extra/alias, mutable/hash mismatch, nonfinite error text, pass/phase/provenance inconsistency, schema/registry mismatch, identity/attempt mismatch, false order, missing terminal-204 target completion/A retirement/projection journal/receipt, non-target DELETE, residue mismatch, unexpected count, post-delete owner call, or release construction from incomplete evidence rejects Cleanup. Exact target/pre-state replacement: delete-retired uses BINARY `(recipeId,attemptId,status)` sorted `DeleteRetiredTarget` and same-order `DeleteRetiredPreStateRow={userId,recipeId,attemptId,status,updatedAt}`; delete-user uses singleton `DeleteUserTarget={userId}` and `DeleteUserPreStateRow={userId}`. Compact exact-field-order row-array bytes have no LF and exclude every credential/email/OAuth/profile/content column. preStateSha256 hashes those bytes; operationKeySha256 hashes compact `{operation,identitySha256,targets,preStateSha256}`.
- Cleanup mutation journals are records inside existing `cleanup-phase-<phase>.json`, not additional output files. Exact `CleanupPhaseRecord` is `{kind:'mutation_journal',journal:CleanupMutationJournal}` or `{kind:'terminal',evidence:CleanupPhaseEvidence}` and exact `CleanupPhaseLog={version:1,identity,phase,records:CleanupPhaseRecord[]}`. The file is compact canonical JSON in that field order with no final LF. Before each irreversible call, the runner appends one journal record semantically by writing/fsyncing a complete token-qualified sibling candidate containing the exact prior record prefix plus the one new record, atomically renaming, fsyncing the parent, and byte-reading it before dispatch. After returned/reconciled results and fact files, it similarly appends exactly one terminal record as the final record; a terminal log is immutable. Records permit zero to two mutation journals in operation order followed by exactly one terminal record, or a nonterminal prefix during recovery; duplicate/reordered/changed committed prefixes, foreign/multiple candidates, terminal-not-last, mutation after terminal, and corrupt main fail closed. A same-token partial candidate beside an intact prior main is removed and the extension rebuilt because dispatch is forbidden before main readback; immutable journal plus fact proofs reconstructs a deterministic terminal extension after a dispatched effect. Every `journalPath` is that phase file and `journalSha256` hashes compact canonical bytes of the nested CleanupMutationJournal only, while the phase Artifact hash covers complete terminal CleanupPhaseLog bytes. Recovery faults every candidate write/fsync/rename/readback boundary and either promotes the one complete prefix extension, removes an absent/zero-byte owned candidate, or, only for foreign/multiple/wrong-token/corrupt-main state, fails closed. The existing six cleanup basenames and 14/38-file closed sets remain exact.
- `CLEANUP_USER_ROW_ITEMS` is the immutable sorted exact set `api/auth rows`, `cook session index rows`, `cookbook/membership rows`, `notification/device rows`, `recipe/child/cover rows`, `save/tag/search rows`, `shopping rows`, `spoon/social rows`, and `user rows`. `shopping rows` explicitly includes `ShoppingListItemSyncTombstone`. Each named query aggregates every current or planned D1 table in that ownership family reachable directly or transitively from identity.userId; config tests fail when a migration/model adds such a table without updating the registry and its zero-row query. - Exact evidence objects are: unit32 `{unit:"unit32",reviewers:Reviewer[]}`; unit33 `{unit:"unit33",deploymentsBefore:Deployment[],cleanupReconcile:CleanupReconcile,deploymentsAfter:Deployment[],newDeploymentIds:string[],qaDeployDisposition:"created"|"existing"|"reconciled",healthSamples:Health[],smokeArtifactPaths:string[],cleanup:Cleanup}`; unit34 `{unit:"unit34",prUrl,prNumber,prHeadSha,prDisposition:"created"|"existing"|"reconciled",reviewers:Reviewer[]}`; unit35 `{unit:"unit35",prHeadSha,branchProtectionStrict,branchProtectionLinearHistory,protectedCheckNames:string[],mandatoryCheckNames:string[],checks:Check[]}`; unit36 `{unit:"unit36",qaHealthSamples:Health[],productionDeploymentsBefore:Deployment[],mergeMethod:"squash",mergeDisposition:"created"|"existing"|"reconciled",squashCommit:SquashCommit}`; unit37 `{unit:"unit37",ciWorkflow:CiWorkflow,workflowCandidates:Workflow[],selectedWorkflow:Workflow,deployJob:DeployJob,releaseArtifactPath,productionRelease:ProductionRelease,productionDeploymentsAfter:Deployment[],newProductionDeploymentIds:string[],healthSamples:Health[],cleanupReconcile:CleanupReconcile,smokeArtifactPaths:string[],visual:Visual,visualReviewers:VisualReviewer[],continuation:Continuation,cleanup:Cleanup}`. - Unit32 begins by fetch/integrate origin/main, finishes every tracked code/doc/progress change, writes and pushes the final task-local AUTOPILOT release-transfer snapshot, then sets testedBaseSha to exact origin/main, branchHeadSha to that clean/pushed HEAD, and branchHeadTreeSha to exact `HEAD^{tree}` before local/QA gates. - After Unit37 pass/finish-run/pushed active validation, terminal cleanup runs outside ProcessCommand on the frozen executionHost. Before validator creation it writes/pushes exact no-extra-fields `TerminalCleanupAttempt={version:1,identitySha256,attemptOrdinal,priorFailedAttemptPaths,priorFailedAttemptSetSha256,mergeSha,validatorMergeSha,branchHeadSha,executionHost,canonicalRepoPath:'/Users/arimendelow/Projects/spoonjoy-v2',validatorRuntimePath,validatorRuntimeTempPath,validatorArchivePath,validatorArchiveTempPath,validatorArchiveSha256,validatorSourceTreeSha256,worktreePath,worktreeDeletePath,worktreeCleanupSha256,branch,phase,activeCommand,commandResults,originMainContainsMerge,canonicalMainContainsMerge,validatorReady,worktreeAbsent,registeredWorktreeAbsent,localBranchAbsent,remoteBranchAbsent,pruned,startedAt,updatedAt}`. `worktreePath=identity.repoCwd`, `branch=identity.branch`, and `branchHeadSha` is the identity-bound release head; repaired closure uses the predecessor identity for original ancestry/ref/worktree cleanup without inventing `identity.worktreePath` or `identity.branchHeadSha`. - The TerminalCleanup phase has one closed no-shell command registry and no unregistered subprocess in that phase. Let `C=/Users/arimendelow/Projects/spoonjoy-v2`, `W=attempt.worktreePath`, `B=attempt.branch`, and `H=attempt.branchHeadSha`. Exact ordered names/argv/cwd are: `fetch-origin`: `["git","fetch","--prune","origin"]` in W; `origin-contains-merge`: `["git","merge-base","--is-ancestor",mergeSha,"origin/main"]` in W; `canonical-fast-forward`: `["git","merge","--ff-only","origin/main"]` in C; `canonical-contains-merge`: `["git","merge-base","--is-ancestor",mergeSha,"HEAD"]` in C; `validator-tree`: `["git","rev-parse",validatorMergeSha+"^{tree}"]` in W; `validator-members`: `["git","ls-tree","-r","--full-tree",validatorMergeSha]` in W; `archive`: `["git","archive","--format=tar","--output",validatorArchiveTempPath,validatorMergeSha]` in W; `archive-members`: `["tar","-tf",validatorArchiveTempPath]` in W; `extract`: `["tar","-xf",validatorArchiveTempPath,"-C",validatorRuntimeTempPath]` in W; `install`: `["pnpm","install","--frozen-lockfile"]` in validatorRuntimeTempPath; `worktree-list-before`: `["git","worktree","list","--porcelain"]` in C; `local-ref-before`: `["git","rev-parse","--verify","--quiet","refs/heads/"+B]` in C; `remote-ref-before`: `["git","rev-parse","--verify","--quiet","refs/remotes/origin/"+B]` in C; `worktree-detach`: `["mv","--",W,attempt.worktreeDeletePath]` in C; `worktree-prune`: `["git","worktree","prune","--expire","now"]` in C; `worktree-list-after`: `["git","worktree","list","--porcelain"]` in C; `local-ref-delete`: `["git","update-ref","-d","refs/heads/"+B,H]` in C; `local-ref-after`: `["git","rev-parse","--verify","--quiet","refs/heads/"+B]` in C; `remote-ref-delete`: `["git","push","origin","--force-with-lease=refs/heads/"+B+":"+H,":refs/heads/"+B]` in C; `final-fetch`: `["git","fetch","--prune","origin"]` in C; `remote-ref-after`: `["git","rev-parse","--verify","--quiet","refs/remotes/origin/"+B]` in C. The before probes must exit zero: worktree-list-before contains exactly one canonical record for W at H on B, and both ref probes equal H; the after worktree probe must omit W and both after `rev-parse --verify --quiet` ref probes must exit one with empty stdout/stderr, which is the registry-defined successful-absence observation. `ls-tree` parses strict mode/type/object/tab/path rows, rejects links/submodules/path traversal/duplicate paths, and must equal the BINARY-sorted non-directory archive-member list; archive directory entries must be trailing-slash exact prefixes of at least one source path; `rev-parse` accepts one lowercase 40-hex line. Archive SHA-256, extracted regular-file SHA-256, lockfile equality, source-member equality, and canonical manifest hashes use in-process typed filesystem/crypto adapters over regular files only, compact canonical JSON, BINARY path order, and no final LF; they spawn no hidden command. Every invocation first pushes/readbacks exact no-extra-fields `TerminalCommandIntent={sequence,name,argv,cwd,timeoutMs,preStateSha256,preparedAt,recoveryObservations}` as activeCommand with `recoveryObservations:[]`, then after observation atomically appends exact no-extra-fields `TerminalCommandResult={sequence,name,argv,cwd,timeoutMs,preStateSha256,postStateSha256,outcome,exitCode,signal,stdoutSha256,stderrSha256,warningCount,recoveryObservations,completedAt}` copies the exact append-only activeCommand.recoveryObservations into the result and clears activeCommand before return/advance where recoveryObservations is empty except for the remote-ref-delete specialization and sequence is its zero-based registry index, name/argv/cwd/timeout match that index, warningCount is a nonnegative safe integer and must be zero to advance, and outcome is `exit|signal|timeout_term|timeout_kill|spawn_error|reconciled`. Exit has integer exitCode 0..255 and null signal; signal has null exitCode and signal `SIGHUP|SIGINT|SIGQUIT|SIGABRT|SIGKILL|SIGALRM|SIGTERM|SIGUSR1|SIGUSR2|SIGPIPE`; timeout_term/timeout_kill have null exitCode and SIGTERM/SIGKILL respectively; spawn_error has both null and empty-stream hashes; reconciled has both null, empty-stream hashes, warningCount zero, and is legal only for a mutation whose exact postStateSha256 is observed after a crash before result persistence. Only registry-defined successful-absence exit one or exit zero is success. Streams are clean UTF-8/NUL-free/sanitized and capped at 1048576 bytes; environment is exactly `PATH=/opt/homebrew/bin:/usr/bin:/bin`, `HOME=/Users/arimendelow`, `USER=arimendelow`, `LOGNAME=arimendelow`, `LANG=C`, `LC_ALL=C`, `CI=1`, `NO_COLOR=1`, `FORCE_COLOR=0`, `GIT_TERMINAL_PROMPT=0`, all other keys unset. Timeout is 600000ms for install, 120000ms for fetch/archive/extract/remote deletion, and 60000ms otherwise, with process-group TERM/5000ms/KILL/reap. `commandResults` is the immutable contiguous registry prefix: every success or failure is persisted if storage remains writable, a failed final entry prevents later entries within that attemptOrdinal until TerminalFailureDisposition authorizes a new ordinal, and no result may be removed/reordered/replaced. Recovery validates the exact prefix, optional activeCommand, and each command's canonical pre/post state. A read-only active command reruns. A mutating active command reruns only when exact preStateSha256 still holds; if exact postStateSha256 holds it appends a reconciled result without fabricating process streams; any other or ambiguous state blocks. Remote-ref-delete is the sole response-loss specialization: after its process group is proven dead, before ordinary success finalization and on every recovery with that active command, run exact read-only `remote-ref-delete-observe=["git","ls-remote","--exit-code","--heads","origin","refs/heads/"+B]` in C. Persist/push/readback exact no-extra-fields `TerminalRecoveryObservation={name:'remote-ref-delete-observe',argv,cwd,outcome:'present'|'absent',remoteSha,stdoutSha256,stderrSha256,observedAt}` by appending it to activeCommand.recoveryObservations; present requires exit zero, one exact `H<TAB>refs/heads/B` line and remoteSha H, while absent requires exit two, empty streams, and remoteSha null. Absent reconciles the prior deletion without another push; present H alone permits exact lease-guarded retry; any other exit/SHA/stream is a typed terminal failure. No mutation retries under weaker authority. Alternate argv/cwd/env, shell use, short write, unexpected probe value, remote lease loss, changed object/member/hash, remote observation, warning, or postcondition mismatch fails closed.
- Terminal command journaling is closed under crashes. activeCommand is null or exactly the next registry entry; it is pushed/read back before process spawn and must be null at every phase-advance checkpoint and in final TerminalCleanup. Canonical state hashing covers every command-specific observable needed to distinguish untouched prestate from complete intended poststate, including refs, worktree registration/path, canonical HEAD, archive/runtime manifests, and remote tracking state. A crash after mutation but before result persistence therefore yields either exact prestate, exact poststate, or a hard failure; recovery never invents an exit code, signal, stdout, or stderr. Tests fault before spawn, after every mutating syscall/process completion, before result append, and at each push/readback.
- Worktree removal never uses recursive `git worktree remove`. - The active non-artifact ordinary set is exact seven files below identity.taskSourcePath: `task.md`, `release-continuity.v1.json`, the four `{feedback-source,planning,doing,continuity}.md` mirrors in dirname(identity.deskDoingPath), and that iteration's `artifacts/.gitkeep`. - Desk archival begins only from identity task/track validating, passed TerminalCleanup, and no validating attempt. Before lifecycle mutation it writes/fsyncs/pushes active-root `desk-archive.attempt.v1.json`. `ArchiveOrdinaryFile={path,sha256}` is exact with normalized identity-task-relative regular-file path, SHA-256, BINARY sort, and unique path. `DeskArchiveAttempt={version:1,identitySha256,task,sourcePath,targetPath,trackPath,doingPath,prNumber,prUrl,mergeSha,terminalCleanupSha256,lifecycleAt,taskBeforeSha256,taskDoneSha256,doingBeforeSha256,doingDoneSha256,trackTargetRowBeforeSha256,trackLandedRowSha256,ordinaryFiles,phase,taskDone,doingDone,trackDone,sourceAbsent,targetPresent,archiveValid,startedAt,updatedAt}` requires task/source/target/track/doing byte-equal ReleaseTaskIdentity; phase is `prepared|lifecycle_done|root_moved|archive_validated`, booleans monotonic, immutable fields frozen, and every checkpoint uses the Git matrix. Prepared precomputes task validating->done, lifecycle timestamp, cleared active iteration, matching merged PR/history; Desk doing VALIDATING->COMPLETE; and a semantic transform removing only the identity target row and inserting its exact Landed row while preserving unrelated rows/order. Concurrent unrelated rows rebase; identity target drift or duplicate Landed fails closed. ordinaryFiles is exact branch-specific closed-set hashes. Recovery accepts only before/done bytes, reparses/reapplies the transform, then exact git mv. Final `DeskArchive` repeats every immutable field with terminal booleans true; attempt unlink plus receipt commit/push is atomic.
- The exact inserted track block is rendered from ReleaseTaskIdentity as `## Landed\n\n| Slug | State | Repos | Tracker link | Doing doc |\n|------|-------|-------|--------------|-----------|\n| \`<identity.task>\` | done | spoonjoy-v2 (local) | <prUrl> @ \`<mergeSha>\` | \`taskdoc:spoonjoy-v2/<identity.task>/<relative iteration directory>/doing.md\` |\n\n`; `<relative iteration directory>` is dirname(identity.deskDoingPath) after removing identity.taskSourcePath, normalized by TaskDocumentLocator. The primary identity renders the Clem row; B/C render their own slugs and document locators. The locator is stable across task and whole-track moves and resolves only by the locator contract below; no active/archive physical path may be stored in the row. The block is inserted once immediately before `## Adoption summary`. The active Tasks table retains its header/separator and every unrelated row in order. Task Landed, iteration PR number, Desk doing Merge, and receipt `doingLocator` use the same prNumber/prUrl/mergeSha/document-locator bytes.
- DeskArchive competing-writer convergence is exact. Each phase candidate is clean L atop predecessor O. On rejection fetch R and require R descends O. For task/doing/protocol paths accept only byte-identical unrelated paths or valid monotonic same-identity successor. For track.md parse R, require the target-row precondition or already-applied Landed row, preserve every unrelated valid row, reapply the semantic transform with lifecycleAt, and create a new candidate L2 atop R; full-file hash equality to O is never required for unrelated row changes. After an already-applied phase, a loser L converges with K whose tree is R and parents R,L via commit-tree, normal-pushes only R->K, then ff-only advances. Retry at most eight races. This covers lifecycle, git-mv, candidate validation, receipt/unlink, and validating cancellation.
- After task archive passes, Desk scans one fetched main tree. `remainingUnarchivedTasks` is the BINARY-sorted unique union of every non-underscore task directory still under `spoonjoy-v2/` regardless of lifecycle status and every `spoonjoy-v2/_archive/<task>` child lacking its hash-valid final task-archive receipt (`desk-archive.v1.json` or `predecessor-supersede.v1.json`) or containing a live archive/terminal attempt. Those final receipts prove root_moved/archive-valid task state without depending on the later track-aware ArchiveValidationReceipt, so no cycle exists; lifecycle `done` alone never suffices. `TrackDisposition={version:1,track:'spoonjoy-v2',triggerTask,taskArchiveKind,taskArchiveSha256,decision:'kept_active'|'archived',remainingUnarchivedTasks,scanDeskSha,trackGeneration,targetPath,trackArchiveSha256,completedAt}` is exact; triggerTask is identity.task, trackGeneration is exact scanDeskSha, targetPath is exact `_archive/spoonjoy-v2/generation-<scanDeskSha>`, kind/hash follow the triggering normal or repaired receipt, kept_active requires nonempty remaining/null archive hash, and archived requires empty remaining/exact TrackArchive hash. Empty scan writes exact `TrackArchiveAttempt={version:1,track:'spoonjoy-v2',sourcePath:'spoonjoy-v2',targetPath,triggerTask,taskArchiveKind,taskArchiveSha256,scanDeskSha,trackGeneration,trackBeforeSha256,trackClosedSha256,remainingUnarchivedTasks:[],phase,trackClosed,sourceTreeMoved,targetPresent,archiveValid,startedAt,updatedAt}`; final TrackArchive repeats every immutable field with all terminal booleans true. Target must be absent before prepared; full SHA qualification prevents generation collision.
- Before the successful root_moved push, every fetch/rescan or rejected push that observes any remainingUnarchivedTasks consumes the attempt as kept_active and never moves the root; an empty rescan may rebuild/retry, at most eight. The accepted normal root_moved push from the last empty scan is the archive linearization point. After it, the archived decision is irrevocable: a later newly created `/Users/arimendelow/desk/spoonjoy-v2` is a distinct active track generation with its own future scanDeskSha/target and is preserved, never moved into or merged with the old generation. `sourceTreeMoved:true` describes only the scanned generation and remains true if the source pathname is recreated. Archived task and repair-index locators resolve through the unique hash-valid TrackArchive.targetPath, never a fixed unqualified `_archive/spoonjoy-v2` root.
- Archive closed-set validation uses the Round 60 phase/state/checkpoint normal/repaired sets and ordering. Ordinary files/artifacts remain exact and matching attempt/temp files are legal only in their journal phase; final rejects attempts, temps, links, lookalikes, drift, and extras. Validation runs from the isolated validatorMergeSha runtime with exact no-shell argv `["pnpm","release:evidence","--","validate","--manifest",<final absolute manifest path>,"--mode","archive"]`, cwd validatorRuntimePath, the terminal closed environment, timeout 120000ms, and exact no-extra-fields `ArchiveValidationCommandResult={sequence:0,name:'archive-validation',argv,cwd,timeoutMs:120000,outcome,exitCode,signal,stdoutSha256,stderrSha256,warningCount}`. Exact `ArchiveValidationAttempt={version:1,attemptOrdinal,priorFailedAttemptPaths,priorFailedAttemptSetSha256,mergeSha,validatorMergeSha,executionHost,validatorRuntimePath,validatorArchivePath,manifestPath,trackDecision,trackDispositionSha256,trackDispositionCommitSha,phase,commandResult,startedAt,updatedAt}` has phase `prepared|failed|validated` and the Round 60 compact `{path,sha256}` retry-set hash. prepared alone has null commandResult; failed has one non-success or positive-warning result and requires TerminalFailureDisposition; validated has exactly exit zero/null signal/zero warnings. A provisional validated attempt may authorize the optional repair index but cannot finalize after a later task mutation. The sole final schema is `ArchiveValidationReceipt={version:1,attemptOrdinal,priorFailedAttemptPaths,priorFailedAttemptSetSha256,mergeSha,validatorMergeSha,executionHost,validatorRuntimePath,validatorArchivePath,validatorArchiveSha256,validatorSourceTreeSha256,manifestPath,trackDecision,trackDispositionSha256,trackDispositionCommitSha,repairIndexPath,repairIndexSha256,commandResult,validatedAt}`. Only the last fresh validated ordinal over the final task-mutating set atomically replaces its attempt with that receipt. Receipt push/readback precedes Desk-control resource cleanup; no task byte changes afterward. Overall completion and Slugger require the ordinary-normal or repaired-root receipt plus external runtime/archive absence, while repair-successor-normal remains an intermediate handoff and cannot notify.
- Validator runtime/archive deletion is a separate host-bound journaled protocol after ArchiveValidationReceipt push/readback and before terminal result or Slugger preparation. Its exact no-extra-fields `TerminalResourceCleanupAttempt={version:1,identitySha256,executionHost,validatorRuntimePath,validatorRuntimeDeletePath,validatorArchivePath,validatorArchiveDeletePath,validatorArchiveSha256,runtimeManifest,runtimeManifestSha256,phase,nextDeleteIndex,runtimeDetached,archiveDetached,archiveDeleted,startedAt,updatedAt}` now lives only at `/Users/arimendelow/desk/_meta/release-terminal/<identitySha256>/terminal-resource-cleanup.attempt.v1.json`, never task root. Delete paths are token-qualified siblings frozen before mutation and absent initially. runtimeManifest is the complete BINARY-relative-path-sorted `TerminalResourceMember={relativePath,kind:'file'|'directory'|'symlink',sha256}[]`; cleanup renames atomically, fsyncs, removes members in deterministic reverse-depth/BINARY order without following links, and reconciles only exact source/tombstone/remaining-manifest state. Phase remains `prepared|runtime_detached|archive_detached|deleting|complete`; complete requires all four resource paths absent. The final Desk-control checkpoint removes the complete attempt only after push/readback and a fresh absence scan. Failures/waits/resolutions use the Round 58 desk_control domain, never alter task/archive bytes, and never authorize repair_successor. Foreign hosts remain read-only. Tests fault every rename, fsync, member deletion, index write, archive deletion, control checkpoint, and final unlink.
- Slugger is owned by release-terminal only after product/task/track/archive finality. Its sole basename and Desk-repo-relative path are `_meta/notifications/spoonjoy-v2/<identity.repairRootTask>/slugger-notification.v1.json`; its physical path is `/Users/arimendelow/desk/_meta/notifications/spoonjoy-v2/<identity.repairRootTask>/slugger-notification.v1.json`; every eligible ReleaseTerminalResult.sluggerPath byte-equals the relative path. The protocol has one ownership generation and no replacement. Exact no-extra-fields `SluggerNotification={version:1,task:identity.repairRootTask,mergeSha,message,ownershipGeneration:1,writerId,phase,generation,resultPath,resultSha256,completedAt,updatedAt}` has phase `prepared|recorded|released|observed|uncertain`; `SluggerSpawnGeneration={generation:1,spawnToken,executionHost,status,gatePath,releasePath,publishPath,resultPath,pid,pgid,processStartIdentity,preparedAt,recordedAt,releasedAt,terminalAt}` has status `prepared|recorded|released|terminal` and the literal monotonic null matrix below. Exact compact canonical no-final-LF bytes are `SluggerGate={version:1,generation:1,spawnToken,executionHost,notificationPath,releasePath,publishPath,resultPath,commandSha256,preparedAt}` `SluggerRelease={version:1,generation:1,spawnToken,releasedAt}` and host-local `SluggerPublish={version:1,generation:1,spawnToken,releaseSha256,publishedAt}`; `notificationDirectory` is exact `/Users/arimendelow/desk/_meta/notifications/spoonjoy-v2/<identity.repairRootTask>`; notificationPath is `<notificationDirectory>/slugger-notification.v1.json`, gatePath is `<notificationDirectory>/slugger-generation-1-gate.v1.json`, releasePath is `<notificationDirectory>/slugger-generation-1-release.v1.json`, and resultPath is `<notificationDirectory>/slugger-generation-1-result.v1.json`. Those four are the only registered regular non-symlink Desk paths and exact siblings; publishPath is exact `/Users/arimendelow/Library/Caches/spoonjoy-release/<spawnToken>/generation-1-publish.v1.json` under a mode-0700 token directory and is never Git-tracked, commandSha256 hashes compact canonical `SluggerCommandSpec`, and every field equals the journal generation. Exact gate argv is `["pnpm","exec","tsx","scripts/release-spawn-gate.ts","--gate",gatePath,"--release",releasePath,"--publish",publishPath,"--result",resultPath,"--spawn-token",spawnToken]` from `/Users/arimendelow/Projects/spoonjoy-v2`, under SluggerCommandSpec's closed environment plus `CI=1`, `NO_COLOR=1`, and `FORCE_COLOR=0`; its process-group identity is PID/PGID plus platform process-start identity and exact argv hash. `SluggerProcessResult={version:1,generation:1,spawnToken,outcome:'exit'|'signal'|'spawn_error'|'not_spawned'|'observation_error',exitCode,signal,stdoutSha256,stderrSha256,startedAt,endedAt}` has exit with integer 0..255/null signal/canonical start/end; signal with null exit/finite signal/canonical start/end; spawn_error with both outcome fields null and canonical start/end; not_spawned with both null, null start, canonical end, and empty-stream hashes; observation_error with both null, nullable start, canonical end, and hashes of whatever sanitized complete stream prefixes were safely observed, using empty hashes when no trustworthy prefix exists. Invalid UTF-8, NUL, cap overflow, short result write, or indeterminate process observation maps only to observation_error. Observed permits only exit; uncertain permits signal, spawn_error, not_spawned, or observation_error. Initial absence CAS creates prepared notification plus immutable SluggerGate bytes and normal-push/fetch/readback proves both before any spawn; a rejected CAS creates neither process nor additional file. The winner spawns exactly one waiting gate and records PID/PGID/start identity in the next pushed/readback journal. A crash between OS spawn and recorded checkpoint is closed explicitly: prepared recovery scans only the frozen executionHost process table for exact generation/token/gate argv/hash/cwd/start identity. Exactly one same-host live waiting gate is adopted by recording its PID/PGID/start identity without spawning; no member terminalizes uncertain/not_spawned; a foreign-host or unverifiable candidate blocks without mutation; multiple or mismatching candidates fail closed. After recorded push/readback, release-terminal atomically creates/pushes/readbacks released journal plus immutable SluggerRelease intent bytes, but the adopted gate remains blocked and never treats release-file presence as permission. Only after fetch/readback proves the released journal and complete release bytes remote-readable does release-terminal create the token directory, write/fsync/rename the mode-0600 SluggerPublish bytes whose releaseSha256 hashes those exact release bytes, and fsync the directory; only that publish token may wake the gate, which revalidates token/generation/release hash before executing the exact child. A same-host crash after remote readback but before publish may recreate byte-identical publish bytes after repeating remote validation; foreign-host recovery blocks. Released recovery observes/reaps only after publication and never spawns another gate or child. Synchronous child-spawn failure writes spawn_error. Every terminal result is immutable, all process-group members are dead/reaped before terminal checkpoint, and the host-local publish file/token directory are removed before the terminal notification checkpoint, and observed/uncertain journal plus result push/readback occurs exactly once. Once prepared exists, every failure terminalizes or blocks generation one; no second token, gate, process, release file, result file, generation, or retry is legal. Repair-successor and repair-intermediate identities have sluggerPath null; only ordinary-normal and repaired-root are eligible. Every mutation uses complete O/C bytes, Git matrix, normal push, fetch, byte-identical readback; alternate path, symlink, field drift, invalid scan evidence, or unproved liveness fails closed, and tests fault every CAS/file/spawn/adoption/record/release/observe boundary.
- Slugger nullability is literal. Notification phases prepared, recorded, and released require resultPath/resultSha256/completedAt null; observed and uncertain require all three nonnull and hash-valid, while updatedAt is nonnull in every phase and strictly increases from the immutable prepared timestamp. Generation prepared requires pid/pgid/processStartIdentity/recordedAt/releasedAt/terminalAt null. recorded requires pid/pgid/processStartIdentity/recordedAt nonnull and releasedAt/terminalAt null. released preserves those four and adds releasedAt while terminalAt remains null. terminal normally preserves the recorded identity/timestamps and adds terminalAt. A gate spawn_error or proven not_spawned before recording alone may terminalize with pid/pgid/processStartIdentity/recordedAt/releasedAt null and terminalAt nonnull; a released child spawn_error preserves recorded/released identity and times. observation_error after process adoption preserves every known identity/time and never nulls a prior value. SluggerProcessResult outcome must agree with notification observed only for exit and uncertain for signal, spawn_error, not_spawned, or observation_error; generation status, notification phase, result timestamps, and publish/release presence must agree exactly.

**REST v1 Compatibility**
- Existing field types and meanings remain unchanged. Any incompatible change requires v2.
- Recipe summary/detail add `stepCount: number`, `course: string | null`, `tags: string[]`, and `isSaved: boolean | null`; `stepCount` is exactly the count of returned active recipe's RecipeStep rows, independent of stepNum values/duplicates/gaps and zero for no rows. No principal and valid bearer principals without exact `kitchen:read` receive null isSaved; cookie-session/trusted-environment principals and bearer principals with exact `kitchen:read` receive their user's boolean. The latter three perform viewer-scoped SavedRecipe lookup; public-only bearer projection performs none. Public/private cache rules remain exact as defined under SavedRecipe. `course` is lowercase controlled; `tags` are custom display labels in normalizedLabel/id order.
- Attribution preserves existing `sourceHost = new URL(sourceUrl).hostname || null` behavior and derives `sourceDisplayName` only from that result, never directly from arbitrary text. Null/empty/non-absolute/malformed sourceUrl gives both null. WHATWG URL parsing owns trimming, scheme, credentials, port removal, IPv4 canonicalization, bracketed IPv6, and IDN-to-ASCII. For a nonempty hostname, lowercase ASCII; for DNS names only remove one trailing dot, then remove one leading `www.` only when a nonempty remainder exists; IPv4 and bracketed IPv6 are not dot/prefix transformed. Return the resulting ASCII hostname (including IPv6 brackets). Tests cover whitespace-wrapped absolute URL, port/credentials, uppercase/one-or-multiple www, trailing dot, punycode Unicode, IPv4, IPv6, `www.`, relative URL, empty, and malformed surrogate input.
- Detail-only `GET /api/v1/recipes/{id}?scaleFactor=<number>` accepts exactly one unsigned decimal matching `^(?:\d+(?:\.\d*)?|\.\d+)$` whose parsed JavaScript Number is finite and in `0.25..50`; signs, exponent/hex notation, whitespace-only, malformed, multiple, nonfinite, and out-of-range values return the existing `validation_error` shape. The returned `scaleFactor` is that parsed Number. When omitted, factor defaults to `1`.
