Detail always returns required `scaleFactor` and required ingredient `scaledQuantity`; at default factor, scaled quantity still uses the same six-decimal exact-rounding algorithm. List/search behavior is unchanged.
- Detail preserves required numeric ingredient `quantity` and adds required numeric `scaledQuantity`; the response includes `scaleFactor`. Convert quantity and the parsed factor's ECMAScript shortest round-trip decimals, never the raw query lexeme, to signed base-10 integer/scale pairs, multiply exactly, then round to six decimals with half ties away from zero; strip trailing fractional zeros and normalize negative zero. Thus `0.25000000000000001` multiplies and returns as `0.25`. If the rounded exact value cannot convert to a finite JavaScript number at or below `Number.MAX_VALUE`, return existing v1 `400 validation_error` with message `scaled quantity is outside supported numeric range`; never serialize null. Scaling does not write recipe data. `servings` remains original nullable freeform string.
- OpenAPI, `api-v1-contract.server.ts`, generator output, developer playground, examples, REST tests, and MCP shopping metadata remain synchronized.

**MCP Recipe Read Compatibility**
- Existing MCP tools remain named `search_recipes` and `get_recipe` with required `recipes:read`; this release adds no parallel tool. Search summaries and get detail add the same neutral `stepCount`, `sourceDisplayName`, `course`, and `tags` values as REST from shared projection helpers. MCP intentionally omits `isSaved` entirely: private save state remains behind the REST kitchen-read entitlement and `/me/saved-recipes` contract rather than widening a public recipe-read tool.
- `get_recipe` alone adds optional JSON-number `scaleFactor` to its MCP tool/input schema. Omission returns `scaleFactor: 1`; otherwise the value must be a finite JavaScript number in `0.25..50`. Strings, null, booleans, NaN/Infinity under direct invocation, and out-of-range values fail with exact `scaleFactor must be a finite number between 0.25 and 50`. Detail always adds ingredient `scaledQuantity` while preserving `quantity` and nullable freeform `servings`; `search_recipes` accepts no scaleFactor and returns no ingredient scaling projection.
- REST and MCP call one transport-neutral metadata helper and one transport-neutral exact-decimal scaling helper. MCP multiplication uses the accepted Number's ECMAScript shortest round-trip decimal and REST uses its already-parsed Number, so both return byte-equivalent numeric results for the same Number, including six-decimal half-away-from-zero rounding and negative-zero normalization. Overflow fails before response with exact `scaled quantity is outside supported numeric range`; neither surface writes recipe data. Unit3/4 architecture tests reject duplicate transport-specific derivation, and Unit27.2 extends the same MCP projections with accepted course/custom tags only.

- Use a SQLite-backed Durable Object for authenticated live state and D1 only as a private, retryable query/history projection.
- Route the internal cook API at Worker level before React Router so WebSocket upgrades retain the Cloudflare `webSocket` handle. Preserve security headers on ordinary responses and test the full default export.
- Use operation-based optimistic concurrency instead of whole-snapshot last-write-wins.
- Use one deterministic DO per user/recipe and one active attempt UUID inside it, with explicit complete, abandon/start-fresh, and partial-failure-safe current-attempt purge lifecycle.
- Do not create RecipeSpoon entries from private cooking progress.
- Keep anonymous cooking local; authenticated local cache/queue is non-canonical.
- Adopt anonymous local progress only into a pristine server object; any server attempt wins regardless of client timestamp.
- Add SavedRecipe as private canonical save state and bridge all cookbook writers for compatibility.
- Keep global recipe search free of private save metadata.
- Ship manual accepted tags only; defer AI suggestions until a review model and UX exist.
- Preserve current navigation unless evidence warrants a focused fix.
- Keep import agent/API-only and reject Pebble-specific behavior.

**Round 35 executable clarifications (normative)**
- These clauses replace any earlier abbreviated field list or contradictory recovery phrase in this document and the doing document; all unaffected requirements remain cumulative. Unit29.2 source/tests encode this precedence literally rather than relying on prose interpretation.
- Provider authority is only canonical `EnsureInvocationAuthority` as defined above. Unit29.2 validates authority files and serializes that object; Unit29.1 accepts the object/null, never paths. A host lacking predispatch_existing or postdispatch_reconciled authority may execute a read-only provider probe in memory only. Only the predispatch intent executionHost may zero-generation materialize; only the dispatch executionHost may prove its gate/process dead, create a missing release file, postdispatch materialize, replay, signal, or terminalize. Permanent loss of that host is a human-only blocker. A prepared generation with synchronous spawn failure and no process/release becomes aborted through the exact `finish-command ... spawn_error` transition. An orphan gate not represented by the manifest is removable only when it is the exact next generation, command/token-valid, release-absent, process-absent, and absent from remote evidence; otherwise recovery fails closed.
- Gate and registered-child environments are exactly the seven-policy table plus the internal keys below. Both roles retain `SPOONJOY_RELEASE_SPAWN_TOKEN` and their exact `SPOONJOY_RELEASE_PROCESS_ROLE`; ensure roles also retain byte-identical `SPOONJOY_RELEASE_ENSURE_AUTHORITY_B64`; cloudflare-rest or cloudflare-d1 gate alone receives nonsecret `SPOONJOY_RELEASE_SECRET_FD` until one-shot consumption and its registered child receives only the resulting CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN. Linux discovery reads exact NUL-delimited `/proc/<pid>/environ` plus stat parent/PGID/start identity. Darwin runs exact `ps -E -ww -axo pid=,ppid=,pgid=,lstart=,command=`, parses only exact markers and process relationships in memory, and never persists/logs environment-bearing output. Tests reject missing/duplicate token or role, bearer in gate environment/argv, inherited secret descriptor/marker, unrelated matches, secret persistence, and every invalid parent/PGID/start/argv relation. No generic `SPOONJOY_*` inheritance exception exists.
- `ProcessSpec.operationPhaseCapMs` and total timeout arithmetic are exactly the values above; a provider horizon and its final 10000ms observation are inside, never larger than, that phase. `prepare-spawn` and `release-spawn` return the exact no-extra success objects above. Process failure/interruption domains and AgentCommand fields/nullability are closed exactly above.
- Retry-After sanitization accepts only canonical decimal `/^[1-9][0-9]*$/` whose parsed safe integer is `1..86400`; larger, zero, signed, padded, fractional, or unsafe values are malformed. Smoke/cleanup retry code still refuses any sleep that violates its own attempt/deadline budget and therefore never waits 86400 seconds merely because the header parsed.
- `WorkflowDiscovery={candidates,selected,observedAt}` is the sole workflow-discovery output and is written to `production-workflow-discovery.json`; the later watch artifact is the selected terminal Workflow. `Continuation={repo,prNumber,sourceSha,treeSha,mergeSha,excludedHeadRef,openPrNumbers,openBranchRefs,openPrCount,openBranchCount,unresolvedThreadIds,followUpIssueIds,ready}` excludes only the current merged PR and exact `ReleaseTaskIdentity.branch`, counts equal arrays, and is included as continuation in Unit37 evidence. `Health` is exactly the HealthSuccess/HealthFailure union above; failed samples contain no raw body/header.
- Generic reviewer reports and visual reviewer reports are distinct exact eight-line formats above. `ReviewInput.requiredArtifacts` selection is immutable by unit: Unit32 all Artifacts from its first eighteen latest-passed ProcessCommands; Unit34 all Artifacts from latest-passed fetch-drift/pr-ensure; each Unit37 visual review all 38 BINARY-sorted direct-child visual runner Artifacts plus the visual command's two log Artifacts. The caller cannot supply or omit paths. Unit37 prompt bytes include exact live target and visual set hash.
- The Git checkpoint matrix is exact. For each declared path, legal precommit worktree/index byte states are only O/O, C/O, and C/C; a multi-file partial state means only a mixture of those whole-file states. O/C, partial bytes, and any blob outside exact O/C are illegal. Recovery rewrites every declared worktree path from frozen complete C bytes or deterministic transform, invokes exactly `git add -- <BINARY-sorted declared paths>`, and verifies all C/C plus tree C. It never invokes `git restore --staged` and never derives bytes from the index.
- Desk validating recovery finds the unique exact transform child L of productHeadBeforeSha. If remote R equals or descends L and repository doing bytes remain the exact transformed bytes, it records `productCommitSha=L` and resumes product_done even when R is a later unrelated descendant. If no such child exists, R descends the predecessor, and before bytes are preserved, it enters cancellation. Multiple transform children, changed doing bytes, wrong ancestry, or an unrecorded transform fails closed.
- Terminal cleanup writes and pushes `TerminalCleanupAttempt` phase prepared before creating an archive/runtime. Its exact schema adds `validatorMergeSha`, `validatorRuntimeTempPath`, and `validatorArchiveTempPath`; `validatorArchiveSha256` and `validatorSourceTreeSha256` are null through canonical_main_ready and become nonnull exactly at validator_ready. Prepared freezes exact final and token-qualified sibling temp paths. Only journal-owned matching temps may be resumed/removed; unknown or preexisting nonidentical paths fail. It builds archive/runtime through those temps, verifies/hashes, atomically renames to final paths, then checkpoints validator_ready. Normal closure has `validatorMergeSha=mergeSha`; repair-intermediate or repair-root closure has original `mergeSha` for branch/ref/worktree cleanup and `validatorMergeSha` from the hash-validated immutable repair leaf PostMergeRepairReceipt. TerminalCleanup and ArchiveValidationReceipt both carry both SHAs; source/archive/tree/lockfile validation binds validatorMergeSha while branchHead/ref cleanup binds original mergeSha.
- Archive-validation closed sets are phase-, branch-, disposition-, and predecessor-state-specific. Ordinary-normal and repair-successor-normal use their declared terminal-cleanup/leaf/desk-archive/disposition/final prefixes. Every repaired-root/intermediate prefix and final set uses the Round 59 authoritative state table, including the distinct relay basename and any retained DeskArchive/leaf receipt. Matching active attempts and token-qualified temps are legal only in their journal phase and absent from final history. Each intermediate requires its attempt-free external repair index before ancestor continuation; root has none, and no validator requires a future receipt.
- Cross-task path fields are logical Desk locators, never persisted physical paths. `TaskRootLocator` is exactly `task:spoonjoy-v2/<slug>`; `TaskReceiptLocator` is `task:spoonjoy-v2/<slug>/<registered-basename>`; `TaskDocumentLocator` is `taskdoc:spoonjoy-v2/<slug>/<normalized-relative-path>`; `TaskArtifactLocator` is `task:spoonjoy-v2/<slug>/artifacts/<normalized-relative-path>`; and `TrackLocator` is `track:spoonjoy-v2/<normalized-relative-path>`. Every normalized segment is nonempty UTF-8 NFC, excludes `.`, `..`, slash, backslash, NUL, percent encoding, and a leading underscore, with one closed exception: a TrackLocator may have exact first segment `_repair-index` and no other underscore-prefixed segment. The full relative path BINARY-round-trips. TaskDocumentLocator permits only identity-registered planning/doing/source/mirror document paths and is the sole durable Landed doing-doc type; TaskReceiptLocator permits only registered terminal basenames; TaskArtifactLocator begins with artifacts. Resolution is phase-aware, never requires a future final receipt, and begins only after fetch plus recovery of any uncommitted Git checkpoint; semantic locator resolution never interprets an O/C worktree/index mixture. With no final receipt or relocation attempt, a task locator selects only the identity-authorized active root. A unique hash-valid task relocation attempt before `root_moved` selects that active root. The `root_moved` checkpoint is one atomic Git candidate tree that moves the complete root and simultaneously replaces the attempt bytes at the frozen target with phase `root_moved`; no legal committed tree contains pre-move attempt bytes at the target or root_moved bytes at the source. Accepted/pushed trees are therefore exactly O with the pre-move attempt at source or C with the advanced attempt at target. Later archive-valid phase and final receipt select only the target. Whole-track relocation is identical: pre-root_moved TrackArchiveAttempt selects active track; one candidate tree moves the generation and advances the target attempt to root_moved; accepted trees are exact O or C; final TrackArchive selects target. A local crash during candidate materialization may leave only per-path legal Git-matrix mixtures; recovery first rematerializes frozen C, reruns BINARY-sorted add/tree verification, commits/pushes/fetches/readbacks or restores O after a rejected winner, and only then invokes the semantic resolver. The resolver probes finite active/frozen locations and requires exactly one schema/hash/phase-consistent attempt or receipt before joining the unchanged normalized relative path and returning one regular non-symlink hash-valid object. Tests fault every path materialization/add/tree/commit/push/readback and restart at O, every legal local mixture, and C. Zero/multiple matches, old/new duplication in a committed tree, wrong-side phase, alias, symlink, unregistered path/basename, traversal, wrong kind/hash/generation, or active-root recreation fails closed; a move changes only physical resolution, never locator bytes.
- Track disposition/archive schemas add `taskArchiveKind:'desk_archive'|'predecessor_supersede'`; `taskArchiveSha256` hashes `desk-archive.v1.json` for normal closure or `predecessor-supersede.v1.json` for repaired closure. TrackDisposition, TrackArchiveAttempt, and TrackArchive carry the same kind/hash. Normal and repaired Unit37 terminal acceptance branches require their respective final file sets above. The repaired validator attests original predecessor evidence plus PostMergeRepairReceipt and uses validatorMergeSha; it does not execute the defective original runtime.
- Slugger's only message bytes are `Done: Shipped Clem feedback end to end`. Exact `SluggerCommandSpec` is argv `["ouro","msg","--to","slugger","Done: Shipped Clem feedback end to end"]`, cwd `/Users/arimendelow/Projects/spoonjoy-v2`, environment exactly `PATH=/opt/homebrew/bin:/usr/bin:/bin`, `HOME=/Users/arimendelow`, `USER=arimendelow`, `LOGNAME=arimendelow`, `LANG=C`, and `LC_ALL=C`, with every other key unset; total timeout is 30000ms, timeout sends SIGTERM to the process group, waits 5000ms, then SIGKILLs the surviving group. Stdout and stderr are independently capped at 65536 bytes, must be clean UTF-8 without NUL, are sanitized in memory, and are never written into product/task/archive state. Spawn error, not-spawned recovery, signal, TERM/KILL timeout, invalid UTF-8, NUL, short injected write, or indeterminate process observation writes the immutable one-generation result and transitions exactly once to `uncertain` under the schema above; a clean ordinary exit `0..255` writes the immutable exit result and transitions exactly once to `observed`. No terminal outcome permits another spawn. A returned process exit 0 means only that the command returned zero; it is recorded as observed and is not proof that Slugger delivered or consumed the message. The durable exactly-one-generation, at-most-one-gate-and-child journal remains authoritative.
- Execution placeholders are disjoint and exact: `<M>` manifest path, `<W>` writerId, `<R>` release run, `<U>` unit, `<G>` stage run, `<L>` logical name, `<A>` command attempt, `<S>` SHA, `<K>` artifact kind, `<P>` artifact path, `<J>` canonical compact JSON, `<N>` generation, `<PID>` process id, `<PGID>` process group id, `<PSI>` process-start identity, `<HOST>` executionHost, `<AGENT>` agent UUID, `<ROLE>` reviewer role, `<VERDICT>` agent verdict, and `<RUN_ATTEMPT>` positive workflow attempt. A placeholder never changes meaning between vectors.

- Ensure ProcessSpecs retain `--intent/--arm/--dispatch` task-relative operands only as lifecycle-owner inputs. After validating them and constructing EnsureInvocationAuthority, Unit29.2 removes those six flag/value argv entries before command hashing/gate registration and injects the authority environment object. Unit29.1 CLI rejects `--intent`, `--arm`, and `--dispatch`; its public normalized operation argv therefore contains no authority path. Operand descriptors remain exhaustive for the stored lifecycle command, while `registeredArgv` is the tested stripped provider argv.

**Round 36 executable definitions (normative replacements)**
- Ensure materialization has two disjoint authorities. `predispatch_existing` requires no global dispatch, zero spawn generations across the operation key, a current running intent owned by the executing intent.executionHost, and a hash-verified exact_effect probe; it materializes disposition existing. `postdispatch_reconciled` requires an authoritative dispatch, exact current host equal dispatch.executionHost, and host-local proof that every released generation member is dead; it materializes disposition reconciled. `materialize-ensure-outcome` accepts exact `--authority predispatch_existing|postdispatch_reconciled`; no other host/state may terminalize. A non-authority host may probe in memory only and reports the host-loss blocker; it never persists a probe or changes manifest state.
- Gate transport/liveness is exact. Both gate and registered child environments carry `SPOONJOY_RELEASE_SPAWN_TOKEN=<token>` plus `SPOONJOY_RELEASE_PROCESS_ROLE=gate|child`. Ensure-only gate and child also carry `SPOONJOY_RELEASE_ENSURE_AUTHORITY_B64=<unpadded base64url of canonical UTF-8 EnsureInvocationAuthority JSON>`; ordinary commands omit it. The gate validates token/file/argv, transports authority bytes unchanged, changes only role to child for child spawn, and never parses authority; Unit29.1 decodes and schema-validates it before provider work. Same-host recovery scans token+role and accepts only one verified gate with no child, one verified gate plus its one same-PGID descendant child, or one verified orphan child in the recorded PGID after gate death. Any other count/role/PGID/start/argv relation fails closed. Any verified member means live, so replay/materialization/signal completion waits for every member's death. ProcessIdentity remains the gate identity and the scanned child identity is runtime proof, never a new manifest authority.
- `ProcessCommand` adds `deadlineStartedAt`, `deadlineAt`, `storedCommandSha256`, and exact `command:StoredArgv`. Preflight starts the total timer in memory; once preflight succeeds, `start-command` persists its original canonical deadlineStartedAt and deadlineAt=`started+timeoutMs` before later work. A crash before start-command has no state/side effect and may begin a fresh preflight; every persisted attempt resumes the original deadline. `StoredOperand={index,kind:'repo_relative'|'task_relative'}`; `StoredArgv={argv:string[],operands:StoredOperand[]}` is no-extra-fields, argv is nonempty strings, operands are numeric-ascending unique/in-range and exactly the nonliteral positions. storedCommandSha256 hashes canonical StoredArgv. `resolveStoredArgv` preserves literals/repo operands and absolutizes only task operands. For ensures Unit29.2 validates lifecycle path operands, removes the six intent/arm/dispatch flag/value entries, and hashes the resulting registeredArgv in the gate; Unit29.1 receives registeredArgv plus authority env and rejects lifecycle flags.
- Ensure zero-spawn terminalization is separate from process finish. Complete grammar adds `finish-command-without-process --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt A --reason predispatch_indeterminate|predispatch_conflict|dispatch_ambiguity`; it requires zero generations for predispatch reasons, or dispatch host + deadline reached + every generation dead for ambiguity, writes empty sanitized logs, and fails with `provider_indeterminate|provider_conflict|dispatch_ambiguity`. `finish-command` remains generation/process-result-only. `materialize-ensure-outcome` itself writes output/log artifacts and terminalizes passed; the executor must return immediately and never call finish afterward. Failure precedence remains unchanged for spawned commands.
- Complete mutating grammar also includes exact `transfer-continuity --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit 32 --stage-run G --tested-base-sha T --branch-head-sha H --branch-head-tree-sha B --out O`. The adapter produces no final receipt. When its command passes, finish-command atomically derives post-transition manifest revision/updatedAt, writes exact ReleaseContinuity and `release-continuity-transfer.json` from that post-finish state, then repairs either file deterministically after every crash boundary. Thus the immutable ContinuityTransfer is born current and remains hash-equal to the post-finish continuity fields.
- The local-db policy adds exact `DATABASE_URL:'file:./test.db?connection_limit=1&socket_timeout=60'`; no shorter URL is legal.
- Exact health schemas are `HealthSuccess={at,url,status:200,bodyBuildSha,headerBuildSha,workerVersionId,error:null}` and `HealthFailure={at,url,status,bodyBuildSha:null,headerBuildSha:null,workerVersionId:null,error}`. `at` is canonical time; `url` is exact normalized `<baseUrl>/health`; success build fields are exact lowercase 40-hex Git SHAs equal to HealthSeries.sourceSha and workerVersionId is null only for QA; failure status is null or safe integer 100..599 and error is `network|timeout|http_status|invalid_json|invalid_body|invalid_header|build_sha_mismatch|worker_version_mismatch`. `Health=HealthSuccess|HealthFailure`; `HealthSeries.samples:Health[]`; `QaDeployOutcome.health:HealthSeries`; every unit evidence healthSamples is the exact series samples.
- CLI success values are no-extra-fields with these domains: UUID/string ids and canonical paths follow named schemas; every count is a nonnegative safe integer. `recover={writerId,interrupted,repaired,abandoned,handoffPath}` uses counts and task-relative handoffPath nonnull iff exactly one accepted handoff was recovered. `start-command` returns resolved absolute `argv:string[]`, sorted envNames, absolute stdout/stderr, absolute outPath or null exactly for log-only specs, and absolute intent/arm/dispatch paths all nonnull only for ensure specs and all null otherwise. prepare/record/release spawn fields use positive generation/PID/PGID and task-relative gate/release paths; materialize returns absolute outPath; agent reportPath is task-relative on both passed-CONVERGED and failed-FINDINGS; finish-stage evidencePath is task-relative on passed and null on failed. Every other listed literal/status/path field is nonnull exactly in its schema state; tests reject every alternate null/type/domain.
- Discovery binds workflow attempts canonically. `CiWorkflow` and `Workflow` add positive safe-integer `runAttempt`. `CiWorkflowDiscovery={candidates,selected,observedAt}` and WorkflowDiscovery both sort ascending by `(createdAt,databaseId,runAttempt)`, collapse byte-identical duplicate records with the same `(databaseId,runAttempt)`, reject differing duplicate records, and select the last/newest unique candidate; equal createdAt is broken numerically by databaseId then runAttempt. CI output becomes `ci-workflow-discovery.json:CiWorkflowDiscovery`; Unit37 ciWorkflow equals selected. watch-workflow, verify-deploy-job, and download-artifact add exact `--run-attempt <RUN_ATTEMPT>` after run-id; terminal Workflow, DeployJob.runAttempt, and artifact metadata must equal frozen selected runAttempt. Reruns are therefore separate candidates and never silently substituted.
- Continuation fields are exact. openPrNumbers is numeric-ascending unique positive safe integers excluding current merged prNumber; openBranchRefs is UTF-8/BINARY-sorted unique normalized nonempty branch names excluding exact excludedHeadRef; unresolvedThreadIds and followUpIssueIds are BINARY-sorted unique nonempty strings. open counts equal paired lengths. ready is exactly source/tree/nonnull merge equality, excludedHeadRef exact, current PR merged, and all four arrays/counts empty/zero.
- Reviewer FINDINGS is durable and sanitized. Prompts require either exact `CONVERGED` or canonical compact JSON `{verdict:'FINDINGS',findings:[ReviewFinding...]}`. `ReviewFinding={code,file,line,summary}` is no-extra-fields: code is `behavior|test|security_privacy|migration_config|design_visual|api_compatibility|provenance|cleanup`, file is normalized repo-relative or task-relative regular-file path, line is positive safe integer, and summary is sanitizer-clean UTF-8 1..500 scalar values without control characters/secrets. CONVERGED finish omits findings-json; FINDINGS exact CLI adds `--findings-json J` after verdict and J must byte-equal returned agent JSON. It writes exact `review-findings.v1.json={version:1,role,agentId,sourceSha,promptSha256,requiredArtifactsSha256,findings}` sorted by `(file,line,code,summary)` with at least one unique item, appends/hashes that report Artifact, and fails the command/stage. Raw unstructured prose is rejected. A review_finding RepairBrief must name/hash this sole report.
- Git states model absence. `BlobState={presence:'absent'}|{presence:'present',sha256,bytes}`; journals freeze O/C BlobState for every declared path. Legal per-path worktree/index pairs remain `(O,O)|(C,O)|(C,C)` where equality includes absence. Delete uses present O/absent C; create absent O/present C; move declares source present->absent and target absent->present. Recovery materializes C presence/absence for every path, runs exact `git add -- <BINARY-sorted paths>` (which stages create/delete), and verifies index C/tree C. Any partial present bytes, undeclared path, or other pair fails.
- Terminal lifecycle has one legal measured owner: import-safe `scripts/release-terminal.ts`, with one discriminated three-mode grammar. Normal is `pnpm release:terminal -- --mode normal --manifest M --writer-id W`; repaired is `pnpm release:terminal -- --mode repaired --manifest M --writer-id W --successor-receipt-locator L --successor-archive-validation-sha X`; successor is `pnpm release:terminal -- --mode successor --journal J --action A` with the action-specific flags defined below. Mode is the first flag after `--`; normal/repaired reject journal/action/predecessor flags, successor rejects manifest/writer and repaired flags except `prepare`'s named predecessor inputs. `createReleaseTerminal(deps)` owns TerminalCleanup, normal DeskArchive or PredecessorSupersede for repair-intermediate or repair-root, TrackDisposition/TrackArchive, archive validation, validator deletion, repair relay/index, successor coordination, and branch-eligible Slugger journal. Work Merger invokes it once per terminal entry or journal action from `/Users/arimendelow/Projects/spoonjoy-v2`, never from identity.repoCwd. After parsing and capturing every required absolute path/dependency, release-terminal immediately `process.chdir('/Users/arimendelow/Projects/spoonjoy-v2')` before validator creation or worktree removal; the parent cwd survives feature-worktree deletion. No manual mutation is legal. It is one of the exact fourteen pre-visual measured executables and remains included when production-visual-dogfood becomes the fifteenth; Unit29.2 tests the three nonoverlapping grammars and every exact result branch.
- Normal terminal entry requires passed Unit37, passed ReleaseRun, pushed continuity, and active validation. Repaired entry requires either a failed post_merge_finding/post_merge_repair ReleaseRun with a stage-kind link or a passed ReleaseRun with a terminal-kind link/hash-valid repair_successor TerminalFailureDisposition; the passed branch never mutates the run. Either repaired branch requires the hash-valid immediate-child v2 PostMergeRepairReceipt, final child ArchiveValidationReceipt, verified child index, no final predecessor ArchiveValidationReceipt, and the disposition-frozen predecessorArchiveState. Original mergeSha/branchHeadSha own ancestry/ref/worktree cleanup while one leaf validatorMergeSha owns runtime/archive validation. ReleaseTerminalResult uses only the Round 59 exact four-branch schema, relay/state fields, and null matrix; no normal-pass fiction or older result shape is legal.
- For ReleaseTerminalResult only, the exact Desk-repo-relative Slugger path and stable track repair-index locator are the explicit exceptions to generic task-relative proof paths.
- TerminalCleanupAttempt phases are exact `prepared|origin_verified|canonical_main_ready|validator_ready|worktree_pruned|local_branch_absent|remote_branch_absent|complete`. Prepared has all booleans false, validator hashes null, and owned temp/final paths absent. origin_verified alone sets originMainContainsMerge. canonical_main_ready additionally sets canonicalMainContainsMerge. validator_ready additionally sets validatorReady, nonnull hashes, final runtime/archive present, temps absent. worktree_pruned additionally requires the hash-valid TerminalWorktreeCleanup receipt, sets nonnull worktreeCleanupSha256, requires both worktreePath/worktreeDeletePath and registration absent, and sets worktreeAbsent/registeredWorktreeAbsent/pruned true. local_branch_absent then localBranchAbsent; remote_branch_absent then remoteBranchAbsent; complete has all booleans true and unchanged files. Every later phase requires all prior invariants. Exact successful commandResults prefix lengths are prepared 0, origin_verified 2, canonical_main_ready 4, validator_ready 10, worktree_pruned 16, local_branch_absent 18, remote_branch_absent 21, and complete 21; a failure may add only the next registry result without advancing phase. After the complete attempt is pushed/read back, release-terminal creates one Git-matrix candidate whose declared paths atomically transform complete attempt present->absent and final receipt absent->present with exact `TerminalCleanup={version:1,attemptOrdinal,priorFailedAttemptPaths,priorFailedAttemptSetSha256,mergeSha,validatorMergeSha,branchHeadSha,executionHost,canonicalRepoPath,validatorRuntimePath,validatorArchivePath,validatorArchiveSha256,validatorSourceTreeSha256,worktreePath,worktreeDeletePath,worktreeCleanupSha256,branch,commandResults,originMainContainsMerge:true,canonicalMainContainsMerge:true,validatorReady:true,worktreeAbsent:true,registeredWorktreeAbsent:true,localBranchAbsent:true,remoteBranchAbsent:true,pruned:true,completedAt}` bytes, where commandResults is the exact complete 21-entry append-only attempt array. It materializes both C states, runs BINARY-sorted add/tree verification, commits, normal-pushes, fetches, and requires receipt-present/attempt-absent byte-identical readback before archive may start. Before commit, a crash may leave any per-path legal Git-matrix mixture `(O,O)|(C,O)|(C,C)` such as receipt+attempt or neither in the worktree/index; recovery rematerializes complete frozen C for both declared paths, reruns exact BINARY-sorted add, and verifies C/C/tree without treating that local partial as a committed state. Committed/fetched Desk trees and rejected-push winners alone must be exact old state or exact final state; a remote receipt+attempt, neither, or drift fails closed. A final receipt with a live attempt or before complete is invalid because no legal committed checkpoint emits that pair. Exact archive argv uses validatorMergeSha, while ancestry/ref argv use mergeSha.
- TrackArchive never owns a task-row transform. It starts from the pushed post-task-archive track bytes whose triggering row is already Landed/removed from Tasks, freezes full trackBeforeSha256, requires `remainingUnarchivedTasks:[]` under the active-root plus archived-receipt scan above, and computes trackClosedSha256 by changing only frontmatter status `active -> closed` while preserving updated and every body byte. Attempt phases are `prepared|track_closed|root_moved|archive_validated`; their exact booleans advance one named effect at a time. Competing pushes re-run the complete unarchived scan and rebuild this track-level transform; any active task directory, incomplete archived child, live terminal/archive attempt, or Tasks/Landed/body drift outside a valid unrelated concurrent row change blocks/rescans under the existing eight-race rule.
- A repair successor writes exact terminal-protocol basename `post-merge-repair.v1.json` at its task root after passed Unit37/active validation and before terminal cleanup. Its hash is frozen in the successor terminal attempt. The exact index locator remains `track:spoonjoy-v2/_repair-index/<successorKey>.json`, resolving through active track or one generation-qualified TrackArchive receipt only. After a successful provisional archive validation, release-terminal retains the Round 58 immutable provisional artifact and alone creates exact `PostMergeRepairIndexCandidate={version:1,successorKey,successorReceiptLocator,successorReceiptSha256,successorArchiveValidationAttemptPath,successorArchiveValidationAttemptSha256,indexedAt}`, `PostMergeRepairIndex={version:1,successorKey,successorReceiptLocator,successorReceiptSha256,successorArchiveValidationAttemptPath,successorArchiveValidationAttemptSha256,indexCommitSha,indexedAt,verifiedAt}`, and temporary `PostMergeRepairIndexAttempt={version:1,successorKey,successorReceiptLocator,successorReceiptSha256,successorArchiveValidationAttemptPath,successorArchiveValidationAttemptSha256,indexLocator,indexPhysicalPath,indexOldState,indexCandidateState,indexFinalState,phase,indexCommitSha,startedAt,updatedAt}`. The existing prepared/index_pushed/verified BlobState, normal-push/fetch/readback, rejected-push convergence, immutable timestamp, and attempt-removal rules remain. Any index failure appends task evidence and invalidates the provisional validation for finality. After verified index and absent attempt, release-terminal runs a fresh archive-validation ordinal; its final receipt binds repairIndexPath/repairIndexSha256. Predecessor entry validates final receipt -> final index -> retained provisional artifact and never a removed attempt or forward receipt hash. A later whole-track archive moves `_repair-index` with the track and preserves bytes. Repair-successor-normal returns only after final receipt, verified index, and attempt removal, with sluggerPath null.
- The repair-index locator remains logical `track:spoonjoy-v2/_repair-index/<successorKey>.json`. Before TrackArchive it resolves only to the active physical path. After TrackArchive it resolves only by reading the unique hash-valid TrackArchive receipt for that generation and joining its generation-qualified targetPath with `_repair-index/<successorKey>.json`; the earlier fixed unqualified archived physical path is invalid. Zero/multiple generation receipts, target collision, or a matching file outside that receipt's target rejects.
- SluggerNotification fields, canonical locator, physical resolution, BlobState transitions, phase/null matrix, process results, and SluggerCommandSpec are exactly the one-generation contract above. Initial creation is one old-byte CAS from absence; only its winning token may create generation-1 gate state, and every loser remains spawn-free. Legal progression is prepared -> recorded -> released -> observed|uncertain. Prepared recovery adopts exactly one matching same-host live waiting gate by recording its identity without spawn, no member becomes uncertain/not_spawned, and foreign/unverifiable or multiple/mismatching members block or fail closed; recorded same-host recovery may release the existing waiting gate after the released checkpoint wins; released recovery only observes/reaps and terminalizes, never spawns; foreign-host live or unverifiable identity blocks. Observed/uncertain writes are the only notification-journal mutations allowed after product/task/track finality. Ordinary-normal or repaired-root overall completion is after its one terminal notification push/readback; repair-successor-normal and repaired-intermediate cannot create one and remain incomplete until root closure. No result permits replacement, a generation number other than one, another release file, or another spawn.

**Round 49 executor identity and recovery definitions (normative replacements)**
- In every ProcessSpec/CLI/prompt/receipt template, `I` is the manifest's immutable ReleaseTaskIdentity; `RCWD=I.repoCwd`, `DR=I.deskTaskRoot`, `RB=I.branch`, `RT=I.prTitle`, `RD=I.prBody`, `RP=I.productPlanningPath`, `RG=I.productDoingPath`, and `RX=I.productContinuityPath`. The primary identity resolves those tokens to the existing Clem literals. A repair successor resolves them to its own frozen values; no current-task literal is a default or fallback.
- The manifest CLI initialization grammar is exactly `init --manifest M --identity-json J`, where J is compact canonical ReleaseTaskIdentity JSON; `--task` and `--branch` initialization flags are invalid. Generic AgentCommand prompt lines are `planning_path: <RP>` and `doing_path: <RG>`. Unit34 `pr-ensure` and its sole child use head RB, title RT, and body RD. Unit37 continuation-scan excludes RB. Every command runs from RCWD and every attempt/output path resolves below DR. Review artifact selection, continuation transfer, and release continuity repeat I.task/I.branch and the RP/RG/RX hashes.
- DeskValidatingAttempt, TerminalCleanupAttempt/receipt, DeskArchiveAttempt/receipt, TrackDisposition/TrackArchive, ArchiveValidationReceipt, ReleaseTerminalResult, and SluggerNotification take task/branch/worktree/source/archive/doing/trigger fields from I. Primary schemas require exact Clem values; successor schemas require exact successor values. Repaired intermediate/root cleanup alone uses each predecessor identity for its original ancestry/ref/worktree while validatorMergeSha comes from the immutable repair leaf. Unit29.2's full lifecycle fixture initializes primary A and repair-successor identities B/C, executes both successor contracts through real implementation gates, drives C Units32-37 through PR/merge/active validation/archive/index, then closes B intermediate and A root in reverse order; any ancestor identity byte in a descendant's cwd/prompt/PR/continuation/Desk evidence fails.
- Unit33 inserts `qa-cleanup-reconcile` immediately after `qa-deployment-before`; Unit37 keeps `production-cleanup-reconcile` immediately after `production-readiness`. Their exact registered argv are the Unit33/37 vectors above, including target/base as applicable, `--reconcile-cleanup`, canonical failed-target JSON, explicit `--release-identity-sha256`, explicit task-relative `--release-attempt-path`, and `--out`; environment is cloudflare-d1 and output policy is `cleanup-reconcile`. Exact no-extra-fields `CleanupReconcileTarget={targetEnvironment:'qa'|'production',targetBaseUrl,sourceIdentitySha256,attemptLocator,diagnosticLocator,diagnosticSha256,lineageEdges,proofChain}` requires QA with QaBaseUrl and production with ProductionBaseUrl. `lineageEdges` is the ordered exact array `{predecessorIdentitySha256,successorIdentitySha256,successorAttemptLocator,successorAttemptSha256}[]`, each receipt locator/hash naming one immediate `PostMergeSuccessorAttempt` edge with adjacent root/depth identities. `proofChain` is the ordered exact array `{kind:'diagnostic'|'reconcile_proof',locator,sha256}[]`: its first entry is the source diagnostic and every later entry is the prior reconciler proof authorizing the same environment/base/source tuple. It never doubles as successor lineage. All locators obey their exact receipt/artifact domains and relocation rules. `targetKeySha256` is lowercase SHA-256 of compact canonical JSON of the complete target in its declared field order; target directories use all 64 hex characters. Comparator is the UTF-8/BINARY comparison of the canonical target bytes, with duplicate canonical bytes rejected. Both required-name plans, evidence aggregates, timeout matrices, and tests include reconcile before broad cleanup/fresh user and cover A->B->C lineage without locator aliasing.
- Reconcile output policy is `cleanup-reconcile`. Exact `CleanupReconcileProof={version:1,target,disposition:'already_clean'|'reconciled',diagnosticLocator,diagnosticSha256,cleanOutcomeLocator,cleanOutcomeSha256,provedAt}` always names a hash-valid immutable proof for the source identity/diagnostic target. Exact aggregate `CleanupReconcile={version:1,attempts:[{target,disposition,proofPath,proofSha256}],completedAt}` repeats every BINARY-sorted target and points to its current-attempt proof. already_clean cross-links a pre-existing clean outcome; reconciled cross-links the newly created target-scoped outcome. Input `[]` creates only aggregate attempts `[]`; every nonempty target creates its declared target directory/proof and optional new outcome. Duplicate/invalid lineage, null proof, global/unrecorded target, identity/hash drift, source-attempt mutation, or extra file fails. Mandatory fixtures cover primary cleanup failure -> QA/production successor reconciliation -> broad zero -> fresh smoke and A->B->C authorization.
- The provider observation split, separate PreMergeFailureDisposition and PostMergeFailureDisposition matrices, cleanup mutation journal/reconciliation, initialization candidate/temp recovery, nonempty unreferenced ensure-reservation recovery, exact 14/15 script membership, GitHubWorkflowConclusion union, generation-qualified TrackArchive target, and SluggerCommandSpec in this Round are authoritative wherever older wording used outcome-bearing probes, "finite declared transient", count-only scripts, fixed track archive path, or an unspecified notification process.

**Round 50 recursive repair and recovery definitions (normative replacements)**
- Repair delivery is a rooted, strictly increasing-depth chain carried by ReleaseTaskIdentity. Exact v2 `PostMergeRepairReceipt={version:2,successorKey,successorTaskPath,successorIdentitySha256,repairSource,repairLeafTaskPath,repairLeafIdentitySha256,repairLeafPrNumber,repairLeafPrUrl,validatorMergeSha,predecessorTaskPath,predecessorIdentitySha256,repairRootTask,successorDepth,predecessorDepth,predecessorReleaseRun,repairBriefSha256s,downstreamRepairIndexPath,downstreamRepairIndexSha256,completedAt,successorArchiveValidationSha256:null}` is no-extra-fields. repairSource is `passed_leaf|repaired_intermediate`; depths are adjacent and identities/root/predecessor fields byte-match. A passed leaf has repairLeaf fields equal itself and null downstream fields. A repaired intermediate inherits immutable leaf fields/validatorMergeSha and requires the hash-valid immediate downstream repair index path/hash that authorized its closure. PostMergeRepairIndex binds this receipt plus the retained provisional validation artifact; the later final ArchiveValidationReceipt binds the index, preserving an acyclic receipt -> index -> provisional chain.
- After a passed repair leaf archives, provisionally validates, indexes, and freshly final-validates itself, Work Merger enters one crash-recoverable unwind loop. For child C and immediate predecessor P it invokes repaired release-terminal with C's final receipt/index. If P.repairDepth is positive, P is an intermediate: the terminal owner writes the v2 relay receipt, resolves P's frozen predecessorArchiveState, validates with the leaf validatorMergeSha, applies state-aware supersede/archive, performs provisional validation -> repair index -> fresh final validation, returns repair_intermediate, suppresses Slugger, and advances C=P. If P.repairDepth is zero, P must equal repairRootTask: it uses the same leaf SHA, state-aware supersede/archive, writes no relay/index, performs final track disposition/archive plus fresh final validation, and alone becomes Slugger-eligible after Desk-control resource cleanup. Depth must decrease by exactly one; a missing/repeated/skipped/cyclic ancestor, mixed root, changed leaf proof, or nonunique active/archive locator fails closed.
- Repaired-intermediate and repaired-root terminal protocol closed sets are exclusively the Round 60 state/checkpoint-specific sets. Every intermediate uses `post-merge-repair-relay.v1.json`, may separately retain `post-merge-repair.v1.json`, and consumes the child index and requires its own pushed/readback created index; root has no relay/created index but requires the consumed child index. SluggerNotification is forbidden whenever identity.repairDepth is positive or terminalKind is `repair_successor|repair_intermediate`; exactly one root notification may release generation 1 only after every chain task has final archive validation, every temporary repair attempt is absent, every required index resolves after track relocation, and the root released journal and release file are pushed/read back, after which the same host alone writes the hash-bound SluggerPublish wake token.
- Unit29.2's production-grammar fixture is now depth two: primary A fails, implemented successor B fails after merge, implemented successor C passes, C archives/indexes, B closes as repaired_intermediate and archives/indexes, A closes as repair_root, and exactly one Slugger process is spawned. Fault every B/C implementation phase, cleanup reconciliation authorization edge, receipt/index/archive relocation, each unwind checkpoint, and final notification boundary; recovery preserves one leaf validator SHA, closes C then B then A exactly once, and never strands an ancestor or notifies from B/C.
- Round 50 cleanup logs, failed-only diagnostic/nonce derivation, ancestry-authorized reconcile targets, exact GitHubWorkflowStatus domain, identity hash bytes, production-cleanup-reconcile deadline, derived post-merge-disposition CLI/union, successor Work Doer implementation phases, and recursive unwind definitions override every older same-identity-only, write-once phase-file, four-phase successor, one-edge repair, or non-root Slugger clause.

**Round 51 executable recovery, capability, and evidence definitions (normative replacements)**
- Health success stores the attested build value as `bodyBuildSha` and `headerBuildSha`, both exact lowercase 40-hex Git SHAs byte-equal to `HealthSeries.sourceSha`; no `bodySha`/`headerSha` field is a SHA-256 digest. A failure sample keeps both fields null. Tests reject 64-hex substitutions and body/header/source disagreement.
- Provider status domains are separate and exact. `GitHubWorkflowStatus=requested|queued|pending|waiting|in_progress|completed` and `GitHubWorkflowConclusion=action_required|cancelled|failure|neutral|skipped|stale|success|timed_out`. `GitHubJobStatus` has the same six status members and `GitHubJobConclusion` has the same eight conclusion members; neither conclusion union contains `startup_failure`. Workflow and job noncompleted statuses require null conclusion/completedAt. Job `requested|queued|pending|waiting` requires null startedAt; `in_progress` requires canonical startedAt; `completed` requires canonical completedAt, nonnull conclusion, and permits canonical/null startedAt because GitHub may terminalize an unstarted job. Unknown members and every other time/null combination reject.
- `QaDeployObservation.inventoryDisposition` is exact `delta|no_delta`. `delta` requires one nonnull normalized Deployment selected as the unique maximum `(createdAt,id)` under canonical-timestamp then UTF-8/BINARY-id order from after-minus-before; it is an inventory observation and makes no causality claim. `no_delta` requires `deployment:null` and exact target health. Provider failure or incomplete inventory is not an observation and remains `indeterminate`. `CheckSet.checks` and `MergeReadiness.checks` sort by `(name,url.provider,url.url,headSha,conclusion)` using UTF-8/BINARY comparison; names are unique and any duplicate, including byte-identical duplicates, rejects before canonical serialization.
- Every durable URL is parsed and canonical-round-tripped before serialization: scheme is exactly `https`, username/password/query/fragment/explicit port are absent, host is lowercase ASCII, percent escapes are uppercase and decode to no slash or dot segment, and path has no empty, `.` or `..` segment. `PrUrl` is exactly `https://github.com/spoonjoy/spoonjoy-v2/pull/<prNumber>`; `GitHubRunUrl` is exactly `https://github.com/spoonjoy/spoonjoy-v2/actions/runs/<runId>` with optional exact `/attempts/<runAttempt>`; `GitHubJobUrl` is exactly `https://github.com/spoonjoy/spoonjoy-v2/actions/runs/<runId>/job/<jobId>`; `GitHubApiRunUrl` is exactly `https://api.github.com/repos/spoonjoy/spoonjoy-v2/actions/runs/<runId>`; `GitHubCheckRunApiUrl` is exactly `https://api.github.com/repos/spoonjoy/spoonjoy-v2/check-runs/<checkRunId>`; `CloudflareApiUrl` is the exact target-bound union `{environment:'qa',url:'https://api.cloudflare.com/client/v4/accounts/<32-lower-hex>/workers/scripts/spoonjoy-v2-qa/deployments'}|{environment:'production',url:'https://api.cloudflare.com/client/v4/accounts/<32-lower-hex>/workers/scripts/spoonjoy-v2/deployments'}`; every capture-deployments request/result carries the same environment and rejects the other script name; `ProductionBaseUrl` is exactly `https://spoonjoy.app`; and `QaBaseUrl` is exactly `https://spoonjoy-v2-qa.mendelow-studio.workers.dev`, with every bracketed id a positive safe integer except the account hex. Exact no-extra-fields `CheckUrl` is `{provider:'github_actions',url:GitHubJobUrl,runId,jobId}|{provider:'github_checks_api',url:GitHubCheckRunApiUrl,checkRunId}`. A github_actions Check binds URL runId/jobId to the union fields and its discovered workflow/job; a github_checks_api Check binds the URL id to checkRunId. `Check={name,url:CheckUrl,conclusion:'success',headSha}` accepts no raw string URL. CiWorkflow and Workflow accept GitHubRunUrl only, with URL runId equal databaseId and optional attempt equal runAttempt; DeployJob accepts GitHubJobUrl only, with URL runId/jobId byte-equal its runId/id; API discovery fields accept only GitHubApiRunUrl with matching databaseId. Health/base fields accept only the named QA or production origin. Raw lifecycle/visual transport URLs, redirect locations, provider text, unbound ids, provider/type mismatch, or any other URL-like string are sanitized and forbidden in durable bytes. CheckSet and MergeReadiness sort checks by `(name,url.provider,url.url,headSha,conclusion)` under UTF-8/BINARY order and reject any repeated name or repeated provider/id identity. Checked ingredient/output ids are duplicate-free subsets emitted in pinned step/ingredient and step/output-use traversal order, never independently sorted. Unit29.2 red/green tests cover every accepted URL variant plus wrong host/repo/path/provider/id/attempt, job-vs-run confusion, duplicate check identity, canonicalization drift, and extra fields.
- Cloudflare REST uses exact import-safe `resolveCloudflareRestBearer(deps)`. It runs `['pnpm','exec','wrangler','auth','token','--json']` from identity.repoCwd under only the `cloudflare-rest` public environment policy (`PATH`, `HOME`, `CI=1`, `NO_COLOR=1`, `FORCE_COLOR=0`, optional resolved `TMPDIR`, and exact account id), with a 10000ms total timeout, process-group TERM/5000ms/KILL/reap, clean UTF-8, no stderr/warnings, exit zero, and at most 4096 stdout bytes. It accepts exact no-extra-fields JSON `{type:'oauth',token:<nonempty UTF-8 string of at most 4096 bytes>}`. The executor creates a one-shot anonymous pipe, writes exactly the bearer bytes, closes its write end, and passes only the read descriptor plus nonsecret decimal `SPOONJOY_RELEASE_SECRET_FD` to the gate; the bearer is absent from gate argv/environment. Before child spawn the gate reads at most 4096 bytes to EOF into transient memory, closes the descriptor, deletes the marker, creates the registered child environment with `CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN`, and spawns the target with neither pipe end nor marker inherited. Only resolver/executor/gate transient memory and the registered child environment may contain the bearer; no file, hash, manifest, log, exception, command JSON, gate environment, or non-target child may contain it. Short/extra/non-UTF-8 pipe data, inherited descriptor, malformed output, timeout, signal, warning, `api_token|api_key`, or absent OAuth maps to sanitized `credential_missing|platform_capability_missing` before provider mutation. Unit29.1/29.2 source, descriptor-liveness, child-environment, crash, and byte-sentinel tests prove isolation and non-persistence.
- Side-effect-free preflight means no provider/product mutation, Git/Desk mutation, manifest/command/wait/disposition mutation, or billing/edit claim; it may execute only the finite read-only credential/account/inventory probes below. Exact no-extra-fields `ProcessPreflightPublic={version:1,logicalName,environmentPolicy,path,home,tmpdir,envNames,accountId,executionHost,capabilities,checkedAt}` carries canonical PATH/HOME/nullable TMPDIR, BINARY-sorted unique exact environment names, nullable exact Cloudflare account, and `CapabilityEntry={name,required:true,status:'available'|'blocked',proof,probe}`. Capability names and order are finite `github_auth|github_actions_read|cloudflare_account_access|cloudflare_oauth|cloudflare_d1_visibility`; membership is `[]` for base/local-db, `[github_auth,github_actions_read]` for github, `[cloudflare_account_access]` for cloudflare, `[cloudflare_account_access,cloudflare_oauth]` for cloudflare-rest, `[cloudflare_d1_visibility]` for cloudflare-d1, and `[github_auth,github_actions_read,cloudflare_account_access]` for cloudflare-github. Probe names/argv are exact: `gh_auth_status=["gh","auth","status","--hostname","github.com"]`; `gh_actions_read=["gh","api","--method","GET","repos/spoonjoy/spoonjoy-v2/actions/workflows?per_page=1"]`; `wrangler_whoami=["pnpm","exec","wrangler","whoami"]`; `wrangler_oauth_token=["pnpm","exec","wrangler","auth","token","--json"]` through the one-shot secret resolver; and `wrangler_d1_list=["pnpm","exec","wrangler","d1","list","--json"]`. Exact import-safe `resolveCloudflareD1Token(deps)` has one production secret source: it spawns `['/usr/bin/security','find-generic-password','-a','arimendelow','-s','spoonjoy-cloudflare-d1-api-token','-w']` with stdin closed, cwd `/Users/arimendelow/Projects/spoonjoy-v2`, exact environment `HOME=/Users/arimendelow`, `USER=arimendelow`, `LOGNAME=arimendelow`, `LANG=C`, `LC_ALL=C`, and every other key unset, 10000ms TERM/5000ms/KILL/reap, stderr empty, and stdout cap 4097 bytes. Exit zero must yield exactly one NUL-free valid UTF-8 token of 1..4096 bytes followed by one LF, with no other LF; the resolver removes only that LF in memory. Nonzero/missing/malformed/timeout/signal maps sanitized credential_missing/platform_capability_missing with raw streams discarded. Tests inject this exact secret-source adapter, but production cannot read a token from process environment, argv, file, caller JSON, or another command. It obtains the resulting raw token only in resolver memory and `runCloudflareD1VisibilityProbe` transports it to only this probe child through the same one-shot anonymous descriptor bootstrap: the parent writes exact token bytes, closes the write end, the bootstrap reads at most 4096 bytes to EOF, closes/unsets the descriptor marker, injects `CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN` only into `wrangler_d1_list`, and spawns with neither descriptor inherited. This side-effect-free probe creates no manifest, lock, attempt, gate file, hash, or provider mutation; token/argv/env/raw output never enter durable bytes, and only the sanitized accountId/databaseId proof survives. Missing, short, extra, non-UTF-8, leaked-descriptor, malformed-list, or nonmatching database state maps to the finite blocked probe code. Available requires a successful matching probe, null `probe`, and one sanitized no-extra-fields proof: `{kind:'github_auth',host:'github.com',authenticated:true}`; `{kind:'github_actions_read',repo:'spoonjoy/spoonjoy-v2',readable:true}`; `{kind:'cloudflare_account_access',accountId,visible:true}`; `{kind:'cloudflare_oauth',accountId,tokenType:'oauth'}` with no token/hash; or `{kind:'cloudflare_d1_visibility',accountId,databaseId,visible:true}` for the exact configured database. Blocked requires null proof and exact `{probeName,code}`; authentication/token absence maps `credential_missing`, and inaccessible repo/account/database or malformed/failed read maps `platform_capability_missing`. Probe processes use their declared public environment, total timeout/stream sanitizer, no shell, and persist only the typed proof/probe, never raw output. Preflight never asserts billing state, D1 edit, Workers Scripts edit, deployment ability, or any permission not returned by these probes. `billing_required` and edit/platform failures are process-positive signals only from the actual registered mutation child; a successful D1/deploy mutation plus its exact provider/product post-state is the sole authority that the needed effect was permitted. Exact `PostMergeCapabilityEvidence` is a discriminated payload union over shared `{version:1,releaseRun,unit,stageRun,logicalName,commandMode,attempt,terminalCode,payload,createdAt}`: preflight has null attempt and `{kind:'preflight',preflight:ProcessPreflightPublic}`; process has positive attempt and `{kind:'process',signal:{version:1,capabilityName,probeName,terminalCode,observedAt}}`; agent has positive attempt and `{kind:'agent',signal:{version:1,agentCommandPath,agentCommandSha256,retryOrdinal,deadlineStartedAt,deadlineAt,terminalCode:'agent_runtime_unavailable',observedAt}}`. Process capabilityName/probeName belongs to the finite registered mutation adapter and its sanitized terminal-code map; a caller-supplied artifact, free-text signal, undeclared probe, or synthetic available proof is invalid. Every later cloudflare-d1 ProcessCommand repeats this descriptor bootstrap with a new pipe: its gate argv/environment contain only the nonsecret decimal marker, the gate reads at most 4096 bytes to EOF, closes the descriptor, unsets the marker, injects CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN only into the one registered D1 child, and spawns it with neither descriptor end nor marker inherited. The raw token never enters a gate environment, argv, file, hash, log, exception, manifest, or non-D1 child.
- The exact Unit37 post-merge derived command is `record-post-merge-disposition --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt none|A`; the obsolete `--capability-artifact` pair rejects. Its retry history tuple is `(ReleaseRun.run,owningUnit,logicalName,terminalCode)`, and historyKeySha256 is lowercase SHA-256 of UTF-8 exact compact JSON with no final LF and field order `{"releaseRun":R,"owningUnit":U,"logicalName":L,"terminalCode":C}`. `retryOrdinal` is one plus the count of prior pushed transient dispositions with that exact key; byte-idempotent replay returns the existing ordinal and never increments it. The first two provider/network dispositions remain transient_retry; the third and later are external_wait, not repair successors. cleanup_incomplete remains retryable twice and then repair_successor with repairCode cleanup because pre-final implementation may be defective.
- Failed StageRuns, dispositions, and capability artifacts are immutable. Durable wait state is task-root manifest-owned evidence outside terminal stage directories. Exact `ExternalWaitCheckpoint={version:1,releaseRun,owningUnit:32|33|34|35|36|37,sourceStageRun,logicalName,terminalCode,historyKeySha256,waitOrdinal,sourceDispositionPath,sourceDispositionSha256,triggerMode:'provider'|'agent_runtime',runtimeEpoch,scheduleSeconds,retryAfterSeconds,delaySeconds,notBefore,createdAt}` lives at `artifacts/external-waits/<historyKeySha256>/wait-<waitOrdinal>.v1.json`; runtimeEpoch is null for provider and positive for agent_runtime. waitOrdinal is one plus prior pushed checkpoints for the key, independent of disposition retryOrdinal. `scheduleSeconds=[60,120,300,600,900][min(waitOrdinal-1,4)]`; Retry-After is null or integer 1..86400; `delaySeconds=min(86400,max(scheduleSeconds,retryAfterSeconds??0))`; notBefore is exact createdAt plus delay. Checkpoints have no resolution fields. Exact `ExternalWaitResolution={version:1,triggerMode,checkpointPath,checkpointSha256,resolutionEvidencePath,resolutionEvidenceSha256,runtimeEpoch,nextRuntimeEpoch,resolvedAt}` lives at sibling `resolution-<waitOrdinal>.v1.json`: provider has both epoch fields null; agent_runtime has positive runtimeEpoch and nextRuntimeEpoch=runtimeEpoch+1. At/after notBefore, triggerMode provider alone uses `resume-external-wait` and typed read-only provider preflight; unavailable appends the next provider checkpoint, while available writes fresh capability evidence plus resolution and permits one fresh same-SHA StageRun. triggerMode agent_runtime rejects resume-external-wait and uses only the completed AgentRuntimeProbe path below; unavailable appends the next same-epoch checkpoint, while available writes the epoch-advancing resolution and permits the fresh StageRun. No current or prior wait/disposition is mutated, and any number of waits never becomes repair evidence.
- A human blocker remains only for credential, billing, or platform capability and uses the preflight-null-attempt or process-positive-attempt branch above. Exact resolve-pre/post-merge-blocker reruns a read-only probe only for a preflight blocker; still blocked returns `{status:'blocked',dispositionPath,dispositionSha256}` with zero mutation, while success writes the Round 58 read_only_probe evidence and exact immutable resolution. A process-positive edit/billing blocker rejects that command and can resume only through the exact authorize-pre/post-merge-blocker human authorization command. The resolution never claims capability success and permits one fresh same-SHA StageRun/attempt; only the actual mutation and post-state can prove success. PreMergeBlockerResolution lives at the Round 58 unit-qualified path; exact `PostMergeBlockerResolution={version:1,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,blockedCapabilityEvidencePath,blockedCapabilityEvidenceSha256,resolutionEvidencePath,resolutionEvidenceSha256,resolvedAt}` lives at `artifacts/post-merge-blocker-resolutions/<dispositionSha256>.v1.json`. Every resolution is idempotent by disposition hash, blocked/resolution evidence paths are distinct/hash-valid, and mixed probe/authorization null matrices reject.
- `AgentCommand` carries canonical deadlineStartedAt/deadlineAt, positive runtimeEpoch, and positive retryOrdinal; deadlineAt is exactly deadlineStartedAt+1800000ms. The owner closes a timed-out agent, persists stalled, and permits at most two fresh attempts for `(releaseRun,unit,logicalName,runtimeEpoch)`; interrupted/idempotent recovery does not increment. Two exhausted attempts create the agent_runtime wait above. Agent-runtime resolution is a Work Merger-owned journaled probe, never a caller boolean. `start-agent-runtime-probe --manifest M --writer-id W --wait-path P` writes the Round 58 running attempt schema, returns the unchanged prompt/deadline, and Work Merger dispatches one fresh context-independent agent. `finish-agent-runtime-probe --manifest M --writer-id W --wait-path P --probe-ordinal N --agent-id D --report-json J` accepts only canonical `{version:1,promptSha256,verdict:'available'|'unavailable',checkedAt}`, atomically replaces the attempt with the immutable completed probe, and derives the outcome. Available writes agent capability evidence plus epoch-advancing ExternalWaitResolution and resumes the same owning unit in one fresh same-SHA StageRun; unavailable appends the next same-epoch wait. Expiry records a completed unavailable probe. Crash recovery validates journal/report/tool identity and never invents available, silently reinvokes, rewrites a completed probe, or leaves an expired probe running.
- Automatic production run identity includes both CI database id and attempt. `.github/workflows/production-deploy.yml` run-name is exact `ci-run-${{ github.event.workflow_run.id }}-attempt-${{ github.event.workflow_run.run_attempt }}`. Workflow discovery argv appends `--triggering-ci-run-attempt <CiWorkflow.runAttempt>` after the database-id pair. `Workflow` and `ProductionRelease` add `triggeringCiRunAttempt`, equal the selected CI runAttempt; discovery, selected run, deploy job, promoted artifact, and evidence cross-check both values. A rerun with the same database id but another attempt is a distinct candidate and cannot satisfy the prior edge.
- D1 cleanup recovery has one explicit digest exception: `credentialKeySha256` is lowercase SHA-256 of the raw preflight-validated D1 token and may exist transiently only in a prepared cleanup-recovery journal, a failed cleanup diagnostic, or reconcile preflight/proof for credential-version equality; it is removed from the retained successful cleanup closed set. No other secret is hashed or persisted. The nonce reveals neither credential. Email is `codex-smoke-<first32 lowercase hex HMAC-SHA-256(token,'spoonjoy-smoke-email-v1\0'+nonce)>@example.com`; password is `Sj1!` plus unpadded base64url HMAC-SHA-256(token,`spoonjoy-smoke-password-v1\0${nonce}`). The distinct domains, exact UTF-8 bytes, casing, and truncation are frozen. Recovery derives both in memory, verifies emailSha256/credentialKeySha256, and never persists raw values.
- Cleanup irreversible targets are operation-discriminated. `DeleteRetiredTarget={recipeId,attemptId,status:'COMPLETED'|'ABANDONED'}` sorts `(recipeId,attemptId,status)` BINARY; `DeleteUserTarget={userId}` is the sole user target. `DeleteRetiredPreStateRow={userId,recipeId,attemptId,status,updatedAt}` and `DeleteUserPreStateRow={userId}` use those exact field orders, compact `JSON.stringify` bytes, no final LF, and the same target comparator; credential, email, OAuth, profile, recipe content, and other columns are forbidden. `preStateSha256` hashes the exact sorted row array. `operationKeySha256` hashes compact canonical `{operation,identitySha256,targets,preStateSha256}` in that field order. Operation/target/pre-state disagreement, duplicates, alternate order, or excluded columns reject before dispatch.
- Cleanup log candidates are recoverable without inventing effects. No irreversible call may dispatch until the complete main log extension is renamed, parent-fsynced, byte-read, and hash-validated. When an intact prior main exists, a same-token candidate, including a partial candidate, is removed and the extension is rebuilt because that candidate cannot have authorized dispatch; foreign/multiple/wrong-token state fails closed. If fact proofs show an already-dispatched operation after a crash, recovery reconstructs the deterministic terminal extension from the immutable journal and fact proofs, never from candidate bytes. A diagnostic candidate with no main is removed because signup cannot precede prepared-main readback; beside a valid main it is removed and recovery resumes that main. Unknown ownership or main corruption still fails closed.
- QA and production both reconcile stranded cleanup before any broad cleanup or fresh user. Unit33 exact order is `qa-deployment-before`, `qa-cleanup-reconcile`, `qa-cleanup-apply-before`, `qa-cleanup-assert-before`, then its existing preflight/deploy/health/smoke/final-cleanup names. Unit37 retains reconcile immediately after readiness. Each lifecycle and visual smoke ProcessSpec, and each reconcile ProcessSpec, passes nonsecret exact operands `--release-identity-sha256 <identitySha256>` and `--release-attempt-path <task-relative command-attempt path>` before `--out`; the child never infers identity/path from out. QA reconcile argv also includes `--target-env qa --base-url QB`; production includes `--target-env production`. Unit29.2/30/31 test every operand and identity mismatch.
- Reconcile output policy is exact `cleanup-reconcile`, not one-file `json`. Fresh passed output contains root `cleanup-reconcile.json` plus one `target-<64-lower-hex targetKeySha256>/` per canonical target. `already_clean` target closed set is exactly `cleanup-reconcile-proof.json`. `reconciled` target closed set is exactly seven files: `cleanup-reconcile-proof.json`, `cleanup-reconcile-phase.json`, `cleanup-reconcile-pre-delete-rows.json`, `cleanup-reconcile-user-delete.json`, `cleanup-reconcile-post-delete-rows.json`, `cleanup-reconcile-retained-do-allowlist.json`, and `cleanup-reconcile-outcome.json`. Every file has its exact no-extra-fields schema and cross-hashes the same target key, environment/base, source identity, attempt locator, diagnostic locator/hash, lineage edges, proof chain, operation journal, and immediately prior phase/fact. A failed command has no aggregate; it retains each prior complete target directory unchanged and, for the current target only, exact `cleanup-reconcile-journal.json`, a contiguous prefix of the six non-proof phase/fact/outcome files authorized by journal.phase, and `cleanup-reconcile-failure.json` hashing every retained file. Missing prefix members, later-phase files, proof on failure, partial bytes, extra target/file, or mutation of a complete predecessor directory fails closed.
- Exact `CleanupReconcileProof={version:1,targetKeySha256,target,disposition:'already_clean'|'reconciled',diagnosticLocator,diagnosticSha256,sourceCleanOutcomeLocator,sourceCleanOutcomeSha256,reconcileOutcomePath,reconcileOutcomeSha256,provedAt}` has already_clean with nonnull source outcome and null reconcile outcome, while reconciled has the reverse; all locators/hashes are verified and no other null matrix is legal. Exact aggregate `CleanupReconcile={version:1,attempts:[{targetKeySha256,target,disposition,proofPath,proofSha256}],completedAt}` sorts by canonical target bytes, requires unique full hashes, and points to every current-attempt proof. Input `[]` writes only aggregate `attempts:[]`. `CleanupReconcileFailure={version:1,targetKeySha256,target,journalPath,journalSha256,retainedPaths,retainedSetSha256,terminalCode,failedAt}` is current-identity evidence and never mutates the source diagnostic or a completed target. `retainedPaths` is the BINARY-path-sorted unique array of every complete retained regular file in the failed current-target directory except `cleanup-reconcile-failure.json`; that receipt is required alongside the listed set but excluded to avoid self-reference. `retainedSetSha256` is lowercase SHA-256 of compact canonical JSON with no final LF for the BINARY-path-sorted unique array `[{path,sha256}]`, where each path byte-equals retainedPaths and each hash covers the complete referenced bytes. Duplicate paths, alternate order, omitted/extra listed files, a listed/unlisted directory member other than the failure receipt, partial bytes, self-inclusion, wrong digest, or noncanonical JSON rejects. Tests cover empty, already-clean, fully reconciled, every contiguous crash prefix, every retained-set mutation/order/duplicate, A->B->C lineage/proof separation, cross-environment/base rejection, full-hash collision resistance, canonical comparator equality, and active/task/archive/TrackArchive relocation.
- The six reconciled phase/fact/outcome artifacts and their temporary journal are fully typed. `CleanupReconcileJournal={version:1,targetKeySha256,target,diagnosticLocator,diagnosticSha256,lineageEdges,proofChain,phase,operationKeySha256,preparedAt,updatedAt}` has phase `prepared|phase_recorded|pre_delete_recorded|user_delete_recorded|post_delete_recorded|retained_recorded|outcome_recorded`; immutable identity/diagnostic/lineage/proof/operation/prepared fields never change and updatedAt strictly increases. `CleanupReconcilePhase={version:1,targetKeySha256,target,targetEnvironment,targetBaseUrl,sourceIdentitySha256,attemptLocator,diagnosticLocator,diagnosticSha256,phase:'recovery',startedAt,endedAt,status:'passed',failureCode:null,calls,purgeCompletions,mutationJournals,priorPhaseSha256}`; `CleanupReconcilePreDeleteRows={version:1,targetKeySha256,target,at,priorArtifactPath,priorArtifactSha256,userRows:1,cookSessionIndexRows:0,sourceOutcomeLocator,sourceOutcomeSha256}`; `CleanupReconcileUserDelete={version:1,targetKeySha256,target,at,priorArtifactPath,priorArtifactSha256,mutationJournalIndex,mutationJournalSha256,disposition:'deleted'|'reconciled',deletedUserRows}` where mutationJournalIndex selects exactly one immutable no-extra-fields CleanupMutationJournal member of the phase artifact, mutationJournalSha256 hashes that complete canonical member, deleted means one affected row, and reconciled means zero only after an exact absence proof; `CleanupReconcilePostDeleteRows={version:1,targetKeySha256,target,at,priorArtifactPath,priorArtifactSha256,userRows:0,productRowCounts}`; `CleanupReconcileRetainedDoAllowlist={version:1,targetKeySha256,target,at,priorArtifactPath,priorArtifactSha256,residues}`; and `CleanupReconcileOutcome={version:1,targetKeySha256,target,phasePath,phaseSha256,preDeleteRowsPath,preDeleteRowsSha256,userDeletePath,userDeleteSha256,postDeleteRowsPath,postDeleteRowsSha256,retainedDoAllowlistPath,retainedDoAllowlistSha256,relationalProductRowsZero:true,contentBearingDoStateZero:true,identifierBearingDoMetadataRetained,completedAt}`. `calls`, `purgeCompletions`, `productRowCounts`, and `residues` reuse the exact no-extra-fields Cleanup phase types and canonical comparators; identifierBearingDoMetadataRetained equals whether residues is nonempty. The pre-delete prior link names the phase artifact; user-delete names pre-delete; post-delete names user-delete; retained names post-delete. Outcome cross-hashes all five predecessors, CleanupReconcileProof cross-hashes outcome, and the aggregate cross-hashes the proof; no mutable outer CleanupReconcileJournal hash is used as irreversible-call authority. Every object uses the displayed field order, compact canonical JSON, no final LF, canonical times, normalized target-relative paths, exact target/environment/base/source identity, and verified locator/hash/lineage/proof equality. While running, the journal plus artifact set must be the exact contiguous phase prefix: prepared has none; each named `_recorded` phase adds exactly its corresponding file in the order phase, pre-delete, user-delete, post-delete, retained, outcome. After outcome_recorded, one atomic checkpoint creates the hash-valid CleanupReconcileProof and removes the journal, yielding the exact seven-file passed set. A failed checkpoint retains the journal, only its phase-authorized prefix, and the failure receipt; skipped/duplicate/later/missing files, altered prefix bytes, nullability drift, or a proof beside a journal rejects. Tests fault before/after every candidate write, rename, irreversible call, fact write, phase advance, proof creation, and journal deletion.
- Terminal-code derivation gives a validated unresolved cleanup diagnostic precedence over generic process timeout, signal, exit, warning, or output codes, producing `cleanup_incomplete`. The cloudflare-d1 credential-key comparison and every specialized reconcile credential/lineage check occur in executor preflight before start-command, so mismatch produces commandMode preflight, attempt null, and zero manifest/attempt/provider/product mutation.
- Repair successor orchestration is executable through measured release-terminal successor mode. Strict action domain is `prepare|create-task|start-planning|finish-planning|wait-runtime|resume-runtime|record-runtime-probe|record-handoff|start-implementation|finish-implementation|recover`. `prepare` alone requires ordered `--predecessor-manifest M --release-run R --stage-run G --disposition-kind stage|terminal --disposition P`; every later action rejects those flags and resolves authority only from J. Action-specific required flags are: finish-planning `--attempt N --agent-id D --artifacts-json A`; wait-runtime `--kind planner|doer --suite-attempt N`; resume-runtime `--kind planner|doer --wait-ordinal N`; record-runtime-probe `--kind planner|doer --wait-ordinal N --agent-id D --report-json J`; record-handoff `--handoff-json H`; finish-implementation `--attempt N --agent-id D --artifacts-json A --implementation-evidence P`; other actions accept no extra flags. Exact no-extra-fields result union shares `{mode:'successor',action,journalPath,journalSha256,phase}` and adds: prepare nothing; create-task `{taskPath,identityPath,identitySha256}`; start-planning/start-implementation `{skill:'work-planner'|'work-doer',cwd,prompt,planningPath,doingPath,attempt,deadlineStartedAt,deadlineAt}`; finish-planning `{planningPath,planningSha256,doingPath,doingSha256}`; wait-runtime `{status:'waiting',waitPath,waitSha256,waitOrdinal,notBefore}`; resume-runtime `{status:'probe_required',prompt,promptSha256,probeOrdinal,deadlineStartedAt,deadlineAt}`; record-runtime-probe is either waiting with the next wait tuple or `{status:'resolved',resolutionPath,resolutionSha256}`; record-handoff `{handoffPath,handoffSha256}`; finish-implementation `{implementationEvidencePath,implementationEvidenceSha256}`; recover `{status:'stable'|'action_required',nextAction}`. Work Merger invokes only the returned skill/cwd/prompt payload, passes no inherited context, waits to the returned deadline, and records the exact agent/artifact result. Every action checkpoints before invocation and validates outputs before phase advance; all results reject extras and every journal mutation uses the Desk Git matrix/push/readback.
- SuccessorSuiteAttempt uses only the Round 59 skill/cwd/prompt/document-bound exact schema and null matrix. Every ordinal has a 1800000ms deadline; completed artifacts remain a BINARY-sorted unique compact-canonical path/hash set, recovery validates existing docs/receipts, completes a provable result, interrupts one expired attempt, or resumes a journal wait, and no recovery may invoke silently, fabricate availability, rewrite a registered artifact, or skip a phase.
- The successor doing doc contains implementation-only red/green/verification/reviewer units for the RepairBrief set and explicitly excludes Units32-37. Exact task-relative manifest PreReleaseArtifact `artifacts/post-merge-successor/post-merge-implementation.v1.json` is `PostMergeImplementationEvidence={version:1,successorKey,successorIdentitySha256,planningPath,planningSha256,doingPath,doingSha256,implementationBaseSha,implementationHeadSha,implementationTreeSha,unitReceiptPaths,unitReceiptSetSha256,reviewReportPaths,reviewReportSetSha256,verificationArtifactPaths,verificationArtifactSetSha256,coverageSummaryPath,coverageSummarySha256,warnings,completedAt}`. Exact `CoverageSummary={version:1,commands,total,changed,artifacts,warningCount,createdAt}` has nonempty `commands:{argv,exitCode:0,stdoutSha256,stderrSha256,warningCount:0}[]`; exact `CoverageMetricSet={statements:{covered,total,pct:100},branches:{covered,total,pct:100},functions:{covered,total,pct:100},lines:{covered,total,pct:100}}` requires every total positive and covered equal total; `total` is CoverageMetricSet.
