Exact `ChangedCoverage` is `{kind:'measured',changedExecutablePaths,changedExecutableSetSha256,statements,branches,functions,lines}` or `{kind:'not_applicable',changedExecutablePaths:[],changedExecutableSetSha256,reason:'no_changed_executable_lines'}`. Measured requires a nonempty BINARY-sorted unique path array, its set hash, and the four positive 100% metric members from CoverageMetricSet. Not_applicable requires `changedExecutableSetSha256` equal lowercase SHA-256 of exact bytes `[]` and is legal only when the independently derived CoverageScope.changedExecutablePaths is empty; the diff, independent production executable registry, instrumented registry, intersection, and hashes are retained in the exact seven machine-readable coverage artifacts. Docs/tests/fixtures/generated outputs and `**/*.d.ts` are excluded only by the exact independent path classifier, while executable root configuration such as `vite.config.ts` remains production executable source and must be instrumented when changed. `coverageSummaryPath` is exact task-relative `artifacts/post-merge-successor/coverage/coverage-summary.json`; `artifacts:{path,sha256}[]` is the execution-contract-exact seven-entry subordinate set and hashes each complete machine-readable file; commands/total/changed equal their corresponding artifact payloads. Arrays in implementation evidence are BINARY-sorted unique task-relative paths; every set hash covers compact canonical `{path,sha256}[]`; all implementation-only units are complete; total is 100%; changed is measured 100% or hash-proven not_applicable; warnings and every command warningCount are zero; branch/head/tree are clean, pushed, and exact. finish-implementation appends every closed successor evidence path to the manifest, then writes/pushes/readbacks this receipt at the exact artifact path before implementation_complete. Only then may universal Units32-37 run once for the successor.
- Recursive terminal validation always uses the immutable repair leaf's `validatorMergeSha`; no active clause uses `successorMergeSha` as an independently inferred value. Ordinary, repair-successor, repair-intermediate, and repair-root are the four exact ReleaseTerminalResult fixtures/branches. Every identity-specific adopted iteration, mirror, Landed slug/path, task source/archive path, and repair locator derives from ReleaseTaskIdentity: iteration root is dirname(identity.deskDoingPath), mirrors use the four fixed basenames there, archive relocation replaces identity.taskSourcePath with identity.taskArchivePath, and the Landed row uses identity.task plus the exact TaskDocumentLocator derived from identity.deskDoingPath. A whole-track archived task resolves only as `<TrackArchive.targetPath>/_archive/<slug>` and a repair index only as `<TrackArchive.targetPath>/_repair-index/<key>.json`; fixed `_archive/spoonjoy-v2` paths are invalid.
- Slugger uses only the exact single `SluggerNotification`, embedded `SluggerSpawnGeneration`, and immutable `SluggerProcessResult` schemas above because `ouro msg` exposes no idempotency key. Prepared gate bytes are remote before the one gate starts; recorded PID/PGID/start identity is remote before release; released journal plus release bytes are remote before the already-recorded gate may spawn the child; result bytes and same-host dead/reaped proof precede observed/uncertain. Prepared-with-no-member and synchronous spawn error terminalize that generation explicitly; same-host recovery may release the existing recorded waiting gate, while released recovery never spawns and foreign-host recovery blocks. This proves one ownership generation and at most one live gate/child without claiming Slugger-side deduplication.
- These Round 51 clauses replace every older `startup_failure`, same workflow/job conclusion, raw lifecycle URL ban, sorted checked-id, caller-supplied capability artifact, exhausted-transient repair, six/four-phase successor, `not_needed`/null proof, one-file reconcile, fixed primary Desk/archive path, `successorMergeSha`, three-branch result, indefinitely running agent, direct OAuth-less Cloudflare REST, and Slugger spawn clause.

- Round 52 terminal/archive closure is exact. `TrackArchiveAttempt` basename is `track-archive.attempt.v1.json` at the active track root; final no-extra-fields `TrackArchive` basename is `track-archive.v1.json`, stable locator `track:spoonjoy-v2/track-archive.v1.json`, and sole physical path `<targetPath>/track-archive.v1.json`. It repeats the frozen generation/trigger/kind/hash/source/target/tree fields, has every terminal boolean true, and hash-equals TrackDisposition.trackArchiveSha256. Final task-root resolution is derived from ReleaseTaskIdentity plus hash-valid DeskArchive or PredecessorSupersede and TrackDisposition: kept_active is `spoonjoy-v2/_archive/<slug>`, archived is `<TrackArchive.targetPath>/_archive/<slug>`. `archive-validation.v1.json` is written only at that already-relocated final root; validation never recreates identity.deskTaskRoot. Track receipt, task receipt, manifest, and validator paths resolve through their registered locator domains and one generation only.
- Terminal closed sets and tests use only the Round 60 stage/state/checkpoint table. Ordinary-normal and repair-successor-normal retain their declared members; every repaired intermediate owns a relay and created index, consumes a child index, and conditionally retains leaf/DeskArchive; root consumes a child index and creates no relay/index. Mutable attempts/candidates exist only in their owning phase and are absent at final validation.
- Round 52 recovery closure is exact. A failed StageRun and every stage-owned disposition/evidence object are permanent bytes; only task-root wait checkpoints, wait resolutions, blocker resolutions, successor-runtime waits, and runtime-probe journals may be appended afterward. Each command result is the exact no-extra-fields union above. Work Merger dispatches every agent probe itself from returned skill/cwd/prompt/deadline bytes, records the returned agent id/report, and never passes a synthetic availability value. Every provider and agent wait can append another checkpoint forever under the capped schedule; a successful receipt restarts the same owning unit, never a hardcoded Unit37. Fault tests cover every write/fsync/rename/manifest/commit/push/readback boundary and all-null/all-nonnull matrices.
- Round 52 process/evidence closure is exact. Seven policies are registered; every deployment capture uses cloudflare-rest; the OAuth bearer crosses the gate only through the consumed one-shot descriptor; ProcessPreflightPublic includes the full public environment and finite proof/probe matrix; capability evidence uses the preflight/process/agent payload union; blocked and resolved capability artifacts are distinct immutable bytes; URL types and deployment source are finite; QA inventory selection is deterministic but noncausal. Unit29.2 rejects every extra field, wrong environment membership, D1 account/database/permission mismatch, unconsumed descriptor, secret sentinel, malformed URL, and capability-code mismatch.
- Round 52 cleanup closure is exact. CleanupRecoveryIdentity, diagnostics, targets, proofs, and facts bind targetEnvironment plus targetBaseUrl. Successor lineage receipt edges and diagnostic/reconcile proofChain are separate typed arrays. Full canonical target bytes define order and the 64-hex target key. Passed already_clean/reconciled and failed-prefix closed sets are those above; successful cleanup removes credentialKeySha256-bearing journal state. Tests cover current identity, A->B->C, active/task archive/whole-track relocation, cross-environment/base/identity attempts, collisions, response loss, every partial write, and zero fresh-user creation before all target proofs plus broad assert-clean.
- Round 52 successor/notification closure is retained only through the Round 58 replacements below. Successor mode keeps its action/result discipline, append-only suite artifact hashes, exact Work Planner/Work Doer payloads, and measured/not_applicable coverage receipt, while Round 58 replaces seven phases, late manifest initialization, task-root waits, and post-receipt task mutation. Slugger retains exactly ownershipGeneration 1 with one token/host/PID/PGID/start identity, immutable gate/release/result paths, phase timestamps, and terminal sanitized result. Prepared/no-member, synchronous spawn error, recorded waiting gate, released execution, same-host reap, foreign-host block, rejected initial CAS, and strict no-second-generation recovery remain fault-tested.

## Round 58 Closure Replacements

The clauses in this section are the final normative replacements for the conflicting successor initialization, external recovery, blocker resolution, terminal-finality, retry-hash, cleanup-code, and Unit37 entry sentences above. Earlier text remains historical context only where this section names a replacement; no implementation may combine old and replacement branches.

- Repair-successor identity and creation are fully derived. successorKey is lowercase SHA-256 of UTF-8 compact JSON with no final LF and exact field order `{"predecessorIdentitySha256":I,"dispositionKind":K,"dispositionPath":P,"dispositionSha256":S}` from validated source values; successorSlug is `repair-<successorKey>`. task/branch/worktree/Desk/product-doc paths are the previously declared full-key formulas. SuccessorBootstrapAttempt uses only the Round 60 exact schema and nine-phase matrix. implementationBaseSha is fetched origin/main at prepare. Exact pre-source commands from canonical product cwd are fetch main, branch at base, and worktree add in that order, each journaled. Source commit-tree message stdin is exact `docs: record repair source <successorKey>\n`; its closed environment sets PATH, LANG/LC_ALL C, author/committer `Codex Release <codex@spoonjoy.app>`, and both dates bootstrap.startedAt, with all other keys unset. Round 60 owns every later source write/index/commit/ref/push/readback and Desk task/seed/identity checkpoint. Recovery accepts only its declared prefixes; collisions, wrong refs/paths/bytes, undeclared dirt, symlinks, partial files, or multiple owners reject without rollback. Identity freezes at task_created; later planning fills only derived document paths.

- The manifest initialization order is replaced. Exact top level is now `{version:1,identity:ReleaseTaskIdentity,writerId,revision,updatedAt,preReleaseArtifacts:PreReleaseArtifact[],terminalArtifacts:TerminalArtifact[],runs:ReleaseRun[]}`. Primary initialization at Unit32 has an empty preReleaseArtifacts array. A repair successor initializes its manifest after handoff and before Work Doer, with runs empty; its phase sequence is exact `prepared -> task_created -> planning_running -> contract_approved -> handoff_recorded -> manifest_ready -> implementation_running -> implementation_complete`. Successor action domain adds `initialize-manifest` between record-handoff and start-implementation. Exact new manifest command `append-pre-release-artifact --manifest M --writer-id W --kind post_merge_successor --path P` is legal only for a repair-successor manifest with no runs, accepts only the Round 59 phase-specific closed registry, hashes complete bytes, BINARY-inserts one unique `PreReleaseArtifact`, and is byte-idempotent. Ordinary `append-artifact` still requires a ReleaseRun/StageRun. At initialize-manifest, every already-existing successor runtime artifact is appended before manifest_ready. At finish-implementation, every registry, red record, unit receipt, review, verification, coverage subordinate/summary, and final implementation receipt is written completely, appended through this command with a pushed/read-back manifest checkpoint after each path, then the closed preReleaseArtifacts set is validated before implementation_complete. Unit32 may start only afterward and never reinitializes the manifest. A crash observes the longest hash-valid prefix and resumes at the first absent artifact; unregistered bytes, registered missing/drifted bytes, extra paths, a run before implementation_complete, or implementation_complete without the exact closed set rejects.

- Successor suite waits are manifest-owned and archive-safe. Exact `SuccessorRuntimeWaitCheckpoint={version:1,successorKey,kind:'planner'|'doer',sourceSuiteAttemptOrdinal,waitOrdinal,scheduleSeconds,retryAfterSeconds,delaySeconds,notBefore,createdAt}` and sibling `SuccessorRuntimeWaitResolution={version:1,checkpointPath,checkpointSha256,probePath,probeSha256,resolvedAt}` live only at `artifacts/post-merge-successor/runtime-waits/<kind>/wait-<waitOrdinal>.v1.json` and `resolution-<waitOrdinal>.v1.json`. Exact `SuccessorRuntimeProbe={version:1,successorKey,kind,waitOrdinal,probeOrdinal,status:'running'|'completed',prompt,promptSha256,deadlineStartedAt,deadlineAt,agentId,reportPath,reportSha256,verdict,endedAt}` uses the AgentRuntimeProbe null matrix below and lives in the same directory. Every path is appended to preReleaseArtifacts when the manifest exists, or at initialize-manifest when it predates the manifest. `runtimeWaitPaths` contains all checkpoints, resolutions, and probes as BINARY-sorted unique paths; runtimeWaitSetSha256 hashes compact canonical BINARY-path-sorted `{path,sha256}[]` with no final LF and is null iff the array is empty. No successor wait/probe file may appear at task root.

- External wait identity and agent recovery are replaced. `historyKeySha256` is lowercase SHA-256 of UTF-8 exact compact JSON with no final LF and field order `{"releaseRun":R,"owningUnit":U,"logicalName":L,"terminalCode":C}`; R is the positive ReleaseRun.run, U is exact 32..37, and L/C are exact stored strings. triggerMode `provider` alone is handled by resume-external-wait and the typed read-only provider preflight; triggerMode `agent_runtime` rejects that route and is handled only by start/finish-agent-runtime-probe. AgentCommand gains positive `runtimeEpoch`; attempts are numbered and capped at two per exact `(releaseRun,unit,logicalName,runtimeEpoch)`, beginning at epoch 1. Agent-runtime wait checkpoint carries that epoch. Exact `AgentRuntimeProbe={version:1,waitPath,waitSha256,runtimeEpoch,probeOrdinal,status,prompt,promptSha256,deadlineStartedAt,deadlineAt,agentId,reportPath,reportSha256,verdict,endedAt}` has running with status running and all five terminal fields null; completed has canonical agentId/report/hash/endedAt plus verdict `available|unavailable`. Expiry writes a completed unavailable probe. Available writes ExternalWaitResolution with exact additional `nextRuntimeEpoch:runtimeEpoch+1`, returns it, and authorizes one fresh same-SHA StageRun whose agent attempts use that next epoch. Unavailable appends the next same-epoch wait. Epoch overflow, mixed trigger routing, attempt reuse across epochs, a third attempt in one epoch, or a resolution without a completed available probe rejects.

- Capability blockers have two honest resolution branches. Exact no-extra-fields `BlockerResolutionEvidence={version:1,kind,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,capabilityName,probeEvidencePath,probeEvidenceSha256,actor,authorizationId,authorizedAt}` has kind `read_only_probe|operator_authorization`. read_only_probe is legal only for a null-attempt preflight blocker, carries the exact fresh successful CapabilityEntry evidence, and has actor/authorizationId null. operator_authorization is legal only for a process-positive `github_pr_write|github_merge_write|cloudflare_workers_edit|cloudflare_d1_edit|cloudflare_billing` blocker, has probe fields null, actor exact `ari`, canonical UUID v4 authorizationId, and canonical authorizedAt supplied by the human; it asserts only permission to make one fresh mutation attempt and never claims capability success. Exact immutable resolutions are `PreMergeBlockerResolution={version:1,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,blockedCapabilityEvidencePath,blockedCapabilityEvidenceSha256,resolutionEvidencePath,resolutionEvidenceSha256,resolvedAt}` at `artifacts/pre-merge-blocker-resolutions/unit-<unit>/<dispositionSha256>.v1.json`, the same-field PostMergeBlockerResolution at its declared path, and TerminalBlockerResolution at its phase/domain path. Existing resolve-* commands accept only read_only_probe. New strict commands `authorize-pre-merge-blocker --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --disposition P --authorization-json J`, `authorize-post-merge-blocker --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --stage-run G --logical-name L --disposition P --authorization-json J`, and the Round 59 task-artifact/Desk-control `authorize-terminal-blocker` variants accept only compact canonical `{version:1,actor:'ari',authorizationId,authorizedAt}`. A resolution authorizes one next ordinal; if the actual mutation still lacks capability it creates a new blocker. Account visibility, D1 visibility, OAuth possession, or operator authorization never fabricates billing/edit proof.

- Terminal failure artifacts and retry hashes are collision-free. Replacement exact `TerminalFailureDisposition={version:1,identitySha256,executionHost,unit37StageRun,storageDomain,terminalPhase,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,logicalName,historyKeySha256,sourceAttemptPath,sourceAttemptSha256,attemptOrdinal,commandMode,terminalCode,snapshotPath,snapshotSha256,evidencePath,evidenceSha256,retryOrdinal,classification,maxRetries,repairCode,createdAt}` uses storageDomain `task_artifact|desk_control`. For task_artifact phases, the exact sibling paths are `artifacts/terminal-failures/<terminalPhase>/<historyKeySha256>/attempt-<attemptOrdinal>-snapshot.v1.json`, `attempt-<attemptOrdinal>-evidence.v1.json`, and `attempt-<attemptOrdinal>-disposition.v1.json`. For post-final control phases they are `_meta/release-terminal/<identitySha256>/failures/<terminalPhase>/<historyKeySha256>/attempt-<attemptOrdinal>-{snapshot,evidence,disposition}.v1.json` relative to Desk. TerminalFailureSnapshot, TerminalFailureEvidence, and the process/git/filesystem/capability/internal payload union use the sole exact Round 60 schemas and total error-code domain. The payload, command mode, source attempt, phase, and total phase/code table must agree; evidence path/hash are always nonnull and exact. Every `priorFailedAttemptSetSha256`, including TerminalCleanupAttempt and ArchiveValidationAttempt/Receipt, hashes UTF-8 compact canonical BINARY-path-sorted unique `[{"path":P,"sha256":S}]` with no final LF, where each hash covers the complete immutable snapshot bytes; priorFailedAttemptPaths is the exact path projection. Empty uses SHA-256 of exact `[]`.

- Terminal finality and repaired predecessor entry use only the Round 60 state/checkpoint model. Task-mutating phases remain `terminal_cleanup -> desk_archive -> track_archive -> archive_validation -> repair_index? -> archive_validation_final`; every task artifact and any created index precedes the final receipt. Stage-kind is validating_active only; terminal-kind may resume all legal checkpoints. The source remains terminal-pending and Slugger-ineligible until fresh repaired final validation.

- Archive validation and repair-index binding are acyclic. A successful ArchiveValidationAttempt is provisional. If no repair index is required and no later task mutation occurs, it may finalize. If an index is required, `PostMergeRepairIndexCandidate`, `PostMergeRepairIndexAttempt`, and `PostMergeRepairIndex` replace `successorArchiveValidationSha256` with `successorArchiveValidationAttemptPath` and `successorArchiveValidationAttemptSha256`; they bind the latest successful provisional attempt and never bind the absent final receipt. Any index failure or other task-root append invalidates that provisional attempt. After the index is verified/attempt-free, release-terminal runs one fresh archive-validation ordinal over the now-final closed set. Replacement `ArchiveValidationReceipt={version:1,attemptOrdinal,priorFailedAttemptPaths,priorFailedAttemptSetSha256,mergeSha,validatorMergeSha,executionHost,validatorRuntimePath,validatorArchivePath,validatorArchiveSha256,validatorSourceTreeSha256,manifestPath,trackDecision,trackDispositionSha256,trackDispositionCommitSha,repairIndexPath,repairIndexSha256,commandResult,validatedAt}` has both repair-index fields nonnull and hash-valid only for repair-successor/intermediate, otherwise both null. The final validated-attempt-to-receipt checkpoint changes no other task byte. Predecessor authorization validates final receipt -> final index -> provisional attempt, so no object self-hashes or points forward.

- Post-receipt resource cleanup cannot invalidate the task archive. TerminalResourceCleanupAttempt and all resource cleanup snapshots/dispositions/waits/resolutions move from task root to exact Desk control directory `/Users/arimendelow/desk/_meta/release-terminal/<identitySha256>/`; they use the same Desk Git matrix and are not manifest artifacts or members of the final task closed set. They begin only after final ArchiveValidationReceipt push/readback. No task/archive byte may change afterward. resource_cleanup and slugger are the only desk_control phases; they can return retrying, waiting, blocked, or resolved through ReleaseTerminalProgressResult, but never repair_successor. Their transient codes retry twice then wait; credential/billing/platform and configuration/provenance/member-authority failures are human_blocker with the honest resolution union above. Slugger Git/network publication failures use the same durable desk_control lifecycle. A foreign-host live gate returns waiting or blocked without mutation; the same generation-one journal resumes on its executionHost. No disposition, resolution, timeout, code repair, or invocation may authorize generation two. Final ReleaseTerminalResult requires resource control state absent/complete and Slugger observed|uncertain push/readback; repair-successor/intermediate branches still suppress Slugger.

- CleanupReconcileFailure terminalCode is exact `credential_missing|billing_required|platform_capability_missing|network_timeout|cleanup_incomplete|spawn|timeout_term|timeout_kill|signal|sanitizer_invalid_utf8|sanitizer_nul|exit_nonzero|warning|output_invalid|configuration_failed|provenance_failed`. Derivation is total and ordered: validated retained unresolved diagnostic -> cleanup_incomplete; credential-key absence -> credential_missing; provider-positive billing/access denial -> billing_required/platform_capability_missing; transport deadline -> network_timeout; spawn/TERM/KILL/signal/invalid-UTF8/NUL -> their exact code; clean nonzero -> exit_nonzero; positive warnings -> warning; malformed clean output -> output_invalid; argv/environment/registry mismatch -> configuration_failed; target/lineage/base/hash/path mismatch -> provenance_failed. Exactly one row must match before writing failure bytes; arbitrary strings, multiple matches, or fallback from a typed row reject without mutation.

- Unit37 branch entry is replaced accordingly. repaired mode accepts a stage-kind failed predecessor only with validating_active/none/absent checkpoint, or a terminal-kind passed predecessor with any Round 60-valid archive state/checkpoint; only the stage-kind branch omits predecessor Unit37 pass. The terminal-kind branch requires the existing passed Unit37/ReleaseRun and never changes them. Both require the immediate child receipt/index and follow the state-specific supersede/resume contract above. The successor manifest is initialized at manifest_ready before Work Doer; implementation_complete gates only start-run/Unit32, not manifest creation.
- Successor identity and probe paths are exact. `identityPath` is successor-task-relative `artifacts/post-merge-successor/successor-identity.v1.json` and its bytes are compact canonical ReleaseTaskIdentity with no final LF; sourceCreated refers only to the exact product feedback-source path derived above. The identity file and every completed bootstrap projection copied into the successor task are registered at initialize-manifest. A running successor probe is mutable temporary `artifacts/post-merge-successor/runtime-waits/<kind>/probe-<probeOrdinal>.attempt.v1.json`, is legal only while its suite attempt is running, and is never a PreReleaseArtifact or runtimeWaitPaths member. Finish atomically replaces it with immutable `probe-<probeOrdinal>.v1.json`, then appends that receipt; crash recovery completes a hash-valid report or interrupts/removes only the owned temporary. External AgentRuntimeProbe uses the same attempt/receipt split under `artifacts/external-waits/<historyKeySha256>/`: running is `probe-<probeOrdinal>.attempt.v1.json`, completed is immutable `probe-<probeOrdinal>.v1.json`, and only completed bytes enter the matching manifest artifact array/resolution hashes. Thus no registered artifact is later rewritten.
- Predecessor supersede state is schema-bound by the Round 60 PredecessorArchiveState plus PredecessorArchiveCheckpoint pair in attempt/receipt. It finalizes archive_validated attempts, creates or retains desk_archive TrackDisposition according to the frozen checkpoint, performs no duplicate lifecycle/move effect, and always runs fresh final archive validation after appended repair protocol. Any content, phase, checkpoint, or locator drift rejects.
- PostMergeSuccessorAttempt uses only the Round 60 exact field order and eight-phase null/status matrix. initialize-manifest advances handoff_recorded to manifest_ready with the extended manifest, append-pre-release-artifact returns exact `{path,sha256}`, blocker results use their domain schemas, and every result rejects extra fields.
- A repair-index provisional validation reference is retained, not dangling. When a repair index is required, a successful provisional ArchiveValidationAttempt is atomically projected before active-attempt removal to immutable manifest artifact `artifacts/archive-validation-provisional/attempt-<attemptOrdinal>.v1.json` with byte-identical attempt payload plus its complete command result; both index path/hash fields reference this artifact, never the removed task-root attempt. The projection itself and every index failure artifact precede a fresh final archive-validation ordinal. Final validation rejects if the provisional artifact, final index, or manifest registration is absent or drifted.
- Successor bootstrap finalization uses only the Round 60 non-self-referential SuccessorBootstrapReceipt, source/tree/commit/task-seed/state/checkpoint fields, path, and atomic attempt-removal checkpoint. PostMergeSuccessorAttempt bootstrap fields become nonnull at task_created and remain immutable; no object hashes itself.
- The sole start-agent-command success object is `{attempt,runtimeEpoch,retryOrdinal,deadlineStartedAt,deadlineAt,prompt,promptSha256,requiredArtifactsSha256,outPath}`. For BlockerResolutionEvidence kind read_only_probe, actor, authorizationId, and authorizedAt are all null while both probe evidence fields are nonnull; for operator_authorization, both probe fields are null while actor, authorizationId, and authorizedAt are nonnull. Mixed null matrices reject.
- Terminal failure classification is total in the replacement model. terminalPhase is exact `terminal_cleanup|desk_archive|track_archive|archive_validation|repair_index|resource_cleanup|slugger`; the first five require storageDomain task_artifact and the last two require desk_control. TerminalCode is exact `credential_missing|billing_required|platform_capability_missing|github_rate_limited|github_5xx|dns_failure|network_timeout|eventual_consistency|cleanup_incomplete|spawn|timeout_term|timeout_kill|signal|sanitizer_invalid_utf8|sanitizer_nul|exit_nonzero|warning|output_invalid|schema_invalid|validation_failed|configuration_failed|provenance_failed`. For task_artifact, credential/billing/platform map human_blocker/0; rate-limit/5xx/DNS/network/eventual/spawn/timeout/signal map retry_terminal/maxRetries 2 at ordinals 1..2 and external_wait at 3+; cleanup_incomplete maps retry_terminal twice then repair_successor/cleanup; sanitizer_invalid_utf8/sanitizer_nul/exit_nonzero/warning/output_invalid/schema_invalid/validation_failed map repair_successor/production_validation; configuration_failed maps repair_successor/configuration; provenance_failed maps repair_successor/provenance. For desk_control, credential/billing/platform/configuration/provenance map human_blocker/0; every transient and cleanup_incomplete retries twice then external_wait; sanitizer_invalid_utf8/sanitizer_nul/exit_nonzero/warning/output_invalid/schema_invalid/validation_failed map human_blocker/0; repairCode is always null and repair_successor is illegal. terminal_cleanup maps typed process results, registry/postcondition/config/provenance in that precedence; Desk/track/index map rejected-push convergence without disposition, observed transport to network/github codes, and schema/tree/ancestry/config to their exact code; archive validation maps typed process transients before clean nonzero/schema/hash semantic rejection; resource cleanup maps declared filesystem error to cleanup_incomplete and authority drift to provenance; Slugger maps Git transport/network, spawn/timeout/signal, publication schema/config/provenance, and process-result sanitization exactly. Exactly one row must match; raw fallback errors, unknown codes, overlapping rows, wrong domain/phase, or repair_successor from desk_control reject without mutation.
- Terminal wait state, prior-probe cross-links, ordinal wait/blocker probes, available/unavailable outcomes, evidence, resolution paths, crash prefixes, schedule, and ReleaseTerminalProgressResult use only the Round 60 exact contracts. The capped schedule remains `[60,120,300,600,900]`; early reinvocation is byte-stable, same-host ownership is frozen, and Slugger preserves ownershipGeneration 1/spawnToken.
- The complete mutating evidence grammar is the earlier ordered list plus `append-pre-release-artifact`, `append-terminal-artifact`, the exact resolve/authorize blocker commands, the Round 59 terminal resume/resolve/authorize domain variants, and successor `initialize-manifest`; no other subcommand or flag is legal. The later Round 59 section is authoritative for every exact operand and result.

### Round 59 Authoritative Replacements

- The sole manifest top level and PreReleaseArtifact/TerminalArtifact schemas are the Round 59 declaration as completed by Round 60. append-pre-release-artifact uses only the Round 60 single-prefix registry; append-terminal-artifact uses only the Round 60 complete task-artifact registry and phase rules. Primary initializes both arrays empty; every member is BINARY-path-sorted unique, complete, regular, hash-valid, pushed/readback, and byte-idempotent. Desk-control files, mutable attempts, root terminal protocol, missing/drifted/extra/wrong-phase members, and every post-final append are forbidden.

- The repair-successor pre-release registry, path domain, and phase closure are exclusively the Round 60 single-prefix suffix registry. manifest_ready, implementation_running, and implementation_complete require their exact attempt-prompt/runtime/implementation prefixes; runtime attempt files are forbidden, and each pushed append resumes from the first absent member.

- Every retry/wait history domain includes its owner. External/post-merge `historyKeySha256` is lowercase SHA-256 of UTF-8 exact compact JSON with no final LF and field order `{"releaseRun":R,"owningUnit":U,"logicalName":L,"terminalCode":C}`; U is exact `32|33|34|35|36|37`. That preimage controls directory path, lookup, prior count, wait, probe, resolution, and migration; the older ownerless preimage is invalid. Replacement `TerminalFailureDisposition={version:1,identitySha256,executionHost,unit37StageRun,storageDomain,terminalPhase,predecessorArchiveState,logicalName,historyKeySha256,sourceAttemptPath,sourceAttemptSha256,attemptOrdinal,commandMode,terminalCode,evidencePath,evidenceSha256,retryOrdinal,classification,maxRetries,repairCode,createdAt}` uses terminal history preimage `{"identitySha256":I,"terminalPhase":P,"logicalName":L,"terminalCode":C}` in that exact field order. `retryOrdinal` is one plus the number of previously pushed hash-valid dispositions with that key. Replaying the same sourceAttemptPath/sourceAttemptSha256 returns the existing byte-identical disposition and ordinal; a different source attempt gets the next ordinal. Every terminal failure/wait/blocker path and lookup is keyed by this hash, so two logical operations in one phase cannot collide.

- Terminal failure snapshot, evidence, payload variants, code table, and nullability use only the Round 60 exact schemas. Filesystem errorCode remains exact `EACCES|EBUSY|EEXIST|EIO|EINVAL|EMFILE|ENFILE|ENOENT|ENOSPC|ENOTEMPTY|EPERM|EROFS|EXDEV|OTHER`; internal diagnosticCode is `schema|validation|configuration|provenance`. Capability and internal payload ownership, all nonnull paths/hashes, exit_nonzero, both sanitizer codes, and CleanupReconcileFailure precedence are exhaustive.

- Terminal wait and blocker probes, evidence, resolution schemas, canonical basenames, write/register ordering, null matrices, and task-artifact versus Desk-control lock domains are exclusively the Round 60 contracts. The older generic TerminalResolutionProbe and unordered resolution prose are invalid.

- Exact terminal recovery argv are domain-disjoint. task_artifact uses `pnpm release:terminal -- --mode <normal|repaired> --action resume-terminal-wait --manifest M --writer-id W --wait P`, `... --action resolve-terminal-blocker --manifest M --writer-id W --disposition P`, or `... --action authorize-terminal-blocker --manifest M --writer-id W --disposition P --authorization-json J`, all under the manifest writer lock and with every new task file appended through append-terminal-artifact. desk_control uses the same three actions with `--identity-sha256 X` in place of `--manifest M --writer-id W`, under exact hard-link lock `/Users/arimendelow/desk/_meta/release-terminal/<X>/control.lock` and the Desk Git push/readback matrix. resolve accepts only the fresh read-only evidence producer; authorize accepts only compact canonical TerminalOperatorAuthorization. Any mixed operand set, wrong domain, extra flag, early notBefore, stale hash, or second use of one authorization rejects with zero mutation.

- Replacement exact `ReleaseTerminalProgressResult={mode,terminalKind,status,terminalPhase,attemptOrdinal,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,waitPath,waitSha256,resolutionPath,resolutionSha256,successorJournalPath,successorJournalSha256,nextAttemptOrdinal}` rejects extra fields and has this complete null matrix: retrying has status retrying, disposition and nextAttemptOrdinal nonnull, all wait/resolution/successor fields null; waiting has disposition plus wait fields nonnull and all resolution/successor/next fields null; blocked has only disposition nonnull; resolved has disposition, resolution, and nextAttemptOrdinal nonnull with wait/successor null; repair_successor has disposition and successor fields nonnull with wait/resolution/next null and is legal only in task_artifact. mode is `normal|repaired`, terminalKind is the matching ReleaseTerminalResult member, terminalPhase is one of all seven phases, attemptOrdinal is the source attempt, and every path resolves in the disposition storage domain. A resume before notBefore returns the same waiting object byte-for-byte; a read-only or authorized resolution returns resolved once, and the next identical invocation enters exactly nextAttemptOrdinal.

- predecessorArchiveState and its exact PredecessorArchiveCheckpoint companion use only the Round 60 derivation table. Every source disposition and repair-lineage object stores both; archive_validated attempt recovery and absent/present TrackDisposition are explicit, while resource_cleanup/slugger remain successor-ineligible.

- Successor bootstrap source bytes, task seed, Git commands, phase/null matrix, legal crash states, commit/ref publication, Desk creation, and final receipt use only the Round 60 contract. The source-containing commit is pushed from the derived local branch before identity exists; task status is processing, and no earlier bare-base push or SHA-source set-upstream form is legal.
- SuccessorDeskTaskSeed is the exact immutable Round 60 task-seed artifact and canonical renderer input. Its task.md projection is lifecycle-mutable, while seed/source/identity bytes are immutable and registered at manifest_ready; every mirror is written from hash-verified product bytes as it becomes available.

- Replacement `SuccessorSuiteAttempt={kind:'planner'|'doer',ordinal,status,skill,cwd,promptPath,promptSha256,planningPath,doingPath,startedAt,deadlineAt,endedAt,agentId,artifacts,artifactSetSha256}` binds every invocation. planner skill is `work-planner`, doer is `work-doer`; cwd byte-equals successor identity.repoCwd; promptPath is exact `artifacts/post-merge-successor/suite/<kind>/attempt-<ordinal>-prompt.txt`, whose complete bytes hash to promptSha256 before dispatch; planningPath/doingPath byte-equal the identity product paths. running has canonical bindings, null endedAt/agentId/artifactSetSha256, and empty artifacts; interrupted retains bindings and has canonical endedAt, nullable agentId, empty artifacts, null set hash; completed retains bindings and has canonical endedAt/agentId plus nonempty exact artifact set/hash. The returned start-planning/start-implementation result repeats these skill/cwd/prompt-path/hash/document fields. Recovery rejects prompt, skill, cwd, document, attempt, or artifact drift and never redispatches unbound bytes.

- Repaired root/intermediate closed sets use only the Round 60 stage/state/checkpoint table. Every intermediate owns a distinct relay, retains a leaf receipt only for terminal-kind, consumes the child's index, and creates its own index; root consumes the child's index and creates none. Archived closure finalizes/validates DeskArchive and creates or retains the exact desk_archive TrackDisposition according to predecessorArchiveCheckpoint. Slugger remains root-only after complete reverse closure.

- Archive-index mutation is legal only through terminal artifact registration. A successful provisional ArchiveValidationAttempt is projected to the declared `artifacts/archive-validation-provisional/attempt-<ordinal>.v1.json`, appended with append-terminal-artifact in phase archive_validation, pushed/readback, and only then may repair-index creation reference its path/hash. Any index failure appends its exact terminal failure members. The final fresh validation reads the registered provisional projection and verified index but emits the final root ArchiveValidationReceipt outside the manifest, preventing self-reference. No terminal artifact append is legal after that receipt.

- PostMergeFailureDisposition, ReleaseTerminalResult, postMergeRepairRelayPath, predecessor archive fields, and consumed-versus-created repair-index nullability use only the Round 60 exact replacements. Every older `repairIndexPath` result field is invalid.

- The complete mutating grammar is the prior grammar as replaced by this Round 59 section: it adds append-terminal-artifact and the exact terminal resume/resolve/authorize variants above; initialize-manifest uses the extended manifest schema; all successor phases are the eight-phase sequence including manifest_ready; and every start-agent-command result includes runtimeEpoch. No ownerless retry key, broad path-prefix append, terminal authorization without manifest-or-identity ownership, or seven-phase successor sequence remains legal.

### Round 60 Authoritative Replacements

- TerminalArtifact membership is replaced by one complete registry. In addition to immutable failure snapshot/evidence/disposition files, exact permitted task-artifact paths are `artifacts/terminal-worktree-cleanup/receipt.v1.json` for terminal_cleanup; `artifacts/terminal-failures/<phase>/<historyKeySha256>/wait-<waitOrdinal>.v1.json`, `wait-probe-<waitOrdinal>.v1.json`, `wait-resolution-evidence-<waitOrdinal>.v1.json`, and `wait-resolution-<waitOrdinal>.v1.json`; `blocker-probe-<probeOrdinal>.v1.json`, `blocker-resolution-evidence-<dispositionSha256>.v1.json`, `authorization-<authorizationId>.v1.json`, and `blocker-resolution-<dispositionSha256>.v1.json`; and the archive-validation provisional projection. `artifacts/terminal-worktree-cleanup/attempt.v1.json`, running probe candidates, and token-qualified write candidates are phase-owned mutable attempts, never TerminalArtifacts, and are legal only while their owning terminal attempt is live. Worktree cleanup complete writes/fsyncs the immutable receipt, appends/pushes/readbacks it through append-terminal-artifact while retaining the attempt, then atomically records its hash in TerminalCleanupAttempt and removes the attempt; only that checkpoint permits later ref commands. Archive validation rejects an absent/unregistered receipt, a retained worktree attempt, or any other registry member mismatch.

- The pre-release registry uses one path domain. After exact task-relative prefix `artifacts/post-merge-successor/`, the only suffixes are `successor-identity.v1.json`, `task-seed.v1.json`, `bootstrap/<successorKey>.v1.json`, `handoff.v1.json`, `suite/<planner|doer>/attempt-<positive>-prompt.txt`, the declared runtime-wait suffixes, implementation registry/unit/red/review/verification suffixes, the eight coverage basenames, and `post-merge-implementation.v1.json`. Every stored PreReleaseArtifact.path includes the prefix exactly once. manifest_ready requires every planner-attempt prompt, including interrupted attempts, and its exact runtime prefix; implementation_running/completed applies the same rule to every doer-attempt prompt. Earlier prose naming a successor file as an ordinary Artifact is replaced by PreReleaseArtifact; running attempt files are neither type.

- Terminal failure bytes are fully serializable. Exact no-extra-fields `TerminalFailureSnapshot={version:1,identitySha256,executionHost,storageDomain,terminalPhase,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,logicalName,historyKeySha256,sourceAttemptPath,sourceAttemptSha256,attemptOrdinal,commandMode,terminalCode,phaseState,priorSuccessfulResultPaths,priorSuccessfulResultSetSha256,capturedAt}` uses the exact phase projection union: terminal_cleanup `{kind:'terminal_cleanup',phase,activeCommandSequence,commandResultCount,worktreeCleanupPhase}`; desk_archive `{kind:'desk_archive',phase}`; track_archive `{kind:'track_archive',phase}`; archive_validation `{kind:'archive_validation',phase,commandResultCount}`; repair_index `{kind:'repair_index',phase}`; resource_cleanup `{kind:'resource_cleanup',phase,nextDeleteIndex}`; or slugger `{kind:'slugger',phase,ownershipGeneration,spawnToken}`. Every member value is copied from the named exact attempt schema; nullable members follow that schema, counts are safe, and prior result paths/hash use the declared canonical set rule. Exact `TerminalFailureEvidence={version:1,identitySha256,executionHost,storageDomain,terminalPhase,logicalName,historyKeySha256,snapshotPath,snapshotSha256,attemptOrdinal,commandMode,terminalCode,payload,observedAt}` has commandMode `process|git|filesystem|capability|internal` iff payload has the matching Round 59 variant; variants have no nullable or extra fields. Replacement TerminalFailureDisposition inserts `predecessorArchiveCheckpoint` after predecessorArchiveState and `snapshotPath,snapshotSha256` immediately before evidencePath. Snapshot is written/fsynced/appended first, evidence second, disposition last; each push/readback is a recoverable prefix and a same-source replay completes the first absent member without changing existing bytes.

- TerminalCode additionally includes `sanitizer_invalid_utf8|sanitizer_nul`. For task_artifact both sanitizer codes map repair_successor/production_validation; for desk_control both map human_blocker with repairCode null. They are classified after spawn/timeout/signal and before exit/warning/output. The total TerminalCode table, snapshot/evidence payload match, CleanupReconcileFailure table, and Unit29.2 Cartesian fixtures all include both codes; no raw invalid byte is persisted.

- Terminal waits use distinct ordinal probes and a closed crash prefix. Replacement `TerminalWaitCheckpoint={version:1,identitySha256,executionHost,storageDomain,terminalPhase,logicalName,historyKeySha256,sourceDispositionPath,sourceDispositionSha256,waitOrdinal,scheduleSeconds,retryAfterSeconds,delaySeconds,notBefore,priorProbePath,priorProbeSha256,createdAt}` has both prior-probe fields null at ordinal 1 and nonnull/hash-valid to the immediately preceding unavailable probe thereafter. Exact `TerminalWaitProbe={version:1,identitySha256,storageDomain,terminalPhase,logicalName,historyKeySha256,checkpointPath,checkpointSha256,waitOrdinal,kind,result,executionHost,observedAt}` has kind `provider_probe|host_liveness` and result `available|unavailable`; it lives at `wait-probe-<waitOrdinal>.v1.json`. Unavailable appends/pushes the probe and then a next checkpoint cross-linking it. Available appends/pushes the probe, then exact `TerminalWaitResolutionEvidence={version:1,checkpointPath,checkpointSha256,probePath,probeSha256,result:'available',executionHost,resolvedAt}` at `wait-resolution-evidence-<waitOrdinal>.v1.json`, then exact `TerminalWaitResolution={version:1,checkpointPath,checkpointSha256,resolutionEvidencePath,resolutionEvidenceSha256,resolvedAt}` at `wait-resolution-<waitOrdinal>.v1.json`. Recovery accepts only absent, probe-only, probe+evidence, or complete resolution prefixes and deterministically performs the first absent write; every other orphan/order/hash rejects.

- Terminal blocker probes are separate from wait probes. Exact `TerminalBlockerProbe={version:1,identitySha256,storageDomain,terminalPhase,logicalName,historyKeySha256,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,probeOrdinal,capabilityName,result:'available'|'unavailable',executionHost,observedAt}` is the sole read-only capability producer at `blocker-probe-<probeOrdinal>.v1.json`. Exact `TerminalOperatorAuthorization={version:1,actor:'ari',dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,authorizationId,action,capabilityName,authorizedAt}` has action `retry_capability|retry_after_manual_repair` and capabilityName nonnull iff retry_capability. Exact `TerminalBlockerResolutionEvidence={version:1,kind,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,probePath,probeSha256,authorizationPath,authorizationSha256,resolvedAt}` has kind read_only_probe with nonnull successful probe fields and null authorization fields, or operator_authorization with the reverse. Exact `TerminalBlockerResolution={version:1,identitySha256,storageDomain,terminalPhase,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,blockedEvidencePath,blockedEvidenceSha256,resolutionEvidencePath,resolutionEvidenceSha256,authorizationPath,authorizationSha256,resolvedAt}` repeats the evidence authorization null matrix. Unavailable probe appends/pushes and returns blocked; available probe precedes resolution evidence then resolution. Operator authorization precedes resolution evidence then resolution. Every prefix is idempotent under the domain lock, and branches cannot mix.

- Exact `PredecessorArchiveCheckpoint={deskArchivePhase,trackDisposition}` travels beside predecessorArchiveState. deskArchivePhase is `none|prepared|lifecycle_done|root_moved|archive_validated|receipt_final`; trackDisposition is `absent|present`. validating_active permits only none/prepared plus absent. archive_in_progress permits lifecycle_done/root_moved plus absent. done_archived_pending permits archive_validated/receipt_final and either track value. A desk_archive failure at archive_validated therefore maps done_archived_pending even before receipt publication. Before repaired mutation, archive_validated deterministically completes the attempt-to-DeskArchive receipt checkpoint without replaying lifecycle/move; receipt_final validates the existing receipt. If trackDisposition is absent, repaired closure creates the exact desk_archive TrackDisposition only after repair protocol finalization; if present, it retains/hash-validates the existing one. Both use taskArchiveKind desk_archive and the final DeskArchive hash. track_archive/archive_validation/repair_index require receipt_final plus present. No state assumes a TrackDisposition merely from DeskArchive completion.

- Stage-kind and terminal-kind state domains are disjoint. Every PostMergeFailureDisposition has predecessorArchiveState validating_active and checkpoint `{deskArchivePhase:'none',trackDisposition:'absent'}`. Stage-kind repaired entry accepts only that pair. TerminalFailureDisposition derives the complete pair from persisted attempts and terminal-kind repaired entry alone may use all three archive states. Every source markdown, RepairBrief, PostMergeSuccessorAttempt, bootstrap attempt/receipt, PostMergeRepairLink, and PredecessorSupersede attempt/receipt carries both fields in that order and rejects lineage drift.

- ReleaseTerminalResult no longer overloads repairIndexPath. It replaces that field with `consumedRepairIndexPath` and `createdRepairIndexPath`. ordinary-normal has both null; repair-successor-normal has consumed null and created nonnull; repaired-intermediate has both nonnull; repaired-root has consumed nonnull and created null. The consumed path is the immediate child's verified index authorizing repaired entry; the created path is the current task's newly published index authorizing the next ancestor. postMergeRepairRelayPath and archive-state nullability remain as declared. No root creates a new index, and no repaired branch may omit the child index it consumed.

- PostMergeSuccessorAttempt is replaced by exact `{version:1,successorKey,predecessorManifest,predecessorReleaseRun,predecessorStageRun,dispositionKind,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,bootstrapPath,bootstrapSha256,phase,taskPath,taskSeedPath,taskSeedSha256,identityPath,identitySha256,planningPath,planningSha256,doingPath,doingSha256,handoffPath,handoffSha256,manifestPath,manifestSha256,manifestWriterId,suiteAttempts,runtimeWaitPaths,runtimeWaitSetSha256,implementationEvidencePath,implementationEvidenceSha256,createdAt,updatedAt}`. prepared has every path/hash after disposition null, empty suites/waits, and null wait-set hash; task_created adds bootstrap/task/task-seed/identity only; planning_running permits planner suite attempts and runtime waits but planning/doing fields remain null; contract_approved additionally requires planning/doing paths/hashes and a latest completed planner attempt; handoff_recorded adds handoff; manifest_ready adds all manifest fields and the exact registered pre-release prefix; implementation_running permits doer attempts/waits with implementation evidence null; implementation_complete requires a latest completed doer, exact closed pre-release set, and nonnull implementation evidence. Fields once nonnull are immutable; suite kind/status and runtime wait members must be legal for the phase, and every other null/state combination rejects.

- Successor bootstrap is crash-complete and never uses identity before creation. Exact `SuccessorBootstrapAttempt={version:1,successorKey,successorSlug,predecessorIdentitySha256,dispositionKind,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,implementationBaseSha,branch,worktreePath,deskTaskRoot,taskPath,sourcePath,identityPath,phase,sourceSha256,sourceTreeSha,sourceCommitSha,remoteBranchSha,taskSeedPath,taskSeedSha256,branchCreated,worktreeCreated,remoteBranchCreated,deskTaskCreated,sourceCreated,identityCreated,startedAt,updatedAt}` is no-extra-fields; its phases are `prepared|branch_created|worktree_created|source_written|source_indexed|source_committed|remote_created|task_created|complete`. sourceSha256/sourceTreeSha/sourceCommitSha/remoteBranchSha and both task-seed fields are null through worktree_created; source_written adds sourceSha256, source_indexed adds sourceTreeSha, source_committed adds sourceCommitSha, remote_created adds equal remoteBranchSha, and task_created adds both task-seed fields plus identity. The derived worktreePath, not identity.repoCwd, owns pre-identity commands. Legal Git recovery states are exactly base ref with source absent/clean, base ref with byte-exact unstaged source, base ref with source staged and write-tree equal sourceTreeSha, or sourceCommit ref with matching index/worktree clean; deterministic commit-tree recreates the same orphan SHA. Any other dirt/index/ref state rejects. The exact source publication suffix in derived worktreePath is `['git','add','--',sourcePath]`, `['git','write-tree']`, `['git','commit-tree',sourceTreeSha,'-p',implementationBaseSha]` with the declared message/environment, `['git','update-ref','refs/heads/'+branch,sourceCommitSha,implementationBaseSha]`, `['git','cat-file','blob',sourceCommitSha+':'+sourcePath]`, and `['git','status','--short']`; canonical product cwd then runs absent `ls-remote`, `['git','push','--porcelain','--force-with-lease=refs/heads/'+branch+':','--set-upstream','origin','refs/heads/'+branch+':refs/heads/'+branch]`, exact branch fetch, matching ls-remote, and remote-tracking rev-parse. Response-loss recovery accepts exact sourceCommitSha remotely and never respawns the push. Exact source markdown bytes are `# Repair Source\n\n- Successor key: \`<successorKey>\`\n- Predecessor identity: \`<predecessorIdentitySha256>\`\n- Disposition kind: \`<stage|terminal>\`\n- Disposition path: \`<normalized path>\`\n- Disposition SHA-256: \`<sha256>\`\n- Predecessor archive state: \`<state>\`\n- Predecessor archive checkpoint: \`<compact canonical checkpoint JSON>\`\n- Implementation base: \`<implementationBaseSha>\`\n` after validated placeholder substitution, with checkpoint field order deskArchivePhase then trackDisposition and exactly one final LF. Desk task status is exact processing. Exact `SuccessorDeskTaskSeed={version:1,slug,title,status:'processing',createdAt,updatedAt,track:'spoonjoy-v2',requester:'ari',validator:'ari',planningComplete:false,adoptedAt,repoName:'spoonjoy-v2',repoLocalPath,repoMode:'local',iterationSlug:'post-merge-successor',iterationTrigger:'repair-successor',iterationOutcome:'in-progress',sourcePath,planningPath,doingPath,continuityPath,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint}` is stored compact-canonical at `artifacts/post-merge-successor/task-seed.v1.json`. Its canonical Desk renderer emits schema_version 1, one repo, one active/history iteration, and exact source-authority links; parse/render is byte-identical. task.md is the mutable projection and may later advance only through declared lifecycle transforms. Exact `SuccessorBootstrapReceipt={version:1,successorKey,successorSlug,predecessorIdentitySha256,dispositionKind,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,implementationBaseSha,branch,worktreePath,deskTaskRoot,sourceSha256,sourceTreeSha,sourceCommitSha,remoteBranchSha,taskPath,taskSeedPath,taskSeedSha256,sourcePath,identityPath,identitySha256,completedAt}` is no-extra-fields. Every source/index/commit/push/task/seed/identity boundary is journaled and fault-tested.

- Replacement exact `RepairBrief={code,artifactPath,artifactSha256,reviewerRole,promptSha256,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,affectedSurfaces}` and PostMergeRepairLink inserts the same two fields immediately after dispositionKind. The successor source template, journal, bootstrap schemas, link, and supersede schemas use byte-equal values from the source disposition; no caller derives or overwrites them. A passed repair leaf retains its leaf receipt; a repaired intermediate writes only the distinct relay receipt while preserving any terminal-kind leaf receipt. All direct tests and execution instructions use the Round 60 stage/state, index, and basename matrices.

### Round 61 Authoritative Replacements

The clauses below replace every conflicting or merely named Round 58-60 artifact, process, successor, terminal, archive, security, smoke, and repair-evidence contract. A schema introduced here as `Exact` or `Replacement` with a complete brace-delimited field list supersedes every older field list for that type. A clause that explicitly says it retains or incorporates an already exact member, matrix, or registry imports only that identified prior definition and applies the stated replacement; no mere name, shorthand, or conflicting older prose can supply missing fields. When two Round 61 clauses refine the same type, the later clause explicitly identifies what it replaces and is final.

- Manifest artifact records are exact. `PreReleaseArtifact={kind,path,sha256}` has kind `successor_identity|task_seed|bootstrap|handoff|suite_prompt|suite_dispatch_intent|suite_dispatch_receipt|suite_wait|suite_probe|suite_resolution|implementation_registry|command|unit_red|unit_receipt|review_prompt|review_dispatch_intent|review_dispatch|review_runtime|review_report|verification|coverage|implementation_receipt`. `TerminalArtifact={kind,terminalPhase,path,sha256}` has kind `worktree_cleanup|failure_snapshot|failure_evidence|failure_disposition|successful_result|wait_checkpoint|wait_probe|wait_resolution_evidence|wait_resolution|blocker_probe|blocker_authorization|blocker_resolution_evidence|blocker_resolution|desk_archive_cancellation|archive_validation_provisional`. Both are no-extra-fields, use that field order, normalized task-relative regular non-symlink paths, complete-file lowercase SHA-256, BINARY path order, and unique path. Their canonical set hash always covers compact canonical BINARY-path-sorted `{path,sha256}[]` bytes with no LF. A path's exact grammar determines exactly one kind; aliases and multi-kind matches reject.
- The complete pre-release path registry after prefix `artifacts/post-merge-successor/` is: `successor-identity.v1.json`; `task-seed.v1.json`; `bootstrap/<successorKey>.v1.json`; `handoff.v1.json`; `suite/<planner|doer>/attempt-<positive>-prompt.txt`; `suite/<planner|doer>/attempt-<positive>-dispatch-intent.v1.json`; `suite/<planner|doer>/attempt-<positive>-dispatch.v1.json`; `runtime-waits/<planner|doer>/wait-<positive>.v1.json`; `runtime-waits/<planner|doer>/probe-<positive>.v1.json`; `runtime-waits/<planner|doer>/resolution-<positive>.v1.json`; `implementation-registry.v1.json`; `commands/<unitId>/command-<positive>.v1.json`; `units/<unitId>/red.v1.json`; `units/<unitId>/receipt.v1.json`; `reviews/<role>/prompt.txt`; `reviews/<role>/dispatch-intent.v1.json`; `reviews/<role>/dispatch.v1.json`; `reviews/<role>/runtime-report.txt`; `reviews/<role>/report.v1.json`; `verification/<unitId>/command-<positive>.v1.json`; the eight already-declared coverage basenames; and `post-merge-implementation.v1.json`. `unitId` and role must come from the parsed registry, so no broad suffix or caller path is accepted. The complete terminal path registry is the exact worktree-cleanup receipt; immutable snapshot/evidence/disposition siblings; ordinal successful-result paths declared below; every wait/blocker member under its exact `artifacts/terminal-failures/<terminalPhase>/<historyKeySha256>/` owner; `artifacts/predecessor-supersede/desk-archive-cancellation.v1.json`; and the provisional archive projection. Desk-control paths are never TerminalArtifacts.
- Exact artifact append argv are `pnpm release:evidence -- append-pre-release-artifact --manifest M --writer-id W --kind K --path P` and `pnpm release:evidence -- append-terminal-artifact --manifest M --writer-id W --terminal-phase T --kind K --path P`. Each command accepts only the matching finite kind/path/phase, validates complete bytes before the manifest lock, then under the writer lock performs one ordinary atomic manifest rewrite and returns exact `{path,sha256}`. The caller performs the standard Desk commit/push/fetch/readback before another artifact or effect. A crash prefix is only complete-unregistered file, registered-local manifest, committed candidate, or pushed/read-back checkpoint; recovery validates existing bytes and performs the first absent transition. Pre-existing mismatch, wrong owner, missing registered bytes, duplicate path, extra field/flag, or post-final append rejects. Task-artifact terminal snapshot/evidence/disposition writes use this append sequence; Desk-control failures instead use the control lock and Desk Git checkpoint and never say append or mutate manifest bytes.
- Exact `ProcessIdentity={pid,pgid,startIdentitySha256}` uses positive safe integers and lowercase SHA-256 of the complete NUL-free bytes returned by the injected same-host role/token member probe for exact `(pid,pgid,spawnToken,role)`. Production probes with closed environment and absolute trusted `ps`, hashes raw bytes in memory, persists no process text, and requires the same hash on every liveness/death/reap observation. `SpawnGeneration={generation,spawnToken,status,gatePath,releasePath,processIdentity,preparedAt,recordedAt,releasedAt,endedAt}` is no-extra-fields. prepared has null identity/recorded/released/ended, exact gate present, release absent. recorded adds identity and recordedAt, keeps released/ended null, gate present, release absent. released adds releasedAt, keeps ended null, and permits exactly two crash prefixes: release absent with the same verified live gate on executionHost, or exact release present; no other host may advance either. aborted has releasedAt null, endedAt nonnull, release absent, no live members, and identity/recordedAt either both null for synchronous spawn failure or both nonnull for a recorded pre-release abort. ended has every identity/time nonnull, exact gate/release present, and all token members dead/reaped. Times are canonical and ordered prepared <= recorded <= released <= ended where present. Every other field/file/status combination rejects.
- Terminal-kind repaired entry never replays original cleanup. Stage-kind begins with the ordinary host-bound TerminalCleanup and requires original worktree/local-ref/remote-ref present at its prepared checkpoint. Terminal-kind requires a hash-valid previously registered `terminal-worktree-cleanup/receipt.v1.json`, proves its original worktree and both refs remain absent, and reuses that receipt as `terminalCleanupPath`; it cannot create another cleanup attempt or run a delete-ref/worktree command. Its leaf validator is built by a separate prepared-first validator journal from `successorReceipt.validatorMergeSha` using the trusted canonical object repository `/Users/arimendelow/Projects/spoonjoy-v2` after exact SHA fetch/object verification, without creating or changing the predecessor branch/ref/worktree. The source repository may be dirty because only its Git object database is read; any worktree/index command there is forbidden. Tests cover stage and terminal entry separately and reject cleanup replay after every Desk/archive failure checkpoint.
- Successful terminal prefixes are immutable evidence. Exact `TerminalSuccessfulResult={version:1,identitySha256,executionHost,storageDomain,terminalPhase,attemptOrdinal,sequence,logicalName,resultKind,result,recordedAt}` is stored for task artifacts at `artifacts/terminal-results/<terminalPhase>/attempt-<attemptOrdinal>/sequence-<sequence>.v1.json` and for Desk control at `_meta/release-terminal/<identitySha256>/results/<terminalPhase>/attempt-<attemptOrdinal>/sequence-<sequence>.v1.json`. sequence is contiguous from zero; resultKind selects exactly one named no-extra-fields process/Git/filesystem/provider/Desk/validator/notification result already declared by its owning phase, and `result` is that complete object. Each successful observation/effect is reconciled if necessary, then its result file is written/pushed/read back before the mutable attempt advances. `priorSuccessfulResultPaths` is the exact contiguous path projection and its set hash covers complete result bytes. A new ordinal copies only those immutable path/hash references; it never copies mutable attempt fields or reruns a prior result. Missing sequence, changed bytes, unregistered task result, foreign control result, or a result not legal for the phase rejects.
- Terminal failure payloads are exact. `TerminalProcessFailure={kind:'process',resultPath,resultSha256,outcome,exitCode,signal,warningCount,stdoutSha256,stderrSha256}` uses outcome `spawn_error|timeout_term|timeout_kill|signal|exit_nonzero|warning|output_invalid|sanitizer_invalid_utf8|sanitizer_nul`; spawn/timeout/signal have their corresponding nullable exit/signal matrix, warning requires exit zero and positive warningCount, other clean process failures have zero warnings, and every stream hash names sanitized complete bytes. `TerminalGitFailure={kind:'git',operation,commandResultPath,commandResultSha256,observation}` has operation `fetch|archive|worktree_detach|prune|local_ref_delete|remote_ref_delete|desk_commit|desk_push|desk_fetch|desk_readback|track_move|repair_index|slugger_publish` and observation `transport|rejected_push|state_drift|ancestry|schema`. `TerminalFilesystemFailure={kind:'filesystem',operation,locator,locatorSha256,errorCode,sourceState,targetState}` has operation `lstat|open|write|fsync|rename|unlink|rmdir|scan`, the finite filesystem code domain already declared, and exact BlobState source/target. `TerminalCapabilityFailure={kind:'capability',capabilityName,probeName,probePath,probeSha256,result:'unavailable'}` uses one declared capability/probe pair. `TerminalInternalFailure={kind:'internal',diagnosticCode,artifactPath,artifactSha256}` uses `schema|validation|configuration|provenance`. `TerminalFailureEvidence.payload` is exactly this discriminated union and commandMode is the matching `process|git|filesystem|capability|internal`. The total phase/code table selects exactly one payload variant: process terminal codes require process; observed Git transport/state codes require git; resource cleanup OS failures require filesystem; honest preflight blockers require capability; pure schema/config/provenance derivation failures require internal. Sanitizer codes retain no raw invalid bytes. Cartesian parser/classifier tests reject null, overlap, extras, wrong path/hash, and phase/code/variant drift.
- Post-final retries have ordinals independent of Slugger ownership generation. Replacement `TerminalResourceCleanupAttempt` inserts `attemptOrdinal,sourceAttemptPath,sourceAttemptSha256,priorFailedAttemptPaths,priorFailedAttemptSetSha256` after executionHost. Exact `TerminalControlAttempt={version:1,identitySha256,executionHost,terminalPhase,attemptOrdinal,sourceAttemptPath,sourceAttemptSha256,priorFailedAttemptPaths,priorFailedAttemptSetSha256,priorSuccessfulResultPaths,priorSuccessfulResultSetSha256,phaseState,startedAt,updatedAt}` wraps every `resource_cleanup|slugger` retry at `_meta/release-terminal/<identitySha256>/attempts/<terminalPhase>/attempt-<attemptOrdinal>.v1.json`; phaseState is the exact current resource-cleanup projection or Slugger notification/generation projection. Ordinal one has null source and empty failed set; later ordinals name the immediately prior failed control attempt and the complete BINARY-sorted immutable failure-snapshot set. A failure writes snapshot/evidence/disposition, atomically closes that control attempt, and only its progress result authorizes ordinal+1. Slugger ownershipGeneration and spawnToken remain byte-equal generation one across every control ordinal; retries reconcile publication/process result and never prepare a second gate.
- Terminal wait probes carry proof. `TerminalProviderProbeEvidence={kind:'provider',probeName,descriptorPath,descriptorSha256,requestSha256,timeoutMs:10000,successCriterion,observationSha256}` and `TerminalHostProbeEvidence={kind:'host',probeName:'process_liveness'|'filesystem_absence',executionHost,targetIdentitySha256,observationSha256}` are no-extra-fields and form `TerminalProbeEvidence`. Replacement TerminalWaitProbe adds `evidence` before observedAt; evidence kind must match probe kind and every hash names immutable sanitized bytes. github_rate_limited/github_5xx use the source command's exact read-only GitHub GET descriptor; dns/network/eventual_consistency use its exact health/provider GET descriptor; cleanup_incomplete uses the owning cleanup assert-clean or filesystem-absence descriptor; spawn/timeout/signal use process_liveness; foreign-host resource/Slugger recovery uses liveness; no permanent schema/config/capability code may enter wait. available requires the descriptor's exact success criterion; unavailable requires its finite sanitized negative result. No boolean-only availability producer is legal.
- Both successor-runtime and terminal waits use exact schedule `[60,120,300,600,900]`: scheduleSeconds is element `min(waitOrdinal-1,4)`. Retry-After is nullable; only one ASCII decimal integer with no sign, whitespace, fraction, leading zero (except `0`), or overflow parses, and accepted range is 1..900. delaySeconds is `max(scheduleSeconds,retryAfterSeconds ?? 0)`, notBefore is exact canonical `createdAt + delaySeconds*1000`, and date overflow rejects before write. Early reinvocation returns byte-identical waiting output without probe. An unavailable probe creates ordinal+1 at the same capped rule; available writes probe, evidence, and resolution with one equal resolvedAt. The same derivation applies to SuccessorRuntimeWaitCheckpoint and tests every ordinal, cap, malformed header, equality, overflow, and early call.

- Predecessor archive checkpoints are narrowed to possible states. `PredecessorArchiveCheckpoint={deskArchivePhase,trackDisposition}` permits: validating_active with `(none|prepared,absent)`; archive_in_progress with `(lifecycle_done|root_moved,absent)`; done_archived_pending with `(archive_validated,absent)` or `(receipt_final,absent|present)`. archive_validated/present is impossible and rejects. track_archive, provisional/final archive validation, and repair_index failures derive `(receipt_final,present)`. Stage-kind remains exactly `(validating_active,{none,absent})`; terminal-kind alone may use the other pairs.
- A terminal-kind validating_active/prepared predecessor first cancels the no-effect DeskArchive attempt. Exact `DeskArchiveCancellation={version:1,predecessorIdentitySha256,deskArchiveAttemptPath,deskArchiveAttemptSha256,attemptPhase:'prepared',taskSourcePath,taskSourceSha256,taskArchivePath,sourcePresent:true,targetAbsent:true,effectCount:0,cancelledAt}` is written at `artifacts/predecessor-supersede/desk-archive-cancellation.v1.json`, appended as a TerminalArtifact, and pushed/read back before supersede preparation. It is legal only when the hash-valid prepared attempt has performed no lifecycle/file/Git/provider effect. One atomic candidate removes that attempt and adds the cancellation receipt; O and C are the only committed trees, and local recovery accepts only the exact per-path O/O, C/O, or C/C matrix before restoring C. PredecessorSupersede attempt/receipt add `deskArchiveCancellationPath,deskArchiveCancellationSha256` immediately after predecessorArchiveCheckpoint; both are nonnull exactly for this checkpoint and null otherwise. Final repaired closed sets retain the cancellation receipt and reject the old attempt.
- Replacement `PredecessorSupersedeAttempt={version:1,predecessorIdentitySha256,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,deskArchiveCancellationPath,deskArchiveCancellationSha256,successorReceiptLocator,successorReceiptSha256,successorArchiveValidationLocator,successorArchiveValidationSha256,predecessorTaskPath,predecessorDoingLocator,predecessorTaskArchivePath,successorJournalSha256,repairLinkSha256,terminalCleanupSha256,phase,taskBeforeSha256,taskDoneSha256,doingBeforeSha256,doingDoneSha256,trackTargetRowBeforeSha256,trackLandedRowSha256,startedAt,updatedAt}` has phase `prepared|lifecycle_done|root_moved|validated`. In prepared, all immutable identity/locator/hash fields through terminalCleanupSha256 and the three before hashes are nonnull; the three derived done/landed hashes are null. validating_active lifecycle_done adds taskDone/doingDone/trackLanded from the one declared lifecycle transform; root_moved preserves them and proves the exact source-to-target move; validated preserves every hash. archive_in_progress first completes its existing DeskArchive attempt to a receipt without replay, then uses the done_archived_pending matrix. For done_archived_pending, lifecycle_done sets taskDone=taskBefore, doingDone=doingBefore, and trackLanded=trackTargetRowBefore without a content write; root_moved proves the already-relocated source/target without moving it; validated appends only repair protocol. Every field once nonnull is immutable, updatedAt advances once per phase, and no skipped/extra/null combination is legal. Replacement PredecessorSupersedeReceipt repeats cancellation fields and every final nonnull hash from validated.
- TrackDisposition publication is exact. The sole basename is `track-disposition.v1.json` at the already-relocated final task root before any whole-track move; its stable logical path is `task:spoonjoy-v2/<identity.task>/track-disposition.v1.json`, a registered TaskReceiptLocator. One Desk candidate adds complete bytes, BINARY-stages, commits, normal-pushes, fetches, and readback-verifies before TrackArchive may start. Response loss adopts byte-identical remote bytes; rejected push accepts only a winner whose same identity/taskArchiveKind/taskArchiveSha256/decision/generation bytes match, otherwise it rebuilds from the fresh scan or blocks. O/C local recovery is exact and no committed tree may contain partial/duplicate disposition bytes. `ReleaseTerminalResult.trackDispositionPath` is this task locator in every branch.
- TrackArchive locators are generation-qualified. Exact `TrackArchiveLocator` is `trackarchive:spoonjoy-v2/<trackGeneration>/<scanDeskSha>` and resolves only the one receipt at `<targetPath>/track-archive.v1.json` whose TrackArchive repeats both members and whose complete bytes match the caller-supplied expected hash. The old naked `track:spoonjoy-v2/track-archive.v1.json` is invalid. TrackDisposition stores this locator/hash for archived and both null for kept_active. Every task/index resolver crossing a whole-track archive carries expected TrackArchiveLocator plus hash; multiple historical generations are legal, but a context-free lookup or zero/multiple matching receipts rejects.
- TerminalPhase is exact `terminal_cleanup|desk_archive|track_archive|archive_validation|repair_index|archive_validation_final|resource_cleanup|slugger`. Both archive phases are task_artifact. Their phaseState uses `{kind:'archive_validation',role:'provisional'|'final',phase,commandResultCount}`, with role fixed by terminalPhase. They have independent owner-qualified history keys, attempts, failure paths, retry counts, wait/blocker paths, and classifiers; a final failure cannot reuse provisional history. The same code/payload precedence applies to both. The task-mutating order remains provisional validation, optional index, then fresh final validation.
- Exact `PostMergeRepairLink={version:1,dispositionKind,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,successorKey,successorTaskLocator,successorReceiptLocator,successorReceiptSha256,successorArchiveValidationLocator,successorArchiveValidationSha256,successorPrNumber,successorPrUrl,successorValidatorMergeSha,predecessorTaskLocator,predecessorReleaseRun,predecessorReleaseStatus,predecessorMergeSha,sourceDispositionPath,sourceDispositionSha256,repairBriefPaths,repairBriefSetSha256,completedAt}` replaces every older link. dispositionKind stage requires failed predecessor status and the fixed stage checkpoint; terminal requires passed status and its disposition-frozen checkpoint. successorValidatorMergeSha equals the deployed immutable leaf receipt validatorMergeSha; there is no `successorMergeSha`. repairBriefPaths is BINARY-sorted unique, and its set hash covers `{path,sha256}` entries resolved through the source disposition. Every locator/hash/identity is lineage-equal and no caller field is inferred after preparation.
- The sole `ReleaseTerminalResult` schema is exact `{mode,terminalKind,terminalCleanupPath,deskArchivePath,postMergeRepairPath,postMergeRepairRelayPath,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,consumedRepairIndexPath,createdRepairIndexPath,predecessorSupersedePath,repairLinkPath,trackDispositionPath,trackArchivePath,archiveValidationPath,sluggerPath}`. ordinary-normal is normal/ordinary with cleanup, DeskArchive, disposition, final validation nonnull; every repair/predecessor/index/link field null; trackArchive nullable by decision; slugger nonnull. repair-successor-normal is normal/repair_successor with cleanup, DeskArchive, leaf post-merge repair, created index, disposition, final validation nonnull; predecessor/consumed/relay/link null; trackArchive nullable; slugger null. repaired-intermediate is repaired/repair_intermediate with cleanup, predecessor state/checkpoint, consumed and created indexes, supersede/link/relay/disposition/final validation nonnull; DeskArchive and retained leaf post-merge repair are nonnull exactly for terminal-kind non-validating/terminal-origin as declared; trackArchive nullable; slugger null. repaired-root is repaired/repair_root with cleanup, predecessor state/checkpoint, consumed index, supersede/link/disposition/final validation and slugger nonnull; created index, relay, root post-merge repair null; DeskArchive nonnull exactly outside validating_active; trackArchive nullable. Every path belongs to its declared task/track/Desk-control locator domain. This section supersedes the four doing-doc record displays and every older result field.
- Slugger lineage is explicit. Replacement SluggerNotification replaces `mergeSha` with adjacent `rootMergeSha,deployedValidatorMergeSha`; rootMergeSha is the repaired root's original merge SHA (or ordinary merge SHA), and deployedValidatorMergeSha is the final deployed leaf validatorMergeSha, equal to rootMergeSha only for ordinary delivery. Both are immutable through every control attempt/generation/result. Depth-two tests prove A root plus C deployed leaf without substituting B or inventing one ambiguous SHA.
- Final ArchiveValidationReceipt never contains sluggerPath. Slugger eligibility/nullability belongs only to ReleaseTerminalResult and the later Desk-control notification journal. Any detail or test sentence requiring a receipt slugger member is invalid.

- Successor paths are deterministic before task creation. Let `D` be bootstrap.startedAt in UTC `YYYY-MM-DD-HHmm` and `K` the full successorKey. Exact product paths are `worker/tasks/<D>-post-merge-repair-<K>-source.md`, `worker/tasks/<D>-planning-post-merge-repair-<K>.md`, `worker/tasks/<D>-doing-post-merge-repair-<K>.md`, and `worker/tasks/<D>-doing-post-merge-repair-<K>/AUTOPILOT-STATE.md`. Exact Desk iteration root is `spoonjoy-v2/<successorSlug>/spoonjoy-v2/<YYYY-MM-DD>-post-merge-successor`; deskDoingPath is that root plus `/doing.md`. The task source/archive/track paths, branch, worktree, repoCwd, PR title/body, and every mirror path follow the existing full-key formulas with these document paths. `SuccessorDeskTaskSeed` stores them before planning. ReleaseTaskIdentity is not created at task_created: it becomes complete only at contract_approved after the exact planning/doing files exist and hash-validate; PostMergeSuccessorAttempt identityPath/identitySha256 are null before that phase. Older task_created identity requirements are invalid.
