- Successor bootstrap uses exact `BootstrapCommandResult={sequence,name,argv,cwd,expectedExitCodes,outcome,exitCode,stdoutSha256,stderrSha256}` with contiguous sequence, finite name, exact argv/cwd, sorted unique expected exits, outcome `expected|unexpected`, and sanitized complete stream hashes. The closed command registry is: canonical product cwd `git fetch origin main`; `git rev-parse refs/remotes/origin/main`; absent `git show-ref --verify --quiet refs/heads/<branch>`; `git branch <branch> <implementationBaseSha>`; `git worktree add <worktreePath> <branch>`; derived worktree `git add -- <sourcePath>`; `git write-tree`; deterministic `git commit-tree <sourceTreeSha> -p <implementationBaseSha>` with the already-declared stdin/environment; `git update-ref refs/heads/<branch> <sourceCommitSha> <implementationBaseSha>`; `git cat-file blob <sourceCommitSha>:<sourcePath>`; `git status --short`; canonical product cwd absent `git ls-remote --exit-code --heads origin refs/heads/<branch>`; the declared local-ref push with empty lease; `git fetch origin refs/heads/<branch>:refs/remotes/origin/<branch>`; matching `git ls-remote --exit-code --heads origin refs/heads/<branch>`; and `git rev-parse refs/remotes/origin/<branch>`. Every argv uses the trusted absolute Git executable at execution; logical arrays above are the persisted portable projection. Absent show-ref/ls-remote require their documented no-match exit, empty sanitized stdout where applicable, and no other nonzero is expected. Every parsed SHA is one exact lowercase 40-hex line. No shell, implicit cwd, alternate fetch refspec, bare SHA push, or unrecorded Git command is legal.
- Replacement `SuccessorBootstrapAttempt={version:1,successorKey,successorSlug,predecessorIdentitySha256,dispositionKind,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,implementationBaseSha,branch,worktreePath,deskTaskRoot,taskPath,sourcePath,phase,sourceSha256,sourceTreeSha,sourceCommitSha,remoteBranchSha,taskSeedPath,taskSeedSha256,deskTaskCommitSha,branchCreated,worktreeCreated,remoteBranchCreated,deskTaskCreated,sourceCreated,commandResults,startedAt,updatedAt}` has phase `prepared|branch_created|worktree_created|source_written|source_indexed|source_committed|remote_created|task_created|complete`. prepared has every hash after phase null, all booleans false, and exact successful fetch/base/absent-ref result prefix. branch_created sets only branchCreated; worktree_created adds only worktreeCreated; source_written adds sourceSha256 and sourceCreated; source_indexed adds sourceTreeSha; source_committed adds sourceCommitSha and requires local branch/index/worktree equal that commit; remote_created adds equal remoteBranchSha and remoteBranchCreated; task_created adds taskSeedPath/hash, deskTaskCommitSha, and deskTaskCreated after one exact Desk candidate containing task.md, task seed, source-authority links, and mirrors; complete changes no effect/hash/boolean and is the pushed/read-back checkpoint immediately replaced by the receipt. commandResults is exactly the registry prefix owned by each Git phase; source/task phases use their atomic file/Desk receipts, not synthetic command rows. Every boolean is false before and true from its named phase onward. There is no identityCreated field. Replacement SuccessorBootstrapReceipt repeats every immutable non-null path/hash/commit and all five true booleans, omits identityPath/identitySha256, and completedAt equals complete.updatedAt.
- Task-seed bytes are deterministic. `SuccessorDeskTaskSeed={version:1,slug,title,status:'processing',createdAt,updatedAt,track:'spoonjoy-v2',requester:'ari',validator:'ari',planningComplete:false,adoptedAt,repoName:'spoonjoy-v2',repoLocalPath,repoMode:'local',iterationSlug,iterationTrigger:'repair-successor',iterationOutcome:'in-progress',sourcePath,planningPath,doingPath,continuityPath,deskIterationPath,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint}` is compact canonical with title=`Repair <successorKey>`, createdAt=updatedAt=adoptedAt=bootstrap.startedAt, iterationSlug=`<YYYY-MM-DD>-post-merge-successor`, repoLocalPath=worktreePath, and all paths equal the deterministic formulas. Its exact task.md renderer uses LF only and one final LF: `---\nschema_version: 1\ntitle: "<title>"\nstatus: processing\ncreated: "<createdAt>"\nupdated: "<updatedAt>"\ntrack: spoonjoy-v2\nrequester: "ari"\nvalidator: "ari"\nplanning_complete: false\nadopted_at: "<adoptedAt>"\nrepos:\n  - name: spoonjoy-v2\n    local_path: <repoLocalPath>\n    mode: local\niterations:\n  active: ./spoonjoy-v2/<iterationSlug>\n  history:\n    - slug: <iterationSlug>\n      repo: spoonjoy-v2\n      trigger: repair-successor\n      pr: null\n      path: ./spoonjoy-v2/<iterationSlug>\n      outcome: in-progress\n---\n\n# <title>\n\nRepair successor `<successorKey>` for predecessor `<predecessorIdentitySha256>`.\n\n## Source authority\n\n- Source: `<sourcePath>`\n- Planning: `<planningPath>`\n- Doing: `<doingPath>`\n- Continuity: `<continuityPath>`\n`. Placeholder values must satisfy their declared scalar grammar and are escaped by rejecting LF, CR, quote, backtick, or YAML-control bytes. Parsing and rerendering must be byte-identical; partial/mismatched task/seed bytes reject.
- Successor suite dispatch is paused and durable. Exact `SuccessorSuiteDispatchIntent={version:1,successorKey,kind,ordinal,invocationToken,promptPath,promptSha256,cwd,planningPath,doingPath,createdAt}` lives at the declared intent path and is appended/pushed/read back before calling `AgentRuntimeAdapter.prepare`. prepare is create-once by invocationToken and returns a paused canonical agentId that cannot read/write the worktree. Exact `SuccessorSuiteDispatchReceipt={version:1,intentPath,intentSha256,invocationToken,agentId,preparedAt,releasedAt}` is written with releasedAt null, appended/pushed/read back, then adapter.release atomically starts that exact paused agent and a final immutable receipt with canonical releasedAt replaces the null candidate through the declared candidate-to-final checkpoint. Adapter.probe(invocationToken) returns exact `absent|paused|running|completed|errored` plus matching nullable agentId/report; only absent before prepare, paused before release, running after release, or terminal after release is legal. Intent-only recovery probes and prepares/adopts once; pushed receipt with null releasedAt releases/adopts once; released/running never redispatches; an unobservable or contradictory runtime becomes uncertain and forbids another agent until honest terminal proof or operator repair. Tests crash every intent/prepare/receipt/release boundary.
- Replacement `SuccessorSuiteAttempt={kind,ordinal,status,skill,cwd,promptPath,promptSha256,planningPath,doingPath,invocationToken,dispatchIntentPath,dispatchIntentSha256,dispatchPath,dispatchSha256,agentId,artifacts,artifactSetSha256,startedAt,deadlineAt,endedAt}` has status `prepared|dispatching|running|uncertain|interrupted|completed`. prepared has token/prompt/bindings and null dispatch/agent/end/artifact hash with empty artifacts. dispatching adds intent only. running adds authorized dispatch receipt and agentId after runtime release. uncertain retains the longest exact prefix, endedAt null, and forbids redispatch. interrupted is legal only after terminal errored/cancelled probe, has endedAt, agentId as observed, empty artifacts/null set hash. completed has terminal completed probe, endedAt/agentId, and exact nonempty `SuiteArtifactRef={kind,path,sha256}[]`; the finite kind/path set is planner `{planning,doing,review}` or doer `{registry,command,unit_red,unit_receipt,review_prompt,review_dispatch_intent,review_dispatch,review_runtime,review_report,verification,coverage,implementation_receipt}` and is derived from validated files/runtime results, never caller JSON. Fields once present are immutable.
- Planner prompt bytes are exact UTF-8 LF text with one final LF: `Spoonjoy repair successor planner v1\nsuccessor_key: <K>\nsource_path: <sourcePath>\nrepair_brief_path: <briefPath>\nrepair_brief_sha256: <briefSha256>\nplanning_path: <planningPath>\ndoing_path: <doingPath>\ncontinuity_path: <continuityPath>\nworktree: <worktreePath>\nskill: work-planner\nrules: preserve operator-locked scope; create only implementation red/green/verification units; exclude Units32-37; run fresh reviewer convergence; write exactly the named planning and doing paths; return only validated artifact locators\n`. Doer prompt bytes are exact: `Spoonjoy repair successor doer v1\nsuccessor_key: <K>\nidentity_path: <identityPath>\nidentity_sha256: <identitySha256>\nplanning_path: <planningPath>\nplanning_sha256: <planningSha256>\ndoing_path: <doingPath>\ndoing_sha256: <doingSha256>\nhandoff_path: <handoffPath>\nhandoff_sha256: <handoffSha256>\nworktree: <worktreePath>\nskill: work-doer\nrules: execute only reviewed implementation units with strict TDD; produce immutable command, red, unit, reviewer, verification, coverage, and implementation receipts; do not run Units32-37; return only validated artifact locators\n`. Every placeholder is validated, no CR/control/extra line is legal, and start-planning/start-implementation results omit raw prompt and return only skill/cwd/prompt path/hash/document bindings plus invocationToken.
- Exact `SuccessorHandoff={version:1,successorKey,identityPath,identitySha256,repairBriefPaths,repairBriefSetSha256,planningPath,planningSha256,doingPath,doingSha256,plannerSuiteAttemptPath,plannerSuiteAttemptSha256,plannerReviewPaths,plannerReviewSetSha256,approvedAt}` lives at `artifacts/post-merge-successor/handoff.v1.json`. It is derived only after the planner attempt completed, planning status approved, doing reviewer gate converged, all reviewer bytes hash-valid, and ReleaseTaskIdentity deterministically matches the reviewed paths. Arrays are BINARY-sorted unique `{path,sha256}`-hashed sets. `record-handoff` accepts this file path only, validates every cross-link, writes no caller JSON, and returns its path/hash.
- Successor implementation evidence is dispatch-bound. `SuccessorCommandEvidence={version:1,successorKey,unitId,ordinal,argv,cwd,expected,startedAt,endedAt,exitCode,signal,stdoutPath,stdoutSha256,stderrPath,stderrSha256,warningCount,sourceHeadSha,treeSha}` lives at `artifacts/post-merge-successor/commands/<unitId>/command-<ordinal>.v1.json`; expected is red|green, paths name immutable sanitized logs, and field/exit/signal/warning matrices are exact. `SuccessorRedEvidence={version:1,successorKey,unitId,commandEvidencePath,commandEvidenceSha256,failingTestIds,expectedFailureCodes,sourceBaseSha,treeSha,createdAt}` lives at the one red path and requires a nonempty BINARY set plus a real expected-red nonzero command before implementation. Replacement `SuccessorImplementationUnitReceipt={version:1,successorKey,unitId,phase,status:'completed',sourceBaseSha,sourceHeadSha,treeSha,redEvidencePath,redEvidenceSha256,commandEvidencePaths,commandEvidenceSetSha256,artifactPaths,artifactSetSha256,completedAt}` uses phase `test|implementation|verification`; test alone requires red fields and every phase requires its exact nonempty command set. Replacement `SuccessorVerificationArtifact={version:1,successorKey,unitId,commandEvidencePath,commandEvidenceSha256,sourceHeadSha,treeSha,createdAt}` names one green command evidence. Every path/set is BINARY unique and hashes complete pairs.
- Every successor review uses the same paused intent/receipt runtime protocol. Exact `SuccessorReviewDispatchIntent={version:1,successorKey,role,invocationToken,promptPath,promptSha256,inputArtifacts,inputArtifactSetSha256,sourceHeadSha,treeSha,createdAt}` lives at `reviews/<role>/dispatch-intent.v1.json` and is appended/pushed/read back before `AgentRuntimeAdapter.prepare`. Exact `SuccessorReviewDispatch={version:1,successorKey,role,intentPath,intentSha256,invocationToken,promptPath,promptSha256,inputArtifacts,inputArtifactSetSha256,sourceHeadSha,treeSha,agentId,authorizedAt}` lives at the declared review dispatch path, is derived after paused prepare, and is appended/pushed/read back before the create-once runtime release bound to its hash. Exact replacement `SuccessorReviewReport={version:1,successorKey,role,verdict:'clean',dispatchPath,dispatchSha256,promptPath,promptSha256,inputArtifacts,inputArtifactSetSha256,agentId,returnedReportPath,returnedReportSha256,sourceHeadSha,treeSha,completedAt}` binds the immutable sanitized runtime copy at `reviews/<role>/runtime-report.txt` and independently derived reviewed set. Review prompt bytes use the existing exact role scopes plus successorKey, source/tree, input-set hash, and read-only/no-edit verdict grammar. Each role uses a distinct invocation token/agent, and intent-only, paused, released, running, terminal, and uncertain recovery follows the suite protocol without redispatch. No report may be projected from unjournaled prose, caller JSON, a changed input set, or a missing terminal runtime result.
- SuccessorImplementationRegistry and PostMergeImplementationEvidence accept only the closed command/red/unit/review/verification/coverage artifacts above. Every set hash includes complete path/hash pairs; every unit/source/tree/role equals the parsed doing registry and final pushed head; red evidence predates its implementation command; all green commands exit zero with zero warnings; review dispatches are terminal clean; and coverage cross-links the command logs. Any inline-only command hash, missing log locator, self-asserted review, arbitrary path, or synthesized zero-line proof rejects.
- RepairBrief is derived by a total registry. Exact `RepairBrief={version:1,code,artifactPath,artifactSha256,reviewerRole,promptSha256,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,affectedSurfaces,createdAt}` lives at `artifacts/post-merge-repair/briefs/brief-<positive>.v1.json`; reviewerRole/prompt are both nonnull only for review_finding and both null otherwise. affectedSurfaces is exact `{ui,api,migrationConfig}` and is derived from the disposition logicalName registry: visual/UI/E2E names set ui; API/MCP/lifecycle-smoke names set api; migration/deploy/workflow/config/build/cleanup names set migrationConfig; a name in multiple classes sets every matching bit; provenance and configuration always set migrationConfig; cleanup with no matched product surface sets all false; review_finding derives classes from each discriminated ReviewFinding file; unknown names/domains reject. `ReviewFinding.file` is exact `{domain:'repo'|'task',path}` and resolves under only that root. repairBriefPaths are BINARY-sorted by normalized path, and repairBriefSetSha256 hashes exact `{path,sha256}[]`; every successor/link uses that pair instead of ownerless `repairBriefSha256s`.

- Security-critical preflight authority lives here, not in UNIT-29.2-DETAIL. Exact `ProcessPreflight={public,secret}` uses the existing exact ProcessPreflightPublic plus in-memory-only `ProcessPreflightSecret={cloudflareD1ApiToken,cloudflareRestBearer}`; each secret is string|null, nonempty only for its exact policy, and this object is never serialized, logged, hashed, returned, or placed in an ordinary environment. The sole D1-token hash exception remains only the named cleanup recovery prepared/failed journal and disappears from successful closed sets. Common public environment is PATH, HOME, CI=1, NO_COLOR=1, FORCE_COLOR=0 plus TMPDIR iff resolved; local-db adds exact DATABASE_URL; github uses GitHub credentials; cloudflare adds account; cloudflare-rest adds the one-shot OAuth descriptor; cloudflare-d1 adds account plus a fresh one-shot D1 descriptor per child; cloudflare-github combines public GitHub/Cloudflare proofs. Exact `executionHost` is lowercase SHA-256 of UTF-8 compact canonical `{hostname,username,platform,arch,home,repoRealPath,deskRealPath}` with no LF after NFC/path validation. UNIT-29.2-DETAIL owns exhaustive tests only and may not define a different schema, key, preimage, or environment.
- Executable identity is frozen before any credential probe or secret-bearing child. Exact `TrustedExecutable={name,absolutePath,realPath,device,inode,mode,uid,size,sha256,version}` and `TrustedToolchain={version:1,node,pnpm,gh,git,ps,security,wranglerEntry,cloudflareClient,checkedAt}` are no-extra-fields. Paths are absolute, real, regular non-symlinks; device/inode/size/mode/uid and complete-file hash are read from one `O_RDONLY|O_NOFOLLOW` descriptor, version is obtained through that same frozen target, and repository entries additionally hash-match the locked package/install graph. Production argv uses these absolute targets, never PATH lookup. The descriptor remains open through spawn; immediate pre-spawn and post-spawn fstat/hash identity must match, and the child wrapper verifies its own entry hash before reading a secret descriptor. Replacement, writable-path substitution, malicious PATH, symlink, inode drift, hash/version drift, or descriptor inheritance rejects before secret acquisition. Secret-bearing Cloudflare children use trusted absolute Node plus the hash-frozen first-party cloudflare client or trusted Wrangler entry; no bare `pnpm`, `wrangler`, `gh`, or shell receives a raw secret.
- Provider probes use strict duplicate-key-rejecting UTF-8 JSON decoding with finite size/depth/member caps. Unknown external fields are ignored only after the complete required projection validates; missing, duplicate, wrong-type, noncanonical identifier, excess cap, or conflicting duplicate entity blocks. GitHub auth argv is trusted-gh `auth status --hostname github.com --json hosts`; required raw projection is `hosts['github.com']` containing exactly one selected record with `state:'success',active:true,host:'github.com',login` nonempty, scopes string, and gitProtocol string. GitHub Actions argv is trusted-gh `api --method GET repos/spoonjoy/spoonjoy-v2/actions/workflows?per_page=1`; raw requires nonnegative safe `total_count` and workflows array whose first member has positive id, path, state, url. Cloudflare account argv is trusted-node plus trusted Wrangler entry `whoami --json`; raw requires `loggedIn:true,authType:'OAuth Token'`, one account with id equal configured CLOUDFLARE_ACCOUNT_ID, nonempty name, and a tokenPermissions string array. OAuth argv is the same target `auth token --json`; raw requires exact selected projection `{type:'oauth',token}` with one NUL/LF-free UTF-8 token 1..4096 bytes, retained only in ProcessPreflightSecret. D1 list argv is the trusted secret-descriptor child `d1 list --json`; raw requires an array with exactly one selected `{uuid,name}` matching configured database id/name and finite canonical metadata types. Exit zero without these projections is blocked, and nonzero/timeout/signal/sanitizer failure takes precedence before parser errors. Only the existing no-extra-fields sanitized CapabilityEntry proofs persist.
- The independent production executable classifier is exact and case-sensitive over normalized tracked regular non-symlink repo paths. Inclusion is `app/**/*.{ts,tsx}`, `workers/**/*.{ts,tsx}`, `scripts/**/*.{ts,mts,mjs}`, and present root `vite.config.ts|vitest.config.ts|playwright.config.ts|react-router.config.ts`. Exclusion is basename suffix `.d.ts` or any exact path segment `test|tests|__tests__|fixtures|generated|node_modules|coverage|dist|build|.react-router|.wrangler`; no substring, case-folded, backslash, percent-decoded, symlink, untracked, ignored, directory, or generated-map interpretation is legal. `public/build` is excluded by the build segment. Every included diff path must occur in the independent instrumented set; an included changed path with no instrumentation rejects rather than becoming not_applicable. Tests enumerate each segment at every depth, near-match/case variant, separators, symlinks, tracked status, root files, and empty/nonempty intersections.
- API smoke evidence is exact. `ApiSmokeCheck={name,status:'passed',requestPath,responsePath,exchangeSha256}` uses name `health|auth|recipes|shopping|saved_recipes|tags|mcp`, each exactly once in that order, and hashes one schema-valid SanitizedExchange whose transport/status/body oracle matches the check. `ApiSmokeReport={version:1,targetBaseUrl,sourceSha,workerVersionId,checks,artifactPaths,artifactSetSha256,passed:true,completedAt}` lives at `api-smoke-results.json`; target/source/version match the release, artifact paths are the exact BINARY-sorted request/response evidence set, and passed is derivable only when all seven checks validate with no error exchange. The shared streaming sanitizer, sensitive-header/key filter, fatal UTF-8/NUL rejection, partial-output deletion, recursive secret-sentinel scan, semantic parser, and complete-file hash acceptance apply before any API artifact or report can enter evidence.
- Lifecycle smoke evidence is exact. `LifecycleSmokeReport={version:1,targetBaseUrl,sourceSha,workerVersionId,identity,lifecycleEvents,lifecycleEventsSha256,attempts,finalResidues,cleanupOutcomePath,cleanupOutcomeSha256,artifactPaths,artifactSetSha256,passed:true,completedAt}` lives at `smoke-results.json`. identity is the exact CleanupIdentity; lifecycleEvents is the already-declared contiguous canonical event sequence and its hash covers compact canonical bytes; attempts are the exact A/B sanitized snapshots and terminal/replacement cross-links; finalResidues byte-equal the cleanup retained proof; cleanup outcome cross-validates every target, retirement, D1/user deletion, and zero-residue flag; artifactPaths is the exact closed lifecycle set. passed is accepted only after every event, frame, exchange, residue, cleanup proof, sanitizer scan, and cross-hash validates. The old property-only lifecycleEvents description is invalid. API and lifecycle raw bodies, provider errors, stdout/stderr, and exception text never persist outside their declared sanitized unions.
- Successor implementation and release ingestion share one anti-fabrication rule: a hash alone never establishes semantics. Every command/reviewer/smoke/visual/provider artifact is accepted only after its no-extra-fields parser, finite pass oracle, identity/attempt/time/path cross-links, sanitization scan, and immutable producer dispatch/result validate. Any missing producer receipt, raw free text, unknown enum, mutable file, orphan log hash, self-reported pass boolean, or semantically invalid but hash-correct bytes rejects.

- Suite dispatch receipts are immutable authorization, not null-to-final records. Replace the earlier Round 61 dispatch receipt with exact `SuccessorSuiteDispatchReceipt={version:1,intentPath,intentSha256,invocationToken,agentId,preparedAt,authorizedAt}`; every field is nonnull, authorizedAt is the one clock reading frozen immediately after paused prepare, and complete bytes are appended/pushed/read back before `AgentRuntimeAdapter.release(invocationToken,agentId,dispatchSha256)`. The adapter's create-once release binds that receipt hash and returns/probes runtime start state; it cannot execute before the receipt is remote-readable. There is no releasedAt-null candidate and no rewrite of dispatch bytes. Intent-only and intent+paused-agent recovery use adapter.probe as declared; a pushed receipt authorizes exactly one release, and runtime proof supplies running/terminal state without modifying the receipt.
- Replacement PostMergeSuccessorAttempt retains the Round 60 exact field list but uses this sole matrix: prepared has every bootstrap/task/document/identity/handoff/manifest/implementation path/hash null, suites/waits empty, wait hash null; task_created adds bootstrapPath/hash, taskPath, and taskSeedPath/hash only; planning_running permits only planner suites/waits and keeps planning/doing/identity null; contract_approved adds planning/doing and successor identity path/hash plus a latest completed planner suite; handoff_recorded adds handoff; manifest_ready adds manifest path/hash/writer and exact registered pre-release prefix; implementation_running permits doer suites/waits with implementation evidence null; implementation_complete requires latest completed doer plus exact closed pre-release set and implementation evidence. identity is therefore never present at task_created. Every dispatching/running/uncertain suite state must be legal for the owning phase, and every nonnull field is immutable.
- Exact replacement `SuccessorBootstrapReceipt={version:1,successorKey,successorSlug,predecessorIdentitySha256,dispositionKind,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,implementationBaseSha,branch,worktreePath,deskTaskRoot,taskPath,sourcePath,sourceSha256,sourceTreeSha,sourceCommitSha,remoteBranchSha,taskSeedPath,taskSeedSha256,deskTaskCommitSha,branchCreated:true,worktreeCreated:true,remoteBranchCreated:true,deskTaskCreated:true,sourceCreated:true,commandResults,completedAt}` replaces every earlier bootstrap receipt. commandResults is the complete successful closed registry, completedAt equals complete.updatedAt, and the receipt contains no identity path/hash.
- Track archive hashing is acyclic. Replacement `TrackDisposition={version:1,track:'spoonjoy-v2',triggerTask,taskArchiveKind,taskArchiveSha256,decision,remainingUnarchivedTasks,scanDeskSha,trackGeneration,targetPath,trackArchiveLocator,trackArchiveExpectedSha256,completedAt}` has both archive fields null for kept_active and both nonnull for archived. For archived, release-terminal freezes exact final TrackArchive bytes before disposition publication; those bytes exclude their own hash and use completedAt equal disposition.completedAt, so their complete SHA-256 is trackArchiveExpectedSha256. Replacement `TrackArchiveAttempt={version:1,track:'spoonjoy-v2',sourcePath:'spoonjoy-v2',targetPath,triggerTask,taskArchiveKind,taskArchiveSha256,scanDeskSha,trackGeneration,trackArchiveLocator,trackArchiveExpectedSha256,trackBeforeSha256,trackClosedSha256,remainingUnarchivedTasks:[],phase,trackClosed,sourceTreeMoved,targetPresent,archiveValid,startedAt,updatedAt}` may carry the expected hash. Exact final `TrackArchive={version:1,track:'spoonjoy-v2',sourcePath:'spoonjoy-v2',targetPath,triggerTask,taskArchiveKind,taskArchiveSha256,scanDeskSha,trackGeneration,trackBeforeSha256,trackClosedSha256,remainingUnarchivedTasks:[],trackClosed:true,sourceTreeMoved:true,targetPresent:true,archiveValid:true,completedAt}` does not. Its bytes must hash to the disposition/attempt expected value. The old `trackArchiveSha256` self-reference and any final receipt containing its expected hash are invalid.
- Replacement SluggerNotification is exact `{version:1,task,rootMergeSha,deployedValidatorMergeSha,message,ownershipGeneration:1,writerId,phase,generation,resultPath,resultSha256,completedAt,updatedAt}` in that field order and otherwise retains the declared one-generation phase/null matrix. Replacement SluggerSpawnGeneration changes only `processStartIdentity` to exact `processIdentity:ProcessIdentity` and retains its full existing field order around that member. Every gate/adoption/liveness/result schema uses the same processIdentity bytes; a free-form processStartIdentity string is invalid. TrustedExecutable.version is a nonempty semantic version for versioned tools and exact literal `not_applicable` for Git/ps/security targets whose identity is fully frozen by path/inode/hash.
- Every persisted process owner uses ProcessIdentity. Replacement `ManifestLockOwner={version:1,writerId,token,executionHost,hostname,pid,processIdentity,acquiredAt}` supersedes the old free-form start field. Exact record argv is `record-process --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt A --generation N --pid I --pgid J --process-identity-json X`, where X is compact canonical ProcessIdentity; the old `--process-start-identity` flag rejects. Its success is `{generation,status:'recorded',pid,pgid,processIdentity}`. Ensure/Slugger adoption, lock death, handoff, timeout, and reap use the same schema/hash probe and cannot compare an opaque string.
- Command logs are first-class pre-release artifacts. `PreReleaseArtifact.kind` additionally includes `command_log`; the complete pre-release registry additionally includes `commands/<unitId>/command-<positive>-stdout.log` and `commands/<unitId>/command-<positive>-stderr.log`, each mapped only to `command_log`. Every `SuccessorCommandEvidence.stdoutPath` and `.stderrPath` names those exact immutable sanitized files, and each log is appended and pushed/read back before its command-evidence record. `SuiteArtifactRef.kind` for doer additionally includes `command_log`. A command record whose logs are absent, unregistered, mutable, path-mismatched, or hash-mismatched rejects.
- Resource-cleanup journals are ordinal. The replacement `TerminalResourceCleanupAttempt` lives only at `_meta/release-terminal/<identitySha256>/attempts/resource_cleanup/attempt-<attemptOrdinal>.v1.json` as the `TerminalControlAttempt.phaseState`; the older fixed mutable basename `_meta/release-terminal/<identitySha256>/terminal-resource-cleanup.attempt.v1.json` is invalid. Its inserted fields and all source/prior-result links obey the TerminalControlAttempt ordinal matrix, so a failed attempt is immutable evidence and a later attempt receives a new positive contiguous ordinal rather than rewriting history.
- The supersede receipt is complete. Exact replacement `PredecessorSupersedeReceipt={version:1,predecessorIdentitySha256,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,deskArchiveCancellationPath,deskArchiveCancellationSha256,successorReceiptLocator,successorReceiptSha256,successorArchiveValidationLocator,successorArchiveValidationSha256,predecessorTaskPath,predecessorDoingLocator,predecessorTaskArchivePath,successorJournalSha256,repairLinkSha256,terminalCleanupSha256,taskSourcePath,taskArchivePath,doingLocator,prNumber,prUrl,validatorMergeSha,taskBeforeSha256,taskDoneSha256,doingBeforeSha256,doingDoneSha256,trackTargetRowBeforeSha256,trackLandedRowSha256,sourceAbsent:true,targetPresent:true,archiveValid:true,completedAt}` is written only from the validated attempt. The cancellation members are both nonnull exactly for validating_active/prepared and both null otherwise; every remaining hash is the byte-identical final nonnull attempt value or its independently validated release/locator projection. No field-list shorthand or older receipt schema remains valid.
- Persisted preflight proof includes the frozen executables. Exact replacement `ProcessPreflightPublic={version:1,logicalName,environmentPolicy,path,home,tmpdir,envNames,accountId,executionHost,trustedToolchain,capabilities,checkedAt}` has `trustedToolchain:TrustedToolchain`, captured and validated before any provider or secret probe. The public proof persists no descriptor or secret, but it does persist the complete trusted path/inode/hash/version identities used by every declared argv. Any later command whose executable projection differs from this frozen member rejects before secret acquisition or spawn.
- Red and final source identities are intentionally different. An expected-red `SuccessorCommandEvidence` and its `SuccessorRedEvidence` use the immutable pre-implementation source head/tree, which is either `implementationBaseSha` and its tree or the pushed predecessor unit head/tree frozen by the doing order; they must not equal a later final tree merely because final receipts do. Green command evidence, unit receipts after their implementation, verification artifacts, review reports, coverage, and `PostMergeImplementationEvidence` use the applicable pushed post-implementation head/tree, with the final closed set converging on `implementationHeadSha` and `implementationTreeSha`. Exact ancestry, unit order, timestamps, dispatch receipts, and Git object lookup prove the transition. A red command run after implementation, a green command bound only to the base tree, or false red/final tree equality rejects.

### Round 61 Parent-Audit Closures

The clauses below are the final Round 61 refinements and replace every conflicting Round 61 clause above.

- Terminal successful payloads use one closed registry. Exact no-extra-fields payloads are `TerminalFilesystemSuccess={operation,locator,beforeStateSha256,afterStateSha256,disposition:'applied'|'reconciled'}`, with operation `rename|unlink|rmdir|scan|fsync`; `TerminalDeskGitSuccess={operation,oldDeskSha,newDeskSha,commitSha,remoteSha,disposition:'pushed'|'adopted'}`, with operation `task_archive|track_archive|repair_index|terminal_evidence|desk_control|slugger_checkpoint`; `TerminalValidatorSuccess={operation,sourceSha,archiveSha256,memberSetSha256}`, with operation `build|member_scan|validate`; and `TerminalProviderSuccess={provider:'github'|'cloudflare'|'ouro',operation,requestSha256,responseSha256,statusCode}`, with statusCode a safe integer 100..599. `TerminalSuccessfulResult.resultKind/result` is exactly `terminal_command:TerminalCommandResult`, `archive_validation_command:ArchiveValidationCommandResult`, `filesystem:TerminalFilesystemSuccess`, `desk_git:TerminalDeskGitSuccess`, `validator:TerminalValidatorSuccess`, `provider:TerminalProviderSuccess`, or `slugger_process:SluggerProcessResult`. Legal phase kinds are terminal_cleanup `terminal_command|filesystem|validator`; desk_archive, track_archive, and repair_index `filesystem|desk_git`; archive_validation and archive_validation_final `archive_validation_command|validator`; resource_cleanup `filesystem`; and slugger `filesystem|desk_git|provider|slugger_process`. storageDomain is `task_artifact` for the first six task phases and `desk_control` for resource_cleanup/slugger. logicalName equals the selected result's name or operation and belongs to that phase's finite registry. No untagged object, alternate result type, or cross-phase kind is legal.
- Desk-control state is a projection, not a nested duplicate attempt. Exact `TerminalResourceCleanupState={kind:'resource_cleanup',validatorRuntimePath,validatorRuntimeDeletePath,validatorArchivePath,validatorArchiveDeletePath,validatorArchiveSha256,runtimeManifest,runtimeManifestSha256,phase,nextDeleteIndex,runtimeDetached,archiveDetached,archiveDeleted}` retains the declared member-deletion order and phase/boolean matrix. Exact `TerminalSluggerState={kind:'slugger',notificationPath,notificationSha256,notification,generation}` contains one complete SluggerNotification and its complete SluggerSpawnGeneration, whose identities/phases cross-validate. `TerminalControlPhaseState` is exactly that union, and `TerminalControlAttempt.phaseState` is one member. The wrapper alone owns version, identitySha256, executionHost, terminalPhase, attemptOrdinal, source/prior-failure/prior-success links, startedAt, and updatedAt; neither phase state repeats them. The standalone `TerminalResourceCleanupAttempt` name and every fixed-basename or inserted-duplicate-field schema are invalid. resource_cleanup selects only the resource state; slugger selects only the Slugger state. Every phase-state transition is an atomic wrapper rewrite, while failed wrappers and successful-result files are immutable.
- Track archive attestation is payload-based and acyclic. Final replacement `TrackDisposition={version:1,track:'spoonjoy-v2',triggerTask,taskArchiveKind,taskArchiveSha256,decision,remainingUnarchivedTasks,scanDeskSha,trackGeneration,targetPath,trackArchiveLocator,completedAt}` has decision kept_active with nonempty remaining tasks and null locator, or archived with empty tasks and exact locator `trackarchive:spoonjoy-v2/<trackGeneration>/<scanDeskSha>`. It contains no TrackArchive hash. After disposition is pushed/read back, exact `TrackArchiveMember={relativePath,sha256}` enumerates every regular non-symlink source-track file in BINARY path order, including the task-root disposition and closed track frontmatter, while excluding only `track-archive.attempt.v1.json` and `track-archive.v1.json`; directories are implicit and every other file is included. Exact `TrackArchiveAttempt={version:1,track:'spoonjoy-v2',sourcePath:'spoonjoy-v2',targetPath,triggerTask,taskArchiveKind,taskArchiveSha256,scanDeskSha,trackGeneration,trackArchiveLocator,sourceMembers,sourceMemberSetSha256,targetMemberSetSha256,remainingUnarchivedTasks:[],phase,trackClosed,sourceTreeMoved,targetPresent,archiveValid,startedAt,updatedAt}` is prepared before the move with targetMemberSetSha256 null; root_moved recomputes the same exclusion-based target manifest and requires equality; archive_validated preserves it. Exact final `TrackArchive={version:1,track:'spoonjoy-v2',sourcePath:'spoonjoy-v2',targetPath,triggerTask,taskArchiveKind,taskArchiveSha256,scanDeskSha,trackGeneration,trackArchiveLocator,sourceMemberSetSha256,targetMemberSetSha256,remainingUnarchivedTasks:[],trackClosed:true,sourceTreeMoved:true,targetPresent:true,archiveValid:true,completedAt}` replaces the attempt and requires both member-set hashes equal. Callers then hash the complete final receipt bytes. Exact replacement `ArchiveValidationReceipt={version:1,attemptOrdinal,priorFailedAttemptPaths,priorFailedAttemptSetSha256,mergeSha,validatorMergeSha,executionHost,validatorRuntimePath,validatorArchivePath,validatorArchiveSha256,validatorSourceTreeSha256,manifestPath,trackDecision,trackDispositionSha256,trackDispositionCommitSha,trackArchiveLocator,trackArchiveSha256,repairIndexPath,repairIndexSha256,commandResult,validatedAt}` has both TrackArchive members null for kept_active and both nonnull/hash-valid for archived. This final validation runs after TrackArchive receipt publication, so the relocated task durably carries the generation-qualified locator plus independently computed receipt hash. Every `trackArchiveExpectedSha256`, `trackClosedSha256`, self-hash, and pre-disposition payload hash is invalid.
- Successor bootstrap is prepared-first. A compact canonical SuccessorBootstrapAttempt with phase prepared, commandResults empty, every derived hash null, and every boolean false is atomically written and pushed/read back before `git fetch` or any other command. While phase remains prepared, each of fetch, base rev-parse, and absent local-ref probe appends its immutable BootstrapCommandResult and pushes/readbacks the wrapper before the next command; only these zero-to-three contiguous results are legal there. branch_created requires the exact first four results through branch creation; worktree_created the first five; each later phase adds exactly the command/file/Desk receipt prefix for its named effect. No effect may precede its prior wrapper checkpoint. A lost fetch response may rerun only the same safe fetch; every later mutation uses its exact pre/post-state recovery rule. The earlier prepared state with a pre-populated successful prefix is invalid.
- Suite attempts have an authorized paused state. Final status domain is `prepared|dispatching|authorized|running|uncertain|interrupted|completed`. prepared has no intent, receipt, or agent. dispatching adds the pushed/read-back intent only. authorized adds the pushed/read-back immutable dispatch receipt and canonical agentId while `AgentRuntimeAdapter.probe` is paused; no worktree read/write has begun. running is legal only after create-once release returns or probe proves running. completed and interrupted require probe completed and errored respectively; there is no cancelled probe result. uncertain retains the longest legal prefix after an unobservable/contradictory adapter result and forbids redispatch. PostMergeSuccessorAttempt permits authorized suite entries in the same owning phase. Suite and review dispatch receipts are never rewritten.
- Handoff artifacts are registered. `PreReleaseArtifact.kind` additionally includes `suite_attempt|planner_review`, and the path registry additionally includes immutable completed `suite/<planner|doer>/attempt-<positive>.v1.json` plus `suite/planner/attempt-<positive>-review-<positive>.v1.json`. A suite attempt path is appendable only after completed and then immutable. Exact `SuccessorPlannerReview={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,reviewOrdinal,agentId,verdict:'approved',planningPath,planningSha256,doingPath,doingSha256,promptPath,promptSha256,returnedReportPath,returnedReportSha256,completedAt}` is the planner-review artifact; ordinals are contiguous, agentIds distinct, and the final review set is the completed planner attempt's BINARY-sorted `planner_review` artifact projection. `SuccessorHandoff.plannerSuiteAttemptPath` is exactly the completed planner suite path, and plannerReviewPaths is exactly that nonempty final review set; both set hashes cover complete `{path,sha256}` pairs and every path is registered before handoff.
- Planner review producers and SuiteArtifactRef kinds are final. `PreReleaseArtifact.kind` additionally includes `planner_review_prompt|planner_review_runtime`; exact paths are `suite/planner/attempt-<positive>-review-<positive>-prompt.txt` and `suite/planner/attempt-<positive>-review-<positive>-runtime-report.txt`. Every SuccessorPlannerReview.promptPath and returnedReportPath names those ordinal-matched files, which are appended/pushed/read back before the final planner_review report. Final `SuiteArtifactRef.kind` sets are planner `planning|doing|planner_review_prompt|planner_review_runtime|planner_review` and doer `registry|command|command_log|red_tree|unit_red|unit_receipt|review_prompt|review_dispatch_intent|review_dispatch|review_runtime|review_report|verification|coverage|implementation_receipt`; each kind has exactly its final registered path grammar. Completed suite attempt receipts are appended separately after terminal projection and never list themselves. A running suite exists only inside the owning PostMergeSuccessorAttempt; no mutable `suite/.../attempt-<n>.v1.json` file exists before the immutable completed projection.
- Planner reviews are dispatch-bound. `PreReleaseArtifact.kind` additionally includes `planner_review_dispatch_intent|planner_review_dispatch`; exact paths are `suite/planner/attempt-<positive>-review-<positive>-dispatch-intent.v1.json` and `suite/planner/attempt-<positive>-review-<positive>-dispatch.v1.json`. Exact `SuccessorPlannerReviewDispatchIntent={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,reviewOrdinal,role,invocationToken,promptPath,promptSha256,planningPath,planningSha256,doingPath,doingSha256,createdAt}` and `SuccessorPlannerReviewDispatch={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,reviewOrdinal,role,intentPath,intentSha256,invocationToken,agentId,authorizedAt}` use the paused intent/authorized receipt/release protocol. Roles and ordinals are exactly `scope`/1, `contract`/2, and `test`/3 for every planner attempt. Replacement `SuccessorPlannerReview={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,reviewOrdinal,role,agentId,verdict:'approved',planningPath,planningSha256,doingPath,doingSha256,promptPath,promptSha256,dispatchPath,dispatchSha256,returnedReportPath,returnedReportSha256,completedAt}` cross-links the matching authorized dispatch and terminal runtime copy. The final planner SuiteArtifactRef kinds additionally include `planner_review_dispatch_intent|planner_review_dispatch`, and handoff requires all three role-complete report chains with distinct agents. No self-asserted planner review or unjournaled reviewer prose is legal.
- Successor prompts bind sets and roles exactly. The final planner prompt replaces singular brief lines with `repair_briefs_json: <briefsJson>` and `repair_brief_set_sha256: <briefSetSha256>`, where briefsJson is one-line compact canonical BINARY-path-sorted unique `[{path,sha256}]` with at least one member and its set hash; every other planner line/order remains the declared exact template. Exact review scope strings are api_compatibility=`API compatibility, schema stability, and transport parity`; design_visual=`rendered behavior, accessibility, layout, and visual consistency`; implementation=`behavioral correctness, recovery, and maintainability`; migration_config=`migration, configuration, workflow, and deployment safety`; security_privacy=`authentication, authorization, privacy, and secret handling`; and test=`test completeness, determinism, warnings, and coverage`. Every successor review prompt is exact LF text with one final LF: `Spoonjoy repair successor review v1\nsuccessor_key: <K>\nrole: <role>\nscope: <scope>\nsource_head_sha: <sourceHeadSha>\ntree_sha: <treeSha>\ninput_artifacts_json: <inputJson>\ninput_artifact_set_sha256: <inputSetSha256>\nrules: read only; do not edit; return CLEAN or FINDINGS with file and line evidence\n`. inputJson is compact canonical BINARY-path-sorted unique `[{path,sha256}]`; placeholders reject CR/LF/control bytes. A singular brief prompt, descriptive/free-form review prompt, or path/hash set drift rejects.
- Red evidence binds the actual uncommitted test tree. Exact `SuccessorRedWorktreeProof={version:1,successorKey,unitId,baseHeadSha,baseTreeSha,statusPorcelainSha256,testFiles,redTreeSha,createdAt}` lives at `units/<unitId>/red-tree.v1.json`; `testFiles:{path,sha256,gitBlobSha}[]` is the exact BINARY-sorted output set of that test unit and nonempty. Immediately before the red command, trusted Git with a private mode-0600 `GIT_INDEX_FILE` runs read-tree on baseHeadSha, adds only those worktree test paths, and write-tree; trusted `git status --porcelain=v2 -z --untracked-files=all` must name exactly the same paths and no implementation path, and its complete bytes hash to statusPorcelainSha256. The private index is removed after fsync and no real index/ref/commit is changed. Expected-red SuccessorCommandEvidence.treeSha equals redTreeSha, executes in that unchanged worktree, and a second status hash after execution must match. Replacement `SuccessorRedEvidence={version:1,successorKey,unitId,redWorktreeProofPath,redWorktreeProofSha256,commandEvidencePath,commandEvidenceSha256,failingTestIds,expectedFailureCodes,sourceBaseSha,redTreeSha,createdAt}` cross-links it. `PreReleaseArtifact.kind` and doer SuiteArtifactRef additionally include `red_tree`; the exact path maps only to that kind. Final committed test blobs must equal testFiles before any green evidence passes. The earlier rule binding red evidence to a predecessor/base commit tree is invalid.
- API smoke is one deterministic file, preserving the closed 14-file release set. Replacement `ApiSmokeCheck={name,method,location,expectedStatus,oracle,observation}` has exact `ApiSmokeObservation={status,requestIdMatched,headerProjection,bodyProjection,bodyProjectionSha256}`. `ApiHeaderProjection` is exactly `{kind:'none'}`, `{kind:'request_id',value}`, `{kind:'cors',allowOrigin:'*',allowMethods,allowHeaders}`, `{kind:'public_cache',cacheControl:'public, max-age=60',vary:['Authorization','Cookie']}`, or `{kind:'health',build,workerVersionId}`. `ApiBodyProjection` is exactly `{kind:'html_marker',marker}`, `{kind:'empty'}`, `{kind:'api_error',requestId,code,status,path}`, `{kind:'openapi',version:'3.1.0',server,paths}`, `{kind:'recipe_list',itemCount,nextCursor,hasMore}`, or `{kind:'health',build,workerVersionId}`. All are no-extra-fields; finite fields and nullability are selected by the oracle, and bodyProjectionSha256 hashes the complete compact canonical bodyProjection bytes. Checks occur exactly in order: `api_docs GET /api 200 api_title`; `api_playground GET /api/playground 200 playground_title`; `error_envelope GET /api/v1/not-a-real-endpoint 404 exact_not_found`; `openapi GET /api/v1/openapi.json 200 openapi_paths`; `sdk_openapi GET /api/v1/openapi.sdk.json 200 sdk_paths`; `oauth_cors OPTIONS /oauth/token 204 oauth_cors`; `delete_cors OPTIONS /api/v1/shopping-list/items/item_1 204 delete_cors`; `public_cache GET /api/v1/recipes?limit=1 200 public_cache`; `health GET /health 200 health_attestation`; `auth GET /api/v1/me 401 authentication_required`; `recipes GET /api/v1/recipes?limit=1 200 recipe_list`; `shopping GET /api/v1/shopping-list 401 authentication_required`; `saved_recipes GET /api/v1/saved-recipes?limit=1 401 authentication_required`; `tags GET /api/v1/tags 401 authentication_required`; and `mcp GET /mcp 200 mcp_title`. Each oracle has one parser: title oracles retain only marker `Spoonjoy API`, `Spoonjoy API Playground`, or `Spoonjoy MCP`; exact_not_found requires requestId `api_smoke_not_found`, code not_found, status 404, and the exact path; openapi_paths retains exact server plus the declared nine-path set, while sdk_paths retains exact server plus `oauth/register|oauth/authorize|oauth/token|oauth/revoke`; CORS oracles require empty body and the exact wildcard/method/header projection; public_cache requires the full recipe-list schema before projecting its count/cursor plus the fixed cache/Vary values; health requires exact source/Worker body and header attestation; authentication_required requires the canonical 401 envelope for the exact path; recipe_list requires the full v1 schema before projection. Exact `ApiSmokeReport={version:1,targetBaseUrl,sourceSha,workerVersionId,checks,passed:true,completedAt}` lives alone at `api-smoke-results.json`; there are no API request/response sidecars or artifactPaths. passed is derived only when all fifteen persisted semantic projections validate. Together with the lifecycle report, six fixed screenshots, and six primary cleanup files already registered, the exact union remains fourteen files.
- Lifecycle attempts and artifact hashing are exact. `LifecycleAttemptSummary={label,recipeId,attemptId,startEventSequence,startEventSha256,terminalEventSequence,terminalEventSha256,replacementAttemptId}` is no-extra-fields. attempts is exactly `[A,B]`: A has label `A`, start sequence 1/revision 0, terminal revision 4, and replacementAttemptId equal B.attemptId; B has label `B`, its later start event/revision 0, terminal revision 2, and null replacementAttemptId. Every sequence/hash resolves uniquely into lifecycleEvents; recipeId is equal, attemptIds are distinct, A terminal precedes B start, and no other attempt exists. Exact replacement `LifecycleSmokeReport={version:1,targetBaseUrl,sourceSha,workerVersionId,identity,lifecycleEvents,lifecycleEventsSha256,attempts,finalResidues,cleanupOutcomePath,cleanupOutcomeSha256,artifactPaths,artifactSetSha256,passed:true,completedAt}` uses exactly this tuple. artifactPaths is the BINARY-sorted exact twelve subordinate lifecycle files - six fixed screenshots and six primary cleanup files - and excludes `smoke-results.json`; artifactSetSha256 hashes their complete compact canonical `{path,sha256}[]`. The StageRun externally hashes the complete report as the thirteenth lifecycle file and unions it with the one API report for fourteen. Any self-inclusion, report hash in its own set, missing/extra subordinate, recovery file, or non-primary cleanup rejects.
- API path projections are literal. openapi_paths stores ordered paths `['/api/v1/openapi.json','/api/v1/openapi.sdk.json','/api/v1/openapi.connector.json','/oauth/register','/oauth/token','/oauth/revoke','/api/tools/start_agent_connection','/api/tools/poll_agent_connection','/mcp']`; sdk_paths stores `['/oauth/register','/oauth/authorize','/oauth/token','/oauth/revoke']`. The earlier phrases `declared nine-path set` and `oauth/register|oauth/authorize|oauth/token|oauth/revoke` are shorthand only and are replaced by these arrays.
- Lifecycle summary ordinals and subordinate paths are literal. A uses startEventSequence 1 and terminalEventSequence 5; B uses startEventSequence 6 and terminalEventSequence 8; the sole residue is sequence 9. The twelve artifactPaths are `01-recipes-after-signup.png`, `02-recipe-detail.png`, `03-cook-mode.png`, `04-shopping-list.png`, `05-account-settings.png`, `06-cook-session-mismatch.png`, `cleanup-outcome.json`, `cleanup-phase-primary.json`, `cleanup-pre-delete-rows.json`, `cleanup-user-delete.json`, `cleanup-post-delete-rows.json`, and `cleanup-retained-do-allowlist.json`, normalized beneath the owning out directory and BINARY-sorted for hashing. No other screenshot, cleanup phase, diagnostic, or report path is a subordinate member.
- Process identity probes are reproducible. Exact `ProcessProbeProjection={platform,pid,pgid,startToken,argvSha256,spawnToken,role}` has platform `darwin|linux`, positive pid/pgid, nonempty ASCII startToken, lowercase SHA-256 of compact canonical argv, canonical UUID spawnToken, and role `gate|child`. On Darwin, trusted absolute `/bin/ps` argv is `['/bin/ps','-ww','-o','pid=,pgid=,lstart=,command=','-p',String(pid)]` under `LANG=C,LC_ALL=C`; stdout is exactly one LF-terminated row parsed as positive pid, pgid, fixed English `lstart` bytes, and command, with empty stderr/exit zero. startToken is the exact lstart substring and command must project the registered argv/token/role. On Linux, O_NOFOLLOW reads exact `/proc/<pid>/stat` and `/proc/<pid>/cmdline`; stat field 5 is pgid, field 22 is canonical unsigned decimal startToken, and cmdline is a nonempty NUL-terminated argv sequence matching the registry/token/role. Any ESRCH/missing file means dead; EPERM, extra row/member, parse drift, partial read, pid/pgid mismatch, or argv mismatch is indeterminate. startIdentitySha256 is SHA-256 of compact canonical ProcessProbeProjection bytes, not unspecified raw output. SpawnGeneration prepared requires gate present/release absent; aborted also requires the immutable gate present, release absent, all members dead/reaped, and the declared identity null pair or nonnull pair; ended requires both immutable gate/release present and all members dead/reaped. Every other file matrix rejects.
- Provider JSON limits are numeric. Every provider response is 1..1048576 bytes, fatal UTF-8 without BOM/NUL, maximum nesting depth 16, maximum 8192 total values, 256 object members, 1024 array elements, and 65536 UTF-8 bytes per string; duplicate object keys, nonfinite/unsafe numbers, or cap overflow reject before projection. GitHub workflow arrays and Cloudflare account/database arrays additionally cap at 1000 members. Identifiers use their declared lowercase SHA/UUID/account grammars. D1 projection reads only required uuid/name from each capped object and ignores other fields after full JSON/cap/duplicate validation; the phrase `finite canonical metadata types` supplies no authority and is invalid. These constants apply identically in production and fixtures.
- The final ReleaseTerminalResult matrix decouples intermediate paths. For repaired-intermediate, deskArchivePath is nonnull exactly when predecessorArchiveState is not validating_active; postMergeRepairPath is nonnull exactly when dispositionKind is terminal and null exactly when stage, independently of deskArchivePath. Every other repaired-intermediate field follows the sole four-branch matrix. Any older phrase coupling both paths to terminal/non-validating state is invalid.
- Slugger control retries never mean delivery retries. The one immutable spawnToken, gate, release, publish/result paths, ProcessIdentity, and ownershipGeneration remain fixed. A new TerminalControlAttempt ordinal may only retry a failed Desk Git checkpoint, same-host liveness observation, publish-file reconciliation, result observation/reap, or push/readback around that same generation; it may not prepare, spawn, release, or invoke another gate/child and may not call `ouro msg` again after the registered child has started. Once SluggerProcessResult is observed or uncertain and pushed/read back, no later ordinal is legal. Earlier `no retry` language means no second notification delivery attempt, generation, gate, child, or provider call; it does not forbid these evidence/control ordinals.
- Terminal successful provider projection is removed. No terminal phase stores a generic provider success inside TerminalSuccessfulResult: GitHub/Cloudflare availability remains typed TerminalProbeEvidence, and the one Ouro notification child is typed SluggerProcessResult. The final resultKind domain is therefore `terminal_command|archive_validation_command|filesystem|desk_git|validator|slugger_process`; the earlier TerminalProviderSuccess schema, provider resultKind, and slugger provider phase member are invalid. logicalName is TerminalCommandResult.name, literal `archive-validation`, the filesystem/Desk/validator operation, or literal `slugger-process` respectively.
- Track payload exclusion has one post-move member. In addition to the attempt and final TrackArchive basenames, TrackArchiveMember enumeration excludes exactly the triggering task's identity-derived final `archive-validation.v1.json`, which must be absent at source scan and is the sole task byte permitted to appear after the move. Every other task's validation receipt remains included. After TrackArchive publication, final validation writes and hashes that excluded trigger receipt, which itself stores TrackArchive locator/hash; a fresh payload scan with the same three exclusions must still equal targetMemberSetSha256. Any other post-move file change, missing included receipt, preexisting trigger final receipt, or broader archive-validation exclusion rejects.
- TrackArchive phase ordering is prepared-first and final. phase is exactly `prepared|track_closed|root_moved|archive_validated`. prepared is pushed/read back at the active track before frontmatter mutation; sourceMembers, sourceMemberSetSha256, and targetMemberSetSha256 are null, all four booleans are false, source is present, and target is absent. One atomic Desk candidate changes only track frontmatter active to closed and the attempt to track_closed; it computes sourceMembers/sourceMemberSetSha256 from those candidate bytes using the final exclusions, keeps target hash null, sets only trackClosed true, and is committed/pushed/read back before any move. root_moved atomically moves that exact closed tree and advances the attempt at target, recomputes equal targetMemberSetSha256, and sets sourceTreeMoved/targetPresent true while archiveValid remains false. archive_validated performs a read-only full target/member/locator scan, sets archiveValid true, and changes no other field. Only then may the immutable TrackArchive receipt replace the attempt. Every timestamp and nonnull member is immutable after first appearance; skipped phase, source members in prepared, active frontmatter in track_closed, move before pushed track_closed, unequal manifests, or any other null/boolean/file matrix rejects.
- Planner review prompts and reports are machine-parseable. Role scope text is scope=`feedback dispositions, product scope, and unresolved decisions`; contract=`schema completeness, ownership, ordering, recovery, and authority`; test=`unit ownership, red-first evidence, edge cases, warnings, and coverage`. Exact prompt bytes are `Spoonjoy repair planner review v1\nsuccessor_key: <K>\nplanner_attempt: <positive>\nreview_ordinal: <1|2|3>\nrole: <scope|contract|test>\nscope: <scopeText>\nplanning_path: <planningPath>\nplanning_sha256: <planningSha256>\ndoing_path: <doingPath>\ndoing_sha256: <doingSha256>\nrules: read only; do not edit; evaluate only the named role; return only compact canonical PlannerReviewRuntimeReport JSON\n`, with one final LF and validated placeholders. Exact runtime bytes are compact canonical no-LF `PlannerReviewRuntimeReport={version:1,role,verdict,findings}` where verdict is `APPROVED|FINDINGS` and `PlannerReviewFinding={severity,domain,path,line,code}` has severity `blocker|major|minor`, domain `product|desk`, normalized path in that root, positive line, and code `scope_drift|unresolved_decision|schema_gap|ownership_gap|ordering_gap|recovery_gap|authority_gap|test_gap|coverage_gap|warning_gap|contradiction|stale_authority`. APPROVED requires findings empty; FINDINGS requires a nonempty BINARY `(domain,path,line,code)`-sorted unique array. AgentRuntimeAdapter terminal output must be exactly these bytes and the stored runtime copy must byte-match. SuccessorPlannerReview may project verdict approved only from APPROVED; any FINDINGS fails that planner attempt and requires a new attempt after document repair. Arbitrary prose, unknown code, malformed order, self-asserted verdict, or report without its authorized dispatch rejects.
- API smoke nullability and header values are total. ApiSmokeObservation.status is a safe integer and must equal ApiSmokeCheck.expectedStatus; requestIdMatched is exactly true when requestId below is nonnull and null otherwise. Final `ApiHeaderProjection={requestId,cache,cors,health}` is no-extra-fields. requestId is `{value,matched:true}` or null; cache is `{cacheControl:'public, max-age=60',vary:['Authorization','Cookie']}` or null; cors is `{allowOrigin:'*',allowMethods,allowHeaders}` or null; health is `{build,workerVersionId}` or null. Rows map exactly: api_docs/api_playground/mcp have all four null and their declared html body; error_envelope uses requestId `api_smoke_not_found` plus exact_not_found body; openapi uses `api_smoke_openapi` plus openapi_paths; sdk_openapi uses `api_smoke_sdk` plus sdk_paths; oauth_cors uses only cors with allowMethods `['POST','OPTIONS']` and allowHeaders `['Content-Type']` plus empty body; delete_cors uses only cors with allowMethods `['GET','POST','PATCH','PUT','DELETE','OPTIONS']` and allowHeaders `['Authorization','Content-Type','X-Request-Id','X-Client-Mutation-Id']` plus empty body; public_cache uses requestId `api_smoke_public_cache` and cache plus recipe_list body; health uses only health with both values equal report sourceSha/workerVersionId plus equal health body; auth, recipes, shopping, saved_recipes, and tags use requestIds `api_smoke_auth|api_smoke_recipes|api_smoke_shopping|api_smoke_saved_recipes|api_smoke_tags` respectively and no other header member. auth/shopping/saved_recipes/tags body is api_error with matching request id, code authentication_required, status 401, and exact request path; recipes body is recipe_list. Every unmentioned member is null. Response status, request-id header/body equality, semantic body kind, fixed marker/path/code, cache/CORS order/value, and report identity must all validate before passed.
- Darwin process identity uses a trusted ready handshake and exact process title, not argv reconstruction. Both the first-party gate and its first-party child wrapper set title exactly `spoonjoy-<gate|child>-<spawnToken>` before work, validate their registered argv hash in memory, and write one compact canonical `ProcessReady={version:1,pid,pgid,spawnToken,role,title,registeredArgvSha256,readyAt}` through the parent-owned one-shot descriptor before it closes; record-process cannot proceed before exact ready bytes. The wrapper remains alive until its registered child process group is dead/reaped, so an orphan effect is never hidden behind wrapper death. On Darwin the final trusted ps probe is `['/bin/ps','-ww','-o','pid=,pgid=,lstart=,command=','-p',String(pid)]`; command must equal the no-space title byte-for-byte, while pid/pgid/lstart parse under the declared C locale. ProcessProbeProjection replaces argvSha256 with `title,registeredArgvSha256`, taking both only from the hash-valid ready record and revalidating the observed title. On Linux `/proc/<pid>/cmdline` must be exactly the title plus one NUL after the same ready handshake, while stat supplies pgid/startToken. Ready bytes are host-control data, never manifest artifacts, and are removed only after terminal dead/reaped proof. The earlier rule attempting to derive arbitrary argv from ps command text is invalid.
- ProcessReady has no durable path. Its descriptor bytes are validated once in memory, the descriptor is closed, and the raw bytes are discarded immediately after record-process derives ProcessIdentity. Later liveness probes reconstruct title and registeredArgvSha256 from the immutable SpawnGeneration command spec/token/role, observe pid/pgid/startToken/title again, rebuild ProcessProbeProjection, and require the same startIdentitySha256. The preceding phrase treating ready bytes as retained host-control data is invalid; no ready file, hash sidecar, or descriptor survives spawn recording.
- Track payload exclusion covers both final-validation paths. The final ArchiveValidationAttempt basename is exactly `archive-validation.attempt.v1.json` at the identity-derived final task root; the final ArchiveValidationReceipt basename remains exactly `archive-validation.v1.json` at that same root, and the atomic validated-attempt-to-receipt checkpoint replaces the former with the latter. The exact four excluded relative paths are the track-root `track-archive.attempt.v1.json`, the track-root `track-archive.v1.json`, that triggering task attempt path, and that triggering task receipt path; no basename-wide or other-task exclusion is legal. The trigger attempt may be absent at the source scan or present in its exact prepared bytes, may advance only through the declared post-move validation protocol, and is atomically replaced by the final receipt. The trigger receipt must be absent at source scan. A fresh target payload scan after every trigger-attempt transition and after receipt replacement uses the same four exclusions and must equal targetMemberSetSha256. Thus those two trigger paths are the only task bytes permitted to appear, change, or be replaced after root_moved; every included member remains byte-identical. The preceding three-exclusion and sole-post-move-member clauses are invalid.
- Planner findings have an executable repair owner. Final replacement `SuccessorPlannerReview={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,reviewOrdinal,role,agentId,verdict,planningPath,planningSha256,doingPath,doingSha256,promptPath,promptSha256,dispatchPath,dispatchSha256,returnedReportPath,returnedReportSha256,completedAt}` permits verdict `approved|findings` and projects it exactly from the matching PlannerReviewRuntimeReport `APPROVED|FINDINGS`; all other fields and dispatch binding remain unchanged. Replacement `SuccessorSuiteAttempt` adds terminalOutcome, which is null before completed; a completed planner attempt has terminalOutcome `approved` only when all three ordinal reviews are approved, or `findings` only when all three are terminal and at least one is findings; a completed doer has terminalOutcome `implemented`. A planner findings completion is immutable evidence, not interrupted/failed runtime state. It cannot authorize handoff or direct document mutation. The next contiguous planner attempt alone owns the repair: its exact planner prompt adds, immediately after repair_brief_set_sha256, `prior_planner_reviews_json: <priorJson>` and `prior_planner_review_set_sha256: <priorSetSha256>`. For ordinal 1 priorJson is exact `[]`; for every later ordinal it is the compact canonical BINARY-path-sorted unique complete `{path,sha256}[]` set of the immediately preceding findings attempt's three planner_review artifacts, and priorSetSha256 hashes those exact bytes. The fresh paused/authorized Work Planner invocation reads those reports, writes new planning/doing bytes at the same registered paths, and then all three fresh distinct-agent reviews run again. PostMergeSuccessorAttempt.planning_running permits only a contiguous sequence of zero or more completed findings attempts followed by at most one nonterminal attempt; contract_approved and SuccessorHandoff require the latest completed attempt terminalOutcome approved. No writer or document mutation exists between attempts, no earlier approval carries forward, and a later prompt that omits or skips the immediately prior findings set rejects. The preceding sentence saying findings merely fail an attempt without this projection/retry owner is invalid.
- Process registration is platform-total and survives ready-byte disposal. Final exact `ProcessMemberRegistration={role,title,registeredArgvSha256}` has role `gate|child`, title exactly `spoonjoy-<role>-<spawnToken>`, and the lowercase SHA-256 of compact canonical registered argv. Final exact `ProcessProbeProjection={platform,pid,pgid,startToken,title,registeredArgvSha256,spawnToken,role}` applies identically on Darwin and Linux; startIdentitySha256 hashes its complete compact canonical bytes. Final replacement `SpawnGeneration={generation,spawnToken,memberRegistrations,status,gatePath,releasePath,processIdentity,preparedAt,recordedAt,releasedAt,endedAt}` and `SluggerSpawnGeneration={generation:1,spawnToken,executionHost,memberRegistrations,status,gatePath,releasePath,publishPath,resultPath,pid,pgid,processIdentity,preparedAt,recordedAt,releasedAt,terminalAt}` are no-extra-fields. memberRegistrations is always the exact two-member array `[gateRegistration,childRegistration]`, fixed before prepared publication; even a synchronous no-child spawn failure retains the deterministic child registration. All prior status/nullability rules remain unchanged. ProcessReady must equal one registration plus observed pid/pgid/time and is discarded after ProcessIdentity derivation. Later probes obtain title and registeredArgvSha256 only from the immutable generation registration, not from ready bytes or an undefined command-spec field; Darwin observes exact title through the trusted ps projection, while Linux observes exact title-plus-NUL cmdline, and both obtain pgid/startToken through their final declared platform probe. The earlier `argvSha256` ProcessProbeProjection, Darwin-only replacement wording, undefined `SpawnGeneration command spec`, and raw-probe hash authority are invalid.
- Manifest locks use a separate reproducible owner identity. `ProcessIdentity` is reserved for registered gate/child generations. Exact `LockOwnerProbeProjection={platform,pid,startToken,executionHost,writerId,token}` uses platform `darwin|linux`, positive safe pid, nonempty ASCII startToken, the frozen executionHost, canonical writerId, and canonical lock token. Exact `LockOwnerIdentity={pid,startToken,probeSha256}` repeats pid/startToken and hashes the complete compact canonical projection. Final `ManifestLockOwner={version:1,writerId,token,executionHost,hostname,pid,lockOwnerIdentity,acquiredAt}` replaces processIdentity. On Darwin capture/recovery executes trusted `['/bin/ps','-ww','-o','pid=,lstart=','-p',String(pid)]` under `LANG=C,LC_ALL=C`, requires exactly one LF-terminated matching row, and uses its fixed English lstart substring; on Linux it O_NOFOLLOW-reads `/proc/<pid>/stat` and uses field 22. ESRCH/missing means dead; EPERM, malformed/extra/partial output, identity mismatch, or foreign executionHost is indeterminate. Recovery reconstructs the projection from the immutable lock fields and newly observed startToken, rejects PID reuse, and never needs spawnToken, role, argv, title, ProcessReady, or retained raw probe bytes. The earlier rule requiring ManifestLockOwner to carry ProcessIdentity or use the gate/child probe is invalid; spawned-command record-process/adoption/timeout/reap continue to use ProcessIdentity unchanged.
- Final archive-validation support evidence is external to the moving payload. `archive_validation_final` now has storageDomain `desk_control`, while its identity-derived `archive-validation.attempt.v1.json` and final `archive-validation.v1.json` remain the only task-root protocol pair and stay under the four-path TrackArchive exclusion. Every successful result, failed snapshot/evidence/disposition, wait checkpoint/probe/evidence/resolution, blocker probe/authorization/evidence/resolution, and retry/control record for that phase lives beneath exact generation root `_meta/release-terminal/<identitySha256>/track-generations/<trackGeneration>/<scanDeskSha>/archive-validation-final/`. Within that root the existing finite basenames and ordinal/history-key suffixes are unchanged, and every record repeats/cross-validates identitySha256, trackGeneration, scanDeskSha, storageDomain, phase, and owning attempt ordinal. They use the Desk-control lock and Git checkpoint, are never PreReleaseArtifact/TerminalArtifact members, and are published/read back before the excluded task attempt advances. Final validation reads those external records by complete path/hash, embeds only its declared command result and prior-failure references in the excluded attempt/receipt, and creates no other task/track byte. The immutable external generation root remains after receipt publication as durable audit evidence and is excluded from post-receipt resource cleanup; only mutable host-control process files are deleted. The earlier task_artifact classification for archive_validation_final and any final-validation append beneath the moving track are invalid.
- Planner attempts review immutable candidate documents. Let `<doing-artifact-directory>` be the exact product-repo path obtained by removing the final `.md` from identity.productDoingPath; for planner ordinal N, exact snapshot paths are `<doing-artifact-directory>/successor-planner/attempt-<N>/planning.md` and `<doing-artifact-directory>/successor-planner/attempt-<N>/doing.md`, and no path is reused. The Work Planner prompt's planning_path/doing_path name only that attempt's snapshots. A planner invocation may create those two files and nothing at the canonical productPlanningPath/productDoingPath; Work Merger accepts them only as one product Git candidate, commits/pushes/readback-verifies both complete blobs before review dispatch, and every SuccessorPlannerReview binds those immutable snapshot paths/hashes. `SuiteArtifactRef.kind` adds `planning_snapshot|doing_snapshot|planner_promotion`, and the snapshot kinds accept only the matching ordinal paths. A findings attempt leaves its committed snapshots forever immutable and performs no canonical write. After all three reviews approve, Work Merger atomically promotes the exact approved pair to the canonical productPlanningPath/productDoingPath in one product Git candidate, stages both in BINARY order, verifies their blob hashes equal the snapshots, commits/pushes/fetches/readbacks, and then appends exact `SuccessorPlannerPromotion={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,planningSnapshotPath,planningSnapshotSha256,doingSnapshotPath,doingSnapshotSha256,canonicalPlanningPath,canonicalPlanningSha256,canonicalDoingPath,canonicalDoingSha256,productCommitSha,productTreeSha,promotedAt}` at `suite/planner/attempt-<N>-promotion.v1.json`. Before the promotion receipt, recovery accepts only canonical pair absent, a legal per-path local O/C mixture rematerialized to C, or both canonical blobs present in the exact accepted/read-back commit; one present remote blob, drift, or another commit tree rejects. A completed approved planner SuiteAttempt requires that promotion artifact and canonical/snapshot byte equality; a findings completion forbids it. The doer and SuccessorHandoff read only the promoted canonical pair and cross-link the promotion. No review or report authenticates a mutable/canonical work path before promotion.
- Planner retry prompt hashing is literal. In the planner-attempt rule, ordinal 1 priorJson is the exact two UTF-8 bytes `[]` with no LF and priorSetSha256 is SHA-256 of those exact bytes. For ordinal greater than one, priorJson is the complete compact canonical BINARY-path-sorted unique `{path,sha256}[]` bytes of the immediately preceding findings attempt's three immutable planner_review artifacts, with no LF, and priorSetSha256 is SHA-256 of exactly those bytes. Empty and nonempty encodings share this one derivation; no semantic/set-only hash or omitted first-attempt value is legal.
- Spawned member discovery is paused, bounded, and persisted before effects. Final ProcessMemberRegistration additionally contains `instanceToken,launchedAtUnixNs`; instanceToken is lowercase SHA-256 of compact canonical `{spawnToken,role,launchedAtUnixNs,registeredArgvSha256}`, launchedAtUnixNs is a positive canonical decimal nanosecond timestamp frozen before spawn, and title is exactly `spoonjoy-<role>-<instanceToken>`. Exact host-local `ProcessMemberRegistry={version:1,generation,spawnToken,executionHost,members,updatedAt}` lives at mode-0600 `<hostControlRoot>/<spawnToken>/members.v1.json`; generation is the owning positive generation and members is the role-ordered array of exact `ProcessMemberRecord={registration,processIdentity}`. The first-party gate atomically writes/fsyncs its one-member registry before waiting; after the pushed recorded gate checkpoint and immutable gate release, it spawns the first-party child wrapper paused, validates the child's ready handshake, atomically replaces the registry with the two-member set, and the child cannot execute the registered command until the parent has pushed/read back the two-member generation and atomically published exact child-run bytes at `<hostControlRoot>/<spawnToken>/child-run.v1.json`. Final `SpawnGeneration={generation,spawnToken,memberRegistrations,memberRegistryPath,childRunPath,status,abortedFrom,gatePath,releasePath,memberRecords,preparedAt,gateRecordedAt,releasedAt,childRecordedAt,runningAt,endedAt}` has status `prepared|recorded|released|child_recorded|running|aborted|ended`. memberRegistryPath and childRunPath are immutable expected paths in every status. prepared has abortedFrom null, memberRecords empty, preparedAt nonnull, every later time null, gate bytes present, and registry/release/child-run absent; recorded adds only the gate record, one-member registry, and gateRecordedAt; released adds only release bytes/releasedAt; child_recorded adds the child record, two-member registry, and childRecordedAt while child-run/runningAt remain absent; running adds child-run/runningAt; ended preserves the running prefix, adds endedAt, and requires every member dead/reaped. aborted has endedAt and abortedFrom exactly `prepared|recorded|released|child_recorded`, preserves that phase's longest legal records/files/times except no child-run/runningAt, and requires every known member dead/reaped plus positive proof no registered command began. Every non-aborted status has abortedFrom null. SluggerSpawnGeneration uses the same registration/registry/record checkpoints; its existing publish file is the child-run authorization and cannot exist before the two-member journal is pushed/read back. The parent derives ProcessIdentity from the complete ProcessProbeProjection, so raw ready bytes may be discarded after the corresponding ProcessMemberRecord is durably stored.
- Crash discovery is finite and title-bound. If the member registry is absent or incomplete after OS spawn, same-host recovery performs one bounded trusted scan: Darwin executes `['/bin/ps','-A','-ww','-o','pid=,pgid=,lstart=,command=']` under the closed C locale, caps stdout at 1048576 bytes and rows at 4096, and accepts only exact registered titles; Linux reads at most 131072 numeric `/proc` directories in numeric order with O_NOFOLLOW stat/cmdline and the same aggregate byte cap. It requires zero or one exact process per registration, the declared gate/child PGID relationship, and no unregistered token title. A found gate or child is kept paused, converted to its exact ProcessMemberRecord, written to the host registry, and pushed into the generation before any release/child-run effect. Zero matches after spawn uncertainty never authorizes another spawn for that generation: recovery records a host-liveness wait, repeats the bounded scan until the original total deadline, and may enter aborted only after the retained process handle/reap result or an exact no-process observation proves the registered command never began. Cap overflow, duplicate title, extra same-token process, partial/malformed probe, foreign host, wrong PGID, or a process that exits before persistence is indeterminate and blocks. Host registry and child-run bytes are removed only after terminal dead/reaped proof. The preceding no-durable-ready-path rule is replaced: raw descriptor bytes remain transient, but the canonical identities derived from them persist in this host-control registry until terminal cleanup.
