- Boot and start identity are collision-resistant. Exact bootIdSha256 is captured before executionHost derivation: Darwin runs trusted `['/usr/sbin/sysctl','-n','kern.boottime']` under `LANG=C,LC_ALL=C`, requires exact regex `^\\{ sec = [1-9][0-9]*, usec = ([0-9]|[1-9][0-9]{1,5}) \\} (Sun|Mon|Tue|Wed|Thu|Fri|Sat) (Jan|Feb|Mar|Apr|May|Jun|Jul|Aug|Sep|Oct|Nov|Dec) [ 0-3][0-9] [0-2][0-9]:[0-5][0-9]:[0-6][0-9] [0-9]{4}\\n$`, additionally validates usec <=999999, and hashes the complete stdout; Linux hashes the exact canonical lowercase UUID-plus-LF from O_NOFOLLOW `/proc/sys/kernel/random/boot_id`. Final executionHost preimage adds bootIdSha256 after arch. Final `ProcessStartToken={bootIdSha256,kernelStartToken,launchedAtUnixNs,instanceToken}` replaces the plain startToken in ProcessProbeProjection; kernelStartToken is Darwin's exact C-locale lstart substring or Linux stat field 22, and the other members come from the immutable registration/title. PID/second/tick reuse cannot match both boot identity and the unique high-resolution instance-bound title. Lock ownership uses the same boot scope without becoming a spawned ProcessIdentity: before publishing a lock, the owner freezes positive acquiredAtUnixNs, derives instanceToken as SHA-256 of compact canonical `{executionHost,writerId,token,acquiredAtUnixNs}`, sets its observable title exactly `spoonjoy-lock-<instanceToken>`, and stores final `LockOwnerProbeProjection={platform,pid,startToken,title,executionHost,writerId,token}` where startToken is `{bootIdSha256,kernelStartToken,acquiredAtUnixNs,instanceToken}`. Recovery must observe that exact title plus kernel token/boot identity; release restores the prior process title only after lock deletion. Final LockOwnerIdentity repeats pid/startToken/probeSha256. A new boot, reused PID, same-second Darwin start, repeated Linux tick, wrong title, or title restoration while the lock exists is dead/indeterminate according to the declared probe result and never live.
- Host-control storage and child authorization are exact. `hostControlRoot` is `/Users/arimendelow/Library/Caches/spoonjoy-release/process-control` on Darwin. On Linux it is `<XDG_RUNTIME_DIR>/spoonjoy-release/process-control` only when XDG_RUNTIME_DIR is absolute, real, same-uid-owned, non-symlink, and mode 0700; otherwise it is `/tmp/spoonjoy-release-<decimal-uid>/process-control`. The implementation creates/validates every ancestor without following symlinks; fallback root and root are same-uid-owned mode 0700, each `<spawnToken>` directory is mode 0700, and every atomic temp/final file is regular same-uid-owned mode 0600. Exact `ProcessChildRun={version:1,generation,spawnToken,executionHost,memberRegistryPath,memberRegistrySha256,childProcessIdentity,registeredArgvSha256,commandSha256,authorizedAt}` cross-links the hash-valid two-member registry, its child record/registration, and the gate's frozen registered-effect command hash. Ordinary child-run bytes are compact canonical no-LF ProcessChildRun at `<hostControlRoot>/<spawnToken>/child-run.v1.json`; the parent writes/fsyncs/renames/fsyncs-directory only after the remote generation's child_recorded checkpoint is pushed/read back, and the child revalidates every field before work. Replacement `SluggerPublish={version:1,generation:1,spawnToken,releaseSha256,childRun:ProcessChildRun,publishedAt}` uses the final publishPath as Slugger's child-run file and additionally binds the exact release bytes. Partial/temp, wrong mode/owner, registry/hash/identity/command drift, pre-checkpoint publication, or alternate root blocks without child work.
- Slugger generation is a complete two-member state machine. Final no-extra-fields `SluggerSpawnGeneration={generation:1,spawnToken,executionHost,memberRegistrations,memberRegistryPath,status,abortedFrom,gatePath,releasePath,publishPath,resultPath,memberRecords,preparedAt,gateRecordedAt,releasedAt,childRecordedAt,runningAt,terminalAt}` replaces every singleton pid/pgid/processIdentity form. It uses status `prepared|recorded|released|child_recorded|running|aborted|terminal` and the regular SpawnGeneration matrix exactly, with publishPath/SluggerPublish in place of childRunPath/ProcessChildRun and terminalAt in place of endedAt; terminal preserves the complete running prefix and requires both members dead/reaped, while aborted preserves one no-effect prefix through child_recorded. Final `TerminalSluggerState={kind:'slugger',notificationPath,notificationSha256,notification,generation}` contains that complete generation. Notification prepared requires generation prepared; recorded requires recorded; released permits released, child_recorded, or running while result members remain null; observed requires terminal plus a hash-valid exit SluggerProcessResult; uncertain requires terminal or aborted plus the corresponding non-exit result. No notification checkpoint may collapse memberRecords back to singleton fields, and publish cannot precede child_recorded push/readback.
- Manifest-lock probes observe the bound title. The final Darwin lock probe is trusted `['/bin/ps','-ww','-o','pid=,lstart=,command=','-p',String(pid)]` under `LANG=C,LC_ALL=C`, with stdout cap 4096 bytes, exactly one LF-terminated row, matching positive pid, exact fixed English lstart, and command byte-equal `spoonjoy-lock-<instanceToken>`; stderr is empty and exit zero. The final Linux lock probe O_NOFOLLOW-reads exact `/proc/<pid>/stat` plus `/proc/<pid>/cmdline` under a 4096-byte aggregate cap; cmdline is exactly that title plus one NUL, stat pid/start field parses canonically, and no extra byte is legal. Matching boot/start/title rebuilds the same LockOwnerProbeProjection and means live. ESRCH, missing proc member, boot mismatch, or a complete parseable row with pid/start/title mismatch means the recorded owner is dead and cannot retain the lock. EPERM, cap overflow, partial read, malformed output, extra row/field/byte, changed observation during the read, or tool identity drift is indeterminate and blocks lock adoption. The earlier pid/lstart-only and stat-only lock probes are invalid.
- Final archive-validation control records use one exact generation envelope. Exact no-extra-fields `FinalArchiveValidationControlEnvelope={version:1,identitySha256,executionHost,trackGeneration,scanDeskSha,trackArchiveLocator,trackArchiveSha256,kind,attemptOrdinal,historyKeySha256,payload,payloadSha256,recordedAt}` has kind `successful_result|failure_snapshot|failure_evidence|failure_disposition|wait_checkpoint|wait_probe|wait_resolution_evidence|wait_resolution|blocker_probe|operator_authorization|blocker_resolution_evidence|blocker_resolution|control_attempt`. payload is exactly the corresponding existing no-extra-fields schema, payloadSha256 hashes its compact canonical bytes, attemptOrdinal equals the payload owner, and historyKeySha256 is null only when that payload schema has no history key. Each existing finite support basename under the generation root stores the envelope instead of a naked payload; all path/hash fields in archive_validation_final attempts, envelopes, and progress results name/hash the complete envelope, and consumers unwrap exactly once before applying the payload schema. trackArchiveLocator/hash equal the final TrackArchive receipt under validation. This envelope is the sole addition of trackGeneration/scanDeskSha; nested payload schemas retain their exact fields. A naked payload, wrong root, recursive envelope, context mismatch, or payload/envelope hash drift rejects.
- Planner promotion is registered and has a full Git checkpoint. `PreReleaseArtifact.kind` and planner SuiteArtifactRef.kind both include `planner_promotion`; its sole task-relative path is exact `artifacts/post-merge-successor/suite/planner/attempt-<N>-promotion.v1.json`, and it is appended/pushed/read back before the completed planner suite receipt. Its mutable sibling `attempt-<N>-promotion.attempt.v1.json` is journal-only, never a PreReleaseArtifact, and must be absent from the completed closed set. Exact `SuccessorPlannerPromotionAttempt={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,planningSnapshotPath,planningSnapshotSha256,doingSnapshotPath,doingSnapshotSha256,canonicalPlanningPath,canonicalDoingPath,productBranch,oldProductHeadSha,oldProductTreeSha,candidatePlanningBlobSha,candidateDoingBlobSha,commitMessage,authorName,authorEmail,commitAt,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,phase,productRemoteSha,startedAt,updatedAt}` has phase `prepared|committed|pushed|readback`. productBranch equals identity.branch; commitMessage is exact `docs: promote successor planner attempt <N>`; authorName/authorEmail are exact `Spoonjoy Release`/`release@spoonjoy.app`; commitAt is one canonical Git timestamp used for both author and committer. prepared is pushed/read back in Desk before product mutation and freezes those commit bytes, parent/tree inputs, and therefore candidate commit/tree SHAs; committed requires clean candidate index/tree plus local branch/ref at candidate and remote at old; pushed requires exact force-with-lease oldProductHeadSha CAS success or response-loss `ls-remote` adoption of candidate, and productRemoteSha candidate; readback requires fetch plus remote-tracking ref/tree/blob equality. Recovery accepts only legal per-path O/C worktree/index mixtures rematerialized to C, local ref old or candidate, and remote ref old or candidate: local candidate/remote old resumes the same push, remote candidate with any legal local state is adopted then fetched/read back, and any third ref/tree/blob rejects. The immutable SuccessorPlannerPromotion is projected only from readback and atomically replaces the attempt in the Desk candidate that appends its registered artifact. A rejected lease never rebuilds on a new parent; it starts no canonical promotion and requires a fresh planner attempt after reconciling product history.
- Final-validation envelopes do not create a third control state. `FinalArchiveValidationControlEnvelope` adds fixed fields `storageDomain:'desk_control'` and `terminalPhase:'archive_validation_final'` immediately after executionHost. Its kind domain removes `control_attempt`; archive_validation_final never uses TerminalControlAttempt or TerminalControlPhaseState, which remain exactly resource_cleanup|slugger. The excluded task-root ArchiveValidationAttempt is the sole mutable phase state, and every external envelope is immutable support evidence around its ordinal. The external failure classifier, wait/blocker progress result, and successful-result rules select desk_control/archive_validation_final through the envelope and existing payload, but no post-final control-attempt path/schema. This clause replaces the earlier requirement for a final-validation retry/control record and any claim that nested payloads themselves repeat generation fields.
- TrackArchive exclusions are one final four-path registry. For every source/target manifest, the excluded relative paths are exactly track-root `track-archive.attempt.v1.json`, track-root `track-archive.v1.json`, the triggering task's final-root `archive-validation.attempt.v1.json`, and that task's final-root `archive-validation.v1.json`. This literal registry replaces line 519's two-path enumeration, the later three-path enumeration, and every basename-wide shorthand; no earlier two/three-path clause retains authority.
- Promotion conflicts are terminal planner evidence, not a dead end. `PreReleaseArtifact.kind` and planner SuiteArtifactRef.kind additionally include `planner_promotion_conflict`; its sole path is `artifacts/post-merge-successor/suite/planner/attempt-<N>-promotion-conflict.v1.json`. Exact `SuccessorPlannerPromotionConflict={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,oldProductHeadSha,candidateCommitSha,observedProductRemoteSha,code:'lease_conflict',conflictedAt}` is emitted only when the frozen force-with-lease sees a third remote SHA, after restoring/cleaning local canonical O/C state and fetching/readback-verifying that remote. It atomically replaces the promotion attempt, projecting every terminal conflict fact into this receipt rather than retaining a dangling attempt locator. The planner SuiteAttempt completes with terminalOutcome `promotion_conflict`, retains its approved reviews and snapshots, forbids promotion/handoff, and registers the conflict. Planning history permits any contiguous completed `findings|promotion_conflict` attempts before the one latest attempt. The final planner prompt replaces `prior_planner_reviews_json/prior_planner_review_set_sha256` with `prior_planner_outcomes_json/prior_planner_outcome_set_sha256`: ordinal 1 uses exact UTF-8 `[]`; after findings the set is the prior three planner_review artifacts; after promotion_conflict it is those three approved planner_review artifacts plus the conflict artifact. Every set is complete compact canonical BINARY-path-sorted unique `{path,sha256}[]` bytes with no LF and its SHA-256. The next Work Planner reads the reconciled product history and writes a new immutable snapshot pair; all three reviews rerun. Only terminalOutcome approved plus registered promotion may authorize handoff.
- Process launch inputs are canonical, complete, and acyclic. Final no-extra-fields schemas are `ProcessMemberRegistration={role,instanceToken,launchedAtUnixNs,title,registeredArgvSha256}`, where launchedAtUnixNs is a positive canonical decimal string; `ProcessLaunchSpec={argv,registrationBundlePathIndex,registrationBundleSha256Index}`, whose distinct safe-integer indices select exact argv sentinels `@registration-bundle-path@` and `@registration-bundle-sha256@`; `ProcessRegistrationBundle={version:1,generation,spawnToken,executionHost,memberRegistrations,memberRegistryPath,childRunPath,gateStartupPath,childReadyPath,createdAt}`; and `ProcessMemberRegistry={version:1,generation,spawnToken,executionHost,members,updatedAt}`. Each registration's registeredArgvSha256 hashes compact canonical ProcessLaunchSpec, not substituted runtime argv, so bundle hashing is nonrecursive; actual gate/child-wrapper argv must normalize only those exact bundle path/hash operands back to the sentinels and hash-equal the registration. memberRegistrations is exact `[gate,child]`; createdAt/updatedAt are canonical ISO timestamps, one-member registry updatedAt equals gate ProcessReady.readyAt, and two-member registry updatedAt equals child ProcessReady.readyAt. Bundle bytes live at `<hostControlRoot>/<spawnToken>/registration.v1.json`, are mode 0600/hash-frozen before prepared publication, and both registrations derive before spawn. Final ordinary gate bytes add `registrationBundlePath,registrationBundleSha256,memberRegistryPath,childRunPath,gateStartupPath,childReadyPath` after commandSha256. SluggerGate adds the same six fields after commandSha256. Exact gate argv appends `--registration-bundle <path> --registration-bundle-sha256 <sha256>` before its standalone registered-command separator; the first-party child wrapper receives the same pair plus `--role child` before that separator. Gate and child read only the hash-valid bundle to set/verify their normalized launch specs and titles; no undeclared environment value supplies registration authority.
- Startup/readiness ownership is crash-safe. Exact `ProcessGateStartup={version:1,generation,spawnToken,executionHost,registrationBundleSha256,state,pid,readyAt}` at gateStartupPath has prepared with pid/readyAt null and ready with both nonnull; the parent writes prepared before spawn and the gate atomically replaces it only after title/argv validation. Gate ProcessReady returns through the parent descriptor; the parent validates it, derives ProcessIdentity, and alone writes the one-member ProcessMemberRegistry before calling record-process. After gate release, the gate spawns the child wrapper paused, validates its descriptor ProcessReady, and atomically writes those exact ready bytes at childReadyPath; the parent validates childReady, derives child ProcessIdentity, and alone replaces the registry with two members before record-child-process. ChildReady is raw host-control readiness and is deleted after two-member registry persistence. A prepared barrier plus no exact registered gate title after the original total deadline proves only that this generation never became releasable; releasePath is permanently forbidden, aborts prepared, and a later generation may start. A ready barrier or exact title is always adopted; it can never be treated absent.
- Spawn phases have explicit local-ahead reconciliation. Final regular status domain is `prepared|spawn_authorized|recorded|released|child_recorded|run_authorized|running|aborted|ended`, with nonnull spawnAuthorizedAt between preparedAt and gateRecordedAt and nonnull runAuthorizedAt between childRecordedAt and runningAt. child_recorded has two-member registry and no child-run. run_authorized is pushed/read back before child-run publication and still has child-run absent. The only legal local-ahead states are: generation released with a hash-valid two-member registry/childReady, which deterministically executes record-child-process without respawn; and generation run_authorized with exact child-run present, which never republishes and deterministically executes record-child-running while the child may already be running. Every other file-ahead/behind mix rejects or waits. running requires child-run present and runningAt copied from ProcessChildRun.authorizedAt; finish-command atomically records terminal ProcessResult and ended before output completion. Host registry/startup/ready/child-run files are removed only after ended/Slugger terminal is pushed/read back and all members are dead/reaped.
- Spawn CLI ownership is exact. The final grammar retains prepare-spawn, gate-only record-process, and release-spawn, then adds ordered `record-child-process --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt A --generation N --member-registry-path P --member-registry-sha256 H`; `authorize-child-run --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt A --generation N`; `record-child-running --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt A --generation N --child-run-path P --child-run-sha256 H`; and `abort-spawn --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt A --generation N --from prepared|spawn_authorized|recorded|released|child_recorded|run_authorized --reason gate_spawn_error|gate_startup_timeout|gate_exit_before_record|gate_exit_before_release|child_spawn_error|child_exit_before_run`. Exact successes are record-process `{generation,status:'recorded',processIdentity}`; release-spawn `{generation,status:'released'}`; record-child-process `{generation,status:'child_recorded',memberRegistrySha256}`; authorize-child-run `{generation,status:'run_authorized',childRunPath,childRunSha256}` where the returned hash is the frozen bytes to publish; record-child-running `{generation,status:'running',childRunSha256}`; and abort-spawn `{generation,status:'aborted',abortedFrom,reason}`. finish-command alone changes running to ended from the terminal process result. Every command validates the preceding pushed/read-back state and exact host file; caller JSON, skipped action, old process-start flag, or stale prepare/record/release-only lifecycle rejects.
- Process discovery uses only observable registered titles. The finite scan candidate set is formed by exact equality to either title in ProcessRegistrationBundle; more than one process for either title, both roles with wrong PGID, or any PID/start/title change across projection reads is indeterminate. No rule refers to an unobservable spawn-token substring or unregistered same-token title. On Linux ENOENT before any bytes means that candidate is absent; disappearance or identity change after a partial stat/cmdline read restarts the complete bounded scan once, and a second race is indeterminate. On Darwin a complete zero-row scan after startup deadline plus a still-prepared startup barrier permits only the prepared abort above; any malformed/partial/multirow observation is indeterminate. After ready, zero candidates never proves no effect by itself: the persisted registry/process result and release/child-run barriers determine aborted versus terminal recovery. No generation respawns a registered member.
- Slugger publish is platform-total and pre-spawns the paused child. Final publishPath is exactly `<hostControlRoot>/<spawnToken>/child-run.v1.json` on Darwin and Linux; the old `/Users/arimendelow/Library/Caches/spoonjoy-release/<spawnToken>/generation-1-publish.v1.json` path is invalid. Slugger follows prepared -> recorded -> released -> child_recorded -> run_authorized -> running -> terminal|aborted with the same registry/barrier semantics. SluggerPublish is written only after run_authorized push/readback and wakes the already-spawned paused child; it never causes gate or child spawn. Notification phase released covers generation released through running, while observed/uncertain require terminal/aborted as already declared.
- Lock titles are process-globally serialized. Exact `ProcessTitleMutex` is a module-global, non-reentrant in-memory owner `{writerId,token,priorTitle}` acquired before title change or lock candidate creation and held through lock deletion, prior-title restoration, and mutex release in that order. If occupied, any same/different writer/token lock acquisition returns finite `lock_title_busy` with no title/file/manifest mutation; nested acquisition is illegal. Recovery within the same owner reuses the held mutex but cannot acquire another lock. A title that changes while a lock file exists without the matching mutex is indeterminate, never dead/adoptable. Tests interleave two manifests, same-token recursion, release failures, and title restoration; no overlapping ManifestLockOwner can exist in one process.
- API smoke uses only owned routes. The final fifteen-row registry replaces saved_recipes location with `GET /api/v1/me/saved-recipes?limit=1` and replaces tags with `native_sync GET /api/v1/me/sync`; both expect 401 authentication_required. The request-id rows are `api_smoke_saved_recipes` and `api_smoke_native_sync`, and each api_error path equals that literal request path. Every earlier `/api/v1/saved-recipes`, `/api/v1/tags`, `tags` row, or `api_smoke_tags` request-id is invalid. Check order remains unchanged except row fourteen immediately before MCP is named native_sync in the former tags position; the one-file report and fourteen-file aggregate are unchanged.
- Final-validation envelope TrackArchive fields follow disposition. FinalArchiveValidationControlEnvelope.trackArchiveLocator and .trackArchiveSha256 are both null exactly when the bound TrackDisposition decision is kept_active, and both nonnull/hash-valid exactly when archived. Archived values resolve/hash the final TrackArchive receipt; kept_active validates target absence and the null pair. Every envelope pair equals the excluded ArchiveValidationAttempt and eventual ArchiveValidationReceipt pair for its ordinal. Mixed nullability, a locator for kept_active, or a missing archived receipt rejects.
- Promotion-conflict recovery is journaled. SuccessorPlannerPromotionAttempt phase domain adds `conflict_detected|conflict_restored|conflict_readback` after prepared/committed. conflict_detected freezes the third observed remote SHA immediately after the rejected lease and before any cleanup; productRemoteSha is that SHA and all candidate metadata remains immutable. conflict_restored records exact canonical worktree/index/local-ref restoration with local ref oldProductHeadSha or the fetched third SHA and no candidate canonical blobs. conflict_readback requires fetch, remote-tracking/local ancestry, clean status, and exact third-SHA tree/blob readback. Recovery at each substate accepts only the declared O/C mixtures, local old/candidate/third ref, and remote exact third ref, performs the first absent transition, and never pushes candidate again. Only conflict_readback may atomically replace the attempt with SuccessorPlannerPromotionConflict and append/register it; a crash before/after candidate cleanup, fetch, ref update, readback, receipt materialization, Desk commit, push, or response-loss resumes that prefix. This branch explicitly supersedes the generic third-ref rejection; any fourth/change-after-freeze remote SHA blocks and requires a new conflict observation only after a fresh planner attempt.
- Planner SuiteArtifactRef membership is final and outcome-specific. The planner kind set is exactly `planning_snapshot|doing_snapshot|planner_review_prompt|planner_review_runtime|planner_review_dispatch_intent|planner_review_dispatch|planner_review|planner_promotion|planner_promotion_conflict`; canonical `planning|doing|review` kinds are invalid. Every completed planner attempt contains its two snapshots and all three complete review chains. terminalOutcome findings adds no promotion member; promotion_conflict adds exactly planner_promotion_conflict and no planner_promotion; approved adds exactly planner_promotion and no conflict. Nonterminal attempts contain only the legal immutable prefix. Canonical planning/doing paths enter only SuccessorPlannerPromotion, handoff, and doer bindings after approved promotion, never planner SuiteArtifactRef.
- Slugger run authorization is explicit. Final SluggerSpawnGeneration inserts `runAuthorizedAt` between childRecordedAt and runningAt, includes status `run_authorized`, and uses exact `abortedFrom`/`abortReason` fields before gatePath. Its status/null matrix is byte-identical to regular SpawnGeneration through run_authorized/running, with terminalAt replacing endedAt. Notification released maps generation released|child_recorded|run_authorized|running; observed/uncertain remain terminal/aborted only. Every earlier Slugger schema/mapping without run_authorized/runAuthorizedAt is invalid.
- Launch vectors and host basenames are literal. ProcessLaunchSpec.argv is a nonempty `string[]` of NUL/control-free strings with each bundle sentinel occurring exactly once at its declared distinct in-range index and nowhere else. gateStartupPath is exact `<hostControlRoot>/<spawnToken>/gate-startup.v1.json`; childReadyPath is exact `<hostControlRoot>/<spawnToken>/child-ready.v1.json`. Ordinary gate launch argv is `['pnpm','exec','tsx','scripts/release-spawn-gate.ts','--gate',gatePath,'--release',releasePath,'--startup',gateStartupPath,'--child-ready',childReadyPath,'--registration-bundle',actualBundlePath,'--registration-bundle-sha256',actualBundleSha256,'--spawn-token',spawnToken,'--','<registered effect argv members...>']`; its ProcessLaunchSpec replaces only value indices 13 and 15 with the two sentinels. The child wrapper argv is `['pnpm','exec','tsx','scripts/release-spawn-gate.ts','--child','--child-ready',childReadyPath,'--registration-bundle',actualBundlePath,'--registration-bundle-sha256',actualBundleSha256,'--spawn-token',spawnToken,'--','<registered effect argv members...>']`, with sentinel value indices 8 and 10. Slugger uses the same gate vector with its Desk gate/release paths and exact `ouro msg --to slugger <message>` effect argv; there is no inherited legacy vector without standalone `--`. Any count/index/sentinel/flag/order drift rejects.
- Child readiness is self-published before acknowledgement. The paused child atomically writes/fsyncs/renames its complete ProcessReady bytes to childReadyPath, fsyncs the directory, rereads/hash-validates them, and only then sends the same bytes to the gate descriptor. The gate may relay/validate but never authors childReady. Therefore gate death after descriptor receipt cannot erase readyAt or identity inputs; recovery reads the durable file and exact title. gateStartupPath, childReadyPath, registration.v1.json, members.v1.json, and child-run.v1.json are retained through ended/Slugger terminal push/readback plus dead/reaped proof, then deleted in reverse dependency order, the token directory is rmdir'd, and the process-control parent is retained. The earlier immediate childReady deletion and any released+two-member state requiring childReady absence are invalid.
- Abort state is deterministic. Final regular `SpawnGeneration={generation,spawnToken,memberRegistrations,memberRegistryPath,childRunPath,status,abortedFrom,abortReason,gatePath,releasePath,memberRecords,preparedAt,gateRecordedAt,releasedAt,childRecordedAt,runAuthorizedAt,runningAt,endedAt}` and the corresponding Slugger schema use abortReason null outside aborted. Exact legal pairs are prepared with gate_startup_timeout only at the expired no-authorization prefix; spawn_authorized with gate_spawn_error|gate_startup_timeout|gate_exit_before_record; recorded with gate_exit_before_release; released with gate_exit_before_release|child_spawn_error|child_exit_before_run; child_recorded with child_exit_before_run; and run_authorized with child_exit_before_run only while child-run is absent. Every aborted prefix preserves prior times/records, has later times null, proves no effect, and sets endedAt/terminalAt. Another pair/reason or retry that changes reason rejects byte-for-byte.
- Linux title probes accept only deterministic padding. For spawned and lock processes, `/proc/<pid>/cmdline` must begin with the exact UTF-8 title and every remaining byte, from at least one byte through the declared original argv-buffer length, must be NUL; any non-NUL suffix, truncation beyond the frozen buffer length, or title mismatch rejects. The parent freezes that positive buffer length in ProcessMemberRegistration and LockOwnerIdentity before title mutation. The final ProcessMemberRegistration adds `argvBufferBytes` after launchedAtUnixNs, and LockOwnerIdentity adds argvBufferBytes before probeSha256. The earlier exact-title-plus-one-NUL requirement is invalid.
- ProcessTitleMutex is title-bound. Final exact `ProcessTitleMutex={writerId,token,instanceToken,lockTitle,priorTitle}` requires lockTitle exact `spoonjoy-lock-<instanceToken>` and all five values equal ManifestLockOwner/LockOwnerIdentity derivation plus the currently observed process title while held. Release records title restoration state before deleting the in-memory owner; any mismatched owner, lock title, instance token, prior title, or recovery lock is indeterminate. No mutex schema lacking instanceToken/lockTitle is valid.
- Final process identity schemas are literal, not additive. Exact no-extra-fields `ProcessMemberRegistration={role,instanceToken,launchedAtUnixNs,argvBufferBytes,title,registeredArgvSha256}` has positive safe-integer argvBufferBytes and the constraints already declared for every other member. Exact no-extra-fields `LockOwnerIdentity={pid,startToken,argvBufferBytes,probeSha256}` has positive safe-integer argvBufferBytes frozen before title mutation. These two complete schemas replace every earlier shorter schema and any wording that merely "adds" argvBufferBytes.
- Final Slugger generation bytes are literal. Exact no-extra-fields `SluggerSpawnGeneration={generation:1,spawnToken,executionHost,memberRegistrations,memberRegistryPath,status,abortedFrom,abortReason,gatePath,releasePath,publishPath,resultPath,memberRecords,preparedAt,gateRecordedAt,releasedAt,childRecordedAt,runAuthorizedAt,runningAt,terminalAt}` uses the final status domain `prepared|recorded|released|child_recorded|run_authorized|running|aborted|terminal`, the regular status/null matrix through running, and terminalAt in place of endedAt. This complete schema replaces every earlier Slugger schema and any additive insertion wording.

### Round 61 Cold-Gate Closures

The clauses below are the final authority for every subject they name and replace every conflicting or merely additive clause above.

- Registration and readiness have complete disjoint schemas. Exact no-extra-fields `ProcessMemberRegistration={role,instanceToken,title,registeredArgvSha256}` freezes role `gate|child`, one unique lowercase UUID instanceToken, exact `spoonjoy-<role>-<instanceToken>` title, and the hash of the final sentinel-normalized ProcessLaunchSpec before prepare-spawn. Exact no-extra-fields `ProcessReady={version:1,platform,pid,pgid,spawnToken,role,instanceToken,launchedAtUnixNs,argvBufferBytes,title,registeredArgvSha256,readyAt}` has platform `darwin|linux`, positive safe pid/pgid, positive canonical-decimal launchedAtUnixNs, argvBufferBytes null on Darwin and a positive safe integer on Linux, and cross-validates only role/instanceToken/title/registeredArgvSha256 against one immutable registration. Exact `ProcessGateStartup={version:1,generation,spawnToken,executionHost,registrationBundleSha256,state,ready,updatedAt}` has state prepared with ready null and state ready with one complete gate ProcessReady; the ready replacement is the durable gate identity, not a pid-only projection. Exact `ProcessGateSpawn={version:1,generation,spawnToken,executionHost,bootIdSha256,pid,pgid,startToken,spawnedAt}` is parent-written only after a successful spawn return and trusted start probe; bootIdSha256 equals startToken.bootIdSha256 and the owning generation/bundle boot hash. No clause requiring ProcessReady to equal runtime fields absent from ProcessMemberRegistration remains valid.
- Linux title length is measured, not guessed. Immediately before mutating its title, each trusted Node gate/child reads its own `/proc/self/cmdline` once with `O_RDONLY|O_NOFOLLOW`, rejects empty/partial/NUL-malformed input, and freezes the exact byte length as argvBufferBytes; after setting the exact UTF-8 title it rereads and requires `cmdline.length === argvBufferBytes`, the byte prefix equal the title, and every remaining byte be NUL with at least one remaining byte. Lock acquisition performs the same self-read before title mutation. Final `LockOwnerIdentity={pid,startToken,argvBufferBytes,probeSha256}` has argvBufferBytes null on Darwin and the measured positive safe integer on Linux; probeSha256 hashes the complete final LockOwnerProbeProjection including that nullable member. Truncation means any unequal total length. Parent-side argv arithmetic and the earlier registration-owned argvBufferBytes/launchedAt wording are invalid.
- Registration ownership is manifest-first and acyclic. Exact `ProcessRegistrationOwner` is `{kind:'release_command',manifestPath,writerId,releaseRun,unit,stageRun,logicalName,attempt}` or `{kind:'slugger',notificationPath,ownershipGeneration:1}`. Exact `ProcessRegistrationBundle={version:1,generation,spawnToken,executionHost,owner,memberRegistrations,memberRegistryPath,gateStartupPath,gateSpawnPath,childReadyPath,runAuthorizationPath,createdAt}` binds every host file to that owner; runAuthorizationPath equals the regular generation's childRunPath or the Slugger generation's publishPath. Final regular `SpawnGeneration={generation,spawnToken,executionHost,owner,registrationBundlePath,registrationBundleSha256,memberRegistrations,memberRegistryPath,gateStartupPath,gateSpawnPath,childReadyPath,childRunPath,status,abortedFrom,abortReason,gatePath,releasePath,memberRecords,preparedAt,spawnAuthorizedAt,gateRecordedAt,releasedAt,childRecordedAt,runAuthorizedAt,runningAt,endedAt}` is no-extra-fields. Final Slugger generation is the same through running, substitutes publishPath for childRunPath, adds resultPath, fixes generation 1, and uses terminalAt for endedAt. prepare-spawn first pushes/readback-verifies prepared generation bytes containing the complete expected bundle path/hash while the token directory is absent; only then may the parent create the mode-0700 token directory and exact mode-0600 bundle. A crash before the generation checkpoint creates no host path; a crash after it leaves only manifest-owned expected bytes that recovery creates or hash-validates. Every earlier bundle-before-manifest ordering and ownerless bundle schema is invalid.
- Gate spawn is separately authorized. Final regular and Slugger status domains are `prepared|spawn_authorized|recorded|released|child_recorded|run_authorized|running|aborted|ended` and `prepared|spawn_authorized|recorded|released|child_recorded|run_authorized|running|aborted|terminal` respectively. Exact CLI adds ordered `authorize-gate-spawn --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt A --generation N`, returning `{generation,status:'spawn_authorized'}`; Slugger performs the equivalent Desk-control transition. It requires the exact bundle and prepared startup file present, pushes/readbacks spawn_authorized with nonnull spawnAuthorizedAt, and only then permits one OS spawn invocation. A synchronous spawn error proves no process and may abort spawn_authorized. If the parent crashes after invocation but before ProcessGateSpawn persistence, recovery may adopt only one exact registered title or complete startup-ready record; zero evidence is `spawn_outcome_unobservable`, blocks without mutation, and can never abort, respawn, or create a later generation. A persisted ProcessGateSpawn plus dead/reaped proof before readiness may abort gate_startup_timeout. Thus no pre-title process can be hidden by a timeout/new generation.
- Spawn timestamps and notification projection are literal. prepared has only preparedAt nonnull; spawn_authorized preserves it and adds spawnAuthorizedAt; recorded adds the gate member/gateRecordedAt; released adds releasedAt; child_recorded adds the child member/childRecordedAt; run_authorized adds runAuthorizedAt; running adds runningAt; ended/terminal adds endedAt/terminalAt; aborted preserves exactly its abortedFrom prefix and adds the terminal time. Every later timestamp is null before its phase and no prior member/time is removed. SluggerNotification prepared permits generation prepared or spawn_authorized, recorded requires recorded, released permits released|child_recorded|run_authorized|running, observed requires terminal with non-aborted exit, and uncertain requires terminal non-exit or aborted. This replaces every older notification/status matrix.
- Unobservable spawn authorization waits durably. Exact task-artifact `ProcessSpawnWait={version:1,releaseRun,unit,stageRun,logicalName,attempt,generation,executionHost,spawnAuthorizedAt,registrationBundleSha256,waitOrdinal,notBefore,createdAt}` lives in that command attempt at `spawn-wait-<waitOrdinal>.v1.json`; Slugger uses the same fields under its Desk-control generation root with notificationPath replacing releaseRun/unit/stageRun/logicalName/attempt. Final no-extra-fields `ProcessCommand={mode:'process',logicalName,attempt,reservationToken,executionHost,status,command,storedCommandSha256,envNames,timeoutMs,deadlineStartedAt,deadlineAt,spawnGenerations,spawnWaitPaths,spawnWaitSetSha256,terminalSource,outPath,intentPath,armPath,dispatchPath,startedAt,endedAt,exitCode,warningCount,failureReason,interruptionReason,stdoutPath,stderrPath}` has spawnWaitPaths in contiguous ordinal order and spawnWaitSetSha256 over complete `{path,sha256}[]` bytes. Final `TerminalSluggerState={kind:'slugger',notificationPath,notificationSha256,notification,generation,spawnWaitPaths,spawnWaitSetSha256}` binds the equivalent Desk-control waits. The executor/terminal owner atomically writes, registers, pushes, and readback-verifies one immutable wait when the original total deadline reaches a spawn_authorized generation with no gate-spawn, ready record, or exact registered title; exact executor stdout is `{status:'waiting',waitPath,waitSha256,notBefore}` with exit zero, no StageRun/terminal failure, and Work Merger resumes the identical release:execute/release:terminal command at notBefore. A later title/ready record reconciles normally. A newly observed boot identity for the same host proves every process from the frozen executionHost boot is dead; after that proof only, recovery may abort gate_startup_timeout and permit the ordinary retry policy. No operator assertion, zero scan on the old boot, elapsed time, or wait ordinal proves absence.
- Host-control atomic writes have one closed recovery matrix. Final basenames are `registration.v1.json`, `gate-startup.v1.json`, `gate-spawn.v1.json`, `members.v1.json`, `child-ready.v1.json`, and `child-run.v1.json`; each has the sole sibling temp `<basename>.tmp`, mode 0600, in the token directory. A parent writer with final absent may promote a complete schema/hash-valid temp, remove a malformed/partial temp and rewrite only when no registered member can read that file, or remove an exact redundant temp when the final bytes already match. For gate-startup/child-ready member writes, a complete valid temp may be promoted; a partial/malformed temp is removed only after that exact member is dead/reaped, otherwise recovery waits. Final+temp disagreement, symlink/nonregular/wrong mode, unknown basename, live-writer ambiguity, or bytes not derivable from the owning generation blocks. Every promotion/removal uses file fsync, rename/unlink, and directory fsync. Terminal cleanup waits for ended/terminal push/readback and all members dead/reaped, removes temps first, then child-run, child-ready, members, gate-spawn, gate-startup, registration in reverse dependency order, fsyncs, and rmdirs only the empty token directory; an unknown residue blocks.
- Launch vectors use frozen absolute executables. Final `TrustedToolchain={version:1,node,pnpm,tsxEntry,gh,git,ps,security,tar,mv,ouro,wranglerEntry,cloudflareClient,checkedAt}` contains TrustedExecutable for every member. Logical command registries may persist portable names, but every actual ProcessLaunchSpec and TerminalCommandIntent argv replaces argv[0] or script entry with its frozen absolute target before hashing/spawn; no PATH lookup is executable authority. Ordinary gate argv is `[node.absolutePath,tsxEntry.absolutePath,'scripts/release-spawn-gate.ts','--gate',gatePath,'--release',releasePath,'--startup',gateStartupPath,'--gate-spawn',gateSpawnPath,'--child-ready',childReadyPath,'--registration-bundle',actualBundlePath,'--registration-bundle-sha256',actualBundleSha256,'--spawn-token',spawnToken,'--','<registered effect argv members...>']`, with bundle sentinel value indices 14 and 16. Child argv is `[node.absolutePath,tsxEntry.absolutePath,'scripts/release-spawn-gate.ts','--child','--role','child','--child-ready',childReadyPath,'--registration-bundle',actualBundlePath,'--registration-bundle-sha256',actualBundleSha256,'--spawn-token',spawnToken,'--','<registered effect argv members...>']`, with sentinel value indices 9 and 11. Slugger uses that gate vector and effect argv `[ouro.absolutePath,'msg','--to','slugger','Done: Shipped Clem feedback end to end']`; TerminalCleanup resolves tar/mv through tar.absolutePath/mv.absolutePath. The earlier bare pnpm/tar/mv/ouro vectors, missing child role, and indices 13/15 or 8/10 are invalid.
- Startup and local-ahead recovery are exhaustive. Legal host-ahead prefixes are: prepared plus missing/exact registration/startup files, which are created/reconciled before authorization; spawn_authorized plus one complete gate ready file with missing gate-spawn/member registry, which derives gate-spawn when possible, writes the one-member registry, and calls record-process; spawn_authorized plus an exact gate-spawn and prepared startup, which waits while live and aborts gate_startup_timeout only after dead/reaped proof; spawn_authorized plus gate ready/one-member registry, which calls record-process; released plus exact childReady with a missing/one-member registry, which derives and writes the two-member registry then calls record-child-process; released plus an exact two-member registry, which calls record-child-process; child_recorded with no child-run, which calls authorize-child-run; run_authorized with child-run absent, which publishes its already-frozen returned bytes; and run_authorized with exact child-run, which calls record-child-running. Gate ready followed by gate death before record aborts spawn_authorized with gate_exit_before_record; child ready followed by child death before two-member recording aborts released with child_exit_before_run. Every other ahead/behind mixture blocks; no member respawns and no file republishes.
- Abort pairs are final. abort-spawn accepts abortedFrom `prepared|spawn_authorized|recorded|released|child_recorded|run_authorized`; legal pairs are prepared with gate_startup_timeout only at the expired no-authorization prefix, spawn_authorized with gate_spawn_error|gate_startup_timeout|gate_exit_before_record, recorded with gate_exit_before_release, released with gate_exit_before_release|child_spawn_error|child_exit_before_run, child_recorded with child_exit_before_run, and run_authorized with child_exit_before_run only while child-run is absent. Each requires exact no-effect proof and preserves the complete prior prefix. `spawn_outcome_unobservable` is a blocker code, never an abort reason. The CLI grammar and tests use this exact domain.
- Process completion uses no undefined ProcessResult. After the registered effect terminates and every stream closes, finish-command validates/sanitizes the complete declared output and log set, then one manifest transition records the existing ProcessCommand terminal fields and changes the named generation to ended with endedAt equal command endedAt. A crash before that manifest rename leaves ProcessCommand running; recover marks it interrupted and the generation ended only after all members are dead/reaped, retaining diagnostics but appending no unvalidated artifact. A crash after rename is already terminal. Host files remain until that terminal/interrupted transition is pushed/read back. There is no persisted ProcessResult schema or output-before-validation ended transition.
- Slugger abort results are total. Final `SluggerProcessResult={version:1,generation:1,spawnToken,outcome,abortReason,exitCode,signal,stdoutSha256,stderrSha256,startedAt,endedAt}` adds outcome `aborted`. Non-aborted outcomes keep the earlier exact matrices and require abortReason null. Every aborted generation produces outcome aborted, notification uncertain, null exitCode/signal, empty-stream hashes, endedAt equal terminalAt, and abortReason equal the generation: gate_spawn_error has startedAt null; gate_startup_timeout and gate_exit_before_record use ProcessGateSpawn.spawnedAt when present else ProcessReady.readyAt; gate_exit_before_release uses gate member readyAt; child_spawn_error uses child startedAt null; and child_exit_before_run uses child ProcessReady.readyAt. Host files are retained through result plus terminal notification push/readback and dead/reaped proof, then follow the final reverse cleanup. No aborted pair projects exit, signal, spawn_error, not_spawned, or observation_error.
- Lock title ownership is field-exact. Final `LockOwnerProbeProjection={platform,pid,startToken,argvBufferBytes,executionHost,writerId,token,instanceToken,lockTitle}` and `ManifestLockOwner={version:1,writerId,token,instanceToken,lockTitle,priorTitle,executionHost,hostname,pid,lockOwnerIdentity,acquiredAt}` are no-extra-fields. ProcessTitleMutex.writerId/token/instanceToken/lockTitle/priorTitle equal those five owner fields; lockTitle is exact `spoonjoy-lock-<instanceToken>` and equals the observed current title while held, while priorTitle is the distinct title captured before mutation and restored on release. If lock unlink fails, mutex/title/owner remain held and the same release retries unlink only. After unlink succeeds, a title-restoration failure retains the mutex and lockTitle with lock absent; the same release retries restoration only and may never recreate/adopt the lock. Only observed priorTitle permits in-memory mutex deletion. Every failure before lock creation restores priorTitle then clears the mutex; any mismatch is indeterminate.
- Planner suite document bindings are outcome-specific and complete. Final no-extra-fields `SuccessorSuiteAttempt={kind,ordinal,status,terminalOutcome,skill,cwd,promptPath,promptSha256,documentBindingKind,planningPath,planningSha256,doingPath,doingSha256,invocationToken,dispatchIntentPath,dispatchIntentSha256,dispatchPath,dispatchSha256,agentId,artifacts,artifactSetSha256,startedAt,deadlineAt,endedAt}` uses documentBindingKind planner_snapshots for planner and canonical_promoted for doer. Planner paths are exactly its ordinal attempt snapshot paths and hashes are null until outputs freeze; doer paths/hashes are exact promoted canonical identity documents from prepared onward. Planner terminalOutcome is `approved|findings|snapshot_conflict|promotion_conflict`; doer is implemented. The final status/dispatch matrix remains prepared|dispatching|authorized|running|uncertain|interrupted|completed. No planner attempt binds or reads canonical paths before promotion, and no doer reads snapshot paths.
- Planner snapshot publication is prepared-first. Exact task-artifact `SuccessorPlannerSnapshotPublicationAttempt={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,oldProductHeadSha,planningPath,planningBefore,planningAfter,doingPath,doingBefore,doingAfter,phase,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,observedProductRemoteSha,startedAt,updatedAt}` lives at `artifacts/post-merge-successor/suite/planner/attempt-<N>-snapshot-publication.attempt.v1.json`, uses phase `prepared|outputs_frozen|committed|pushed|readback|conflict_restored`, and is pushed/read back with both before BlobStates absent and after/commit fields null before planner dispatch. If the planner is interrupted before outputs_frozen, recovery removes only absent-before, regular, non-symlink files confined to that attempt directory after proving no agent live and no unrelated change; unknown/dirty bytes block. outputs_frozen records both complete after BlobStates atomically before Git mutation. committed freezes the exact two-blob candidate commit/tree; pushed uses force-with-lease against oldProductHeadSha; readback requires fetch plus exact remote commit/tree/blob bytes. Exact immutable `SuccessorPlannerSnapshotPublication={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,oldProductHeadSha,planningPath,planningSha256,doingPath,doingSha256,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,publishedAt}` replaces the attempt at `artifacts/post-merge-successor/suite/planner/attempt-<N>-snapshot-publication.v1.json` after readback. A rejected lease restores/cleans local candidate state, fetches the observed noncandidate remote, and emits exact `SuccessorPlannerSnapshotConflict={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,oldProductHeadSha,candidateCommitSha,observedProductRemoteSha,code:'lease_conflict',conflictedAt}` at `artifacts/post-merge-successor/suite/planner/attempt-<N>-snapshot-conflict.v1.json`; the suite completes snapshot_conflict with no reviews/promotion, registers only `planner_snapshot_conflict`, and the next planner attempt starts from that remote. SuiteArtifactRef and PreReleaseArtifact kinds add `planner_snapshot_publication|planner_snapshot_conflict`; every file/write/commit/push/readback/cleanup response-loss prefix resumes exactly once.
- Planner attempt histories include snapshot outcomes. Every planner attempt that reaches reviews contains exactly one planner_snapshot_publication member before its three complete review chains; findings then has no promotion member, approved adds planner_promotion, and promotion_conflict adds planner_promotion_conflict. snapshot_conflict contains exactly planner_snapshot_conflict and no snapshot publication, review, promotion, or handoff member. The contiguous prior terminal-outcome domain is `findings|snapshot_conflict|promotion_conflict`; the final planner prompt's prior_planner_outcomes_json set contains the immediately prior attempt's three review artifacts for findings, its sole snapshot-conflict artifact for snapshot_conflict, or its three approved reviews plus promotion-conflict artifact for promotion_conflict. Ordinal one remains exact `[]`. No outcome is skipped and no approval/review carries across attempts.
- Promotion conflict cannot deadlock on a moving remote. After a rejected promotion lease, candidate metadata remains frozen; recovery restores a clean local canonical state at oldProductHeadSha, performs one fetch, and freezes that first observed remote SHA. If it equals candidate, exact tree/blob readback converts to successful promotion. If it differs, that observation is sufficient conflict evidence and recovery may atomically emit SuccessorPlannerPromotionConflict immediately after clean-state proof; later remote movement does not rewrite or invalidate the truthful receipt, and the next attempt reads current remote. The candidate is never pushed again. The earlier requirement for a stable third SHA, scalar mutation, fourth-SHA block, conflict_readback deadlock, or a fresh attempt before terminal conflict is invalid.
- Track archival linearizes disposition, close, and move together. Final TrackArchiveAttempt phase is `prepared|root_moved|archive_validated`; track_closed is invalid. prepared is pushed/read back at the active root with no TrackDisposition and null member hashes. Each retry rescans every task. If nonempty, one candidate writes kept_active TrackDisposition, removes the attempt, preserves active track frontmatter/root, commits/pushes/readbacks, and returns; archived bytes never existed. If empty, one atomic Desk candidate writes archived TrackDisposition at the trigger task, changes track frontmatter active to closed, computes the exact four-exclusion source manifest from those candidate bytes, moves that complete root to its unique target, rewrites the attempt there as root_moved with equal source/target hashes and booleans true, commits, and CAS-pushes. That accepted push is the sole archive linearization point. A rejected push discards the candidate, fetches, and rescans; a newly committed task therefore selects kept_active without replacing an archived disposition. A task created after the accepted move belongs to a distinct recreated active generation. archive_validated and receipt replacement remain read-only over the moved generation. Every earlier separately published archived disposition or track_closed checkpoint is invalid.
- API smoke matches the shipped contracts. Final health body projection is `{kind:'health',build}` and build equals sourceSha from exact raw body `{status:'ok',service:'spoonjoy',buildSha}`; workerVersionId exists only in ApiHeaderProjection.health and equals the release Worker header. Final public-cache projection requires exact `cacheControl:'public, max-age=60, stale-while-revalidate=300'` and `vary:['Authorization','Cookie']`. The final fifteen-row owned-route replacements remain unchanged. Any health body projection containing workerVersionId or shortened cache value is invalid.
- Red-first ownership is final. All ManifestLockOwner, LockOwnerIdentity, LockOwnerProbeProjection, Linux/Darwin lock-title probe, ProcessTitleMutex, unlink/restoration failure, and recursion/interleaving tests belong to Unit29.2.1a and their implementation belongs to Unit29.2.1b. Unit29.2.2a may consume those already-green primitives only to test executor interaction; it cannot introduce a new lock schema or first red lock behavior.

### Round 61 Cold-Gate Follow-up Closures

These clauses are later and final for every named subject.

- Stable host and boot identity are separate. executionHost reverts to the exact boot-independent hash/preimage declared in the security-critical preflight clause; the earlier clause adding bootIdSha256 to that preimage is invalid. Final `ProcessGateSpawnToken={bootIdSha256,kernelStartToken}` contains the boot hash plus parent-observable Darwin C-locale lstart or Linux stat field 22. ProcessGateSpawn.startToken is exactly that type. Final ProcessStartToken remains `{bootIdSha256,kernelStartToken,launchedAtUnixNs,instanceToken}` and a ready-derived ProcessIdentity requires its first two members equal ProcessGateSpawnToken, its pid/pgid equal ProcessGateSpawn, its instanceToken equal the registration/ready record, and its launchedAtUnixNs equal ProcessReady. Final ProcessRegistrationBundle, regular/Slugger SpawnGeneration, ProcessSpawnWait, ProcessSpawnBlocker, LockOwnerIdentity, ManifestLockOwner, and LockOwnerProbeProjection each add top-level bootIdSha256 immediately after executionHost or pid as applicable. Same executionHost plus unequal current bootIdSha256 proves every prior-boot member/lock owner dead; same boot retains ordinary probes. A different executionHost remains foreign and read-only.
- Final boot-scoped schemas are literal. `ProcessRegistrationBundle={version:1,generation,spawnToken,executionHost,bootIdSha256,owner,memberRegistrations,memberRegistryPath,gateStartupPath,gateSpawnPath,childSpawnPath,childReadyPath,runAuthorizationPath,deadlineAt,createdAt}`. Final regular SpawnGeneration is the preceding complete schema with bootIdSha256 immediately after executionHost and childSpawnPath immediately before childReadyPath; Slugger applies the same additions. Exact `LockOwnerStartToken={kernelStartToken,acquiredAtUnixNs,instanceToken}`, `LockOwnerIdentity={pid,bootIdSha256,startToken,argvBufferBytes,probeSha256}`, `LockOwnerProbeProjection={platform,pid,startToken,argvBufferBytes,executionHost,bootIdSha256,writerId,token,instanceToken,lockTitle}`, and `ManifestLockOwner={version:1,writerId,token,instanceToken,lockTitle,priorTitle,executionHost,bootIdSha256,hostname,pid,lockOwnerIdentity,acquiredAt}` replace every shorter form.
- Manifest-owned host timestamps are reproducible. ProcessRegistrationBundle.createdAt and prepared ProcessGateStartup.updatedAt both equal SpawnGeneration.preparedAt exactly; ready ProcessGateStartup.updatedAt equals its ready.readyAt. ProcessChildSpawn.createdAt/errorAt and every run-authorization timestamp follow their explicit generation timestamps below. Recovery therefore reconstructs every expected prepared byte and hash from the pushed generation without a fresh clock read.
- Child spawn is journaled symmetrically. Final basename `child-spawn.v1.json` and temp join the host-control registry. Exact `ProcessChildSpawn={version:1,generation,spawnToken,executionHost,bootIdSha256,registrationBundleSha256,state,pid,pgid,startToken,createdAt,errorAt}` has state spawned with positive pid/pgid, ProcessGateSpawnToken startToken, createdAt nonnull, errorAt null; or spawn_error with pid/pgid/startToken/createdAt null and errorAt nonnull. ProcessRegistrationBundle adds bootIdSha256, deadlineAt, and childSpawnPath; regular/Slugger generations add bootIdSha256 and childSpawnPath. The gate may attempt one child spawn only while current time is strictly before bundle.deadlineAt; it atomically records spawned after successful return/start probe or spawn_error after synchronous failure. A ready child cross-validates its later ProcessStartToken against child-spawn exactly as the gate does. Cleanup removes child-spawn after child-run/child-ready and before members.
- Host temp replacement permits only monotonic successors. Besides final-absent promotion, exact prepared gate-startup final plus one complete ready temp may replace to ready, and exact one-member registry final plus one complete two-member temp may replace to two-member, only after the named writer is proven dead/reaped or the current writer is resuming its own exact write. The candidate must preserve every immutable owner/generation/member and change only the declared state/member suffix. Live foreign writer waits. Any skipped, regressed, unrelated, malformed, or non-monotonic final/temp pair remains blocking.
- Release and child-spawn recovery are exhaustive. recorded with release absent calls release-spawn; released with release absent reconstructs and atomically publishes exact release bytes from immutable releasedAt before any child observation. released with release present then accepts: child-spawn spawn_error -> abort child_spawn_error; child-spawn spawned plus ready -> derive/persist two-member registry and record-child-process; child-spawn spawned plus dead/no-ready -> abort child_exit_before_run; no child-spawn plus one exact child title/ready -> adopt and persist child-spawn before the same reconciliation; and no child-spawn/title/ready -> the role child uncertainty protocol. Before deadline a live/ready child may continue only through record-child-process; at or after the immutable deadline any late gate/child is adopted solely to TERM/5000ms/KILL/reap and aborts the no-effect prefix, never release, child-run authorization, or registered effect. Same-host new-boot proof aborts gate uncertainty as gate_startup_timeout and child uncertainty as child_exit_before_run; no respawn occurs in either generation.
- Spawn waits are finite and role-qualified. Final `ProcessSpawnWait={version:1,releaseRun,unit,stageRun,logicalName,attempt,generation,role,executionHost,bootIdSha256,spawnAuthorityAt,registrationBundleSha256,waitOrdinal,notBefore,createdAt}` uses role gate|child, with spawnAuthorityAt equal generation.spawnAuthorizedAt for gate and generation.releasedAt for child, and exact command path `spawn-<role>-wait-<1|2|3>.v1.json`; Slugger path is `_meta/release-terminal/<identitySha256>/slugger/spawn-<role>-wait-<1|2|3>.v1.json` and substitutes notificationPath for releaseRun/unit/stageRun/logicalName/attempt. Initial arrays are [] with set hash SHA-256 of exact bytes `[]`. Wait ordinal N has notBefore exactly original deadlineAt plus N*30000ms and createdAt equal the observation time at or after the preceding boundary; reconciliation/termination/boot-change probes always run before time comparison. An early call returns the latest wait unchanged. At each reached boundary without evidence, append exactly the next ordinal; after ordinal 3 notBefore, atomically persist exact `ProcessSpawnBlocker={version:1,role,executionHost,bootIdSha256,generation,waitPaths,waitSetSha256,code:'host_reboot_required',createdAt}` at command `spawn-<role>-blocker.v1.json` or the same Slugger Desk-control root. Final no-extra-fields `ProcessCommand={mode:'process',logicalName,attempt,reservationToken,executionHost,status,command,storedCommandSha256,envNames,timeoutMs,deadlineStartedAt,deadlineAt,spawnGenerations,spawnWaitPaths,spawnWaitSetSha256,spawnBlockerPath,spawnBlockerSha256,terminalSource,outPath,intentPath,armPath,dispatchPath,startedAt,endedAt,exitCode,warningCount,failureReason,interruptionReason,stdoutPath,stderrPath}` and `TerminalSluggerState={kind:'slugger',notificationPath,notificationSha256,notification,generation,spawnWaitPaths,spawnWaitSetSha256,spawnBlockerPath,spawnBlockerSha256}` require blocker members both null before the cap and both nonnull/hash-valid afterward. The blocker is byte-stable and creates no more waits; only late-member terminate/reap or same-stable-host new-boot proof resolves it. Every resumed command has zero effect budget: it performs recovery probes/termination/abort only and can never release or authorize a child after original deadlineAt.
- Slugger aborted timestamps use persisted sources only. gate_spawn_error startedAt is null. gate_startup_timeout uses ProcessGateSpawn.spawnedAt when present, else ProcessGateStartup.ready.readyAt when present, else generation.spawnAuthorizedAt. gate_exit_before_record and gate_exit_before_release use ProcessGateStartup.ready.readyAt. child_spawn_error is null. child_exit_before_run uses childReady ProcessReady.readyAt when present, else ProcessChildSpawn.createdAt when present, else generation.releasedAt. endedAt always equals terminalAt. No undeclared member-ready or child-start field is referenced.
- Lock restoration failure has one state. Any failure to restore priorTitle while the lock path is absent, whether before lock creation, after failed acquisition, or after successful unlink, enters restoration_pending: the mutex and lockTitle remain held, lock recreation/adoption/acquisition is forbidden, and the same release/unwind retries title restoration only. Only observing priorTitle clears the mutex. A pre-lock failure clears immediately only when restoration already succeeded.
- Platform tools are total. Final `TrustedToolchain={version:1,node,pnpm,tsxEntry,gh,git,ps,sysctl,security,tar,mv,ouro,wranglerEntry,cloudflareClient,checkedAt}` has sysctl/security typed TrustedExecutable|null. Darwin requires both nonnull and invokes boot capture through sysctl.absolutePath; Linux requires both null and uses only the frozen descriptor read of proc boot_id. Every other member is nonnull on both platforms. Tests replace/race every nonnull target and reject the wrong platform null matrix.
- Planner workspaces and durable snapshots are distinct. Final SuccessorSuiteAttempt adds workspacePlanningPath/workspaceDoingPath immediately before documentBindingKind. Planner workspace paths are the product-repo ordinal attempt paths named to Work Planner; planner planningPath/doingPath are exact task-owned `artifacts/post-merge-successor/suite/planner/attempt-<N>-snapshots/planning.md` and `.../doing.md`. Doer workspace/document paths all equal the promoted canonical product paths. Replacement SnapshotPublicationAttempt adds workspacePlanningPath/workspaceDoingPath and durable planningPath/doingPath, and phase `snapshots_published` after outputs_frozen. After outputs_frozen, Work Merger atomically copies both exact bytes to the two task-owned paths, writes their hashes into the attempt, pushes/readbacks the task artifacts and snapshots_published attempt, and registers planning_snapshot/doing_snapshot before any product Git commit or lease. Reviews and promotion read only these durable bytes; the product candidate snapshot blobs must hash-equal them. Product workspace cleanup never removes task-owned snapshots.
- Snapshot publication leases are response-loss safe. SnapshotPublicationAttempt phase is `prepared|outputs_frozen|snapshots_published|committed|push_inflight|pushed|readback|conflict_detected|conflict_restored`. push_inflight, containing oldProductHeadSha/candidateCommitSha/candidateTreeSha, is pushed/read back in the task repo before the one product force-with-lease invocation. Recovery from push_inflight never reissues the push and fetches product remote: candidate means adopt pushed/readback; old head records conflict_detected code push_outcome_unobservable; any other head records lease_conflict. The conflict observation is task-pushed/read back before product cleanup. Final `SuccessorPlannerSnapshotConflict={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,planningPath,planningSha256,doingPath,doingSha256,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,observedProductRemoteSha,code,conflictedAt}` uses code `lease_conflict|push_outcome_unobservable`. snapshot_conflict SuiteAttempt retains exactly planning_snapshot, doing_snapshot, and planner_snapshot_conflict artifacts with resolvable bindings; no publication receipt/reviews/promotion exist.
- Promotion leases use the same push-inflight fence. SuccessorPlannerPromotionAttempt phase is `prepared|committed|push_inflight|pushed|readback|conflict_detected|conflict_restored`. push_inflight is task-pushed/read back before the sole product lease and is never reissued. Recovery fetches product remote: candidate adopts success; old head persists conflict_detected with code push_outcome_unobservable; any other head persists lease_conflict. Exact final SuccessorPlannerPromotionConflict expands code to `lease_conflict|push_outcome_unobservable`; its observedProductRemoteSha is the fetched SHA persisted before cleanup. conflict_restored proves clean canonical local state, then emits the terminal receipt. No unfenced promotion push or mutable first-observation scalar is legal.
- Track-move local crashes retain atomic semantics. Before constructing the archived move candidate, release-terminal persists exact Desk-control `TrackArchiveLinearizationAttempt={version:1,track,triggerTask,scanDeskSha,trackGeneration,sourceCommitSha,sourceTreeSha,targetPath,candidateTreeSha,phase,candidateCommitSha,observedDeskRemoteSha,startedAt,updatedAt}` at `_meta/release-terminal/<identitySha256>/track-generations/<trackGeneration>/<scanDeskSha>/linearization.attempt.v1.json`. Its phase domain is `prepared|candidate_built|push_inflight|observed`; push_inflight is pushed/read back outside the moving track before the sole move-CAS invocation, after which the candidate is rebuilt with that exact checkpoint as parent. Recovery accepts only remote checkpoint plus exact local source or exact target candidate, or remote accepted target candidate. Remote checkpoint proves the move absent, restores the exact source prepared tree, rescans, and may create a new contiguous linearization attempt; it writes kept_active only if that rescan is nonempty. Accepted target adopts root_moved. Any other remote discards local candidate, restores/fetches, and rescans. Unknown mixed roots/trees block. Thus filesystem move, commit, push, and response-loss crashes cannot publish archived disposition separately or lose a concurrent task.

### Round 61 Third Cold-Gate Closures

These clauses replace the corresponding follow-up clauses above.

- Spawn-event times equal persisted authority. ProcessGateSpawn.spawnedAt equals generation.spawnAuthorizedAt. ProcessChildSpawn.createdAt for spawned and errorAt for spawn_error equal generation.releasedAt. ProcessChildRun.authorizedAt and SluggerPublish.publishedAt equal generation.runAuthorizedAt. Every original/adopted write uses those values; no event-time clock read participates in host bytes. ProcessRegistrationBundle.createdAt and prepared startup updatedAt remain preparedAt, and ready startup updatedAt remains ready.readyAt.
- Release recovery is liveness-gated. At every initial or resumed boundary, `now < deadlineAt` is required immediately before OS gate spawn, release-spawn transition, release-file publication, gate child spawn, child-run/SluggerPublish publication, and registered-effect start; equality or later permits only probe, TERM/5000ms/KILL/reap, wait/blocker, no-effect abort, and command terminalization. Before deadline, recorded+release-absent first probes the exact same-boot gate: live calls release-spawn; dead/new-boot aborts gate_exit_before_release; indeterminate/foreign waits without mutation. released+release-absent does the same: live publishes reconstructed release bytes; dead/new-boot aborts gate_exit_before_release when release never became observable, while indeterminate/foreign waits. Released+release-present uses the final child-spawn matrix. No initial invocation receives authority that a resumed invocation lacks.
- Spawn blocker results and resolution are exact. When the finite cap persists a blocker, ordinary executor returns one LF-terminated compact canonical `{status:'blocked',blockerPath,blockerSha256,code:'host_reboot_required'}` on stdout, empty stderr, exit zero; Slugger returns the same fields inside ReleaseTerminalProgressResult blocked. Work Merger records the human-only host-reboot blocker and re-enters the identical command only after user action or an independently observed late member. Re-entry preserves every wait/blocker artifact, performs only boot/member proof and terminate/reap, aborts the generation, and for ordinary commands invokes exact `finish-command-after-abort --manifest M --writer-id W --release-run R --unit U --stage-run G --logical-name L --attempt A --generation N --reason host_reboot_required`, returning `{status:'failed',warningCount:null,failureReason:'spawn'}`; the StageRun then follows its ordinary same-unit retry/disposition policy with a fresh command deadline. Slugger directly writes the exact aborted SluggerProcessResult and uncertain terminal journal. No resolution creates another wait/blocker or effect.
- ProcessTitleMutex state is explicit and path-independent. Final `ProcessTitleMutex={state,writerId,token,instanceToken,lockTitle,priorTitle,lockDisposition}` has state `held|restoration_pending` and lockDisposition `absent|owned|foreign`. held/owned is the normal acquired lock and may retry only its own unlink; held/absent is pre-create; held/foreign follows EEXIST without ownership. Any prior-title restoration failure transitions to restoration_pending while preserving the observed disposition, regardless of path presence. restoration_pending never unlinks, adopts, recreates, or acquires any lock, including a foreign one; it retries only title restoration and clears the mutex only after observing priorTitle.
- Snapshot publication schema and phases are literal. Final `SuccessorPlannerSnapshotPublicationAttempt={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,oldProductHeadSha,workspacePlanningPath,workspacePlanningBefore,workspacePlanningAfter,workspaceDoingPath,workspaceDoingBefore,workspaceDoingAfter,planningPath,planningState,doingPath,doingState,phase,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,observedProductRemoteSha,conflictCode,pushGeneration,startedAt,updatedAt}` is no-extra-fields. prepared has both workspace-before BlobStates absent; workspace-after null; durable planning/doing states absent; candidate/observed/conflict/pushGeneration null. outputs_frozen adds both present workspace-after BlobStates and nothing else. snapshots_published changes both durable states to present with hashes equal their workspace-after bytes; only at this phase do SuiteAttempt planningSha256/doingSha256 become nonnull. committed adds candidate commit/tree while pushGeneration remains null. push_inflight adds one complete prepared registered-process pushGeneration before the sole product push; every later phase preserves that generation. pushed/readback add observedProductRemoteSha equal candidate with conflict null. conflict_detected adds observed noncandidate plus conflictCode; conflict_restored preserves both after clean product restoration. No field regresses or changes after first nonnull.
- Planner snapshot artifact membership is complete. PreReleaseArtifact and planner SuiteArtifactRef kinds add `planning_snapshot|doing_snapshot` with sole paths `artifacts/post-merge-successor/suite/planner/attempt-<N>-snapshots/planning.md` and `.../doing.md`. Every review-reaching attempt contains exactly those two snapshots, one planner_snapshot_publication receipt, and all three complete prompt/runtime/dispatch-intent/dispatch/review chains. findings adds no promotion/conflict; approved adds planner_promotion; promotion_conflict adds planner_promotion_conflict and no promotion. snapshot_conflict contains exactly the two snapshots plus planner_snapshot_conflict and no publication receipt/reviews/promotion. Every completed attempt also registers its suite_attempt receipt; PreReleaseArtifact is the exact corresponding union and no workspace product path is a task artifact.
- Track linearization is ordinal, cycle-free, and terminal. Exact mutable `TrackArchiveLinearizationAttempt={version:1,identitySha256,ordinal,predecessorPath,predecessorSha256,track,triggerTask,scanDeskSha,trackGeneration,sourceCommitSha,sourceTreeSha,targetPath,movePayloadSetSha256,commitMessage,authorName,authorEmail,commitAt,phase,observedDeskRemoteSha,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,outcome,startedAt,updatedAt}` lives at `_meta/release-terminal/<identitySha256>/track-generations/<trackGeneration>/<scanDeskSha>/linearization/attempt-<N>.attempt.v1.json`. Ordinal one has null predecessor pair; later ordinals bind the immediately prior receipt. prepared has phase prepared and all observed/candidate/outcome members null. push_inflight preserves those nulls and is pushed/read back before any private-index mutation or CAS; it fences source lease/target/move payload/commit metadata but deliberately contains no whole-tree or commit self-hash. From its fetched checkpoint SHA, release-terminal uses one fresh private index, exact trusted Git read-tree/update-index/write-tree/commit-tree arrays, the frozen deterministic commit environment/stdin, and that checkpoint as sole parent to derive one candidate, then performs one lease-CAS. observed adds observed remote and outcome `moved|absent|conflict`; moved alone has candidate commit/tree nonnull, while absent/conflict keep them null in the attempt.
- Track linearization recovery and receipts are exact. Fetch/readback after push_inflight locates at most one direct child of the checkpoint whose sole tree transform equals the frozen disposition/frontmatter/move/root_moved payload. Remote equal checkpoint is absent. Remote equal that child or any descendant preserving every moved-generation byte is moved. A descendant of checkpoint with no matching child is conflict; multiple matching children or changed moved bytes block. Local source/target/private-index states must be exact checkpoint or derived candidate and are restored/removed accordingly. observed is pushed/read back, then atomically replaces the attempt with exact immutable `TrackArchiveLinearizationReceipt={version:1,identitySha256,ordinal,predecessorPath,predecessorSha256,track,triggerTask,scanDeskSha,trackGeneration,sourceCommitSha,sourceTreeSha,targetPath,movePayloadSetSha256,observedDeskRemoteSha,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,outcome,completedAt}` at sibling `attempt-<N>.v1.json`; moved requires candidate fields, absent/conflict require them null. Only an absent/conflict receipt may authorize ordinal N+1 after a fresh rescan. A moved receipt authorizes root_moved adoption and no successor. These external Desk-control receipts are retained audit evidence, never TrackArchive members; final archive validation requires one latest moved receipt, no live `.attempt`, and no later ordinal.
- Track private-index commands are closed. privateIndexPath is the ordinal/token-qualified mode-0600 regular file under the terminal host-control root and is absent initially. Exact logical argv/cwd are `git read-tree --index-output=<privateIndexPath> <checkpointSha>` in Desk root; `git update-index -z --index-info` in Desk root with sole extra environment `GIT_INDEX_FILE=<privateIndexPath>` and the exact NUL-terminated BINARY-path-sorted mode/object/path stdin defined below; `git write-tree` with that same sole extra environment; `git commit-tree <candidateTreeSha> -p <checkpointSha>` under the already-frozen author/message/time/stdin environment; one `git push origin --force-with-lease=refs/heads/main:<checkpointSha> <candidateCommitSha>:refs/heads/main`; then `git fetch origin refs/heads/main:refs/remotes/origin/main`. Actual argv uses git.absolutePath. The external push-inflight checkpoint contains no candidate tree/commit field; the host-control journal derives and retains them for the exact lease command, and candidateTreeSha/candidateCommitSha first enter Desk evidence in observed/receipt after fetch identifies the direct child. Every command has the terminal intent/result checkpoint, and private index/temp removal is required before observed publication.

### Round 61 Fourth Cold-Gate Closures

These clauses are the final authority for their named fields and transitions.

- Prepared generations can expire without a spawn. abort-spawn additionally permits prepared with gate_startup_timeout exactly when now >= deadlineAt, spawnAuthorizedAt and every later timestamp/member are null, no gate spawn/title/ready exists, and the manifest proves authorize-gate-spawn never occurred. The aborted generation has abortedFrom prepared and no-effect proof; Slugger aborted result startedAt is null. finish-command-after-abort reason domain is `pre_spawn_deadline|host_reboot_required|spawn_abort`, with pre_spawn_deadline selecting this pair. Prepared has no other abort reason.
- Released may prove the gate never received release. The final abort matrix additionally permits released with gate_exit_before_release only when release bytes are absent and the exact recorded gate is dead/reaped or prior-boot; it preserves releasedAt and the one gate member.
