Indeterminate, live same-boot, or foreign gate cannot take this pair.
- Child liveness is a complete Cartesian branch. For child-spawn spawned plus no ready: same-boot live waits before deadline; dead/reaped or new-boot aborts child_exit_before_run; indeterminate/foreign enters role-child waits; at/after deadline a live child is terminated/reaped then aborts. For spawned plus ready: same-boot live before deadline writes/reconciles the two-member registry and records the child; dead/reaped or new-boot aborts child_exit_before_run; indeterminate/foreign waits; at/after deadline terminate/reap then abort. spawn_error aborts child_spawn_error. No child-spawn/title/ready uses uncertainty waits; an exact title/ready without receipt is adopted into spawned first and then follows this table. No ready child is recorded without a live same-boot proof.
- Terminal progress has two blocked variants. Final no-extra-fields `ReleaseTerminalProgressResult={mode,terminalKind,status,terminalPhase,attemptOrdinal,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,waitPath,waitSha256,resolutionPath,resolutionSha256,blockerPath,blockerSha256,blockerCode,successorJournalPath,successorJournalSha256,nextAttemptOrdinal}` preserves all prior retrying/waiting/resolved/repair-successor matrices with blocker fields null. disposition-blocked has status blocked, nonnull disposition pair, blocker fields null. host-reboot-blocked is legal only for slugger, has disposition/wait/resolution/successor/next fields null, blockerPath/blockerSha256 nonnull, and blockerCode host_reboot_required. No mixed blocked form is legal.
- Finish-after-abort is a distinct no-effect terminalization. It requires one hash-valid aborted generation plus its retained waits/blocker when applicable, all members dead/reaped, empty sanitized stdout/stderr files, absent out tree, and no appended output artifact. It atomically sets ProcessCommand status failed, terminalSource `aborted`, endedAt equal generation.endedAt, exitCode null, warningCount null, failureReason spawn, interruptionReason null, retains log paths/hashes, advances manifest revision/updatedAt and ReleaseContinuity once, and changes no generation field. Exact success stdout object is `{status:'failed',warningCount:null,failureReason:'spawn'}`. Byte-identical replay is a no-op.
- Boot identity has one equality class. One generation.bootIdSha256 is frozen at prepare-spawn and must byte-equal registration bundle, gate/child spawn top-level boot hash, every nested ProcessGateSpawnToken/ProcessStartToken, ProcessReady platform probe, member registry ProcessIdentity, ProcessSpawnWait/Blocker, and Slugger copies. One lock owner boot hash must byte-equal ManifestLockOwner, LockOwnerIdentity, LockOwnerProbeProjection, and its observed current boot. Any disagreement is schema-invalid before live/dead/new-boot classification.
- Suite artifacts are append-only at every status. Final SuccessorSuiteAttempt.artifacts is always the complete BINARY-path-sorted immutable prefix of validated SuiteArtifactRef files already published for that attempt; artifactSetSha256 always hashes exact compact canonical `{kind,path,sha256}[]` bytes, including SHA-256 of `[]` before the first artifact, and is never null. Status prepared/dispatching/authorized/running/uncertain/interrupted may retain any legal contiguous producer prefix: empty before durable snapshots, then planning_snapshot+doing_snapshot together, then optional planner_snapshot_publication, then each review chain only in ordinal/field order, then promotion/conflict. uncertain/interrupted preserve the longest prefix and never discard files. completed requires exactly the outcome set in the final artifact-membership clause plus suite_attempt registration outside its self-referential artifact array. Doer follows the same append-only rule over its existing registry order.
- Snapshot conflict receipts retain their lease basis. Final `SuccessorPlannerSnapshotConflict={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,oldProductHeadSha,planningPath,planningSha256,doingPath,doingSha256,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,observedProductRemoteSha,code,conflictedAt}` requires push_outcome_unobservable iff observedProductRemoteSha equals oldProductHeadSha, and lease_conflict iff it differs from both oldProductHeadSha and candidateCommitSha.
- Promotion attempt conflict fields are literal. Final no-extra-fields `SuccessorPlannerPromotionAttempt={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,planningSnapshotPath,planningSnapshotSha256,doingSnapshotPath,doingSnapshotSha256,canonicalPlanningPath,canonicalDoingPath,productBranch,oldProductHeadSha,oldProductTreeSha,candidatePlanningBlobSha,candidateDoingBlobSha,commitMessage,authorName,authorEmail,commitAt,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,phase,productRemoteSha,conflictCode,pushGeneration,startedAt,updatedAt}` has phase `prepared|committed|push_inflight|pushed|readback|conflict_detected|conflict_restored`. pushGeneration is null in prepared/committed, is one complete prepared registered-process generation at push_inflight, and is preserved thereafter. conflictCode is null through successful readback; conflict_detected/conflict_restored require it `lease_conflict|push_outcome_unobservable`, with push_outcome_unobservable iff productRemoteSha equals oldProductHeadSha and lease_conflict iff productRemoteSha differs from old/candidate. The terminal conflict receipt preserves the same equality.
- Product lease pushes use the registered process protocol. ProcessRegistrationOwner adds `{kind:'planner_product_push',successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,pushKind:'snapshot'|'promotion'}`. SuccessorPlannerSnapshotPublicationAttempt and SuccessorPlannerPromotionAttempt each carry the complete nullable pushGeneration defined above. push_inflight begins with its prepared generation; the exact force-with-lease command runs through manifest-first bundle, spawn authorization, gate/child registry, deadline, waits/blocker, streams, finish, and dead/reaped cleanup defined above. Recovery never fetches/classifies product remote while any push member is live; same-boot live waits, dead/reaped proceeds, indeterminate/foreign blocks, and new boot proves dead. Only after terminal/dead proof may candidate/old/third remote map to success or conflict. This process evidence is part of the attempt, not a separate mutable product path.
- Track scans reprepare atomically. Final TrackArchiveAttempt adds `scanOrdinal,priorLinearizationReceiptPath,priorLinearizationReceiptSha256` after trackGeneration. Initial prepared scanOrdinal is 1 with null prior pair. After an absent/conflict linearization receipt, release-terminal fetches/rescans. A nonempty scan writes kept_active. An empty scan atomically replaces the active prepared attempt with scanOrdinal+1, new scanDeskSha equal the fetched commit actually scanned, newly derived trackGeneration/target/locator, null source/target manifests, and prior pair equal the immediately preceding receipt; it commits/pushes/readbacks before linearization ordinal N+1. The prior receipt preserves the replaced attempt hash. No ordinal reuses stale scan identity.
- Track command evidence is host-control until observation. Exact mode-0600 `TrackLinearizationCommandJournal={version:1,identitySha256,linearizationOrdinal,executionHost,bootIdSha256,fenceDeskSha,privateIndexPath,phase,nextCommandOrdinal,commands,activeCommand,startedAt,updatedAt}` lives under `<hostControlRoot>/track-linearization/<identitySha256>/attempt-<N>/journal.v1.json`, never Desk. ProcessRegistrationOwner adds `{kind:'track_linearization',identitySha256,linearizationOrdinal,commandOrdinal}`. commands is the contiguous immutable prefix of the exact TerminalCommandResult schema and activeCommand is null or the exact TerminalCommandIntent schema; in both, sequence equals commandOrdinal and name is exactly `track-read-tree|track-update-index|track-write-tree|track-commit-tree|track-lease-push|track-fetch` for ordinals 0 through 5. Each active command is persisted before spawn and runs through the exact registered process protocol; phase `prepared|building|push_inflight|observing|complete` and nextCommandOrdinal equal the contiguous immutable result prefix. No Desk mutation occurs between the external push_inflight checkpoint and lease-push. Live command waits; dead/reaped resumes only safe read/build/fetch commands, while lease-push is never reissued and is classified only by fetched ancestry/tree after dead proof. Foreign/indeterminate blocks. After complete, exact sanitized command results/hash are projected once into the external observed TrackArchiveLinearizationAttempt, then host journal/private index cleanup precedes receipt replacement.
- Private index bytes are unambiguous. The host token directory is created under umask 0077; after read-tree, release-terminal O_NOFOLLOW-opens/fstats the private index, requires a regular same-uid-owned mode-0600 inode, idempotently fchmods 0600, fsyncs, and rereads the same device/inode before update. update argv is exact `git update-index -z --index-info`; stdin is the complete NUL-terminated BINARY-path-sorted mode/object/path record set and permits tabs/newlines only through `-z`. A missing index is legal only while the registered read-tree command is absent or safely resumable; wrong mode/owner/type, symlink, identity drift, or partial temp blocks without chmod or command advance. The final fetch is exact `git fetch origin refs/heads/main:refs/remotes/origin/main`.

### Round 61 Fifth Cold-Gate Closures

These clauses are the final authority for their named fields, envelopes, producer orders, and transitions.

- Owner-local registered commands have one durable envelope. Exact no-extra-fields `RegisteredProcessWait={role,generation,executionHost,bootIdSha256,spawnAuthorityAt,registrationBundleSha256,waitOrdinal,notBefore,createdAt}` uses role `gate|child`, contiguous ordinal 1..3, and the same finite timing/liveness rules as ProcessSpawnWait. Exact `RegisteredProcessBlocker={role,generation,executionHost,bootIdSha256,waits,waitSetSha256,code:'host_reboot_required',createdAt}` embeds the complete immutable wait prefix. Exact `RegisteredProcessTerminalResult={outcome,exitCode,signal,stdoutSha256,stderrSha256,warningCount,failureReason,startedAt,endedAt}` has outcome `exit|signal|timeout_term|timeout_kill|spawn_error|observation_error|aborted`: exit has integer exitCode 0..255/null signal and failureReason null only for zero else process_exit; signal has null exitCode/finite declared signal/failureReason signal; timeout_term|timeout_kill have null exitCode and SIGTERM|SIGKILL with failureReason timeout; spawn_error|observation_error have null exit/signal and failureReason spawn|observation; aborted has null exit/signal/warningCount, failureReason spawn, and startedAt null only for a prepared abort. Every result has complete sanitized stream hashes and canonical endedAt. Exact `RegisteredProcessCommandEnvelope={version:1,owner,commandOrdinal,logicalName,intent,stdinSha256,executionHost,bootIdSha256,status,timeoutMs,deadlineStartedAt,deadlineAt,generation,waits,waitSetSha256,blocker,stdoutPath,stderrPath,result,updatedAt}` uses one exact ProcessRegistrationOwner, nonnegative safe commandOrdinal, exact TerminalCommandIntent with matching sequence/name/argv/cwd/timeout, SHA-256 of complete stdin including the empty byte string, and status `prepared|active|waiting|blocked|terminal`. prepared has a prepared generation, empty waits/hash of `[]`, null blocker/result; active has a legal nonterminal generation; waiting has a nonempty immutable wait prefix and null blocker/result; blocked has the complete matching blocker and null result; terminal has an ended or aborted generation, a complete result, preserved waits/blocker, and every member dead/reaped. Re-entry may move waiting/blocked back to active only after the declared late-member or new-boot proof and preserves all prior evidence. Every generation transition, wait, blocker, stream close, abort, result, and cleanup boundary atomically rewrites the owner-local envelope before the next effect; byte-identical replay is a no-op.
- Owner-local hashes are literal. RegisteredProcessCommandEnvelope.waitSetSha256 hashes exact compact canonical waits bytes, RegisteredProcessBlocker.waitSetSha256 hashes its byte-identical waits, and every empty wait set hashes exact UTF-8 `[]`. Track commandResultSetSha256 hashes exact compact canonical commandResults bytes. No path-set preimage or omitted empty hash is legal for these inline sets.
- Planner push evidence is complete and survives terminal receipt replacement. Final no-extra-fields `SuccessorPlannerSnapshotPublicationAttempt={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,oldProductHeadSha,workspacePlanningPath,workspacePlanningBefore,workspacePlanningAfter,workspaceDoingPath,workspaceDoingBefore,workspaceDoingAfter,planningPath,planningState,doingPath,doingState,phase,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,observedProductRemoteSha,conflictCode,pushGeneration,pushCommand,startedAt,updatedAt}` and `SuccessorPlannerPromotionAttempt={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,planningSnapshotPath,planningSnapshotSha256,doingSnapshotPath,doingSnapshotSha256,canonicalPlanningPath,canonicalDoingPath,productBranch,oldProductHeadSha,oldProductTreeSha,candidatePlanningBlobSha,candidateDoingBlobSha,commitMessage,authorName,authorEmail,commitAt,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,phase,productRemoteSha,conflictCode,pushGeneration,pushCommand,startedAt,updatedAt}` use their previously final phase domains. pushGeneration and pushCommand are both null before push_inflight; push_inflight atomically adds one prepared generation and one prepared RegisteredProcessCommandEnvelope owned by the matching planner_product_push, and pushCommand.generation is byte-equal pushGeneration after every rewrite. The sole lease command may begin only from that pushed/read-back state. Final immutable receipts are `SuccessorPlannerSnapshotPublication={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,oldProductHeadSha,planningPath,planningSha256,doingPath,doingSha256,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,pushGeneration,pushCommand,publishedAt}`, `SuccessorPlannerSnapshotConflict={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,oldProductHeadSha,planningPath,planningSha256,doingPath,doingSha256,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,observedProductRemoteSha,code,pushGeneration,pushCommand,conflictedAt}`, `SuccessorPlannerPromotion={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,planningSnapshotPath,planningSnapshotSha256,doingSnapshotPath,doingSnapshotSha256,canonicalPlanningPath,canonicalPlanningSha256,canonicalDoingPath,canonicalDoingSha256,productCommitSha,productTreeSha,pushGeneration,pushCommand,promotedAt}`, and `SuccessorPlannerPromotionConflict={version:1,successorKey,plannerAttemptOrdinal,oldProductHeadSha,candidateCommitSha,observedProductRemoteSha,code,pushGeneration,pushCommand,conflictedAt}`. Every receipt requires terminal pushCommand, byte-equal pushGeneration, dead/reaped members, retained waits/blocker/streams/result, and completed host cleanup; code equality remains old=head -> push_outcome_unobservable and third SHA -> lease_conflict. No remote fetch/classification or attempt replacement occurs while pushCommand is nonterminal.
- Planner push phase domains are literal. SuccessorPlannerSnapshotPublicationAttempt phase is exactly `prepared|outputs_frozen|snapshots_published|committed|push_inflight|pushed|readback|conflict_detected|conflict_restored`; SuccessorPlannerPromotionAttempt phase is exactly `prepared|committed|push_inflight|pushed|readback|conflict_detected|conflict_restored`. During every pushCommand rewrite the attempt remains push_inflight; only a terminal envelope permits pushed or conflict_detected, and readback or conflict_restored alone permits immutable receipt replacement.
- Ordinary abort terminalization is total. finish-command-after-abort reason domain is exactly `pre_spawn_deadline|host_reboot_required|spawn_abort`: pre_spawn_deadline selects only prepared/gate_startup_timeout at the expired no-authorization prefix; host_reboot_required selects only an abort reached after the retained blocker resolves; spawn_abort selects every other legal no-effect abort pair from the final abort matrix. All three require the same final no-output/dead-reaped proof and terminalize ProcessCommand identically with warningCount null. No aborted ordinary ProcessCommand can remain nonterminal.
- Track scan lineage is literal. Final no-extra-fields `TrackArchiveAttempt={version:1,track:'spoonjoy-v2',sourcePath:'spoonjoy-v2',targetPath,triggerTask,taskArchiveKind,taskArchiveSha256,scanDeskSha,trackGeneration,scanOrdinal,priorLinearizationReceiptPath,priorLinearizationReceiptSha256,priorTrackArchiveAttemptPath,priorTrackArchiveAttemptSha256,trackArchiveLocator,sourceMembers,sourceMemberSetSha256,targetMemberSetSha256,remainingUnarchivedTasks:[],phase,trackClosed,sourceTreeMoved,targetPresent,archiveValid,startedAt,updatedAt}` uses positive scanOrdinal. Initial prepared uses ordinal 1 and both prior pairs null. Every linearization ordinal equals scanOrdinal. After absent/conflict, one atomic fetched rescan replaces the active attempt with scanOrdinal+1; its prior receipt pair names the immediately preceding immutable linearization receipt and its prior-attempt pair names/hashes the exact TrackArchiveAttempt bytes cited by that receipt. New scanDeskSha, trackGeneration, targetPath, locator, source members, and hashes derive only from the fetched tree actually scanned. A moved receipt permits no successor attempt.
- Track linearization evidence has complete literal schemas. Final no-extra-fields `TrackArchiveLinearizationAttempt={version:1,identitySha256,ordinal,scanOrdinal,predecessorPath,predecessorSha256,trackArchiveAttemptPath,trackArchiveAttemptSha256,track,triggerTask,scanDeskSha,trackGeneration,sourceCommitSha,sourceTreeSha,targetPath,movePayloadSetSha256,commitMessage,authorName,authorEmail,commitAt,phase,observedDeskRemoteSha,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,commandResults,commandResultSetSha256,outcome,startedAt,updatedAt}` requires ordinal=scanOrdinal and the attempt path/hash to resolve the current TrackArchiveAttempt. prepared and push_inflight have null observed/candidate/outcome, commandResults `[]`, and its exact hash. observed has nonnull observed/candidate tree/candidate commit, exactly six results, and outcome moved|absent|conflict. Final no-extra-fields `TrackArchiveLinearizationReceipt={version:1,identitySha256,ordinal,scanOrdinal,predecessorPath,predecessorSha256,trackArchiveAttemptPath,trackArchiveAttemptSha256,track,triggerTask,scanDeskSha,trackGeneration,sourceCommitSha,sourceTreeSha,targetPath,movePayloadSetSha256,observedDeskRemoteSha,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,commandResults,commandResultSetSha256,outcome,completedAt}` preserves every observed field for all outcomes; candidate fields are never discarded after construction. The next TrackArchiveAttempt copies this receipt pair and its trackArchiveAttempt path/hash as the two prior lineage pairs.
- The track host journal owns registered commands and resolves lease response loss without a prefix deadlock. Final ProcessRegistrationOwner track variant is `{kind:'track_linearization',identitySha256,linearizationOrdinal,commandOrdinal,processAttemptOrdinal}` with positive processAttemptOrdinal. Exact no-extra-fields `TrackLinearizationCommandResult={ordinal,name,priorProcesses,process,remoteOutcome,completedAt}` contains a BINARY-stable append-only array of terminal failed/reconciled RegisteredProcessCommandEnvelopes followed by the one terminal completing process; name is `track-read-tree|track-update-index|track-write-tree|track-commit-tree|track-lease-push|track-fetch`, remoteOutcome is moved|absent|conflict exactly for ordinal 4 and null otherwise. Exact `TrackLeasePushObservation={pushCommand,fetchAttemptOrdinal,priorFetchCommands,fetchCommand,observedDeskRemoteSha,outcome,updatedAt}` begins only after the sole ordinal-4 pushCommand is terminal and every member dead/reaped; fetchAttemptOrdinal starts at 1, priorFetchCommands is empty, and fetchCommand is null, then one registered ordinal-5 track-fetch envelope. A terminal unsuccessful fetch appends immutably to priorFetchCommands, increments fetchAttemptOrdinal, and permits a fresh read-only fetch only after the existing failure/wait disposition; a successful terminal fetch alone sets observed SHA/outcome. Final `TrackLinearizationCommandJournal={version:1,identitySha256,linearizationOrdinal,executionHost,bootIdSha256,fenceDeskSha,trackArchiveAttemptPath,trackArchiveAttemptSha256,privateIndexPath,indexInfoStdinSha256,candidateTreeSha,candidateCommitSha,phase,nextCommandOrdinal,commands,priorCommandProcesses,activeCommand,pushObservation,startedAt,updatedAt}` has phase `prepared|building|lease_ready|push_running|observing|complete`. commands is initially `[]`, then the immutable contiguous results 0..3; write-tree result atomically freezes candidateTreeSha and commit-tree freezes candidateCommitSha. priorCommandProcesses contains only terminal failed/reconciled attempts for nextCommandOrdinal; activeCommand is null or one nonterminal RegisteredProcessCommandEnvelope for ordinals 0..4. A safe read/build command may get a fresh processAttemptOrdinal only under the exact TerminalCommand pre/post-state retry/reconcile rule and preserves the prior terminal envelope; successful completion appends one TrackLinearizationCommandResult and clears the prior/current fields. lease_ready has results 0..3 and both candidate fields; push_running has active ordinal 4 and no prior attempt because the lease command is invoked once. The lease command is never reissued: after dead proof it moves atomically from activeCommand to pushObservation, commands remains 0..3, nextCommandOrdinal remains 4, and phase becomes observing. The nested registered fetch may then run despite the unresolved ordinal-4 remote outcome. Once one fetch succeeds, ancestry/tree classification sets observedDeskRemoteSha/outcome and one atomic journal rewrite appends result 4 with empty priorProcesses and that remoteOutcome plus result 5 with priorFetchCommands and null remoteOutcome, clears pushObservation, sets nextCommandOrdinal 6, and completes. Live waits, foreign/indeterminate blocks, and no second active process exists. The complete six-result array and its SHA are projected byte-for-byte into the external observed attempt and final receipt before host cleanup.
- Track private-index input is byte-exact. Exact no-extra-fields `TrackIndexInfoRecord={path,kind,mode,objectId}` has a normalized relative UTF-8 path with no NUL, kind add|delete, add mode `100644|100755` with the exact lowercase 40-hex blob object ID, and delete mode `0` with objectId `0000000000000000000000000000000000000000`. There is exactly one record for each changed index path: a moved-away source is delete, a created/moved-to/modified target is add, and an in-place modification is add only. Records are unique and BINARY-sorted by raw UTF-8 path bytes. Each record serializes as exact `ASCII(mode) + 0x20 + ASCII(objectId) + 0x09 + UTF8(path) + 0x00`; tabs and newlines inside path remain raw path bytes after the single delimiter tab, while NUL is forbidden. Concatenation of all records with no prefix/suffix is the sole stdin to `git update-index -z --index-info`; its SHA-256 is journal.indexInfoStdinSha256 and byte-equals the ordinal-1 process stdinSha256. Empty, duplicate, unsorted, mode/object mismatch, stage-form input, missing source deletion, extra path, or a SHA mismatch blocks before Git.
- Suite producer prefixes are branch-exact. Planner starts empty, atomically adds planning_snapshot then doing_snapshot, then either adds planner_snapshot_conflict and completes snapshot_conflict, or adds planner_snapshot_publication and proceeds. A review-reaching attempt then adds for ordinal 1, 2, and 3 exactly planner_review_prompt, planner_review_dispatch_intent, planner_review_dispatch, planner_review_runtime, planner_review before beginning the next ordinal. findings completes after review 3; approved adds planner_promotion; promotion_conflict adds planner_promotion_conflict. After every producer step artifacts is the complete BINARY-path-sorted set published so far, even when the new path sorts before an older path. Doer starts with registry. For each SuccessorImplementationRegistry group in BINARY groupId order, its test phase adds red_tree, then every expected-red command's stdout command_log, stderr command_log, and command, then unit_red; its implementation phase adds each green command in the same log/log/command order. After all groups reach one final clean pushed implementation head/tree, each group in the same order runs its final green test replay and verification commands in log/log/command order and adds the group's verification artifacts in BINARY path order. Only after that final head/tree is frozen are unit_receipts added for every group's test, implementation, and verification unit in that order, so every receipt binds the same final sourceHeadSha/treeSha required by its schema. Then each reviewRole in the registry's exact order adds review_prompt, review_dispatch_intent, review_dispatch, review_runtime, review_report; every coverage artifact follows in its frozen BINARY path order; implementation_receipt is last. uncertain/interrupted preserves exactly the longest legal producer prefix. No undefined existing-registry order remains.

### Round 61 Sixth Cold-Gate Closures

These clauses are the final authority for registered-command terminal proof, track receipt completeness, and doer command plans.

- Registered process terminal proof distinguishes execution from reconciliation. Replacement no-extra-fields `RegisteredProcessTerminalResult={outcome,disposition,exitCode,signal,stdoutSha256,stderrSha256,warningCount,failureReason,preStateSha256,postStateSha256,startedAt,endedAt}` has outcome `exit|signal|timeout_term|timeout_kill|spawn_error|observation_error|aborted|reconciled` and disposition `succeeded|failed|reconciled|aborted`. preStateSha256 always equals intent.preStateSha256. exit zero with warningCount zero is succeeded, null failureReason, and nonnull registry-validated postStateSha256; exit nonzero or any positive warningCount is failed with process_exit|warning and nullable observed post state. signal/timeout are failed with nonnegative warningCount and nullable observed post state. spawn_error/observation_error are failed with null warningCount and nullable observed post state. reconciled has disposition reconciled, null exit/signal, SHA-256 of empty stdout/stderr, warningCount zero, null failureReason, nullable startedAt, and nonnull postStateSha256 byte-equal the registry-derived expected post state observed only after every prior member is dead/reaped. aborted has disposition aborted, null exit/signal/warningCount/post state, failureReason spawn, and startedAt null only for the prepared abort. No failed observation can be relabeled reconciled, and no synthetic exit result may represent a recovered post state.
- Registered process attempts are contiguous and retained. For a track command, the owner processAttemptOrdinal values across TrackLinearizationCommandResult.priorProcesses followed by process are exactly 1..N with no gap/duplicate; priorProcesses contains only terminal envelopes whose result.disposition is failed. For ordinals 0,1,2,3,5, the completing process disposition is succeeded|reconciled and its postStateSha256 equals the command registry's expected state. Ordinal 4 has exactly one process attempt, may have any terminal disposition, and is completing only because the nested fetched observation supplies remoteOutcome. Journal priorCommandProcesses and TrackLeasePushObservation.priorFetchCommands obey the same contiguous owner ordinals; a reconciled envelope always occupies the completing process field, never a prior array. Every terminal envelope preserves pre/post proof after host cleanup and is copied byte-for-byte into the external command results.
- Track linearization receipts preserve commit authority. Final no-extra-fields `TrackArchiveLinearizationReceipt={version:1,identitySha256,ordinal,scanOrdinal,predecessorPath,predecessorSha256,trackArchiveAttemptPath,trackArchiveAttemptSha256,track,triggerTask,scanDeskSha,trackGeneration,sourceCommitSha,sourceTreeSha,targetPath,movePayloadSetSha256,commitMessage,authorName,authorEmail,commitAt,observedDeskRemoteSha,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,commandResults,commandResultSetSha256,outcome,completedAt}` carries the four commit-authority fields in the same order and byte-equal values as the observed attempt. Trusted Git recomputation from source parent, candidate tree, commitMessage, authorName, authorEmail, and commitAt must reproduce candidateCommitSha for moved, absent, and conflict before attempt replacement.
- Doer command plans are registry-owned. Replacement no-extra-fields `SuccessorImplementationRegistry={version:1,successorKey,doingPath,doingSha256,groups,reviewRoles,createdAt}` uses `groups:{groupId,testUnitId,implementationUnitId,verificationUnitId,phasePlans}[]` and exact no-extra-fields `SuccessorImplementationPhasePlan={phase,unitId,commands}`. phasePlans is exactly `[test,implementation,verification]`, unitId matches the corresponding group field, and `commands` is a nonempty array of `SuccessorCommandPlan={commandOrdinal,logicalName,argv,cwd,envNames,timeoutMs,executionWindow,expected,replayOfCommandOrdinal}`. commandOrdinal is contiguous from 1 within each phase; logicalName is finite and unique within the phase; argv is a nonempty no-shell string array; cwd is the successor repo cwd; envNames is BINARY-sorted unique and secret-free; timeoutMs is positive; executionWindow is red|implementation|final_verification; expected is red|green. Test has at least one red-window/red command and one final-verification/green command whose replayOfCommandOrdinal points to the matching red command and whose logicalName/argv/cwd/envNames/timeoutMs are byte-equal; implementation commands are implementation/green with null replay; verification commands are final_verification/green with null replay. The three planner reviews approve the complete registry-bound doing bytes before Work Doer release; registry creation deterministically extracts these literal command tables from the approved doing document's machine-readable per-unit command blocks and rejects a missing/extra/ambiguous block.
- Successor doing command blocks have one grammar. Immediately after each implementation-only unit's Acceptance line, Work Planner writes exactly one LF-delimited fenced block whose opening line is three backticks plus `spoonjoy-command-plan-v1`, whose second line is the compact canonical JSON array of that unit's complete SuccessorCommandPlan objects, and whose closing line is three backticks; no blank or additional line is legal. The block array byte-equals the matching registry phasePlan.commands. Unit status/What/Output/Acceptance remain the ordinary doing template; these blocks are unit-local machine data, not extra top-level sections. Planner review prompts require literal block/schema/ordinal/replay validation, and the promotion hash binds the reviewed doing bytes before registry projection.
- Doer prefix completeness is plan-derived. For each group in registry order, producer steps consume the exact phasePlans command arrays and append command logs/evidence with matching commandOrdinal; no evidence ordinal may skip, duplicate, reorder, or alter a plan member. Red windows run first and produce red_tree/unit_red, implementation windows run second, and after the final clean pushed head every final_verification window runs in group/phase/commandOrdinal order. Unit receipts contain exactly the complete plan-aligned evidence set for their phase, including the test red/green replay pair. The review, coverage, and implementation-receipt tail remains as declared above. Generic phrases such as every expected-red command or each green command have no authority outside these registry arrays.

### Round 61 Seventh Cold-Gate Closures

These clauses are the final authority for registered terminal nullability and plan-to-evidence validation.

- Registered terminal outcome/nullability is complete. Final `RegisteredProcessTerminalResult={outcome,disposition,exitCode,signal,stdoutSha256,stderrSha256,warningCount,failureReason,preStateSha256,postStateSha256,startedAt,endedAt}` retains the Sixth fields and uses this sole matrix. exit has exitCode integer 0..255, signal null, warningCount a nonnegative safe integer, nonnull canonical startedAt/endedAt, and complete sanitized stream hashes; exitCode nonzero always means disposition failed/failureReason process_exit regardless of warnings, exitCode zero plus positive warnings means failed/warning, and zero/zero means succeeded/null. signal has null exitCode, one declared finite signal, nonnegative safe warningCount, failed/signal, nonnull start/end, and complete hashes. timeout_term|timeout_kill have null exitCode, SIGTERM|SIGKILL, nonnegative safe warningCount, failed/timeout, nonnull start/end, and complete hashes. spawn_error has null exit/signal/warning/start/post, failed/spawn, canonical end, and empty-stream hashes. observation_error has null exit/signal/warning, failed/observation, nullable start/post, canonical end, and hashes of only the trustworthy sanitized prefixes. aborted has null exit/signal/warning/post, aborted/spawn, start null exactly for prepared abort otherwise nonnull, canonical end, and empty hashes. reconciled has null exit/signal, zero warning, reconciled/null, nullable start, nonnull expected post, canonical end, and empty hashes. Every outcome has preStateSha256 equal intent.preStateSha256; succeeded/reconciled postStateSha256 is the registry-derived expected post-state hash, while failed post is null or the exact safely observed non-expected state.
- Reconciled envelope generations are legal in exactly two forms. RegisteredProcessCommandEnvelope status terminal normally requires generation ended or aborted. For result disposition reconciled it instead permits: an ended generation with nonnull result.startedAt when the registered effect actually ran and the expected post state was recovered after all members died/reaped; or a prepared generation with null result.startedAt only for track command ordinal 0,1,2,3,5 when no spawn authorization, gate/title/startup/ready/member/run artifact ever existed for that generation, every priorProcesses member is dead/reaped, priorProcesses is nonempty, and the expected post state is independently observed. The prepared form neither mutates nor aborts its generation and is forbidden for planner_product_push and track lease ordinal 4. No other non-ended terminal envelope is legal.
- Test command plans are a bijective red/replay sequence. For a test phase with 2K commands, K is positive; ordinals 1..K are exactly executionWindow red, expected red, replayOfCommandOrdinal null. Ordinals K+1..2K are exactly executionWindow final_verification, expected green, and command K+i has replayOfCommandOrdinal i plus byte-equal logicalName/argv/cwd/envNames/timeoutMs to command i. Thus every red command has exactly one later replay, every replay target is unique/backward, replay order equals red order, and no interleaved, forward, duplicate, missing, or extra command is legal. Implementation phase commands are all implementation/green/null replay; verification phase commands are all final_verification/green/null replay.
- Command-plan blocks attach to exact units. Every parsed successor group has exact status-bearing `a` test, `b` implementation, and `c` verification unit headers. The test command block appears immediately after the `a` unit Acceptance line, implementation after `b`, verification after `c`; each block phase/unitId must match that header and the registry group. The earlier phrase implementation-only unit means each of these three implementation-suite units, not implementation phase alone. A block outside that position, an unparsed unit, or a group/header/block mismatch rejects before registry creation.
- Successor command evidence binds every plan member. Final no-extra-fields `SuccessorCommandEvidence={version:1,successorKey,unitId,ordinal,logicalName,planEntrySha256,argv,cwd,envNames,timeoutMs,executionWindow,expected,replayOfCommandOrdinal,startedAt,endedAt,exitCode,signal,stdoutPath,stdoutSha256,stderrPath,stderrSha256,warningCount,sourceHeadSha,treeSha}` replaces the earlier schema. planEntrySha256 hashes the complete compact canonical SuccessorCommandPlan bytes. unitId and ordinal select exactly one phasePlan entry; logicalName, argv, cwd, envNames, timeoutMs, executionWindow, expected, replayOfCommandOrdinal, and planEntrySha256 must byte-equal that entry before execution and again before append, producer-prefix advance, unit-receipt projection, or archive validation. Red/green exit/signal/warning matrices remain unchanged. Command evidence paths are contiguous by commandOrdinal within each phase unit, and each SuccessorImplementationUnitReceipt.commandEvidencePaths is exactly the BINARY path-sorted complete plan set for that unit with no omission or extra.

### Round 62 Quality Closures

These clauses are the final authority for successor runtime cancellation, bootstrap publication, Work Doer mutation state, and migration survivor timestamps.

- Successor agent cancellation is persisted before control. AgentRuntimeAdapter.probe final domain is `absent|paused|running|completed|errored|cancelled`. Exact no-extra-fields `SuccessorAgentCancellationIntent={version:1,successorKey,runtimeKind,attemptOrdinal,reviewOrdinal,reviewRole,invocationToken,agentId,dispatchPath,dispatchSha256,deadlineAt,reason:'deadline_exceeded',cancellationId,createdAt}` uses runtimeKind planner|doer|planner_review|implementation_review; reviewOrdinal is nonnull only for planner_review; reviewRole is scope|contract|test for planner_review, one registry reviewRole for implementation_review, and null for suite kinds. cancellationId equals SHA-256 of compact canonical `{runtimeKind,attemptOrdinal,reviewOrdinal,reviewRole,invocationToken,agentId,dispatchSha256,deadlineAt}`. Suite paths are `artifacts/post-merge-successor/suite/<planner|doer>/attempt-<N>-cancel-intent.v1.json`; planner-review paths are `artifacts/post-merge-successor/suite/planner/attempt-<N>-review-<R>-cancel-intent.v1.json`; implementation-review paths are `artifacts/post-merge-successor/reviews/<role>/cancel-intent.v1.json`. The intent is appended/pushed/read back at now >= deadlineAt while probe is running and precedes `AgentRuntimeAdapter.cancel(invocationToken,agentId,cancellationId,intentSha256)`. cancel is create-once/idempotent by cancellationId and can request termination only for that exact released runtime. Exact `SuccessorAgentCancellationReceipt={version:1,successorKey,runtimeKind,attemptOrdinal,reviewOrdinal,reviewRole,intentPath,intentSha256,invocationToken,agentId,cancellationId,outcome,resolvedAt}` has outcome completed|errored|cancelled from a terminal probe and uses the same owner path with `-receipt` replacing `-intent`; it is appended/pushed/read back before any worktree cleanup, attempt replacement, or new runtime. A lost/failed cancel response only probes/waits on the same id; it never issues another identity or dispatch.
- Cancellation closes every suite/review deadline branch. PreReleaseArtifact and SuiteArtifactRef kinds add `agent_cancel_intent|agent_cancel_wait|agent_cancel_receipt` with only the exact owner-ordinal paths above and `-wait-<W>.v1.json` siblings. Exact no-extra-fields `SuccessorAgentCancellationWait={version:1,successorKey,runtimeKind,attemptOrdinal,reviewOrdinal,reviewRole,cancellationId,waitOrdinal,probeOrdinals,nextProbeAt,outcome:'still_running',createdAt}` has positive contiguous waitOrdinal; each owner invocation performs exactly three new contiguous probes at least 30 seconds apart, records their ordinals in order, and if all remain running appends/pushes/readbacks one wait plus returns nonterminal code `agent_cancellation_pending` without cleanup. A later invocation adopts the same intent/cancellationId and next wait ordinal. SuccessorSuiteAttempt status remains running while cancellation is pending and retains the cancellation artifact prefix. A terminal completed probe plus receipt outcome completed permits normal output parsing/completion; errored or cancelled plus matching receipt permits interrupted with the longest artifact prefix. Planner and implementation reviews use the same matrix. No absent/paused/running/uncertain runtime is cleaned, restored, redispatched, or replaced; only durable completed|errored|cancelled proof releases ownership.
- Successor bootstrap publication is fenced, ordinal, and observable. ProcessRegistrationOwner adds `{kind:'successor_bootstrap_push',successorKey,bootstrapAttemptOrdinal}`. Final no-extra-fields `SuccessorBootstrapAttempt={version:1,successorKey,successorSlug,bootstrapAttemptOrdinal,predecessorIdentitySha256,dispositionKind,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,implementationBaseSha,branch,worktreePath,deskTaskRoot,taskPath,sourcePath,priorPushOutcomePaths,priorPushOutcomeSetSha256,phase,sourceSha256,sourceTreeSha,sourceCommitSha,remoteBranchSha,pushCommand,pushObservation,taskSeedPath,taskSeedSha256,deskTaskCommitSha,branchCreated,worktreeCreated,remoteBranchCreated,deskTaskCreated,sourceCreated,commandResults,startedAt,updatedAt}` has positive bootstrapAttemptOrdinal and phase `prepared|branch_created|worktree_created|source_written|source_indexed|source_committed|push_inflight|remote_created|push_absent|push_conflict|task_created|complete`. Its exact mutable path is `artifacts/post-merge-successor/bootstrap/attempt-<N>.attempt.v1.json`. Ordinal one has priorPushOutcomePaths exact `[]` and its set hash; ordinal N>1 carries exactly the immutable BINARY-path-sorted outcomes for ordinals 1..N-1, and no ordinal may be skipped or reused. pushCommand/pushObservation are null through source_committed. push_inflight is pushed/read back before the sole branch push and adds one prepared RegisteredProcessCommandEnvelope owned by successor_bootstrap_push. commandResults contains only the closed safe bootstrap command prefix and never fabricates the push or its observation.
- Bootstrap push response loss has one observation substate. Exact no-extra-fields `SuccessorBootstrapPushObservation={pushCommand,fetchAttemptOrdinal,priorFetchCommands,fetchCommand,observedRemoteSha,outcome,updatedAt}` uses outcome candidate|absent|conflict. Only after pushCommand is terminal and all members are dead/reaped may registered read-only branch fetch attempts run; failed attempts remain append-only with contiguous processAttemptOrdinal and retry only through the ordinary wait/failure disposition. The first completing fetch is retained in fetchCommand: candidate requires observedRemoteSha=sourceCommitSha and advances remote_created; absent requires null observedRemoteSha and advances terminal push_absent; conflict requires a noncandidate SHA and advances terminal push_conflict. The lease push is never reissued within that bootstrapAttemptOrdinal. Exact immutable `SuccessorBootstrapPushOutcome={version:1,successorKey,bootstrapAttemptOrdinal,sourceCommitSha,branch,pushCommand,pushObservation,outcome,observedRemoteSha,completedAt}` replaces a push_absent|push_conflict attempt at `artifacts/post-merge-successor/bootstrap/attempt-<N>-push-outcome.v1.json` and is registered as bootstrap_push_outcome. Only after its host cleanup/readback may a fresh contiguous bootstrapAttemptOrdinal reconcile local state and receive mutation authority. Final no-extra-fields `SuccessorBootstrapReceipt={version:1,successorKey,successorSlug,bootstrapAttemptOrdinal,predecessorIdentitySha256,dispositionKind,predecessorArchiveState,predecessorArchiveCheckpoint,dispositionPath,dispositionSha256,implementationBaseSha,branch,worktreePath,deskTaskRoot,taskPath,sourcePath,priorPushOutcomePaths,priorPushOutcomeSetSha256,sourceSha256,sourceTreeSha,sourceCommitSha,remoteBranchSha,pushCommand,pushObservation,taskSeedPath,taskSeedSha256,deskTaskCommitSha,branchCreated:true,worktreeCreated:true,remoteBranchCreated:true,deskTaskCreated:true,sourceCreated:true,commandResults,completedAt}` requires a complete candidate observation, atomically replaces the successful attempt at `artifacts/post-merge-successor/bootstrap/<successorKey>.v1.json`, and retains every failed prior outcome through that exact prior set; no response-loss stream field is fabricated or discarded.
- Successor Work Doer uses a mutable product-worktree runtime copy, never the promoted authority document or the Desk artifact tree. Final no-extra-fields doer `SuccessorSuiteAttempt={kind:'doer',ordinal,status,terminalOutcome,skill,cwd,promptPath,promptSha256,documentBindingKind,planningPath,planningSha256,doingPath,doingSha256,executionBaseSha,runtimeDoingPath,runtimeDoingInitialSha256,runtimeDoingFinalSha256,runtimeDoingArchivePath,runtimeDoingArchiveSha256,doerTransitionPath,doerTransitionSha256,doerLedgerPath,doerLedgerSha256,invocationToken,dispatchIntentPath,dispatchIntentSha256,dispatchPath,dispatchSha256,agentId,artifacts,artifactSetSha256,startedAt,deadlineAt,endedAt}` replaces every shorter doer form while planner retains the Round 61 final schema. planningPath/doingPath are the immutable promoted canonical product paths; runtimeDoingPath is exact product-relative `<doing-artifact-directory>/successor-doer/attempt-<N>/runtime-doing.md`. Before dispatch, the transition protocol below copies the exact promoted doing bytes there, commits/pushes/readback-verifies that setup as a clean product head, freezes ordinal-one executionBaseSha at that accepted setup commit, sets runtimeDoingInitialSha256 equal doingSha256, and creates/pushes/readbacks the Desk-owned ledger. Later doer ordinals retain that executionBaseSha. `$work-doer` is invoked explicitly against runtimeDoingPath and may update unit status/progress only there while committing it with product code/evidence; it revalidates the canonical pair before every unit and never writes either canonical document. runtimeDoingFinalSha256 and both archive fields are null until terminal classification. Then Work Merger copies the exact terminal runtime bytes to unique Desk-task-relative `artifacts/post-merge-successor/suite/doer/attempt-<N>-runtime-doing.md`, freezes equal final/archive hashes, and registers that immutable copy exactly once as doer_runtime_doing for completed or doer_runtime_checkpoint for errored|cancelled. The mutable product path is never a PreReleaseArtifact/SuiteArtifactRef; PreReleaseArtifact and doer SuiteArtifactRef add `doer_runtime_transition|doer_runtime_doing|doer_runtime_checkpoint|doer_ledger` only after each named file freezes. Final implementation evidence binds both canonical hashes plus executionBaseSha and the completed product runtime path/hash and Desk archive path/hash.

- Doer runtime transitions are registered product mutations. ProcessRegistrationOwner adds `{kind:'successor_doer_transition_push',successorKey,doerAttemptOrdinal}`. Exact no-extra-fields `SuccessorDoerRuntimeTransitionAttempt={version:1,successorKey,doerAttemptOrdinal,predecessorLedgerPath,predecessorLedgerSha256,oldProductHeadSha,oldProductTreeSha,runtimeDoingPath,runtimeDoingBefore,runtimeDoingAfter,adoptedPaths,adoptedPathSetSha256,phase,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,pushCommand,pushObservation,startedAt,updatedAt}` lives at `artifacts/post-merge-successor/suite/doer/attempt-<N>-runtime-transition.attempt.v1.json` with phase `prepared|candidate_materialized|committed|push_inflight|pushed|readback`. Ordinal one requires absent runtimeDoingBefore, runtimeDoingAfter equal the canonical doing bytes, and adoptedPaths `[]`. A retry requires a complete prior ledger/runtime archive, restores the old runtime path to its ledger before BlobState, creates the new unique runtime path from the archived terminal bytes, and lists exactly every independently validated partial code/test/evidence path adopted from the prior terminal worktree. A private index rooted at oldProductHeadSha materializes only those exact BlobStates plus the runtime transition; trusted commit-tree freezes one candidate without consuming the real dirty index/worktree. push_inflight with one prepared registered force-with-lease command is Desk-pushed/read back before the sole product push; response loss runs a registered fetch observation and permits candidate->pushed, old head->terminal push_absent, or third head->terminal push_conflict, never push reissue. Candidate readback atomically restores the real ref/index/worktree to the exact accepted candidate after proving every owned byte, then projects immutable no-extra-fields `SuccessorDoerRuntimeTransition={version:1,successorKey,doerAttemptOrdinal,oldProductHeadSha,runtimeDoingPath,runtimeDoingSha256,adoptedPaths,adoptedPathSetSha256,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,pushCommand,pushObservation,completedAt}` at the same basename without `.attempt`; this is the doer_runtime_transition artifact and must precede dispatch. push_absent or push_conflict freezes the analogous outcome receipt, releases no agent, and requires a fresh ordinal or conflict resolution respectively.
- Doer attempt Git/worktree state is journaled in Desk while the agent alone owns product writes. Exact no-extra-fields `SuccessorDoerAttemptLedger={version:1,successorKey,doerAttemptOrdinal,predecessorLedgerPath,predecessorLedgerSha256,canonicalPlanningPath,canonicalPlanningSha256,canonicalDoingPath,canonicalDoingSha256,runtimeDoingPath,runtimeDoingBefore,runtimeDoingAfter,baseHeadSha,baseTreeSha,baseIndexTreeSha,baseStatusSha256,phase,dispatchPath,dispatchSha256,agentId,terminalProbeOutcome,terminalHeadSha,terminalTreeSha,terminalIndexTreeSha,terminalStatusSha256,changedPaths,changedPathSetSha256,recoveryDisposition,startedAt,updatedAt}` lives at exact task-relative `artifacts/post-merge-successor/suite/doer/attempt-<N>-ledger.v1.json` and has phase `prepared|authorized|running|cancelling|terminal_observed|classified|complete`. It is journal-owned mutable and unregistered through classified; complete freezes its final hash and registers it once as doer_ledger. prepared captures exact clean product Git HEAD/tree/private read-only index tree/status-porcelain-v2-z hash plus runtime-before BlobState after the setup commit and before dispatch. Only the Work Doer agent may write the product worktree through running/cancelling; only Work Merger may update the Desk ledger. terminal_observed is legal only after completed|errored|cancelled probe/cancellation receipt and atomically captures every terminal Git/runtime field; changedPaths is the exact BINARY-sorted status path set and hash. classified sets recoveryDisposition `completed|resume_clean|resume_partial|restore_runtime_only|conflict_blocked` from the matrix below. complete pushes/readbacks the frozen ledger, runtime archive, and decision before another attempt.
- Doer retry state has a closed recovery matrix. completed requires terminal probe completed, clean status, canonical documents byte-equal, runtimeDoingAfter present, all plan evidence complete, and terminal head/tree equal implementation evidence. resume_clean requires errored|cancelled, clean status, a descendant terminal head whose commits touch only registry-declared implementation/test/product-runtime/evidence paths, and runtime progress/evidence exactly matching those commits. resume_partial requires errored|cancelled plus a fully captured status whose changed paths are only the current plan unit's declared output/test/product-runtime/evidence paths and whose blobs/index/worktree form one exact adoptable prefix. restore_runtime_only requires base head/index/tree with only runtimeDoingPath changed. For every nonconflict retry, Work Merger first archives/freezes/registers the old runtime bytes and complete ledger; the next transition restores the old product runtime path to runtimeDoingBefore, creates the new unique runtime path from the exact archived checkpoint bytes, adopts only the matrix-authorized path bytes, and commits/pushes/readback-verifies that complete transition. Any canonical-doc change, unknown path, mismatched status/index/tree, unbound commit, missing evidence, live agent, or mixed prefix is conflict_blocked and permits no restore/retry. A fresh contiguous doerAttemptOrdinal binds the prior complete ledger, starts from its exact accepted head/index/worktree/runtime state, and uses a unique invocation token; no partial code, index entry, worktree byte, or mutable runtime document is silently discarded.

- Successor implementation source identity follows the runtime transition. For every successor-only unit receipt, red record, command evidence, coverage diff, review, and final PostMergeImplementationEvidence, executionBaseSha replaces the earlier implementationBaseSha/sourceBaseSha authority; bootstrap implementationBaseSha remains separately immutable only as the branch-creation base. Exact final `PostMergeImplementationEvidence={version:1,successorKey,successorIdentitySha256,planningPath,planningSha256,doingPath,doingSha256,bootstrapBaseSha,executionBaseSha,runtimeDoingPath,runtimeDoingSha256,runtimeDoingArchivePath,runtimeDoingArchiveSha256,implementationHeadSha,implementationTreeSha,unitReceiptPaths,unitReceiptSetSha256,reviewReportPaths,reviewReportSetSha256,verificationArtifactPaths,verificationArtifactSetSha256,coverageSummaryPath,coverageSummarySha256,warnings,completedAt}` uses bootstrapBaseSha equal the bootstrap receipt's implementationBaseSha and executionBaseSha equal the first doer transition commit. Coverage diff is exact executionBaseSha...implementationHeadSha; every successor SuccessorImplementationUnitReceipt.sourceBaseSha and SuccessorRedEvidence.sourceBaseSha equals executionBaseSha. No setup/runtime-transition-only product path is classified as production executable.
- Migration 0024 survivor writes are branch-specific. An active-containing duplicate group mutates its reconciled survivor and assigns migrationSyncAt. An all-tombstone group derives canonical checked projections without writing, selects the first original tombstone, and preserves that survivor byte-for-byte; only loser ledger rows and the parent list receive migrationSyncAt. Unit1 migration fixtures assert both branches, survivor checked/checkedAt/updatedAt byte identity, and rerun stability. No generic normalization or reconciled-survivor clause may write the all-tombstone survivor.

### Round 63 Quality Closures

These clauses are the final authority for authenticated Work Doer dispatch, successor pre-dispatch push recovery, implementation-review identity, and sync ordering.

- Work Doer receives only authenticated runtime authority. Planner keeps the preceding SuccessorSuiteDispatchIntent/receipt form. Final no-extra-fields `SuccessorDoerDispatchIntent={version:1,successorKey,doerAttemptOrdinal,priorDoerOutcomes,priorDoerOutcomeSetSha256,invocationToken,promptPath,promptSha256,cwd,canonicalPlanningPath,canonicalPlanningSha256,canonicalDoingPath,canonicalDoingSha256,executionBaseSha,runtimeDoingPath,runtimeDoingInitialSha256,doerTransitionPath,doerTransitionSha256,createdAt}` and `SuccessorDoerDispatchReceipt={version:1,intentPath,intentSha256,successorKey,doerAttemptOrdinal,priorDoerOutcomes,priorDoerOutcomeSetSha256,invocationToken,canonicalPlanningPath,canonicalPlanningSha256,canonicalDoingPath,canonicalDoingSha256,executionBaseSha,runtimeDoingPath,runtimeDoingInitialSha256,doerTransitionPath,doerTransitionSha256,agentId,preparedAt,releasedAt}` replace the generic doer forms; every repeated field byte-equals the intent and releasedAt follows the paused create-once protocol. D=1 uses priorDoerOutcomes exact `[]` and its hash; D>1 uses the complete BINARY-sorted unique `{path,sha256}` terminal outcome/checkpoint set of D-1 with no skipped attempt. Final doer prompt bytes are exact UTF-8 LF with one final LF: `Spoonjoy repair successor doer v2\nsuccessor_key: <K>\ndoer_attempt: <D>\nprior_doer_outcomes_json: <priorDoerOutcomesJson>\nprior_doer_outcome_set_sha256: <priorDoerOutcomeSetSha256>\nidentity_path: <identityPath>\nidentity_sha256: <identitySha256>\ncanonical_planning_path: <canonicalPlanningPath>\ncanonical_planning_sha256: <canonicalPlanningSha256>\ncanonical_doing_path: <canonicalDoingPath>\ncanonical_doing_sha256: <canonicalDoingSha256>\nexecution_base_sha: <executionBaseSha>\nruntime_doing_path: <runtimeDoingPath>\nruntime_doing_initial_sha256: <runtimeDoingInitialSha256>\ndoer_transition_path: <doerTransitionPath>\ndoer_transition_sha256: <doerTransitionSha256>\nhandoff_path: <handoffPath>\nhandoff_sha256: <handoffSha256>\nworktree: <worktreePath>\nskill: work-doer\nrules: treat canonical planning and doing as immutable read-only authority; execute and update only the authenticated runtime doing path; consume only the bound immediately-prior outcome set; before the first unit verify its initial hash, then require each unit receipt runtime-after hash to equal the next unit receipt runtime-before hash; revalidate every immutable hash before each unit; use strict TDD; do not run Units32-37; return only validated artifact locators\n`. start-implementation returns exactly `{skill,cwd,promptPath,promptSha256,priorDoerOutcomes,priorDoerOutcomeSetSha256,canonicalPlanningPath,canonicalPlanningSha256,canonicalDoingPath,canonicalDoingSha256,executionBaseSha,runtimeDoingPath,runtimeDoingInitialSha256,doerTransitionPath,doerTransitionSha256,invocationToken}`. AgentRuntimeAdapter receives only these prompt bytes and the authorized receipt; an unlisted runtime path, bad initial hash, skipped prior attempt, or broken unit-to-unit runtime hash chain cannot be read, written, or accepted. The mutable coordinator-owned doer ledger is intentionally absent from prompt/intent/receipt and may advance without invalidating released agent authority.

- Runtime doing mutations form one receipt chain. Final SuccessorImplementationUnitReceipt adds `runtimeDoingPath,runtimeDoingBeforeSha256,runtimeDoingAfterSha256` immediately before completedAt. The first unit executed by a doer attempt has before hash equal SuccessorDoerDispatchIntent.runtimeDoingInitialSha256; every later unit in that attempt has before hash equal the immediately preceding executed unit's after hash; after hash covers the complete runtime doing bytes after that unit's sole status/progress update. Registry order and bound priorDoerOutcomes prove any earlier completed/skipped units. A unit appends its receipt only after product code/evidence and runtime bytes are committed/pushed/read back at the receipt sourceHeadSha/treeSha. The completed doer suite's runtimeDoingFinalSha256 equals the final executed unit after hash, and the Desk runtime archive must hash to it. A missing, reordered, duplicated, or uncommitted runtime transition rejects even when code/tests are green.

- Runtime-transition registered commands and observations are literal. ProcessRegistrationOwner adds exact `{kind:'successor_doer_transition',successorKey,doerAttemptOrdinal,transitionAttemptOrdinal,commandKind:'push'|'fetch'}`. Push intent argv is the trusted Git projection `['git','push','--porcelain','--force-with-lease=refs/heads/'+branch+':'+oldProductHeadSha,'origin',candidateCommitSha+':refs/heads/'+branch]` from canonical product cwd; fetch intent argv is `['git','fetch','origin','refs/heads/'+branch+':refs/remotes/origin/'+branch]` from the same cwd. Each is one RegisteredProcessCommandEnvelope with commandOrdinal 0 for push or the positive contiguous fetch attempt ordinal, exact empty stdin hash, inherited total deadline, complete terminal result, and dead/reaped proof. Exact no-extra-fields `SuccessorDoerTransitionPushObservation={pushCommand,fetchAttemptOrdinal,priorFetchCommands,fetchCommand,observedRemoteSha,outcome,updatedAt}` has outcome candidate|old|conflict; failed fetch envelopes occupy priorFetchCommands, the first succeeded/reconciled fetch occupies fetchCommand, candidate equals candidateCommitSha, old equals oldProductHeadSha, and conflict is any other 40-hex SHA. No observation starts while the push envelope or any member is live.

- Runtime-transition attempts have a separate pre-dispatch retry lineage. Exact no-extra-fields `SuccessorDoerChangedEntry={path,head,index,worktree,selected}` contains normalized product-relative path plus exact BlobState for HEAD, real index, and worktree; selected is byte-equal to the sole matrix-authorized adopted state. The BINARY-path-sorted array and SHA-256 of compact canonical bytes replace every prior changedPaths/adoptedPaths-only projection. Final no-extra-fields `SuccessorDoerRuntimeTransitionAttempt={version:1,successorKey,doerAttemptOrdinal,transitionAttemptOrdinal,priorTransitionOutcomes,priorTransitionOutcomeSetSha256,predecessorLedgerPath,predecessorLedgerSha256,oldProductHeadSha,oldProductTreeSha,branch,runtimeDoingPath,runtimeDoingBefore,runtimeDoingAfter,adoptedEntries,adoptedEntrySetSha256,phase,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,pushCommand,pushObservation,startedAt,updatedAt}` lives at `artifacts/post-merge-successor/suite/doer/attempt-<D>-runtime-transition-<T>.attempt.v1.json`, with phase `prepared|candidate_materialized|committed|push_inflight|observing|pushed|readback|push_absent|push_conflict`. transitionAttemptOrdinal is contiguous within one doerAttemptOrdinal. T=1 has priorTransitionOutcomes exact `[]`, its set hash, and uses the initial or prior-ledger recovery matrix. push_inflight is Desk-pushed/read back before the one push. After terminal/dead proof, observing runs registered fetches and stores the complete observation. Candidate advances pushed/readback. Old advances push_absent; exact immutable `SuccessorDoerRuntimeTransitionOutcome={version:1,successorKey,doerAttemptOrdinal,transitionAttemptOrdinal,oldProductHeadSha,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,branch,pushCommand,pushObservation,outcome,completedAt}` uses outcome `push_absent|push_conflict` and replaces the attempt at `artifacts/post-merge-successor/suite/doer/attempt-<D>-runtime-transition-<T>-outcome.v1.json`. T+1 binds the complete BINARY-sorted `{path,sha256}` outcome set, requires no predecessor ledger when no agent was released, independently proves the same old remote/candidate commit/tree/runtime bytes, and receives new push authority without rebuilding or discarding them. Conflict emits outcome push_conflict, is a durable `doer_transition_branch_conflict` blocker, releases no agent, and permits neither another transition nor branch cleanup without an explicit branch-ownership resolution. Candidate readback projects exact `SuccessorDoerRuntimeTransition={version:1,successorKey,doerAttemptOrdinal,transitionAttemptOrdinal,priorTransitionOutcomes,priorTransitionOutcomeSetSha256,oldProductHeadSha,runtimeDoingPath,runtimeDoingSha256,adoptedEntries,adoptedEntrySetSha256,candidateCommitSha,candidateTreeSha,pushCommand,pushObservation,completedAt}` at `artifacts/post-merge-successor/suite/doer/attempt-<D>-runtime-transition.v1.json`. PreReleaseArtifact and doer SuiteArtifactRef kinds/paths add `doer_runtime_transition_outcome|doer_runtime_transition`; outcome members precede the one successful transition, and the suite's doerTransitionPath/hash names only the successful receipt.

- Doer terminal capture is sufficient for exact adoption. Final SuccessorDoerAttemptLedger replaces changedPaths/changedPathSetSha256 with `changedEntries,changedEntrySetSha256`, using the exact SuccessorDoerChangedEntry array above; base and terminal status/index/tree hashes remain. terminal_observed captures every entry before classification. resume_partial is legal only when each selected BlobState is an output/test/product-runtime/evidence byte owned by the current plan unit and the complete selected set forms one plan-evidence prefix; the next transition's adoptedEntries are byte-identical. restore_runtime_only requires the sole entry be runtimeDoingPath. resume_clean has an empty terminal entry set. Any missing path state, symlink/nonregular file, ambiguous staged-versus-worktree byte, unselected difference, or set/hash mismatch is conflict_blocked.

- Bootstrap retry adopts exact retained local state instead of replaying creation. Final SuccessorBootstrapAttempt replaces priorPushOutcomePaths with `priorPushOutcomes:{path,sha256}[]`, adds `initializationKind:'create'|'adopt_after_absent'`, and uses the Round 62 remaining fields. Ordinal one is create with empty prior set and the existing prepared-first create matrix. A terminal push_absent outcome permits only ordinal N+1 adopt_after_absent. Before its prepared checkpoint, the exact read-only BootstrapCommandResult sequence is canonical product cwd `['git','rev-parse','refs/heads/'+branch]`, then `['git','worktree','list','--porcelain','-z']`; derived worktree cwd `['git','rev-parse','HEAD']`, `['git','status','--porcelain=v2','-z','--untracked-files=all']`, and `['git','cat-file','blob',sourceCommitSha+':'+sourcePath]`. Results must prove the sole branch/worktree mapping, branch and HEAD equal sourceCommitSha, empty status bytes, and source blob hash sourceSha256. Its prepared state already has branchCreated/worktreeCreated/sourceCreated true, sourceSha256/sourceTreeSha/sourceCommitSha nonnull, remoteBranchCreated false, remoteBranchSha null, and commandResults exactly that five-row adoption sequence; it proceeds directly to push_inflight without branch/worktree/source mutation. The prior push outcome remains immutable and the same branch receives a new ordinal's sole push authority only after the prior observation proved remote absent. A push_conflict outcome instead emits durable code `bootstrap_branch_conflict`, permits no fresh ordinal/local cleanup/remote mutation, and requires explicit ownership resolution because the conflicting remote branch is shared state. Final SuccessorBootstrapReceipt carries priorPushOutcomes/priorPushOutcomeSetSha256 from the successful attempt. Bootstrap push outcome paths/kind remain the Round 62 exact registry; no retained branch/worktree is represented as absent or recreated.

- Implementation reviews are attempt-qualified and collision-free. Exact roots are `artifacts/post-merge-successor/doer-attempts/<D>/reviews/<role>/attempt-<R>/`; every prompt, dispatch-intent, dispatch, runtime-report, cancellation intent/wait/receipt, and final report lives only below that root. Final no-extra-fields `SuccessorReviewDispatchIntent={version:1,successorKey,doerAttemptOrdinal,reviewAttemptOrdinal,role,invocationToken,promptPath,promptSha256,inputArtifacts,inputArtifactSetSha256,sourceHeadSha,treeSha,createdAt}`, `SuccessorReviewDispatch={version:1,successorKey,doerAttemptOrdinal,reviewAttemptOrdinal,role,intentPath,intentSha256,invocationToken,promptPath,promptSha256,inputArtifacts,inputArtifactSetSha256,sourceHeadSha,treeSha,agentId,authorizedAt}`, and `SuccessorReviewReport={version:1,successorKey,doerAttemptOrdinal,reviewAttemptOrdinal,role,verdict,dispatchPath,dispatchSha256,promptPath,promptSha256,inputArtifacts,inputArtifactSetSha256,agentId,returnedReportPath,returnedReportSha256,sourceHeadSha,treeSha,completedAt}` use verdict clean|findings and bind every path to D/R/role. reviewAttemptOrdinal is positive contiguous per doer attempt and role. errored/cancelled terminal runtime plus its cancellation receipt permits R+1 under the same doer attempt; findings freezes that report, ends the doer attempt without implementation completion, and requires a new doer attempt; clean is the only report accepted by final implementation evidence. PreReleaseArtifact/doer SuiteArtifactRef path grammars and producer order use these exact roots and retain every historical terminal prefix without collision.

- Implementation-review output and findings ownership are executable. Exact prompt bytes include successorKey, doerAttemptOrdinal, reviewAttemptOrdinal, role/scope, sourceHeadSha/treeSha, inputArtifacts compact canonical JSON and set hash, then require read-only output as compact canonical no-LF `SuccessorImplementationReviewRuntimeReport={version:1,role,verdict,findings}`. verdict CLEAN requires findings exact `[]`; verdict FINDINGS requires the nonempty unique ReviewFinding array from the release contract, BINARY-sorted by `(file,line,code,summary)`. The stored runtime-report bytes must match exactly; SuccessorReviewReport projects CLEAN to clean or FINDINGS to findings. A findings report produces exact immutable `SuccessorDoerReviewFindingOutcome={version:1,successorKey,doerAttemptOrdinal,reviewReports,reviewReportSetSha256,affectedGroupIds,affectedGroupSetSha256,completedAt}` under `artifacts/post-merge-successor/suite/doer/attempt-<D>-review-findings.v1.json`; PreReleaseArtifact and doer SuiteArtifactRef add kind `doer_review_findings` for only that path. affectedGroupIds is the nonempty BINARY-sorted set deterministically selected from the implementation registry's declared output/test paths and each finding file; an unmapped or multi-owner path is conflict_blocked. The next doer attempt's priorDoerOutcomes set binds this outcome plus the complete prior ledger/runtime checkpoint, copies the checkpoint, resets exactly those groups' a/b/c statuses to pending, and runs each reopened group red-first with fresh attempt-qualified evidence before reviews repeat. It may not alter canonical documents or invent a group/command.

- All retryable doer evidence is doer-attempt-qualified. Except the shared `implementation-registry.v1.json` and final `post-merge-implementation.v1.json`, final path grammar inserts `doer-attempts/<D>/` immediately after `artifacts/post-merge-successor/` for commands/logs, red-tree/red evidence, unit receipts, verification, coverage, and implementation reviews; every corresponding exact schema adds doerAttemptOrdinal immediately after successorKey. PreReleaseArtifact and SuiteArtifactRef retain every historical immutable attempt member. A retry writes no prior path. Final PostMergeImplementationEvidence selects exactly one latest accepted receipt per registry unit and the complete clean review/verification/coverage set from the final doer attempt; its set projections include each attempt-qualified path/hash. Superseded attempt artifacts remain registered evidence but are excluded from those final selected sets. Command-plan ordinals remain contiguous within `(doerAttemptOrdinal,unitId)`, and the runtime hash chain plus predecessor outcome proves cross-attempt continuation.

- Cancellation review identity follows the qualified review path. SuccessorAgentCancellationIntent/Wait/Receipt reviewOrdinal is the planner review ordinal for planner_review and the positive implementation reviewAttemptOrdinal for implementation_review; reviewRole is nonnull for both. attemptOrdinal is plannerAttemptOrdinal or doerAttemptOrdinal respectively. cancellationId includes all three owner fields, and each cancellation path is below the exact planner-review or implementation-review attempt root. Suite kinds retain null reviewOrdinal/reviewRole. No singleton `reviews/<role>/` cancellation path or attempt-free implementation-review schema remains legal.

- Sync migration and cursor order are final. An all-tombstone duplicate survivor remains byte-for-byte original, including checked/checkedAt/updatedAt, while loser ledger projections may use derived canonical checked state at migrationSyncAt. Every shopping/native in-memory sort and after-cursor predicate uses compareUtf8Binary over the same complete key bytes; tests include ASCII case inversions, composed/decomposed Unicode, and multi-byte identifiers tied at one timestamp. Any localeCompare, UTF-16 comparison, or bare string relational operator in these cursor paths fails Unit1.

### Round 64 Quality Closures

These clauses are the final authority for reachable remote observation, doer terminal outcomes, per-unit evidence timing, globally finite cancellation, review repair ownership, and persisted BlobState bytes.

- Bootstrap remote absence uses ls-remote, not a successful fetch. ProcessRegistrationOwner adds `{kind:'successor_bootstrap_observe',successorKey,bootstrapAttemptOrdinal,commandKind:'ls_remote'|'fetch',processAttemptOrdinal}`. After the sole terminal/dead push, exact registered ls-remote argv is `['git','ls-remote','--exit-code','--heads','origin','refs/heads/'+branch]` from canonical product cwd. Exit zero is legal only with exact UTF-8 `<40hex>\trefs/heads/<branch>\n` and yields candidate or conflict; documented no-match exit 2 is legal only with empty stdout and yields absent/null SHA; every other exit, signal, timeout, malformed stream, or stderr warning is a failed observation retained for a fresh read-only processAttemptOrdinal. Candidate/conflict then run exact registered fetch `['git','fetch','origin','refs/heads/'+branch+':refs/remotes/origin/'+branch]` and validate the fetched SHA/tree/blob before classification; absent has fetchCommand null. Final no-extra-fields `SuccessorBootstrapPushObservation={pushCommand,lsRemoteAttemptOrdinal,priorLsRemoteCommands,lsRemoteCommand,fetchCommand,observedRemoteSha,outcome,updatedAt}` uses outcome candidate|absent|conflict and retains every terminal envelope. This replaces the unreachable fetch-only absent rule and feeds the existing adopt_after_absent matrix.

- Doer findings are a legal terminal suite outcome. Final SuccessorSuiteAttempt doer terminalOutcome domain is `implemented|review_findings`; both require status completed, canonical endedAt, terminal Work Doer proof, a complete frozen ledger, and a Desk runtime archive. A completed Work Doer probe freezes the archive bytes/path but does not register either runtime kind while implementation reviews are pending. Suite terminalization alone registers those immutable bytes: implemented uses doer_runtime_doing and requires every selected unit/review/verification/coverage artifact plus implementation_receipt; review_findings uses doer_runtime_checkpoint and requires all accepted unit artifacts, the terminal review chain through the findings report, doer_review_findings, doer_ledger, and no coverage/implementation_receipt/implementation evidence. Its completed suite_attempt receipt is appended last. Exact D+1 priorDoerOutcomes is the BINARY-sorted `{path,sha256}` set containing D's suite_attempt, doer_review_findings, doer_runtime_checkpoint, and doer_ledger; no other member or skipped D is legal. PostMergeSuccessorAttempt.implementation_running permits a contiguous history of completed review_findings attempts plus interrupted attempts followed by at most one current attempt; implementation_complete requires the latest completed attempt terminalOutcome implemented and exact PostMergeImplementationEvidence. A findings attempt never authorizes Unit32. The earlier probe-outcome-only runtime-kind registration timing is invalid for completed Work Doer.

- Unit receipts bind their own pushed commits. The Round 61 final-head-delayed unit_receipt producer sentence is invalid. Successor action domain adds `record-doer-unit`, legal only in implementation_running for the one running doer attempt D. Its complete required-flag grammar is `--doer-attempt D --unit U --source-head H --runtime-before-sha256 B --runtime-after-sha256 A`; it rejects every other action flag and every unknown flag. Its exact no-extra-fields result extends the shared successor envelope with `{doerAttemptOrdinal,unitId,receiptPath,receiptSha256,sourceHeadSha,runtimeDoingAfterSha256}`. For each executed registry unit, Work Doer commits its declared product output/test files plus one runtime status/progress change and pushes/fetches/readbacks that exact product commit. It then invokes exact coordinator command `pnpm release:terminal -- --mode successor --journal <J> --action record-doer-unit --doer-attempt <D> --unit <unitId> --source-head <sourceHeadSha> --runtime-before-sha256 <before> --runtime-after-sha256 <after>`; release-terminal validates the registered plan/evidence/product readback and alone appends/pushes/readbacks the Desk command/unit evidence and SuccessorImplementationUnitReceipt before returning that exact result. Work Doer cannot begin the next unit until the result and named receipt hash-validate. sourceHeadSha/treeSha are that unit commit/tree, runtimeDoingAfterSha256 names the runtime blob in that tree, sourceHeadSha is a strict descendant-or-equal of the preceding accepted unit head and an ancestor-or-equal of final implementationHeadSha, and all declared output/test blobs match. Later units never rewrite a receipt. Final evidence validates the complete ancestry chain and selects one latest accepted receipt per unit; only final reviews, verification, coverage, and PostMergeImplementationEvidence require final implementationHeadSha/treeSha. If a resumed doer executes zero units, runtimeDoingFinalSha256 equals runtimeDoingInitialSha256 and no new unit receipt is created. This clause replaces every requirement that all unit receipts share the final head/tree.

- Cancellation has one global three-probe budget. For one cancellationId, probe ordinals are exactly 1..3 across all invocations, at least 30 seconds apart; no waitOrdinal can reset that budget. A terminal result at any probe writes the cancellation receipt. If probe 3 remains running, exact no-extra-fields `SuccessorAgentCancellationBlocker={version:1,successorKey,runtimeKind,attemptOrdinal,reviewOrdinal,reviewRole,cancellationId,intentPath,intentSha256,probePaths,probeSetSha256,code:'agent_cancellation_unconfirmed',createdAt}` freezes the three BINARY-path-sorted `{path,sha256}` probe receipts, is registered as agent_cancel_blocker under the owner attempt root, and returns the same nonterminal blocker byte-for-byte thereafter. Later calls may only invoke idempotent `AgentRuntimeAdapter.cancelStatus(cancellationId)` against the same adapter record: still-running returns the existing blocker with no new probe/wait/artifact; completed|errored|cancelled writes the matching cancellation receipt and resolves the blocker. No new cancellation, runtime, cleanup, or attempt is legal while it exists. PreReleaseArtifact/SuiteArtifactRef add only the exact agent_cancel_blocker path; the earlier unbounded waitOrdinal rule is invalid.

- Doer release authorization is immutable before release. Final SuccessorDoerDispatchReceipt replaces releasedAt with nonnull `authorizedAt`. After paused prepare returns agentId, Work Merger freezes authorizedAt, writes the complete receipt, appends/pushes/readbacks it once, then calls `AgentRuntimeAdapter.release(invocationToken,agentId,dispatchSha256)` against those immutable bytes. The receipt is never rewritten. Runtime start/completion times exist only in AgentRuntimeAdapter probe/terminal evidence and SuccessorSuiteAttempt startedAt/endedAt. A release before remote readback, a null authorizedAt, a releasedAt field, or any post-release receipt mutation rejects.

- Runtime terminal failures do not require fictional cancellation. Across planner suites, doer suites, planner reviews, and implementation reviews, a terminal errored probe observed before any cancellation intent is sufficient terminal authority and requires no cancellation receipt; suite status becomes interrupted and the owning ledger/history binds that probe. Cancelled is legal only after a cancellation intent and requires its matching cancellation receipt. Once an intent exists, an errored terminal result also requires the matching receipt so recovery cannot bypass an in-flight cancellation.
