Exact no-extra-fields `SuccessorReviewRuntimeTermination={version:1,successorKey,doerAttemptOrdinal,reviewAttemptOrdinal,role,dispatchPath,dispatchSha256,agentId,outcome,cancellationIntentPath,cancellationIntentSha256,cancellationReceiptPath,cancellationReceiptSha256,terminalProbePath,terminalProbeSha256,returnedReportPath,returnedReportSha256,completedAt}` uses outcome errored|cancelled|invalid_output and lives at the attempt root's `termination.v1.json`. For spontaneous errored, all four cancellation fields are null and the terminal probe alone authorizes R+1. For errored|cancelled after cancellation intent, all four fields are nonnull and hash-valid and R+1 requires the matching receipt. invalid_output requires terminal completed probe, null cancellation fields, and a nonnull immutable sanitized returned-report path/hash whose bytes fail only the declared runtime-report grammar; errored/cancelled require both returned-report fields null. PreReleaseArtifact/doer SuiteArtifactRef add review_termination. No errored/malformed runtime is required to manufacture a deadline or cancellation receipt.

- Reopen mutation is coordinator-owned and hash-bound before dispatch. Exact no-extra-fields `SuccessorDoerRuntimeReopen={version:1,successorKey,doerAttemptOrdinal,priorRuntimeArchivePath,priorRuntimeArchiveSha256,reviewFindingOutcomePath,reviewFindingOutcomeSha256,affectedGroupIds,affectedGroupSetSha256,runtimeDoingPath,runtimeDoingBeforeSha256,runtimeDoingAfterSha256,completedAt}` lives at `artifacts/post-merge-successor/suite/doer/attempt-<D>-runtime-reopen.v1.json`. Work Merger alone parses the prior runtime checkpoint, changes exactly the affected groups' a/b/c status markers from completed to pending without altering any other byte, verifies before/after hashes, and registers kind doer_runtime_reopen before the runtime-transition candidate. D=1 and non-findings retries have no reopen artifact; review-findings D>1 requires it. SuccessorDoerRuntimeTransitionAttempt/receipt and SuccessorDoerDispatchIntent add nullable reopenPath/reopenSha256, nonnull exactly for this branch; runtimeDoingAfter/initial hash equals reopen.runtimeDoingAfterSha256. Work Doer never resets statuses and its first executed unit chains from this authenticated after hash.

- Successor group path ownership is machine-readable. Immediately after each successor group's c-unit `spoonjoy-command-plan-v1` closing fence, Work Planner emits with no blank line one three-line `spoonjoy-owned-paths-v1` fence whose sole compact-canonical JSON line is exact `{ownedPaths,sharedPaths}`. Each array is nonempty/possibly-empty respectively, BINARY UTF-8 sorted unique normalized product-relative regular-file paths; ownedPaths are disjoint across groups and no path appears in both domains. Replacement SuccessorImplementationRegistry adds per group `ownedPaths,ownedPathSetSha256,sharedPaths,sharedPathSetSha256` and top-level `sharedPathOwners:{path,groupIds}[]`, all compact-canonical hashes including exact `[]`. Every shared path lists the complete BINARY groupId owner set and appears in each listed group's sharedPaths. Review finding domain repo maps an owned path to its sole group or a shared path to all declared owners; task-domain findings, unknown paths, empty owner sets, and inconsistent shared membership are conflict_blocked rather than guessed. affectedGroupIds is the BINARY union.

- Implementation-review bytes and hashes are literal. Final no-extra-fields `ReviewFinding={code,file,line,summary}` uses code from the existing finite review code domain, exact file `{domain:'repo'|'task',path}` with normalized path in that root, positive safe line, and sanitizer-clean 1..500-scalar summary; this replaces every string-only file form. Exact prompt is UTF-8 with one final LF: `Spoonjoy successor implementation review v1\nsuccessor_key: <K>\ndoer_attempt: <D>\nreview_attempt: <R>\nrole: <role>\nscope: <roleScope>\nsource_head_sha: <sourceHeadSha>\ntree_sha: <treeSha>\ninput_artifacts_json: <compactCanonicalPathHashArray>\ninput_artifact_set_sha256: <sha256>\nrules: read only; return only compact canonical SuccessorImplementationReviewRuntimeReport JSON\n`, where roleScope is the exact existing successor review-role scope string. Runtime report is exact compact canonical no-LF `{version:1,role,verdict,findings}`. CLEAN uses findings exact `[]`; FINDINGS uses nonempty unique ReviewFinding values sorted by `(file.domain,compareUtf8Binary(file.path),line,code,summary)`. SuccessorDoerReviewFindingOutcome.reviewReports is a BINARY-path-sorted unique `{path,sha256}[]` whose set hash covers its compact canonical bytes; affectedGroupSetSha256 hashes compact canonical affectedGroupIds string-array bytes. Empty reviewReports/affectedGroupIds are illegal for findings; every `[]` elsewhere hashes exact UTF-8 `[]`.

- Persisted BlobState bytes are canonical and bounded. Final no-extra-fields `BlobState={presence:'absent'}|{presence:'present',encoding:'base64',byteLength,sha256,bytesBase64}` replaces every prior form. byteLength is a safe integer `0..16_777_216`; bytesBase64 is canonical RFC 4648 standard alphabet with required padding, no whitespace, and re-encoding decoded bytes is byte-identical; decoded length equals byteLength and SHA-256 equals sha256. Files above the limit, malformed/noncanonical base64, hash/length drift, symlink/nonregular inputs, and undecodable binary states are conflict_blocked before mutation. Empty and arbitrary binary/NUL fixtures are mandatory. Every BlobState compact-canonical hash uses this literal field order.

### Round 65 Quality Closures

These clauses are the final authority for grouped TDD checkpoints, bootstrap observation retries, suite interruption recovery, conflict rollover, trusted spawn-gate survival, runtime probes, review-finding identity, and final archive-validation attempts.

- Successor TDD receipts follow repository checkpoint timing. The Round 63 unit-by-unit runtime chain, Round 64 `record-doer-unit` action/result, and any requirement to commit or push an intentionally red tree are invalid. Each registry group has exactly two ordered checkpoints: `red_green` covers exact unitIds `[testUnitId,implementationUnitId]`, and `verification` covers exact `[verificationUnitId]`. Work Doer runs the test unit's expected-red command while leaving its product changes uncommitted, then invokes the existing coordinator-owned command/log/red-evidence producer so those immutable task artifacts bind the preimplementation source tree without granting Work Doer Desk write ownership; it then implements, runs the bound green replay, changes exactly the test and implementation status/progress markers, commits those tests/implementation/runtime bytes together, and pushes/fetches/readbacks that one red_green commit. Verification changes exactly its status/progress plus declared evidence in a later pushed/read-back commit. Final no-extra-fields `SuccessorImplementationUnitReceipt={version:1,successorKey,doerAttemptOrdinal,unitId,phase,status:'completed',checkpointKind,checkpointUnitIds,checkpointUnitSetSha256,sourceBaseSha,sourceHeadSha,treeSha,redEvidencePath,redEvidenceSha256,commandEvidencePaths,commandEvidenceSetSha256,artifactPaths,artifactSetSha256,runtimeDoingPath,runtimeDoingBeforeSha256,runtimeDoingAfterSha256,completedAt}` replaces every earlier form. phase is test|implementation|verification; checkpointKind is red_green for test/implementation and verification for verification; both red_green receipts carry the same exact two unit IDs, source head/tree, runtime before/after, and completedAt, while only test has nonnull red evidence. Verification carries its one ID and null red evidence. The first checkpoint before hash equals the dispatch initial hash; each later checkpoint before equals the prior checkpoint after. Receipts within one checkpoint do not chain to each other.

- Exact successor action `record-doer-checkpoint` replaces `record-doer-unit`. It is legal only in implementation_running for the one running doer attempt and requires only ordered flags `--doer-attempt D --group G --checkpoint red_green|verification --units-json U --source-head H --runtime-before-sha256 B --runtime-after-sha256 A`; U is compact canonical no-LF JSON and byte-equals the registry checkpoint unit array. Exact no-extra-fields success is `{mode:'successor',action:'record-doer-checkpoint',journalPath,journalSha256,phase:'implementation_running',doerAttemptOrdinal,groupId,checkpointKind,unitReceipts,unitReceiptSetSha256,sourceHeadSha,runtimeDoingAfterSha256}`, where unitReceipts is the checkpoint-order `{unitId,receiptPath,receiptSha256}[]` and its set hash covers those compact canonical bytes. release-terminal validates the preexisting immutable red/command evidence, exact product commit/tree/runtime blob, group order, status mutations, and all output/test blobs; atomically appends/pushes/readbacks both red_green receipts or the one verification receipt before returning. Work Doer cannot start the next checkpoint until that full result and every receipt validate. The final Work Doer prompt version is `Spoonjoy repair successor doer v3`; its rules line is byte-identical to v2 through `consume only the bound immediately-prior outcome set;` and then exact ` execute and evidence each red test without committing its red tree; accept one red_green checkpoint for each a+b pair and one verification checkpoint for c; require each checkpoint runtime-after hash to equal the next checkpoint runtime-before hash; revalidate every immutable hash before each checkpoint; use strict TDD; do not run Units32-37; return only validated artifact locators\n`. All other v2 prompt lines/order remain byte-identical. Final implementation evidence selects one receipt per registry unit, but ancestry/runtime ordering is over the two checkpoints per group; two red_green receipts sharing one commit/runtime transition are required, not duplication.

- Bootstrap remote observation has immutable fetch retry lineage. Replacement `SuccessorBootstrapPushObservation={pushCommand,lsRemoteAttemptOrdinal,priorLsRemoteCommands,lsRemoteCommand,fetchAttemptOrdinal,priorFetchCommands,fetchCommand,observedRemoteSha,outcome,updatedAt}` uses priorLsRemoteCommands and priorFetchCommands as contiguous processAttemptOrdinal-ordered terminal RegisteredProcessCommandEnvelope arrays. No-match ls-remote sets fetchAttemptOrdinal null, priorFetchCommands exact `[]`, fetchCommand null, observedRemoteSha null, and outcome absent. A matching ls-remote sets positive fetchAttemptOrdinal; every failed/signal/timeout/warning fetch is appended immutably to priorFetchCommands and authorizes only the next ordinal of the same read-only registered fetch, while the first succeeded/reconciled clean fetch occupies fetchCommand and alone permits candidate|conflict classification after exact ref/tree/blob readback. No final observation exists with a failed fetch, no command result is overwritten, and response-loss recovery resumes from the longest pushed/read-back envelope prefix.

- Runtime probes are immutable typed evidence. Exact no-extra-fields `SuccessorAgentRuntimeProbe={version:1,successorKey,runtimeKind,attemptOrdinal,reviewOrdinal,reviewRole,probeKind,probeOrdinal,cancellationId,agentId,adapterObservationId,status,returnedBytesSha256,observedAt}` uses runtimeKind planner_suite|doer_suite|planner_review|implementation_review; suite kinds have null review fields, review kinds have their exact positive ordinal/role; probeKind lifecycle has null cancellationId and its own positive contiguous ordinal, while cancellation has the exact cancellationId and global ordinal 1..3. status is running|completed|errored|cancelled; returnedBytesSha256 is nonnull only for completed and hashes the complete sanitized adapter bytes, otherwise null. adapterObservationId is the adapter's create-once immutable observation token, so response-loss reuses byte-identical evidence rather than probing again. Exact paths are `suite/planner/attempt-<N>-runtime-<lifecycle|cancellation>-probe-<P>.v1.json`, `suite/doer/attempt-<N>-runtime-<lifecycle|cancellation>-probe-<P>.v1.json`, `suite/planner/attempt-<N>-review-<R>-runtime-<lifecycle|cancellation>-probe-<P>.v1.json`, or the implementation-review attempt root's `runtime-<lifecycle|cancellation>-probe-<P>.v1.json`. PreReleaseArtifact and the owning SuiteArtifactRef add kind agent_runtime_probe. Every probe is appended/pushed/read back before it can advance status, authorize termination/cancellation, or appear in a probe set; recovery validates the contiguous path/token/hash prefix and never fabricates or rewrites a probe.

- Interrupted suites have an executable successor. Exact no-extra-fields `SuccessorSuiteRuntimeTermination={version:1,successorKey,runtimeKind,attemptOrdinal,dispatchPath,dispatchSha256,agentId,outcome,cancellationIntentPath,cancellationIntentSha256,cancellationReceiptPath,cancellationReceiptSha256,terminalProbePath,terminalProbeSha256,runtimeCheckpointPath,runtimeCheckpointSha256,completedAt}` lives at `suite/<planner|doer>/attempt-<N>-termination.v1.json`, uses outcome runtime_errored|runtime_cancelled, and is registered as suite_termination after every named artifact is immutable. Spontaneous runtime_errored has all cancellation fields null; runtime_cancelled and errored after intent require all four cancellation fields. Planner runtimeCheckpoint fields are null after the snapshot-publication cleanup/reconciliation matrix; doer fields name the frozen doer_runtime_checkpoint and require the complete doer ledger. Final SuccessorSuiteAttempt status interrupted has terminalOutcome runtime_errored|runtime_cancelled, includes agent_runtime_probe and suite_termination in its legal immutable artifact prefix, is registered as suite_attempt, and has canonical endedAt. The next planner ordinal's prior_planner_outcomes set is exactly the prior suite_attempt plus suite_termination; the next doer ordinal's priorDoerOutcomes is exactly the prior suite_attempt, suite_termination, doer_runtime_checkpoint, and doer_ledger. Planner/doer histories permit these interrupted outcomes in contiguous order, and the corresponding v3 prompt consumes the immediately prior set before fresh dispatch. No errored or cancelled suite dead-ends, skips an ordinal, or requires fictional cancellation.

- Implementation findings are product-path repair inputs only. Final implementation `ReviewFinding.file` is exact `{domain:'repo',path}`; domain task and every unknown domain reject at runtime-report parsing before a finding report or suite outcome exists. Planner reviews remain the sole review surface for planning/doing/task-document findings. The total unique-array comparator is `compareUtf8Binary(file.path)`, then numeric line ascending, then `compareUtf8Binary(code)`, then `compareUtf8Binary(summary)`; equality across all four components is a duplicate. code uses its existing finite ASCII domain, and path/summary compare their exact UTF-8 bytes without locale or normalization. Mandatory fixtures include domain rejection, ASCII case inversion, composed/decomposed Unicode, multi-byte values, numeric line ties, duplicate equality, and every later-tuple tie break. Every finding/set hash uses the array produced by this comparator.

- Branch conflicts roll over without mutating shared state or asking the operator. Bootstrap push_conflict and doer-transition push_conflict freeze their existing conflict receipt, mark the current successor terminal branch_conflict, and permit only exact coordinator action `rollover-conflict --conflict-receipt P`. Work Merger builds compact canonical preimage `{version:1,predecessorSuccessorKey,conflictKind,conflictReceiptPath,conflictReceiptSha256,acceptedBaseSha,observedRemoteSha,rolloverOrdinal}`; rolloverOrdinal is the first positive ordinal whose derived branch/worktree/task paths are all proven absent by registered read-only observations. rolloverKeySha256 hashes that preimage; the new successorKey is rolloverKeySha256 and branch is `worker/<successorSlug>-rollover-<first12>`. Exact no-extra-fields `SuccessorBranchConflictRollover={version:1,predecessorSuccessorKey,conflictKind,conflictReceiptPath,conflictReceiptSha256,acceptedBaseSha,observedRemoteSha,rolloverOrdinal,rolloverKeySha256,successorKey,branch,worktreePath,taskPath,createdAt}` is appended/pushed/read back before fresh prepared bootstrap. Exact action result is `{mode:'successor',action:'rollover-conflict',journalPath,journalSha256,phase:'branch_conflict',rolloverPath,rolloverSha256,successorKey,branch,worktreePath,taskPath}`. The conflicting local/remote branch and worktree become immutable evidence and are never deleted, reset, force-pushed, or reused; the fresh successor starts from acceptedBaseSha and retains the conflict/rollover pair in lineage. Path collision advances rolloverOrdinal through another read-only observation only. The older explicit branch-ownership-resolution gates are invalid.

- Spawn-gate source identity survives terminal cleanup. Exact no-extra-fields `TrustedSourceFile={absolutePath,device,inode,byteLength,sha256}` is captured with no-follow regular-file reads; TrustedToolchain adds `spawnGateScript:TrustedSourceFile`. Final `ProcessLaunchSpec={argv,cwd,scriptPath,scriptSha256,registrationBundlePathIndex,registrationBundleSha256Index}` requires cwd and scriptPath absolute, scriptPath/sha256 byte-equal spawnGateScript, and argv's script operand equal that absolute path rather than `scripts/release-spawn-gate.ts`. For eligible ordinary-normal/repaired-root Slugger, spawnGateScript is exact `<validatorRuntimePath>/scripts/release-spawn-gate.ts`, cwd is validatorRuntimePath, and source/inode/hash are frozen before spawn authorization. After ArchiveValidationReceipt, release-terminal prepares, authorizes, and pre-spawns the paused gate and child through child_recorded while the validator runtime exists; both registered processes must prove they loaded the hash-frozen source and wait only on child-run authorization. Only then may TerminalResourceCleanup remove validator runtime/archive. After cleanup absence is pushed/read back, release-terminal advances run_authorized, publishes the child-run bytes, and observes the one child; aborted/terminal pre-cleanup outcomes still permit cleanup but no second generation. Noneligible identities skip this preparation. Overall completion requires terminal/aborted Slugger plus resource cleanup; Slugger effect authorization still requires cleanup first. Substitution, cwd drift, inode/hash change, deletion before child_recorded, post-cleanup spawn, or a second gate/child rejects. This ordering replaces every rule requiring validator absence before Slugger preparation while preserving absence before the `ouro msg` effect.

- Final archive validation carries its TrackArchive proof in every phase. Exact replacement `ArchiveValidationAttempt={version:1,attemptOrdinal,priorFailedAttemptPaths,priorFailedAttemptSetSha256,mergeSha,validatorMergeSha,executionHost,validatorRuntimePath,validatorArchivePath,validatorArchiveSha256,validatorSourceTreeSha256,manifestPath,trackDecision,trackDispositionSha256,trackDispositionCommitSha,trackArchiveLocator,trackArchiveSha256,repairIndexPath,repairIndexSha256,phase,commandResult,startedAt,updatedAt}` has immutable fields through prepared|failed|validated. trackDecision kept_active requires both TrackArchive fields null and target absence; archived requires both nonnull and exact final TrackArchive locator/receipt hash. validator hashes are always nonnull and match TerminalCleanup; repair-index fields are both null or both nonnull according to the already-declared branch. prepared alone has commandResult null; failed has one terminal non-success/positive-warning result; validated has exact clean exit zero. Final `ArchiveValidationReceipt={version:1,attemptOrdinal,priorFailedAttemptPaths,priorFailedAttemptSetSha256,mergeSha,validatorMergeSha,executionHost,validatorRuntimePath,validatorArchivePath,validatorArchiveSha256,validatorSourceTreeSha256,manifestPath,trackDecision,trackDispositionSha256,trackDispositionCommitSha,trackArchiveLocator,trackArchiveSha256,repairIndexPath,repairIndexSha256,commandResult,validatedAt}` projects every member byte-identically, replacing only phase/startedAt/updatedAt with validatedAt equal the validated attempt updatedAt. The final control envelope repeats the same pair. Mixed nullability, field drift, attempt mutation, missing archived proof, kept-active locator, or receipt projection mismatch rejects.
